                        āūṃ 
medskip

                śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ 
medskip

         atha bṛhatpārāśarahorāśāstram 

gajānanaṃ bhūtagaṇādisevitaṃ kapitthajambūphalasārabhakṣaṇam 
umāsutaṃ śokavināśakāraṇaṃ namāmi vighneśvarapādapaṃkajam 

medskiphrulemedskip

          sṛṣṭikramakathanādhyāyaḥ  
medskip

athaikadā muniśreṣṭhaṃ trikalajñaṃ parāśaram 
papracchopetya maitreyaḥ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ  

bhagavan paramaṃ puṇyaṃ guhyaṃ vedāṅgamuttamam 
triskandhaṃ jyautiṣaṃ horā gaṇitaṃ saṃhiteti ca  

eteṣvapi triṣu śreṣṭhā horeti śrūyate mune 
tvattastāṃ śrotumicchāmi kṛpayā vada me prabho  

kathaṃ sṛṣṭiriyaṃ jātā jagataśca layaḥ katham 
khasthānāṃ bhūsthatānāṃ ca sambandhaṃ vada vistarāt  

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā vipra lokānugrahakārinā 
athāhaṃ paramaṃ brahma tacchaktiṃ bhāratīṃ punaḥ  

sūrya natvā grahapatiṃ jagadutpattikāraṇm 
vakṣyāmi vedanayanaṃ yathā brahmamukhācchrutam  

śāntāya gurubhaktāya sarvadā satyavādine 
āstikāya pradatavyaṃ tataḥ śreyo hyavāpsyati  

na deyaṃ paraśiṣyāya nāstikāya śaṭhaya vā 
datte pratidinaṃ duḥkhaṃ jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  

eko'vyaktātmako viṣṇuranādiḥ prabhurīśvaraḥ 
śuddhasatvo jagatsvāmī nirguṇastriguṇānvitaḥ  

saṃsārakārakaḥ śrīmānnimittātmā pratāpavān 
ekāṃśena jagatsarva sṛjatyavati līlayā  

tripādaṃ tasya devatya hyamṛtaṃ tattvadarśinaḥ 
vidanti tatpramāṇaṃ ca sapradhānaṃ tathaikapāt  

vyaktāvyaktātmako viṣṇurvāsudevastu gīyate 
yadavyaktātmako viṣṇuḥ śktitadvayasamanvitaḥ  

vyaktātmakastribhiryuktaḥ kathyate'nantaśaktimān 
sattvapradhānā śrīśaktirbhūśktiśca rajoguṇā  

śaktistṛtīyā yā prāktā nīlākhyā dhvāntarūpiṇī 
vāsudevaścaturtho'bhūcchrīśaktyā prerito yadā  

saṃkarṣaṇaśca pradyumno'niruddha iti mūrtidhṛk 
tamaḥśktyā'nvitā viṣṇurdevaḥ saṃkarṣaṇābhidhaḥ  

pradyumno rajasā śaktyā'nirudhhaḥ sattvayā yutaḥ 
mahān saṃkarṣaṇājjātaḥ pradyumnādyadahaṃakṛtiḥ  

aniruddhāt svayaṃ jāto brahmāhaṃkākamūrtidhṛk 
sarvaṣu sarvaśaktiśca svaśaktyā'dhikayā yutaḥ  

ahaṃkārastridha bhūtvā sarvametadvistarāt 
sāttviko rājasaścaiva tāmasaścedahaṃkṛtiḥ  

devā vaikārikājjātāstaijasādindriyāṇi 
tāmasaccaivabhū tāni khādīni svasvaśaktibhiḥ  

śrīśaktyā sahito viṣṇuḥ sadā pāti jagattrayam 
bhūśaktyā sṛjate brahmā nīlaśaktyā śivo'tti hi  

sarveṣu caiva jīveṣu paramātmā virājate 
sarvaṃ hi tadidaṃ brahman sthitaṃ hi paramātmani  

sarveṣu caiva jīveṣu sthitaṃhyaṃśadvayaṃ kvacit 
jīvāṃśo hyadhikastadvat paramātmāṃśakaḥ kila  

sūryādayo grahāḥ sarve brahmakāmadviṣādayaḥ 
ete cānye ca bahavaḥ paramātmāṃśakādhikāḥ  

śaktayaśca tathaiteṣamadhikāṃśāḥ śriyādayaḥ 
svasvaśaktiṣu cānyāsu jñeyā jīvāṃśakādhikāḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

        athāvatārakathanādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

rāmakṛṣṇādayo ye hyavatārā ramāpateḥ 
te'pi jīvāṃśasaṃyuktāḥ kiṃvā brūhi muniśvara  

rāmaḥ kṛṣṇaśca bho vipra nṛsiṃhaḥ sūkarastathā 
ete pūrṇāvatārāśca hyanye jīvāṃśakānvitāḥ  

avatārāṇyanekāni hyajasya paramātmanaḥ 
jīvānāṃ karmaphalado graharūpī janārdanaḥ  

daityānāṃ balanāśāya devānāṃ balabṛddhaye 
dharmasaṃstāpanārthāya grahājjātāḥ śubhāḥ kramāt  

rāmo'vatāraḥ sūryasya candrasya yadunāyakaḥ 
nṛsiṃho bhūmiputrasya buddhaḥ somasutasya ca  

vāmano vibudhejyasya bhārgavo bhārgavasya ca 
kūrmo bhāskaraputrasya saiṃhikeyasya sūkaraḥ  

ketormīnāvatāraśca ye cānye te'pi kheṭajāḥ 
parātmāṃśo'dhiko yeṣu te sarve khecarābhidhaḥ  

jīvāṃśohyadhiko yeṣu jīvāste cai prakīrtitaḥ 
sūryādibho grahebhyaśca paramātmāṃśaniḥsṛtāḥ  

rāmakṛṣṇādayaḥ sarva hyavatārā bhavanti cai 
tatraiva te vilīyante punaḥ kāryottara sadā  

jīvāṃśaniḥsṛtāsteṣāṃ tebhyo jātā narādayaḥ 
te'pi tatraiva līyante te'vyakte samayanti hi  

idaṃ te kathitaṃ vipra sarvaṃ yasmin bhavediti 
bhūtānyapi bhaviṣyanti tattajjātanti tadvidaḥ  

vinā tajjyaitiṣaṃ nānyo jñātuṃ śaknoti karhicit 
tatmādavaśyamadhyeyaṃ bhāhmaṇeśca viśeṣataḥ  

yo naraḥ śāstramajñātvā jyautiṣaṃ khalu nindati 
rauravaṃ narakaṃ bhuktvā cāndhatvaṃ cānyajanmani  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha grahaguṇasvarūpādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

kathitaṃ bhavatā premṇā grahāvataraṇaṃ mune 
teṣaṃ guṇasvarūpādyaṃ kṛpayā kathyatāṃ punaḥ  

śṛṇu vipra pravakṣyāmi bhagrahāṇāṃ paristhitim 
ākāśe yāni dṛśyante jyotirbimbātyanekaśaḥ  

teṣu nakṣatrasaṃjñāni grahasaṃjñāni kānicit 
tāni nakṣatranāmāni sthirasthānāni yāni cai  

gacchanto bhāni gṛhṇanti satataṃ ye tu te grahaḥ 
bhacakrasya nagaśvyaṃśā aśvinyādisamāhvayāḥ  

taddvādaśavibhāgāstu tulya meṣādisaṃjñakāḥ 
prasiddhā rāśayaḥ santi grahāstvarkādisaṃjñakāḥ  

rāśīnāmudayo lagnaṃ tadvaśādeva janminām 
grahayogviyogābhyāṃ phalaṃ cintyaṃ śubhāśubham  

saṃjñā nakṣatravṛndānāṃ jñeyāḥ sāmānyaśāstrataḥ 
etacchāstrānusāreṇa rāśikeeṭaphalaṃ bruve  

yasmin kāle yataḥ kheṭā yānti dṛggaṇitaikatām 
tata eva sphuṭāḥ kāryāḥ dikkālau ca sphuṭau vida  

svasvadeśodbhavaiḥ sādhyaṃ lagnaṃ rāśyudayaiḥ sphuṭam 
athādau vacmi kheṭānāṃ jātirūpaguṇānaham  

atha kheṭā raviścandro maṅgalaśca budhastathā 
guruḥ śukraḥ śanī rāhuḥ ketuścaite yathākramam  

tatrārkaśanibhūputrāḥ kṣīṇendurāhuketavaḥ 
krūrāḥ śeṣagrahā saumyāḥ krūraḥ krūrayuto budhaḥ  

sarvātmā ca divānātho manaḥ kumudabāndhavaḥ 
sattvaṃ kujo budhaiḥ prokto budho vāṇīpradāyakaḥ  

devejyo jñānasukhado bhṛgurvīryapradayakaḥ 
ṛṣibhiḥ prāktanaiḥ proktaśchāyāsūnuśca duḥkhadaḥ  

ravicandrau tu rājānau netā jñeyo dharātmajaḥ 
budho rājakumāraśca sacivau gurubhārgavau  

preṣyako raviputraśca senā svarbhānupucchakau 
evaṃ krameṇa vai vipra sūryādīn pravicintayet  

raktaśyāmo divādhīśo gauragātro niśākaraḥ 
nātyuccāṅgaḥ kujo rakto dūrvāśyāmo budhastathā  

gauragātro gururjñeyaḥ śukraḥ śyāvastathaiva ca 
kṛṣṇadeho raveḥ putro jñāyate dvijasattama  

vahnyambuśikhijā viṣṇuviḍhaujaḥ śacikā dvija 
sūryādīnāṃ khagānāṃ ca devā jñeyāḥ krameṇa ca  

klīvau dvau saumyasaurī ca yuvatīndubhṛgū dvija 
narāḥ śeṣāśca vijñeyā bhānurbhaumo gurustathā  

agnibhūminabhastoyavāyavaḥ kramato dvija 
bhaumādīnāṃ grahāṇāṃ ca tattvānīti yathākramam  

guruśukrau vipravarṇau kujārkau kṣatriyau dvija 
śaśisomyau vaiśyavarṇau śaniḥ śūdro dvijottam  

jīvasūryendravaḥ sattvaṃ budhaśukrau rajastathā 
sūryaputrabharāputrau tamaḥprakṛtikau dvija  

madhupiṅgaladṛksūryaścaturasraḥ śucirdvija 
pittaprakṛtiko dhīmān pumānalpakaco dvija  

bahuvātakaphaḥ prājñaścandro bṛttatanurdvija 
śubhadṛṅmadhuvākyaśca  cañcalo madanāturaḥ  

krūro raktekṣaṇo  bhaumaścapalodāramūrtikaḥ 
pittaprakṛtikaḥ krodhī kṛśamadhyatanurdvija  

vapuḥśreṣṭhaḥ śliṣṭavākca hyatihāsyarucirbudhaḥ 
pittavān kaphavān vipra mārutaprakṛtistathā  

bṛhadgātro guruścaiva piṅgalo mūrddhajekṣaṇe 
kaphaprakṛtiko dhīmān sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ  

sukhi kāntavapu śreṣṭhaḥ sulocano bhṛgoḥ sutaḥ 
kāvyakartā kaphādhikyo'nilātmā vakramūrdhajaḥ  

kṛśdīrghatanuḥ śauriḥ piṅgadṛṣṭyanilātmakaḥ 
sthūladanto'lasaḥ paṃguḥ khararomakaco dvija  

dhūmrākāro nīlatanurvanastho'pi bhayaṃkaraḥ 
vātaprakṛtiko dhīmān svarbhānustatsamaḥ śikhī  

asthi raktastathā majjā tvag vasā vīryameva ca 
snāyureṣāmadhīśāśca kramāt sūryādayo dvija  

devālayajalaṃ vahnikrīḍādīnāṃ tathaiva ca 
kośaśayyotkarāṇāntu nāthāṃ sūryādayaḥ kramāt  

ayanakṣaṇavārartumāsapakṣasamā dvija 
sūryādīnāṃ kramājjñeyā nirviśaṃkaṃ dvijottama  

kaṭukṣāratiktamiśramadhurāmlakaṣāyakāḥ 
krameṇa sarve vijñeyāḥ sūryādīnāṃ rasā iti  

budhejyau balinau pūrve ravibhaumau ca dakṣiṇe 
paścime sūryaputraśca sitacandrau tathottare  

niśāyāṃ balinaścandrakujasaurā bhavanti hi 
sarvadā jño balī jñeyo dine śeṣā dvijottama  

kṛṣṇe ca balinaḥ krūrāḥ saumyā vīryayutāḥ site 
saumyāyane saumyakheṭo balī yāmyāyane'paraḥ  

varṣamāsāhahorāṇāṃ patayo balinastathā 
śamaṃbuguśucaṃrādyā vṛddhito vīryavattaraḥ  

sūrye janayati sthūlān durbhagān sūryaputrakaḥ 
kṣīropetāṃstathā candraḥ kaṭukādyān dharāsutaḥ  

puṣpavṛkṣaṃ bhṛgoḥ putre gurujñau saphalāphalau 
nīrasān sūryaputraśca evaṃ jñeyāḥ khagā dvija  

rāhuścāṇḍālajātiśca keturjātyantarastathā 
śikhisvarbhānumandānāṃ valmīkaḥ sthānamucyate  

citrakanthā phanīndrasya ketuśchidrayuto dvija 
sīsaṃ rahornīlamaṇiḥ ketorjñeyo dvijottama  

guroḥ pītāmbaraṃ vipra bhṛgoḥ kṣaumaṃ tathaiva ca 
raktakṣaumaṃ bhāskarasya indoḥ kṣaumaṃ sitaṃ dvija  

budhasya kṛṣṇakṣaumaṃ tu raktavastraṃ kujasya ca 
vastraṃ citraṃ śanervipra paṭtavastraṃ tathaiva ca  

bhṛgorṛturvasantaśca kujabhānvośca grīṣmakaḥ 
candrasya varṣā vijñeyā śaraccaiva tathā vidaḥ  

hemanto'pi gurorjñeyaḥ śanestu śiśiro dvija 
aṣṭau māsāśca svarbhānoḥ ketormāsatrayaṃ dvija  

rāhvārapaṃgucandraśca vijñeyā dhātukhecarāḥ 
mūlagrahau sūryaśukrau aparā jīvasaṃjñakāḥ  

graheṣu mando vṛddho'sti āyurvṛddhipradāyakaḥ 
naisargike bahusamān dadāti dvijasattama  

meṣo vṛṣo mṛgaḥ kanyā karko mīnastathā tulā 
sūryādīnāṃ kramādete kathitā uccarāśyaḥ  

bhāgā daśa trayo'ṣṭāśvyastithyo'kṣā bhamitā nakhāḥ 
uccāt saptamabhaṃ nīcaṃ tairevāṃśaiḥ prakīrtitam  

raveḥ simhe nakhāṃśāśca trikoṇamapare svabham 
uccamindorvṛṣe tryaṃśāstrikoṇamapareṃ'śakāḥ  

meṣe'rkāṃśāstu bhaumasya trikoṇamapare svabham 
uccaṃ budhasya kanyāyāmuktaṃ pañcadaśāṃśakāḥ  

tataḥ pañcāṃśakāḥ proktaṃ trikoṇamapare svabham 
cāpe daśāṃśā jīvasya trikoṇamapare svabham  

tule śukrasya tithyaṃśāstrikoṇamapare svabham 
śaneḥ kumbhe nakhāṃśāśca  trikoṇamapare svabham  

trikoṇāt svātsukhasvā'ntyadhīdharmāyuḥsvatuṅgapāḥ 
suhṛdo ripavaśvānve samāścobhayalakṣaṇāḥ  

daśavandhvāyasahajasvāntyasthāstu parasparam 
tatkāle mitratāṃ yānti ripavo'nyatra saṃsthitāḥ  

tatkāle ca nisarge ca mitraṃ cedadhimitrakam 
mitraṃ mitrasamatve tu śatruḥ śatrusamatvake  

samo mitrariputve tu śatrutve tvadhiśatrutā 
evaṃ vivicya daivajño jātakasya phalaṃ vadet  

svocce śubhaṃ phalaṃ pūrṇa trikoṇe pādavarjitam 
svarkṣe'rdhaṃ mitragehe tu pādamātraṃ prakīrtitam  

pādārdhaṃ samabhe proktaṃ śūnyaṃ nīcāstaśatrubhe 
tadvadduṣṭaphalaṃ brūyad vyatyayena vicakṣaṇaḥ  

tryaṃśāḍhyaviśvabhāgaiśca caturbhaiḥ sahito raviḥ 
dhūmo nāma mahādoṣaḥ sarvakarmavināśakaḥ  

dhūmo maṇḍalataḥ śuddho vyatīpāto'tra doṣadaḥ 
saṣadbho'tra vyatīpātaḥ pariveṣo'tidoṣakṛt  

pariveṣaścyutaścakrādindracāpastu doṣadaḥ 
vitryaṃśāsyaṣṭibhāgādhyaścāpaḥ ketukhago'śubhaḥ  

ekarāśiyutaḥ ketuḥ sūryatulyaḥ prajāyate 
aprakāśagrahāścaite pāpā doṣapradāḥ smṛtāḥ  

sūryendulagnageṣveṣu vaṃśāyurjñānanāśanam 
iti dhūmādidoṣāṇāṃ sthitiḥ padmāsanoditā  

ravivārādiśanyantaṃ gulikādi nirūpyate 
divasānaṣṭadhā bhaktvā vāreśād gaṇeyat kramāt  

aṣṭmoṃ'śo nirīśaḥ syācchanyaṃśo gulikaḥsmṛtaḥ 
rātrimapyaṣṭadhā kṛtvā vāreśāt pañcamāditaḥ  

gaṇayedaṣṭamaḥ khaṇḍo niṣyatiḥ parikīrtitaḥ 
śnyaṃśo gulikaḥ prokto ravyaṃśaḥ kālasaṃjñakaḥ  

bhaumāṃśo mṛtyurādiṣṭo gurvaṃśo yamaghaṇṭkaḥ 
somyāṃśo'rdhapraharakaḥ svasvadeśodbhavaḥ sphuṭaḥ  

gulikeṣṭavaśāllagnaṃ sphuṭaṃ yat svasvadeśajam 
gulikaṃ procyate tasmājjātakasya phalaṃ vadet  

bhāṃśapādasamaiḥ prāṇaiścarādyarkatrikoṇabhāt 
udayādiṣṭakālāntaṃ yadbhaṃ prāṇapadaṃ hi tat  

sveṣṭakālaṃ palīkṛtya tithyāptaṃ bhādikaṃ ca yat 
carāgadvibhasaṃsthe'rke bhanau yuṅ navame sute  

sphuṭaṃ prāṇapadākhyaṃ tallagnaṃ jñeyaṃ dvijottama 
lagnād dvikoṇe turye ca rājye prāṇapadaṃ tadā  

śubhaṃ janma vijānīyāttathaivaikādaśe'pi ca 
anyasthāne sthitaṃ cet syāt tadā janmāśubhaṃ vadet  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha rāśisvarūpādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

ahorātrasya pūrvāntyalopād horā'vaśiṣyate 
tasya vijñānamātreṇa jātakarmaphalaṃ vadet  

yadavyaktātmako viṣṇuḥ kālarupo janārdanaḥ 
tasyāṅgāni nibodha tvaṃ kramānmeṣādirāśyaḥ  

meṣo vṛṣaśca mithunaḥ karkasiṃhakumārikāḥ 
tulāli'śca dhanurnakre kumbho mīnastataḥ param  

śīrṣānane tathā bāhū hṛtkroḍakaṭibastayaḥ 
guhyoruyugale jānuyugme vai jaṅghake tathā  

caranau dvau tathā meṣāt jñeyāḥ śīrṣādayaḥ kramāt 
carasthiradvisvabhāvāḥ krūrākrūrau narastriyau  

pittānilatridhātvaukyaśleṣmikāśca kriyādayaḥ 
raktavarṇo bṛhadgātraścatuṣpādrātrivikramī  

pūrvavāsī nṛpajñātiḥ śailacārī rajoguṇī 
pṛṣṭhodayī pāvakī ca meṣarāśiḥ kujādhipaḥ  

śvetaḥ śukrādhipo dīrghaścatuṣpāccharvarībalī 
yāmyeṭ grāmyo vaṇigbhūmirajaḥ pṛṣṭhodayo vṛṣaḥ  

śīrṣodayī nṛmithunaṃ sagadaṃ ca savīṇakam 
pratyagvāyurdvipādrātribalī grāmavrajo'nilī  

samagātro haridvirṇo mithunākhyo budhādhipaḥ 
pāṭalo vanacārī ca brāhmaṇo niśi vīryavān  

bahupādacaraḥ sthaulyatanuḥ sattvaguṇī jalī 
pṛṣṭhodayī karkarāśirmṛgāṃkā'dhipatiḥ smṛtaḥ  

siṃhaḥ sūryādhipaḥ sattvī catuṣpāt kṣatriyo vanī 
śīrṣodayī bṛhadgātraḥpāṇḍuḥ pūrveḍ dyuvīryavān  

pārvatīyātha kanyākhyā rāśirdinabalānvitā 
śīrṣodayā ca madhyāṃgā dvipādyāmyacarā ca sā  

sā sasyadahanā vaiśyā citravarṇā prabhañjinī 
kumārī tamasā yuktā bālabhāvā budhādhipā  

śīrṣodayī dyuvīryāḍhyastulaḥ kṛṣṇo rajoguṇī 
paścimo bhūcaro ghātī śūdro madhyatanurdvipāt  

śukrā'dhipo'tha svalpāṃgo bahupādbrāhmaṇo bilī 
saumyastho dinavīryāḍhyaḥ piśaṃgo jalabhūvaḥ  

romasvāḍhyo'titīkṣṇāgro vṛścikaśca kujādhipaḥ 
pṛṣṭhodayī tvatha dhanurgurusvāmī ca sāttvikaḥ  

piṃgalo niśivīryāḍhyaḥ pāvakaḥ kṣatriyo dvipād 
ādāvante catuṣpādaḥ samagātro dhanurdharaḥ  

pūrvastho vasudhācārī tejasvī brahmaṇā kṛtaḥ 
mandādhipastamī bhaumī yāmyeṭ ca niśi vīryavān  

pṛṣṭhodayī bṛhadgātraḥ karburo vanabhūcaraḥ 
ādau catuṣpadonte tu vipado jalago mataḥ  

kumbhaḥ kumbhī naro babhruvarṇo madhyatanurdvipāt 
dyuvīryo jalamadhyastho vātaśīrṣodayī tamaḥ  

śūdraḥ paścimadeśasya svāmī daivākariḥ smṛtaḥ 
mīnau pucchāsyasaṃlagnau mīnarāśirdivābalī  

jalī sattvaguṇāḍhyaśca svastho jalacaro dvijaḥ 
apado madhyadehī ca saumyastho hyubhayodayī  

surācāryādhipaśceti rāśīnāṃ gaditā guṇāḥ 
triṃśadbhāgātmakānāṃ ca sthūlasūkṣmaphalāya ca  

athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣva munipuṃgava 
janmalagnaṃ ca saṃśodhya niṣekaṃ pariśodhayet  

tadahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi maitreya tvaṃ vidhāraya 
janmalagnāt parijñānaṃ niṣekaṃ sarvjantu yat  

yasmin bhāve sthito mandastasya mānderyadantaram 
lagnabhāgyāntaraṃ yojyaṃ yacca rāśyādi jāyate  

māsādi tanmitaṃ jñeyaṃ janmataḥ prak niṣekajam 
yadyadṛśyadaleṅgeśastadendorbhuktabhāgayuk  

tatkāle sādhayellagnaṃ śodhayet pūrvavattanum 
tasmācchubhāśubhaṃ vācyaṃ garbhasthasya viśeṣataḥ  

śubhāśubhaṃ vadet pitrorjīvanaṃ maraṇaṃ tathā 
evaṃ niṣekalagnena samyag jñeyaṃ svakalpanāt  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha viśeṣalagnādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

athāhaṃ sampravakṣyāmi tavāgre dvijasattama 
bhāvahorāghaṭīsaṃjñalagnānīti pṛthak pṛthak  

sūryodayaṃ samārabhya ghaṭikānāṃ tu paṃcakam 
prayāti janmaparyantaṃ bhāvalagnaṃ tadeva hi  

iṣṭaṃ ghaṭyādikaṃ bhaktvā paṃcabhirbhādijaṃ phalam 
yojyamaudayike sūrye bhāvalagnaṃ sphuṭaṃ ca tat  

tathā sārdhadvighaṭikāmitādarkodayād dvija 
prayāti lagnaṃ tannāma horālagnaṃ pracakṣate  

iṣṭaghaṭyādikaṃ dvighnaṃ pañcāptaṃ bhādikaṃ ca yat 
yojyamaudayike bhānau horālagnaṃ sphuṭaṃ hi tat  

kathayāmi ghaṭīlagnaṃ sṛnu tvaṃ dvijasattama 
sūryodayat samārabhya janmakālāvadhi kramāt  

ekaikaghaṭikāmānāt lagnaṃ yadyāti bhādikam 
tadeva ghaṭikālagnaṃ kathitaṃ nāradādibhiḥ  

rāśayastu ghaṭītulyāḥ palārdhapramitāṃśakāḥ 
yojyamaudayike bhanau ghaṭīlagnaṃ sphuṭaṃ hi tat  

kramādeṣāṃ ca lagnānāṃ bhāvakoṣṭhaṃ pṛthak likhet 
ye grahā yatra bhe tatra te sthāpyā rāśilagnavat  

varṇadākhyadaśāṃ bhānāṃ kathayāmyatha te'grataḥ 
yasya vijñānamātreṇa vadedāyurbhavaṃ phalam  

ojalagnaprasūtānāṃ meṣādergaṇayet kramāt 
samalagnaprasūtānām mīnāderapasavyataḥ  

meṣamīnādito janmalagnāntaṃ gaṇayet sudhīḥ 
tathaiva horālagnāntaṃ gaṇayitvā tataḥ param  

ojatvena samatvena sayātīye ubhe yadi 
tarhi saṃkhye yojayīta vaijātye tu viyojayet  

meṣamīnāditaḥ paścādyo rāśiḥ sa tu varṇadaḥ 
etatprayojanaṃ vakṣye sṛṇu tvaṃ dvijapuṃgavaḥ 
horālagnabhayorneyā sabalādvarṇadā daśā  

yatsaṃkhye varṇado lagnāt tattatsaṃkhyākrameṇa tu 
kramayutkramabhedena daśā syādojayugmayo  

pāpadṛṣṭiḥ pāpayogo varṇdasya trikoṇake 
yadi syāt tarhi tadrāśiparyantaṃ tasya jīvanaṃ  

rudraśūle yathaivāyurmaraṇādi nirūpyate 
tathaiva varṇadasyapi trikoṇe pāpasaṃgame  

varṇadādapi bho vipra lagnavaccintayet phalam 
varṇadāt saptamād bhāvat kalatrāyurvicintayet  

ekādaśādagrajasya tṛtīyāttu yavīyasaḥ 
sutasya paṃcame vidyānmātuścaturthabhāvat  

pituśca navamād bhāvādayureevaṃ vicintayet 
śūlarāśidaśāyāṃ vai pravalāyāmariṣṭakam  

evaṃ tanvādibhāvānāṃ kartavyā varṇā daśā 
pūrvavacca phalaṃ jñeyaṃ dehināṃ ca śubhāśubham  

grahanāṃ varṇadā naiva rāśīnāṃ varṇdā daśā 
kṛtvārkadhā rāśidaśāṃ kramādantardaśāṃ vadet  

evamantardaśādiṃ ca kṛtvā tena phalaṃ vadet 
kramavyutkramabhedena likhedantardaśāmapi  

svasvadeśodbhavaṃ lagnaṃ janmalagnamimihocyate 
bhāvahorādilagnānāṃ sarvatraiva samakriyā  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha ṣoḍaśavargādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

śrutā grahaguṇāstvattastathā rāśiguṇa mune 
śrotamicchāmi bhāvānāṃ bhedāṃstān kṛpayā vada  

vargān ṣoḍaśa yānāha brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
tānahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi maitreya srūyatāmiti  

kṣetraṃ horā ca dreṣkāṇasturyāṃśaḥ saptamāṃśakaḥ 
navāṃśo daśamāṃśaśca sūryāmśaḥ ṣoḍaśāṃśakaḥ  

viṃśāṃśo vedavāhvaṃśo bhāṃśastriṃśāṃśakastataḥ 
khavedāṃśo'kṣavedāṃśaḥ ṣaṣṭhyaṃśaśca tataḥ param  

tatkṣetraṃ tasya kheṭasya rāśeryo yasya nāyakaḥ 
sūryendvorviṣame rāśau same tadviparītakam  

pitaraścandrahoreśā devāḥ sūryasya kīrtitāḥ 
rāśerarddhaṃ bhaveddhorā tāścaturviṃśatiḥ smṛtā 
meṣādi tāsāṃ horāṇāṃ parivṛttidvayaṃ bhavet  

rāśitribhāgādreṣkāṇāste ca ṣaṭtriṃśadīritāḥ 
parivṛttitrayaṃ teṣāṃ meṣādeḥ kramaśo bhavet  

svapaṃcanavamānāṃ ca rāśīnāṃ kramaśaśca te 
nāradā'gastidurvāsā dreṣkāṇeśāścarādiṣu  

svarkṣādikendrapatayasturyāṃśeśāḥ kriyādiṣu 
sanakaśca sanandaśca kumāraśca sanātanaḥ  

saptāṃśapāstvojagṛhe gaṇanīyā nijeśataḥ 
yugmarāśau tu vijñeyāḥ saptamarkṣādināyakāt  

kṣārakṣīrau ca dadhyājyau tathekṣurasasambhavaḥ 
madhyaśuddhajalāvoje same śuddhajalādikāḥ  

navāṃśeśāścare tasmātsthire tannavamāditaḥ 
ubhaye tatpaṃcamāderiti cintyaṃ vicakṣaṇauḥ 
devā nṛrākṣasāścaiva carādiṣu gṛheṣu ca  

daśamāṃśāḥ svataścaije yugma tannavamāt smṛtāḥ 
daśa pūrvādidikpālā indrā'gniyamarākṣasāḥ  

varuṇo mārutaścaiva kubereśānapadmajāḥ 
anantaśca kramādīye same vā vyutkrameṇa tu  

dvādaśāṃśasya gaṇanā tattatkṣetrādvinirdiśet 
teṣāmaghīśāḥ kramaśo gaṇeśā'śviyamāhayāḥ  

ajasiṃhā'śvito jñeyā ṣoḍaśāṃśāścarādiṣu 
ajaviṣṇū haraḥ sūrye hyoje yugme pratīpakam  

atha viṃśatibhāgānāmadhipā brahmaṇoditāḥ 
kriyāccare sthire cāpān mṛgundrād dvisvabhāvake  

kālī gaurī lakṣmīvijayā vimalā satī 
tārā jvālāmukhī śvetā lalitā bagalāmukhī  

pratyaṅgirā śacī raudrī bhavānī varadā jayā 
tripurā sumukhī ceti viṣame paricintayet  

samarāśau dayā medhā chinnaśīrṣā piśācinī 
dhūmāvatī ca mātaṅgī bālā bhadra'ruṇānalā  

piṅgalā chucchukā ghorā vārāhī vaiṣṇavī sitā 
bhuvaneśī bhairavī ca maṅgalā hyaparājitā  

siddhāṃśakānāmadhipāḥ siṃhādojabhage grahe 
karkadyugmabhage kheṭe skandaḥ parśudharo'nalaḥ  

viśvakarmā bhago mitro mayo'ntakavṛṣadhvajāḥ 
govindo madano bhīmaḥ siṃhādau viṣame kramāt 
karkādau samabhe bhīmādvilomena vicintayet  

bhāṃśādhipāḥ kramāddasrayamavahnipitāmahāḥ 
candreśāditijīvāhipitaro bhagasaṃjñitāḥ  

aryamārkatvaṣṭṭamarucchakrāgnimitravāsavāḥ 
nirṛtyudakaviśve'jagovindo vasavo'mbupaḥ  

tato'japādahirbudhnyaḥ pūṣā caiva prakīrtitāḥ 
nakṣatreśāstu bhāṃśeśā meṣādicarabhakramāt  

triṃśāṃśeśāśca viṣame kujarkījyajñabhārgavāḥ 
paṃcapaṃcāṣṭasaptākṣabhāgānāṃ vyatyayāt same  

vahniḥ samīraśakrau ca dhanado jaladastathā 
viṣameṣu kramājjñeyāḥ samarāśau viparyayāt  

catvāriṃśadvibhāgānāmadhipā viṣame kriyāt 
samabhe tulato jñeyāḥ svasvādhipasamanvitāḥ  

viṣṇuścandro marīciśca tvaṣṭā dhātā śivo raviḥ 
yamo yakṣaśca gandharvaḥ kālo varuṇa eva ca  

tathākṣavedabhāgānāmadhipāścarabhe kriyāt 
sthire siṃhād dvibhecāpāt vidhīśaviṣṇavaścare  

īśācyutasurajyeṣṭhā viṣṇukeśāḥ sthire dvibhe 
devāḥ paṃcadaśāvṛttyā vijñeyā dvijasattama  

rāśīn vihāya kheṭasya dvighnamaṃśādyamarkahṛt 
śeṣaṃ saikaṃ tadrāśerbhapāḥ ṣaṣṭyaṃśāpāḥ smṛtāḥ  

ghoraśca rākṣaśo devaḥ kubero yakṣakinnarau 
bhraṣṭaḥ kulaghno garalo vahnirmāyā purīṣakaḥ  

apāmpatirmarutvāṃśca kālaḥ sarpāmṛtendukāḥ 
mṛduḥ komalaherambabrahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ  

devārdrau kalināśaśca kṣitīśakamalākarau 
guliko mṛtyukālaśca dāvāgnirghorasaṃjñakaḥ  

yamaśca kaṇṭakasudhā'mṛtau pūrṇaniśākaraḥ 
viṣadagdhakulāntaśca mukhyo vaṃśakṣayastathā  

utpātakālasaumyākhyāḥ komalaḥ śītalābhidhaḥ 
karāladaṃṣṭracandrāsyau pravīṇaḥ kālapāvakaḥ  

daṇḍabhṛnnirmalaḥ saumyaḥ krūro'tiśītalo'mṛtaḥ 
payodhibhramaṇākhyau ca candrarekhā tvayugmapāḥ  

same bhe vyatyayājjñeyāḥ ṣaṣṭyaṃśeśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
ṣaṣṭyāṃśasvāminastvoje tadīśādavyatpayaḥ same  

śubhaṣaṣṭayaṃśasaṃyuktā grahāḥ śubhaphalapradāḥ 
krūraṣaṣṭyaṃśāsaṃyuktā nāśayanti khacāriṇaḥ  

vargabhedānahaṃ vakṣye maitreya tvaṃ vidhāraya 
ṣaḍvargāḥ saptavargāśca digvargā nṛpavargakāḥ  

bhavanti vargasaṃyoge ṣaḍavarge kiṃśukādayaḥ 
dvābhyāṃ kiṃśukanāmā ca tribhirvyañjanamucyate  

caturbhiścāmarākhyaṃ ca chatraṃ pañcabhireva ca 
ṣaḍbhiḥ kuṇḍalayogaḥ syānmukuṭākhyaṃ ca saptabhiḥ  

saptavarge'tha digvarge pārijātādisaṃjñakāḥ 
pārijātaṃ bhaveddvābhyāmuttamaṃ tribhirucyate  

caturbhirgopurākhyaṃ syāccharauḥ siṃhāsanaṃ tathā 
pārāvataṃ bhavet ṣaḍbhirdevalokaṃ ca saptabhiḥ  

vasubhirbrahmalokākhyaṃ navabhiḥ śakravāhanam 
digbhiḥ śrīdhāmayogaḥ syādatha ṣoḍaśavargake  

bhedakaṃ ca bhaveddvābhyāṃ tribhiḥ syāt kumumākhyakam 
caturbhirnāgapuṣpaṃ syāt paṃcabhiḥ kandukāhvayam  

keralākhyaṃ bhavet ṣaḍbhiḥ saptabhiḥ kalpavṛkṣakam 
aṣṭabhiścandanavaṃ navabhiḥ pūrṇacandrakam  

digbhiruccaiḥśravā nāma rudrairdhanvantarirbhavet 
sūryakāntaṃ bhaved sūryairviśvaiḥ syādvidrumākhyakam  

śakrasiṃhāsanaṃ śakrairgolokaṃ tithibhirbhavet 
bhūpaiḥ srīvallabhākhyaṃ syādvargā bhedairudāhṛtāḥ  

svoccamūlatrikoṇasvabhavanādhipateḥ śubhāḥ 
svāruḍhāt kendranāthānāṃ vargā grāhyāḥ sudhīmatā  

astaṃgatā grahajitā nīcagā durbalāśca ye 
śayanādigatāstebhya utpannā yoganāśakāḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha vargavivekādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atha ṣoḍaśavargeṣu vivekaṃ ca vadāmyaham 
lagne dehasya vijñānaṃ horāyāṃ sampadādikam  

dreṣkāṇe bhrātṛjaṃ saukhyaṃ turyāṃśe bhāgyacintanam 
putrapautrādikānāṃ cai cintanaṃ saptamāṃśake  

navamāṃśe kalatrāṇāṃ daśamāṃśe mahatphalam 
dvādaśāṃśe tathā pitrościntanaṃ ṣoḍaśāṃśake  

sukhā'sukhasya vijñānaṃ vāhanānāṃ tathaiva ca 
upāsanāyā vijñānaṃ sādhyaṃ viṃśatibhāgake  

vidyāyā vedabāhvaṃśe bhāṃśe caiva balā'balam 
triṃśāṃśake riṣṭaphalaṃ khavedāṃśe śubhā'śubham  

akṣavedāṃśake caiva ṣaṣṭyaṃśe'khilamīkṣayet 
yatra kutrāpi samprāptaḥ krūraṣaṣṭyaṃśakādhipaḥ  

tatra nāśo na sande ho gargādīnāṃ vaco yathā 
yatra kutrāpi samprāptaḥ kalāṃśādhipatiḥ śubhaḥ  

tatra vṛddhiśca puṣṭiśca gargādināṃ vaco yathā 
iti ṣoḍaśavargāṇāṃ bhedāste pratipāditāḥ  

udayādiṣu bhāveṣu kheṭasya bhavaneṣu vā 
vargaviṃśopakaṃ vīkṣya jñeyaṃ teṣāṃ śubhā'śubham  

athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi vargaviṃśopakaṃ balam 
yasya vijñānamārteṇa vipākaṃ dṛṣṭigocaram  

gṛhaviṃśopakaṃ vīkṣyaṃ sūryādīnāṃ khacāriṇām 
svagṛhocce balaṃ pūrṇaṃ śūnyaṃ tatsaptamasthite  

grahasthitivaśājjñeyaṃ dvirāśyadhipatistathā 
madhye'nupātato jñeyaṃ ojayugmarkṣabhedataḥ  

sūryahorāphalaṃ dadyurjīvārkavasudhātmajāḥ 
candrāsphujidarkaputrāścandrahorāphalapradāḥ  

phaladvayaṃ budho dadyāt same cāndraṃ tadanyake 
raveḥ phalaṃ svahorādau phalahīnaṃ virāmake  

madhye'nupātāt sarvatra dreṣkāṇe'pi vicintayet 
gṛhavat turyabhāgepi navāṃśādāvapi svayam  

sūryaḥ kujaphalaṃ dhatte bhārgavasya niśāpatiḥ 
triṃśāṃśake vicintyauvamatrāpi gṛhavat smṛtam  

lagnahorādṛkāṇāṃkabhāgasūryakā iti 
triṃśāṃśakaśca ṣaḍvargā atra viṃśopakāḥ kramāt  

ramanetrābidhapaṃcāśvibhūmayaḥ saptavargake 
sasaptamāṃśake tatra viśvakāḥ paṃca locanam  

trayaḥ sārddhaṃ dvayaṃ sārddhavedā dvau rātrināyakaḥ 
sthūlaṃ phalaṃ ca saṃsthāpya tatsūkṣmaṃ ca tatastataḥ  

daśavargāṃ digaṃśāḍhyāḥ kalāṃśāḥ ṣaṣṭibhāgakāḥ 
trayaṃ kṣetrasya vijñeyaḥ paṃcaṣaṣṭyaṃśakasya ca  

sārddhaukabhāgāḥ śeṣāṇāṃ viśvakāḥ parikīrtitā 
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa balaṃ viṃśopakāhvayam  

kramāt ṣoḍaśavargāṇāṃ kṣetrādīnāṃ pṛthak pṛthak 
horātriṃśāṃśadṛkkāṇe kucandraśaśinaḥ kramāt  

kalāṃśasya dvayaṃ jñeyaṃ trayaṃ nandāṃśakasya ca 
kṣetre sārddhaṃ ca tritayaṃ vedāḥ ṣaṣṭyaṃśakasya hi  

arddhamardhaṃ tu śeṣāṇāṃ hyetat svīyamudāhṛtam 
pūrṇaṃ viṃśopakaṃ viṃśo dhṛtiḥ syādadhimitrake  

mitre paṃcadaśa proktaṃ same daśa prakīrtitam 
śatrau saptādhiśatrau ca paṃcaviṃśopakaṃ bhavet  

vargaviśvāḥ svaviśvaghnāḥ punarviṃśatibhājitāḥ 
viśvāphalopayogyaṃ tatpañconaṃ phalado na hi  

tadūrdhvaṃ svalpaphaladaṃ daśordhvaṃ madhyamaṃ smṛtam 
tiyyūrdhaṃ pūrṇaphaladaṃ bodhyaṃ sarvaṃ khacāriṇām  

athā'nyadapi vakṣye'haṃ maitreya tvaṃ vidhāraya 
khetāḥ pūrṇaphalaṃ dadyuḥ sūryāt saptamake sthitāḥ  

phalābhāvaṃ vijānīyāt same sūryanabhaścare 
madhye'nupātāt sarvatra hyudayāstaviṃśopakāḥ  

vargaviṃśopakaṃ jñeyaṃ phalamasya dvijarṣabha 
yacca yatra phalaṃ buddhvā tatphalaṃ parikīrtitam  

vargaviṃśopakaṃ cādāvudayāstamataḥ param 
pūrṇaṃ pūrṇetipūrnaṃsyāt sarvadauvaṃ vicintayet  

hīnaṃ hīnetihīnaṃ syāt svalpelpātyalpakaṃ smṛtam 
madhyaṃ madhyetimadhyaṃ syādyāvattasya daśāsthitiḥ  

athā'nyadapi vakṣyāmi maitreya srṛṇu suvrat 
lagnaturyāstaviyatāṃ kendrasaṃjñā viśeṣataḥ  

dvipaṃcarandhralābhānāṃ jñeyaṃ paṇapharābhidham 
triṣaṣṭhabhāgyariṣphānāmāpoklimamiti dvija  

lagnāt paṃcamabhāgyasya koṇasaṃjñā vidhīyate 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭavyayabhābānāṃ duḥsaṃjñāstrikasaṃjñakāḥ  

caturasraṃ turyarandhraṃ kathayānte dvijottama 
svasthādupacayarkṣāṇi triṣaḍāyāmbarāṇi hi  

tanurdhanaṃ ca sahajo bandhuputrārayastathā 
yuvatīrandhradharmākhyakarmālābhavyayāḥ kramāt  

saṃkṣepeṇautaduditamanyad buddhyanusārataḥ 
kiñcidviśeṣaṃ vakṣyāmi yathā bhahmamukhārcchutam  

navame'pi piturjñānaṃ sūryācca navame'thavā 
yatkiñciddaśame lābhe tatsūryāddaśame bhave  

turye tanau dhane lābhe bhāgye yaccintanaṃ ca tat 
candrātturye tanau lābhe bhagye taccintayed dhruvam  

lagnād duścikyabhavane yatkujādvikrame'khilam 
vicāryaṃ ṣaṣṭhabhāvasya budhāt ṣaṣṭhe vilokayet  

putrasya ca guroḥ putre jāyāyāḥ saptame bhṛgoḥ 
aṣṭamasya vyayasyāpi mandānmṛtyau vyaye tathā  

yadbhāvādyatphalaṃ cintyaṃ tadīśāttatphalaṃ viduḥ 
jñeyaṃ tasya phalaṃ taddhi tatra cintyaṃ śubhā'śubham  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha rāśidṛṣṭikathanādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atha meṣādirāśīnāṃ carādīnāṃ pṛthak pṛthak 
dṛṣṭibhedaṃ pravakṣyāmi śrṛṇu tvaṃ dvijasattama  

rāśayo'bhimukhaṃ vipra tathā paśyanti pārśvabhe 
yathā caraḥ sthirānevaṃ sthiraḥ paśyati vai carān  

dvisvabhāvo vinā'tmānāṃ dvisvabhāvān prapaśyati 
samīpasthaṃ parityajya kheṭāstatra gatāstathā  

careṣu saṃsthitāḥ kheṭāḥ paśyanti sthirasaṅgatān 
sthireṣu saṃsthitā evaṃ paśyanti carasaṃsthitān  

ubhayasthāstu sūryādyā paśyanyubhayasaṃsthitān 
nikaṭasthaṃ vinā kheṭāḥ paśyantītyayamāgamaḥ  

dṛṣṭicakramahaṃ vakṣye yayāvad brahmaṇoditam 
tasya vinyāsamātreṇa dṛṣṭibhedaḥ prakāśyate  

prāci meeṣavṛṣau lekhyau karkasiṃhau tathottare 
tulā'lī paścime vipra mṛgakumbhau ca dakṣiṇe  

īśakoṇe tu mithunaṃ vāyavye kanyakāṃ tathā 
naurṛrtyāṃ cāpamālikhya vahnikoṇe chaṣaṃ likhet  

evaṃ caturbhujākāraṃ vṛttākāramathāpi vā 
dṛṣṭicakraṃ pravinyasyaivaṃ tato dṛṣṭiṃ vicārayet  

medskiphrulemedskip

            athāriṣṭādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

ādau janmāṅgato vipra riṣṭā'riṣṭaṃ vicārayet 
tatastanvādibhāvānāṃ jātakasya phalaṃ vadet  

caturviṃśativarṣāṇi yāvad gacchanti janmataḥ 
janmāriṣṭaṃ tu tāvat syādāyurdāyuṃ na cintayet  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭariṣphagaścandraḥ krūrauḥ kheṭaiśca vīkṣitaḥ 
jātasya mṛtyudaḥ sadyastvaṣṭarṣaiḥ śubhakṣitaḥ  

śaśivanmṛtyudāḥ saumyāścedvakrāḥ krūravīkṣitāḥ 
śiśorjātasya māsena lagne saumyavivarjite  

yasya janmani dhīsthāḥ syuḥ sūryārkīndukujābhadhāḥ 
tasya tvāśu janitrī ca bhrātā ca nidhanaṃ vrajet  

pāpekṣito yuto bhaumo lagnago na śubhekṣitaḥ 
mṛtyudastvaṣṭamastho'pi saureṇārkeṇa vā yutaḥ  

candrasūryagrahe rāhuścandrasūryayuto yadi 
sauribhaumekṣitaṃ lagnaṃ pakṣamekaṃ sa jīvati  

karmasthāne sthitaḥ sauriḥ śatrusthāne kalānidhiḥ 
kṣitijaḥ saptamasthāne saha mātrā vipadyate  

lagne bhāskaraputraśca nidhane candramā yadi 
tṛtīyastho yadā jīvaḥ sa yāti yamamandiram  

horāyāṃ navame sūryaḥ saptamasthaḥ śanaiścaraḥ 
ekādaśe guruḥ sukro māsamekaṃ sa jīvati  

vyaye sarve grahā neṣṭāḥ sūryeśukrendurāhavaḥ 
viśeṣānnāśakartāro dṛṣṭyā vā bhaṅgakāriṇaḥ  

pāpānvitaḥ śaśī dharme dyūnalagnagato yadi 
śubhairavekṣitayutastadā mṛtyupradaḥ śiśoḥ  

sandhyāyāṃ candrahorāyāṃ gaṇḍānte nidhanāya vai 
pratyekaṃ candrapāpaiśca kendragaiḥ syādvināśanam  

ravestu maṇḍalārddhāstāt sāyaṃ saṃdhyā trināḍikā 
tathaivārddhodayāt pūrvaṃ prātaḥ saṃdhyā trināḍikā  

cakrapūrvāparārddheṣu krūrasaumyeṣu kīṭabhe 
lagnage nidhanaṃ yāti nā'tra kāryā vicāraṇā  

vyayaśatrugataiḥ krūrairmṛtyudravyagatairapi 
pāpamadhyagate lagne satyameva mṛtiṃ vadet  

lagnasaptamagau pāpau candro'pi krūrasaṃyutaḥ 
yadā nāvekṣitaḥ saumyaiḥ śīghrānmṛtyurbhavettadā  

kṣīṇe śaśini lagnasthe pāpaiḥ kendrāṣṭasaṃsthitaiḥ 
yo jāto mṛtyumāpnoti sa vipreśa na saṃśayaḥ  

pāpayormadhyagaścandro lagnāṣṭāntimasaptamaḥ 
acirānmṛtyumāpnoti yo jātaḥ sa śiśustadā  

pāpadvayamadhyagate candre lagnasamāśrite 
saptāṣṭamena pāpena mātrā saha mṛtaḥ śiśuḥ  

śanaiścarārkabhaumeṣu riṣphadharmāṣṭameṣu ca 
śabhairavīkṣyamāṇeṣu yo jāto nidhanaṃgataḥ  

yaddreṣkāṇe ca yāmitre yasya syāddāruṇo grahaḥ 
kṣīṇacandro vilagnasthaḥ sadyo harati jīvatam  

āpoklimasthitāḥ sarve grahā balavivarjitāḥ 
ṣaṇmāsaṃ va dvimāsaṃ va tasyāyuḥ samudāhṛtam  

tribhiḥ pāpagrahaiḥ sūtau candramā yadi dṛśyate 
mātṛnāśo bhavettasya śubhardṛṣṭe śubhaṃ vadet  

dhane rāhurbudhaḥ śukraḥ sauriḥ sūryo yadā sthitaḥ 
tasya māturbhavenmṛtyurmṛte pitari jāyate  

pāpātsaptamarandhrasthe candre pāpasamanvite 
balibhiḥ pāpakairdṛṣṭe jāto bhavati mātṛhā  

uccastho vā'tha nīcasthaḥ saptamastho yadāraviḥ 
pānahīno bhavedbāla ajākṣīreṇa jīvati  

candrāccaturthagaḥ pāpo ripukṣetre yadā bhavet 
tadā mātṛvadhaṃ kuryāt kendre yadi śubho na cet  

dvādaśe ripubhāve ca yadā pāpagraho bhavet 
tadā māturbhayaṃ vidyāccaturthe daśame pituḥ  

lagne krūro vyaye krūro dhane saumyastathaiva ca 
saptame bhavane krūraḥ parivārakṣayaṃkaraḥ  

lagnasthe ca gurau saurau dhane rāhau tṛtīyage 
iti ceñjanmakāle syānmātā tasya na jīvati  

kṣīṇacandrāttrikoṇasthaiḥ pāpaiḥ saumyavivarjitaiḥ 
mātā parityajedbalaṃ ṣaṇmāsācca na saṃśayaḥ  

ekāṃśakasthau mandārau yatra kutrasthitau yadā 
śaśikendragatau tau vā dvimātṛbhyāṃ na jīvati  

lagne sando made bhaumaḥ ṣaṣṭhasthāne ca candramāḥ 
iti cejjanmakāle syāt pitā tasya na jīvati  

lagne jīvo dhane mandaravibhaumabudhāstathā 
vivāhasamaye tasya bālasya mriyate pitā  

sūryaḥ pāpena saṃyukto hyathavā pāpamadhyagaḥ 
sūryāt saptamagaḥ pāpastadā pitṛvadho bhavet  

saptame bhavane sūryaḥ karmastho bhūmanandanaḥ 
rāhurvyaye ca yusyaiva pitā kaṣṭena jīvati  

daśamastho yadā bhaumaḥ śatrukṣetrasamāsritaḥ 
mriyate tasya jātasya pitā śīghraṃ na saṃśayaḥ  

ripusthāne yadā candro lagnasthāne śanaiścaraḥ 
kujaśca saptame sthāne pitā tasya na jīvati  

bhaumāṃśakasthite bhānau śaninā ca nirīkṣite 
prāgjanmano nivṛttiḥ syānmṛtyurvā'pi śiśoḥ pituḥ  

caturthe daśame pāpau dvādaśe ca yadā sthitau 
pitaraṃ mātaraṃ hatvā deśāddeśāntaraṃ vrajet  

rāhujīvau ripukṣetre lagne vā'tha caturthake 
trayoviṃśatime varṣe putrastātaṃ na paśyati  

bhānuḥ pitā ca jantūnāṃ candro mātā tathaiva ca 
pāpadṛṣṭiyuto bhānuḥ pāpamadhyagato'pi vā  

pitrariṣṭaṃ vijānīyācchiśorjātasya niścitam 
bhānoḥ ṣaṣṭhaṣṭamarkṣasthaiḥ pāpaiḥ saumyavivarjitaiḥ 
sukhabhāvagatairvā'pi pitrariṣṭaṃ vinirdiśet  

evaṃ candrāt sthitaiḥ pāpairmātu kaṣṭaṃ vicārayet 
balā'balavivekena kaṣṭaṃ vā mṛtyumādiśet  

medskiphrulemedskip

         athā'riṣṭabhaṃgādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

ityariṣṭaṃ mayā proktaṃ tadbhaṅgaścāpi kathyate 
yat samālokyaṃ jātānāṃ riṣtā'riṣṭaṃ vadedbudhaḥ  

eko'pi jñāryaśukrāṇāṃ lagnāt kendragato yadi 
ariṣṭaṃ nikhilaṃ hanti timiraṃ bhāskaro yathā  

eka eva balī jīvo lagnastho riṣṭasaṃcayam 
hanti pāpakṣayaṃ bhaktyā praṇāma iva śūlinaḥ  

eka eva vilagneśaḥ kendrasaṃstho balānvitaḥ 
ariṣṭaṃ nikhilaṃ hanti pinākī tripuraṃ yathā  

śuklapakṣe kṣapājanma lagne saumyanirīkṣite 
viparītaṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe tathāriṣṭavināśanaṃ  

vyayasthāne yadā sūryastulālagne tu jāyate 
jīvet sa śatavarṣāṇi dīrghāyurbālako bhavet  

gurubhaumau yadā yuktau gurudṛṛṭo'thavā kujaḥ 
hatvā'riṣṭamaśeṣaṃ ca jananyāḥ śubhakradbhavet  

caturthadaśame pāpaḥ saumyamadhye yadā bhavet 
pituḥ saukhyakaro yogaḥ śubhaiḥ kendratrikoṇagaiḥ  

saumyāntaragataiḥ pāpaiḥ śubhaiḥ kendratrikoṇagaiḥ 
sadyo nāśayate'riṣṭaṃ tadbhāvotthaphalaṃ na tat  

medskiphrule

medskiphrulemedskip

            atha bhāvavivekādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

ariṣṭaṃ tatprabhaṅgaṃ ca śrutaṃ tvatto mayā mune 
kasmād bhāvāt phalaṃ kiṃ kiṃ vicāryamiti me vada  

dehaṃ rūpaṃ ca jñānaṃ ca varṇaṃ caiva balābalam 
sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ svabhāvañca lagnabhāvānnirīkṣayet  

dhanadhānyaṃ kuṭumbāṃśca mṛtyujālamamitrakam 
dhāturatnādikaṃ sarvaṃ dhanasthānānnirīkṣayet  

vikramaṃ bhṛtyabhrātrādi copadeśaprayāṇakam 
pitrorvai maraṇaṃ vijño duścikyācca nirīkṣayet  

vāhanānyatha bandhūṃśca mātṛsaukhyādikānyapi 
nidhi kṣetraṃ gṛhaṃ cāpi caturthāt paricintayet  

yantramantrau tathā vidyāṃ buddheścaiva prabandhakam 
putrarājyāpabhrāṃśādīn paśyet putrālayād budhaḥ  

mātulāntakaśaṃkānāṃ śatrūṃścaiva vraṇādikān 
sapatnīmātaraṃ cāpi ṣaṣṭhabhāvānnirīkṣayet  

jāyāmadhvaprayāṇaṃ ca vāṇijyaṃ naṣṭavīkṣaṇam 
maraṇaṃ ca svadehasya jāyābhāvānnirīkṣayet  

āyu raṇaṃ ripuṃ cāpi durgaṃ mṛtadhanaṃ tathā 
gatyanukādikaṃ sarvaṃ paśyedrandhrādvicakṣaṇaḥ  

bhāgyaṃ śyālaṃ ca dharmaṃ ca bhrātṛpatnyādikāṃstathā 
tīrthayātrādikaṃ sarvaṃ dharmasthānānnirīkṣayet  

rājyaṃ cākāśaṃvṛttiṃ ca mānaṃ caiva pitustathā 
pravāsasya ṛṇasyāpi vyomasthānānnirīkṣaṇam  

nānāvastubhavasyāpi putrajāyādikasya ca 
āyaṃ vṛddhiṃ paśūnāṃ ca bhavasthānānnirīkṣaṇam  

vyayaṃ ca vairivṛttāntariḥphamantyādikaṃ tathā 
vyayāccaiṣa hi jñātavyamini sarvatra dhīmatā  

yo yo śubhairyuto dṛṣṭo bhāvo vā patidṛṣṭayuk 
yuvā pravṛddho rājyasthaḥ kumāro vā'pi yatpatiḥ  

tadīkṣaṇavaśāt tattadbhābasaukhyaṃ vaded budhaḥ 
yadyad bhāvapatirnaṣṭastrikeśādyaiśca saṃyutaḥ  

bhāvaṃ na vīkṣate samyak supto vṛddhomṛto'thavā 
pīḍito vā'sya  bhāvasya phalaṃ naṣṭaṃ vaded dhruvam  

medskiphrulemedskip

           atha tanubhāvaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

sapāpo dehapo'ṣṭārivyayago dehasaukhyahṛt 
kendre koṇe sthito'ṅgeśaḥ sadā dehasukhaṃ diśet  

lagnapo'staṅgato nīce śatrubhe rogakṛd bhavet 
śubhaḥ kendratrikoṇasthā sarvarogaharāḥ smṛtāḥ  

lagne candre'thava krūragrahairdṛṣṭe'thavā yute 
śubhadṛṣṭivihīne ca jantordehasukhaṃ na hi  

lagne saumye surūpaḥ syāt krūrerūpavivarjitaḥ 
saumyakheṭairyute dṛṣṭe lagne dehasukhānvitaḥ  

lagneśo jñā gururvā'pi śukro vā kendrakoṇagaḥ 
dīrghāyurdhanavān jāto buddhimān rājavallabhaḥ  

lagneśe cararāśisthe śubhagrahanirīkṣite 
kīrtiśrīmān mahābhogī dehasaukhyasamanvitaḥ  

budho jīvo'thavā śukro lagne candrasamanvitaḥ 
lagnāt kendragato vā'pi rājalakṣaṇasaṃyutaḥ  

sasaure sakuje vāpi lagne meṣe vṛṣe harau 
rāśyaṃśasadṛśau gātre sa jāto nālaviṣṭitaḥ  

catuṣpadagato bhānuḥ pare vīryasamanvitāḥ 
dvisvabhāvagatā jātau yamalāviti nirdiśet  

ravaundū ekabhāvasthāvekaṃśakasamanvitau 
trimātrā ca thibhirmāsaiḥ pitrā bhrātrā ca poṣitaḥ  

evameva phalaṃ vācyaṃ candrādapi sadā budhaiḥ 
atha jātanarasyāṅge vraṇacihnādikaṃ bruve  

śiro netre tatha karṇau nāsike ca kapolakau 
hanūrmukhaṃ ca lagnādyā tanāvādyadṛkāṇake  

madhyadreṣkāṇage lagne kaṇṭhoṃ'sau ca bhujau tathā 
pārśve ca hṛdaye kroḍe nābhiśceti yathākramam  

vastirliṅgagude muṣkāvūrū jānū ca jaṃghake 
pādaścetyuditairvāmamaṅgaṃ jñeyaṃ tṛtīyake  

yasminnaṅge sthitaḥ pāpo vraṇaṃ tatra samādiśet 
niyataṃ sabudhaiḥ krūraiḥ saumyairlakṣma vaded budhaḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha dhanabhāvaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

dhanabhāvaphalaṃ vacmi srṛṇu tvaṃ dvijasattama 
dhaneśo dhanabhāvasthaḥ kendrakoṇagato'pi vā  

dhanavṛddhikaro jñeyastrikastho dhanahānikṛt 
dhanadaśca dhane saumyaḥ pāpo dhanavināśakṛt  

dhanādhipo gururyasya dhanabhāvagato bhavet 
bhaumena sahito vā'pi dhanavān sa naro bhavet  

dhaneśe lābhabhāvasthe lābheśe vā dhanaṃ gate 
tāvubhau kendrakoṇasthau dhanavān sa naro bhavet  

dhaneśe kendrarāśisthe lābheśe tattrikoṇage 
guruśukrayute dṛṣṭe dhanalābhamudīrayet  

dhaneśo ripubhāvastho lābheśastadgato yadi 
dhanāyau pāpayuktau vā dṛṣṭau nirdhana eva saḥ  

dhanalābhādhipāvastau pāpagrahasamanvitau 
janmaprabhṛtidāridraṃ bhikṣānnaṃ labhate naraḥ  

ṣaṣṭhe'ṣṭame vyaye vā'pi dhanalābhādhipau yadi 
lābhe kujodhane rāhū rājadaṇḍād dhanakṣayaḥ  

lābhe jīve dhane śukre dhaneśe śubhasaṃyute 
vyaye ca śubhasaṃyukte dharmakārye dhanavyayaḥ  

svabhoccasthe dhanādhīśe jātako janapoṣakaḥ 
paropakārī khyātaśca vijñeyo dvijasattama  

sthite pārāvatāṃśādau dhaneśe śubhasaṃyute 
tadgṛhe sarvasampattirvinā'yāsena jāyate  

netreśe balasaṃyukte śobhanākṣo bhavennaraḥ 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyayasthe ca netravaikalyavān bhavet  

dhaneśe pāpasaṃyukte dhane pāpasamanvite 
piśuno'satyavādī ca vātavyādhisamanvitaḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha sahajabhāvaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atha vikramabhāvasya phalaṃ vakṣyāmi bho dvija 
sahaje saumyayugdṛṣṭe bhrātṛmān vikramī naraḥ  

sabhaumo bhrātṛbhāveśo bhrātṛbhāvaṃ prapaśyati 
bhrātrkṣetragato vā'pi bhrātṛbhāvaṃ vinirdiśet  

pāpayogena tau pāpakṣetrayogena vā punaḥ 
utpāṭya sahajān sadyo nihantarau na saṃśayaḥ  

strīgraho bhrātṛbhāveśaḥ strīgraho bhrātṛbhāvagaḥ 
bhaginī syāt tathā bhrātā puṃgṛhe puṃgraho yadi  

miśre miśraphalaṃ vācyaṃ balābalavinirṇayāt 
mṛtau kujatṛtīyeśau sahodaravināśakau  

kendratrikoṇage vā'pi svoccamitrasvavargage 
kārake sahajeśe yā bhrātṛsaukhyaṃ vinirdiśet  

bhrātṛbhe budhasaṃyukte tadīśe candrasaṃyute 
kārake mandasaṃyukte bhaginyekāgrato bhavet  

paścāt sahodaro'pyekastṛtīyastu mṛto bhavet 
kārake rāhusaṃyukte sahajeśe tu nīcage  

paścāt sahodarābhāvaṃ pūrvaṃ tu tattrayaṃ vadet 
bhrātṛsthānādhipe kendre kārake tattrikoṇage  

jīvena sahite cocce jñeyā dvādaśa sodarāḥ 
tatra jyeṣṭhadviyaṃ tadvajjātakācca tṛtīyakam  

saptamaṃ navamaṃ caiva dvādaśaṃ ca mṛtaṃ vadet 
śeṣāḥ sahodarāḥ ṣaḍ vai bhaveyurdīrghajīvanāḥ  

vyayeśena yuto bhaumo guruṇā sahito'pi vā 
bhrātṛbhāve sthite candre saptasaṃkhyāstu sodarāḥ  

bhrātṛsthāne śaśiyute kevalaṃ puṅgrahekṣite 
sahajā bhrātaro jñeyāḥ śukrayuktekṣite'nyathā  

agre jātaṃ ravirhanti pṛṣṭhe jātaṃ śanaiścaraḥ 
agrajaṃ pṛṣṭhajaṃ hanti sahajastho dharāsutaḥ  

eteṣāṃ vipra yogānāṃ balābalavinirṇayāt 
bhrātṛṇāṃ bhaginīnāṃ vā jātakasya phalaṃ vadet  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha sukhabhāvaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

uktaṃ tṛtīyabhāvasya phalaṃ saṃkṣepato mayā 
sukhabhāvaphalaṃ cā'tha kathayāmi dvijottama  

sukheśe sukhabhāvasthe lagneśe tadgate'pi vā 
śubhadṛṣṭe ca jātasya pūrṇaṃ gṛhasukhaṃ vadet  

svagehe svāṃśake svocce sukhasthānādhipo yadi 
bhūmiyānagṛhādīnāṃ sukhaṃ vādyabhavaṃ tathā  

karmādhipena saṃyukte kendre koṇe gṛhādhipe 
vicitrasaudhaprākārairmaṇḍitaṃ tadgṛhaṃ vadet  

bandhusthāneśvare saumye śubhagrahayutekṣite 
śaśije lagnasaṃyukte bandhupūjyo bhavennaraḥ  

mātuḥsthāne śubhayute tadīśe svoccarāśige 
kārake balasaṃyukte māturdīrghāyurādiśet  

sukheśe kendrabhāvasthe tatha kendrasthito bhṛguḥ 
śaśije svoccarāśisthe mātuḥ pūrṇaṃ sukhaṃ vadet  

sukhe raviyute mande candre bhāgyagate sati 
lābhasthānagato bhaumo gomahiṣyādilābhakṛt  

caragehasamāyukto sukhe tadrāśināyake 
ṣaṣṭhe vyaye sthite bhaume naraḥ prāpnoti mūkatām  

lagnasthānādhipe saumye sukheśe nīcarāśige 
kārake vyayabhāvasthe sukheśe lābhasaṅgate  

dvadaśe vatsare prāpte vāhanasya sukhaṃ vadet 
vāhane sūryasaṃyukte svocce tadbhāvanāyake  

śukreṇa saṇyute varṣe dvātriṃśe vāhanaṃ bhavet 
karmeśena yute bandhunāthe tuṅgāṃśasaṃyute  

dvicatvāriṃśake varṣe naro vāhanabhāg bhavet 
lābheśe sukharāśisthe sukheśe lābhasaṃyute  

dvādaśe vastare prāpte jāto vāhanabhāg bhavet 
śubhaṃ śubhatve bhāvasya pāpatve phalamanyathā  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha pañcamabhāvaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atha pañcamabhāvasya kathayāmi phalaṃ dvija 
lagnape sutabhāvasthe sutape ca sute sthite  

kendratrikoṇasaṃsthe vā pūrṇaṃ putrasukhaṃ vadet 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyayasthe tu sutādhīśe tvaputratā  

suteśestaṃgate vā'pi pāpākrānte ca nirbale 
tadā na jāyate putro jāto vā mriyate dhruvam  

ṣaṣṭhasthāne sutādhīśe lagneśe kujasaṃyute 
mriyate prathamāpatyaṃ kākabandhyā ca gehinī  

sutādhīśo hi nīcastho vyayaṣaṣṭhāṣṭamasthitaḥ 
kākabandhyā bhavennārī sute ketubudhau yadi  

suteśo nīcago yatra sutasthāna na paśyati 
tatra sauribudhau syātāṃ kākabandhyātvamāpnuyāt  

bhāgyeśo mūrtivartī cet suteśo nīcago yadi 
sute ketubudhau syātāṃ sutaṃ kaṣṭād vinirdiśet  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyayastho vā nīco vā śatrurāśigaḥ 
suteśaśca sute tasya kaṣṭād putraṃ vinirdiśet  

putrabhāve budhakṣetre mandakṣetre'thavā punaḥ 
mande māndiyutau dṛṣṭe tadā dattādayaḥ sutāḥ  

ravicandrau yadaikasthāvekāṃśakasamanvitau 
trimātṛbhirasau yādvā dvipitrā'pi ca poṣitaḥ  

pañcame ṣaḍgrahairyukte tadīśe vyayarāśige 
lagneśendū balāḍhayau cet tadā dattasutodbhavaḥ  

sute jñajīvaśukraiśca sabalairavalokite 
bhavanti bahavaḥ putrāḥ suteśe hi balānvite  

suteśe candrasaṃyukte taddreṣkāṇagate'pi vā 
tadā hi kanyakotpattiḥ pravaded daivacintakaḥ  

suteśe cararāśisthe rāhuṇā sahite vidhau 
putrasthānaḥ gate mande parajātaṃ vadecchiśum  

lagnādaṣṭamage candre candrādaṣṭamage gurau 
pāpagrahairyute dṛṣṭe parajāto na saṃśayaḥ  

putrasthānādhipe svocce lagnādvā dvitrikoṇage 
guruṇā saṃyute dṛṣṭe putrabhāgyamupaiti saḥ  

tricatuḥpāpasaṃyukte sute saumyāvivirjite 
suteśe nīcarāśisthe nīcasaṃsthau bhavecchiśuḥ  

putrasthānaṃ gate jīve tadīśe bhṛgusaṃyute 
dvātriṃśe ca trayastriṃśe vatsare putrasaṃbhavaḥ  

suteśe kendrabhāvasthe kārakeṇa samanvite 
ṣaḍtriṃśe triṃśadabde ca putrotpattiṃ vinirdiśet  

lagnād bhāgyagate jīve jīvād bhāgyagate bhṛgau 
lagneśe bhṛguyukte vā catvāriṃśe sutaṃ vadet  

putrasthānaṃ gate rāhau tadīśe pāpasaṃyute 
nīcarāśigato jīvo dvātriṃśe putramṛtyudaḥ  

jīvāt pañcamage pāpe lagnāt pañcamage'pi ca 
ṣaḍtriṃśe ca trayastriṃśe catvāriṃśe sutakṣayaḥ  

lagne mānditamāyukte lagneśe nīcarāśige 
ṣaḍpañcāśattame'bde ca putraśokasamākukaḥ  

caturthe pāpasaṃyukte ṣaṣṭhabhāve tathaiva hi 
suteśe paramoccasthe lagneśena samanvite  

kārake śubhasaṃyukte daśasaṃkhyāstu sūnavaḥ 
paramoccagate jīve dhaneśe rāhusaṃyute  

bhāgyeśe bhāgyasaṃyukte saṃkhyātā nava sūnavaḥ 
putrabhāgyagate jīve suteśe balasaṃyute  

dhaneśe karmabhāvasthe vasusaṃkhyāstu sūnavaḥ 
pañcamāt pañcame mande sutasthe ca tadīśvare  

sūnavaḥ saptasaṃkhyaśca dvigarbhe yamalau vadet 
vitteśe pañcamasthāne satasthe ca sutādhipe  

jāyante ṣaṭ sutāstasya  teṣāṃ ca triprajāmṛtiḥ 
mandāt pañcamage jīve jīvāt pañcamage śanau  

sutabhe pāpasaṃyukte putramekaṃ vinirdiśet 
pañcame pāpayukte vā jīvāt pañcamage śanau  

patnyantare putralābhaṃ kalatratrayabhāg bhavet 
pañcame pāpasaṃyukte jīvāt pañcamage śanau  

lagneśe dhanabhāvasthe suteśo bhaumasaṃyutaḥ 
jātaṃ jātaṃ śiśuṃhanti dīrghāyuśca svayaṃ bhavet  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha ṣaṣṭhabhāvaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atha vipra phalaṃ vakṣye ṣaṣṭhabhāvasamudbhavam 
dehe rogavraṇādyaṃ tat śrūyatāmekacetasā  

ṣaṣṭhādhipaḥ svagehe vā dehe vā'pyaṣṭame sthitaḥ 
tadā vraṇā bhaveddehe ṣaṣṭharāśisamāśrate  

evaṃ pitrādibhāveśāstattatkārakasaṃyutāḥ 
vraṇādhipayutāścāpi ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamayutā yadi  

teṣāmapi vraṇaṃ vācyamāditye na śirovraṇam 
indunā ca mukhe kaṇṭhe bhaumena jñena nābhiṣu  

guruṇā nāsikāyāṃ ca bhṛguṇā nayane pade 
śaninā rāhuṇā kukṣau ketunā ca tathā bhavet  

lagnādhipaḥ kujakṣetre budhabhe yadi saṃsthitaḥ 
yatra kutra sthito jñena vīkṣito mukharukpradaḥ  

lagnādhipau kujabudhau candreṇa yadi saṃyutau 
rāhuṇā śaninā sārddhaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ tatra vinirdiśet  

lagnādhipaṃ vinā lagne sthitaścettamasā śaśī 
svetakuṣṭhaṃ tadā kṛṣṇakuṣṭhaṃ ca śaninā saha  

kujena raktakuṣṭhaṃ syāttattadevaṃ vicārayet 
lagne ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamādhośau raviṇā yadi saṃyutau  

jvaragaṇḍaḥ kuje granthiḥ śastravraṇamathāpi vā 
budhena pittaṃ guruṇā rogābhāvaṃ vinirdiśet  

strībhiḥ śukreṇa śaśinā vāyunā saṃyuto yadi 
gaṇḍaścāṇḍālato nābhau tamaḥketuyute bhayam  

candreṇa gaṇḍaḥ salilaiḥ kaphaśleṣmādinā bhavet 
evaṃ pitrādibhānāṃ tattatkārakayogataḥ  

gaṇḍaṃ teṣāṃ vadedevamuhyamatra manīṣibhiḥ 
rogasthānagate pāpe tadīśe pāpasaṃyute  

rāhuṇā saṃyute mande sarvadā rogasaṃyutaḥ 
rogasthānagate bhaume tadīśe raṃdhrasaṃyute  

ṣaḍvarṣe dvādaśe varṣe jvararogī bhavennaraḥ 
ṣaṣṭhasthānagate jīve tadgṛhe candrasaṃyute  

dvāviṃśaukonaviṃśe'bde kuṣṭharogaṃ vinirdiśet 
rogasthānaṃ gato rāhuḥ kendre māndisamanvite  

lagneśe nāśarāśisthe ṣaḍviṃśe kṣayarogatā 
vyayeśe rogarāśisthe tadīśe vyayarāśige  

triṃśadvarṣaikonavarṣe gulmarogaṃ vinirdiśet 
ripusthenagate candre śaśinā saṃyute sati  

pañcapañcāśadabdeṣu raktakuṣṭhaṃ vinirdiśet 
lagneśe lagnarāśisthe mande śatrusamanvite  

ekonaṣaṣṭivarṣe tu vātarogārdito bhavet 
raṃdhreśe ripurāśisthe vyayeśe lagnasaṃsthite  

candre ṣaṣṭheśsaṃyukte vasuvarṣe mRīgādbhayam 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamagato rahustasmādaṣṭagate śanau  

jātasya janmato vipra prathame ca dvitīyake 
vastare'gnibhayaṃ tasya trivarṣe pakṣidoṣabhāk  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamagate sūrye tadvyaye candrasaṃyutaḥ 
paṃcame navame'bde tu jalabhītiṃ vinirdiśet  

aṣṭame mandasaṃyukte tasmādvā dvādaśe kujaḥ 
triṃśābde daśame'bde tu sphoṭakādi vinirdiśet  

raṃdhreśe rāhusaṃyukte tadaṃśe raṃdhrakoṇage 
dvāviṃśe'ṣṭādaśe varṣe granthimehādipīḍanam  

lābheśe ripubhāvasthe rogeśe lābharāśige 
ekatriṃśatsame varṣe śatrumūlāddhanavyayaḥ  

suteśe ripubhāvasthe ṣaṣṭheśe gurusaṃyute 
vyayeśe lagnabhāvasthe tasya putro ripurbhavet  

lagneśe ṣaṣṭharāśisthe tadīśe ṣaṣṭharāśige 
daśamaikonaviṃśe'bde śunakādbhītirucyate  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha jāyābhāvaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

jāyābhāvaphalaṃ vakṣye srṛṇu tvaṃ dvijasattama 
jāyādhipe svabhe svocce strīsukhaṃ pūrṇamādiśet  

kalatrapo vinā svarkṣaṃ vyayaṣaṣṭhāṣṭamasthitaḥ 
rogiṇīṃ kurute nārīṃ tathā tuṅgādikaṃ vinā  

saptame tu sthite śukre'tīvakāmī bhavennaraḥ 
yatrakutrasthite pāpayute strīmaraṇaṃ bhavet  

jāyādhīśaḥ śubhairyukto dṛṣṭo vā balasaṃyutaḥ 
tadā jāto dhanī mānī sukhasaubhāgyasaṃyutaḥ  

nīce śatrugṛhe'ste vā nirbale ca kalatrape 
tasyāpi rogiṇī bhāryā bahubhāryo naro bhavet  

mandabhe śukragehe vā jāyādhīśe śubhekṣite 
svoccage tu viśeṣeṇa bahubhāryo naro bhavet  

vandhyāsaṅgo made bhānau candre rāśisamastriyaḥ 
kuje rajasvalāsaṅgo vandhyāsaṅgaśca kīrtitaḥ  

budhe veśyā ca hīnā ca vaṇik strī vā prakīrtitā 
gurau brāhmaṇabhāryā syādgarbhiṇīsaṅga eva ca  

hīnā ca puṣpiṇī vācyā mandarāhuphaṇīśvaraiḥ 
kuje'tha sustanī mande vyādhidaurbalyasaṃyutā  

kaṭhinordhvakucārye ca śukre sthūlottamastanī 
pāpe dvādaśakāmasthe kṣīṇacandrastu pañcame  

jātaśca bhāryāvaśyaḥ syāditi jātivirodhakṛt 
jāmitre mandabhaume ca tadīśe mandabhūmije  

veśyā vā jāriṇī vā'pi tasya bhāryā na saṃśayaḥ 
bhaumāṃśakagate śukre bhaumakṣetragate'thavā  

bhaumayukte ca dṛṣṭe vā bhagacumbanabhāg bhavet 
mandāṃśakagate śukre mandakṣetragate'pi ca  

mandayukte ca dṛṣṭe ca śiśnacumbanatatparaḥ 
dāreśe svoccarāśisthe made śubhasamanvite  

lagneśo balasaṃyuktaḥ kalatrasthānasaṃyutaḥ 
tadbhāryā sadguṇopetā putrapautrapravardhinī  

kalatre tatpatau vāpi pāpagrahasamanvite 
bhāryāhāniṃ vadet tasya nirbale ca viśeṣataḥ  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyayasthāne mandeśo durbalo yadi 
nīcarāśigato vāpi dāranāśaṃ vinirdiśet  

kalatrasthānage candre tadīśe vyayarāśige 
kārako balahīnaśca dārasaukhyaṃ na vidyate  

saptameśe svanīcasthe pāparkṣe pāpasaṃyute 
saptame klīvarāśyaṃśe dvibhāryo jātako bhavet  

kalatrsthānage bhaume śukre jātamitrage śanau 
lagneśe randhrarāśisthe kalatratrayavān bhavet  

dvisvabhāvagate śukre svocce tadrāśināyake 
dāreśe balasaṃyukte bahudārasamanvitaḥ  

dāreśe śubharāśisthe svoccasvarkṣagato bhṛguḥ 
pañcame navame'bde tu vivāhaḥ prāyaśo bhavet  

dārastānaṃ gate sūrye tadīśe bhṛgusaṃyute 
saptamaikādaśe varṣe vivāhaḥ prāyaśo bhavet  

kuṭumbasthānage śukre dāreśe lābharāśige 
daśame ṣoḍaśā'bde ca vivāhaḥ prāyaśo bhavet  

lagnakendragate śukre lagneśe mandarāśige 
vatsaraikādaśe prāpte vivāhaṃ labhate naraḥ  

lagnāt kendragate śukre tasmāt kāmagate śanau 
dvādaśaikonaviṃśe ca vivāhaḥ prāyaśo bhavet  

candrājjāmitrage śukre śukrājjāmitrage śanau 
vatsare'ṣṭādaśe prāpte vivāhaṃ labhate naraḥ  

dhaneśe lābharāśisthe lagneśe karmarāśige 
abde pañcadaśe prāpte vivāhaṃ labhate naraḥ  

dhaneśe lābharāśiśte lābheśe dhanarāśige 
abde trayodaśe prāpte vivāhaṃ labhate naraḥ  

randhrājjāmitrage śukre tadīśe bhaumasaṃyute 
dvāviṃśe saptaviṃśe'bde vivāhaṃ labhate naraḥ  

dārāṃśakagate lagnanāthe dāreśvare vyaye 
trayoviṃśe ca ṣaḍviṃśe vivāhaṃ labhate naraḥ  

randhreśe dārarāśisthe lagnāṃśe bhṛgusaṃyute 
pañcaviṃśe trayastriṃśe vivāhaṃ labhate naraḥ  

bhāgyādbhāgyagate śukre taddvaye rāhusaṃyute 
ekatriṃśāstrayastriṃśe dāralābhaṃ vinirdiśet  

bhāgyājjāmitrage śukre taddvūne dāranāyake 
triṃśe vā saptaviṃśābde vivāhaṃ labhate naraḥ  

dāreśe nīcarāśisthe śukre randhrārisaṃyute 
aṣṭādaśe trayastriṃśe vatsare dāranāśanam  

madeśe nāśarāśisthe vyayeśe madarāśige 
tasya caikonaviṃśābde dāranāśaṃ vinirdiśet  

kuṭumbasthānago rāhuḥ kalatre bhaumasaṃyute 
pāṇigrahe ca tridine sarpadaṣṭe vadhūmṛtiḥ  

randhrasthānagate śukre tadīśe saurirāśige 
dvādaśaikonaviṃśābde dāranāśaṃ vinirdiśet  

lagneśe nīcarāśisthe dhaneśe nidhanaṃ gate 
trayodaśe tu samprāpte kalatrasya mṛtirbhavet  

śukrājjāmitrage candre candrājjāmitrage budhe 
randhreśe sutabhāvasthe prathamaṃ daśamābdikam  

dvāviṃśe ca dvitīyaṃ ca trayastriṃśe tṛtīyakam 
vivāhaṃ labhate martyo nā'tra kāryā vicāraṇā  

ṣaṣṭhe ca bhavane bhaumaḥ saptame rāhusaṃsthitiḥ 
aṣṭame ca yadā sauristasya bhāryā na jīvati  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha āyurbhāvaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

āyurbhāvaphalaṃ cā'tha kathayāmi dvijottama 
āyuḥsthānādhipaḥ kendre dīrghamāyuḥ prayacchati  

āyusthānādhipaḥ pāpaiḥ saha tatraiva saṃsthitaḥ 
karotyalpāyuṣaṃ jātaṃ lagneśo'pyatra saṃsthitaḥ  

evaṃ hi śaninā cintā kāryā tarkairvicakṣaṇaiḥ 
karmādhipena ca tathā cintanaṃ kāryamāyuṣaḥ  

ṣaṣṭhe vyaye'pi ṣaṣṭheśo vyayādhīśo ripau vyaye 
lagne'ṣṭame sthito vā'pi dīrghamāyuḥ prayacchati  

svasthāne svāṃśake vā'pi mitreśe mitramandire 
dīrghāyuṣaṃ karotyeva lagneśo'ṣṭamapaḥ punaḥ  

lagnāṣṭamapakarmeśamandāḥ kendratrikoṇayoḥ 
lābhe vā saṃsthitāstadvad diśeyurdīrghamāyuṣam  

evaṃ bahuvidhā vidvannāyuryogāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
eṣu yo balavāṃstasyā'nusārādāyurādiśet  

aṣṭamādhipatau kendre lagneśe balavarjate 
viṃśadvarṣāṇyasau jīved dvātriṃśatparamāyuṣam  

randhreśe nīcarāśisthe randhre pāpagrahairyute 
lagneśe durbale janturalpāyurbhavati dhruvam  

randhreśe pāpasaṃyukte randhre pāpagrahairyute 
vyaye krūragrahākrānte jātamātraṃ mṛtirbhavet  

kendratrikoṇagāḥ pāpāḥ śubhāḥ ṣaṣṭhāṣṭagā yadi 
lagne nīcastharandhreśo jātaḥ sadyo mṛto bhavet  

pañcame pāpasaṃyukte randhreśe pāpasaṃyute 
randhre pāpagrahairyukte svalpamāyuḥ prajāyate  

randhreśe randhrarāśisthe candre pāpasamanvite 
śubhadṛṣṭivihīne ca māsānte ca mṛtirbhavet  

lagneśe svoccarāśisthe candre lābhasamanvite 
randhrasthānagate jīve dīrghamāyurna saṃśayaḥ  

lagneśo'tibalī dṛṣṭaḥ kendrasaṃsthaiḥ śubhagrahaiḥ 
dhanaiḥ sarvaguṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ dīrghamāyuḥ prayacchati  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha bhāgyabhāvaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atha bhāgyabhāvaṃ vipra phalaṃ vakṣye tavā'grataḥ 
sabalo bhāgyape bhāgye jāto bhāgyayuto bhavet  

bhāgyasthānagate jīve yadīśe kendrasaṃasthite 
lagneśe balasaṃyukte bahubhāgyayuto bhavet  

bhāgyeśe balasaṃyukte bhāgye bhṛgusamanvite 
lagnāt kendragate jīve pitā bhāgyasamanvitaḥ  

bhāgyasthānād dvitīye vā sukhe bhaumasamanvite 
bhāgyeśe nīcarāśisthe pitā nirdhana eva hi  

bhāgyeśe paramoccasthe bhāgyāṃśe jīvasaṃyute 
lagnāccatuṣṭaye śukre tatpitā dīrghajīvanaḥ  

bhāgyeśe kendrabhāvasye guruṇā ca nirīkṣite 
tatpitā vāhanairyukto rājā vā tatsamo bhavet  

bhāgyeśe karmabhāvasthe karmeśe bhāgyarāśige 
śubhadṛṣṭe dhanāḍhyaśca kīrtimāṃstatpitā bhavet  

paramoccāṃśage sūrye bhāgyeśe lābhasaṃsthite 
dharmaṣṭho nṛpavātsalyaḥ pitṛbhakto bhavennaraḥ  

lagnāttrikoṇage sūrye bhāgyeśe saptamasthite 
guruṇā sahite dṛṣṭe pitṛbhaktisamanvitaḥ  

bhāgyeśe dhanabhāvasthe dhaneśe bhāgyarāśige 
dvātriṃśātparato bhāgyaṃ vāhanaṃ kīrtisambhavaḥ  

lagneśe bhāgyarāśisthe ṣaṣṭheśena samanvite 
anyonyavairaṃ bruvate janakaḥ kutsito bhavet  

karmādhipena sahito vikrameśo'pi nirbalaḥ 
bhāgyapo nīcamūḍhastho yogo bhikṣāśanapradaḥ  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye bhānū randhreśe bhāgyasaṃyute 
vyayeśe lagnarāśisthe ṣaṣṭheśe pañcame sthite  

jātasya jananātpūrvaṃ janakasya mṛtirbhavet 
randhrasthānagate sūrye randhreśe bhāgyabhāvage  

jātasya prathamābde tu piturmaraṇamādiśet 
vyayeśe bhāgyarāśisthe nīcāṃśe bhāgyanāyake  

tṛtīye ṣoḍaśe varṣe janakasya mṛtirbhavet 
lagneśe nāśarāśisthe randhreśe bhānusaṃyute  

dvitīye dvādaśe varṣe piturmaraṇamādiśet 
bhāgyādrandhragate rāhau bhāgyādbhāgyagate ravau  

ṣoḍaśe'ṣṭādaśe varṣe janakasya mṛtirbhavet 
rāhuṇā sahite sūrye candrādbhāgyagate śanau  

saptamaikonaviṃśābde tātasya maraṇaṃ dhruvam 
bhāgyeśe vyayarāśisthe vyayeśe bhāgyarāśige  

vadābdhimitavarṣācca piturmaraṇamādiśet 
ravyaṃśe ca sthite candre lagneśe randhrasaṃyute  

pañcatriṃśaikacatvāriṃśadvarṣe maraṇaṃ pituḥ 
pitṛsthānādhipe sūrye mandabhaumasamanvite  

pañcāśadvatsare prāpte janakasya mṛtirbhavet 
bhāgyāt saptamage sūrye bhrātṛsaptamagastamaḥ  

ṣaṣṭhe'bde pañcaviṃśābde piturmaraṇamādiśet 
randhrajāmitrage mande mandājjāmitrage ravau  

triṃśaikaviṃśe ṣaḍviṃśe janakasya mṛtirbhavet 
bhāgyeśe nīcarāśisthe tadīśe bhāgyarāśige  

ṣaḍviṃśe'bde trayastriṃśe piturmaraṇamādiśet 
evaṃ jātasya daivajño phalaṃ jñātvā vinirdiśet  

paramoccāṃśage śukre bhāgyeśena samanvite 
bhrātṛsthāne śaniyute bahubhāgyādhipo bhavet  

guruṇā saṃyute bhāgye tadīśe kendrarāśige 
viṃśadvarṣāt paraṃ caiva bahubhāgyaṃ vinirdiśet  

paramoccāṃśage saumye bhāgyeśe bhāgyarāśige 
ṣaṭtriṃśācca paraṃ caiva bahubhāgyaṃ vinirdiśet  

lagneśe bhāgyarāśisthe bhāgyeśe lagnasaṃyute 
guruṇā saṃyute dyūne dhanavāhanalābhakṛt  

bhāgyādbhāgyavato rāhustadīśe nidhanaṃ gate 
bhāgyeśe nīcarāśisthe bhāgyahīno bhavennaraḥ  

bhāgyasthānagate mande śaśinā ca samanvite 
lagneśe nīcarāśisthe bhikṣāśī ca naro bhavet  

evaṃ bhāgyaphalaṃ vipra saṃkṣepāt kathitaṃ mayā 
lagneśabhāgyabhāveśasthityā'nyadapi nirdiśet

medskiphrulemedskip

           atha karmabhvaphaldhyya  

medskip

karmabhvaphala c'tha kathaymi tavgrata 
su maitreya tattvena brahmagargdibhitam  

sabale karmabhvee svocce sve svarige 
jtasttasukhenhyo yaasv ubhakarmakt  

karmdhipo balonacet karmavaikalyamdiet 
saihi kendratrikoastho jyotiomdiygakt  

karmee ubhasayukte ubhasthnagate tath 
rjadvre ca vijye sad lbho'nyathnyath  

daame ppasayukte lbhe ppasamanvite 
dukti labhate martya svajann vidaka  

karmee naristhe rhu sayute tath 
janadve mahmrkho dukti labhate nara  

karmee dynaristhe mandabhaumasamanvite 
dynee ppasayute inodaraparyaa  

tugari samritya karmee gurusayute 
bhgyee karmaristhe mnaivaryapratpavn  

lbhee karmaristhe karmee lagnasayute 
tvubhau kendragau vpi sukhajvanabhg bhavet  

karmee balasayukte mne gurusamanvite 
vastrbharaasaukhydi labhate ntra saaya  

lbhasthnagate srye rhubhaumasamanvite 
raviputrea sayukte karmacchett bhavennara  

mne jve bhguyute lagnee balasayute 
svoccarigate candre samyagjnrthavn bhavet  

kendree lbharisthe lbhee lagnasasthite 
karmaristhite ukre ratnavn sa naro bhavet  

kendratrikoage karmanthe svoccasamrite 
guru sahite de sa karmasahito bhavet  

karmee lagnabhvasthe lagneena samanvite 
kendratrikoage candre satkarmanirato bhavet  

karmasthnagate mande ncakhecarasayute 
karme ppasayukte karmahno bhavennara  

karmee naristhe randhree karmasasthite 
ppagrahea sayukte dukarma nirato bhavet  

karmee ncaristhe karmasthe ppakhecare 
karmabhtkarmage ppe karmavaikalyamdiet  

karmasthnagate candre tade tattrikoage 
lagnee kendrabhvasthe satkrtisahito bhavet  

lbhee karmabhvasthe karmee balasayukte 
devendraguru de satkrtisahito bhavet  

karmasthndhipe bhgye lagnee karmasayute 
lagnt pacamage candre khytanm naro bhavet  

iti karmaphala prokta sakepea dvijottama 
lagnakarmeasambandhdhyamanyadapi svayam  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha lbhabhvaphaldhyya  

medskip

lbhabhvaphalactha kathaymi dvijottama 
ryat jtako loke yacchubhatve sad sukh  

lbhdhipo yad lbhe tiet kendratrikoayo 
bahulbha tad kuryducce sryago'pi v  

lbhee dhanaristhe dhanee kendrasasthite 
guru sahite bhve gurulbha vinirdiet  

lbhee vikrame bhve ubhagrahasamanvite 
atrie vatsare prpte sahasradvayanikabhk  

kendratrikoage lbhanthe ubhasamanvite 
catvrie tu samprpte sahasrrdhasunikabhk  

lbhasthne guruyute dhane candrasamanvite 
bhgyasthnagate ukre asahasrdhipo bhavet  

lbhcca lbhage jve budhacandrasamanvite 
dhanadhnydhipa rmntratndybharaairyuta  

lbhee lagnabhvasthe lagnee lbhasayute 
trayastrie tu samprpte sahasranikabhg bhavet  

dhanee lbharisthe lbhee dhanarige 
vivhtparatacaiva bahubhgya samdiet  

bhrtpe lbharisthe lbhee bhrtsasthite 
bhrtbhvddhanaprptidivybharaasayuta  

lbhee ncabhe'ste v trike ppasamanvite 
kte bhriprayatne'pi naiva lbha kadcana  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha vyayabhvaphaldhyya  

medskip

athha vyayabhvasya kathaymi phala dvija 
vyayee ubhasayukte svabhe svoccagate'pi v  

vyaye ca ubhasayukte ubhakrye vyayastad 
candro vyaydhipo dharmalbhamantreu sasthita  

svocce svarke nije v lbhadharmtmajake 
divygrdiparyako divyagandhaikabhogavn  

parrdhyaramao divyavastramlydibhaa 
parrdhyavittasayuto vijo dinni nayati prabhu  

evasvaatrunce'ame v'ame ripau 
sasthita kurute jta kntsukhavivarjitam  

vyaydhikyapariklnta divyabhoganirktam 
sa hi kendratrikoastha svastriy'lakta svayam  

yath lagnt phala caitadtmana parikrtitam 
eva bhrtrdibhveu tattatsarva vicrayet  

dyacakrrdhag khe pratyakaphaladyak 
adyrdhagat khe paroke phalad smt  

vyayasthnagato rhurbhaumrkiravisayuta 
tade'pyarkasayukte narake patana bhavet  

vyayasthnagate saumye tade svoccarige 
ubhayukte subhairde moksa synntra saaya  

vyayee ppasayukte vyaye ppasamanvite 
ppagrahea sade deddentara gata  

vyayee ubharisthe vyayarke ubhasayute 
ubhagrahea sade svadet sacaro bhavet  

vyaye manddisayukte bhmijena samanvite 
subhaderna samprpti ppamlddhanrjanam  

lagnee vyayaristhe vyayee lagnasayute 
bhguputrea sayukte dharmamlddhanavyaya

         atha bhveaphaldhyya  

medskip

lagnee lagnage dehasukhabhg bhujavikram 
manasv cacalacaiva dvibhryo parago'pi va  

lagnee dhanage blo lbhavn paita sukh 
sulo dharmavinmn bahudraguairyuta  

lagnee sahaje jta sihatulyaparkram 
sarvasampadyuto mn dvibhryo matimn sukh  

lagnee sukhage bla pitmtsukhnvita 
bahubhrtyuta km guarpasamanvita  

lagnee sutage janto sutasaukhya ca madhyamam 
prathampatyana synmn krodh npapriya  

lagnee ahage jto dehasaukhyavivarjita 
pphye atruta p saumyadivivarjite  

lagnee saptame ppe bhry tasya na jvati 
ubhe'ano daridro v virakto v npo'pi v  

lagnee'amage jta siddhavidyvirada 
rog cauro mahkrodh dyt ca paradraga  

lagnee bhgyage jto bhgyavjanavallabha 
viubhakta paurvgm draputradhanairyuta  

lagnee daame jta pitsaukhyasamanvita 
npamnyo jane khyta svrjitasvo na saaya  

lagnee lbhage jta sad lbhasamanvita 
sula khytakrtica bahudraguairyuta  

lagnee vyayabhvasthe dehasaukhyavivarjita 
vyarthavyay mahkrodh ubhadgyogavarjite  

dhanee lagnage jta putravn dhanasayuta 
kuumbakaaka km nihura parakryakt  

dhanee dhanage jto dhanavn garvasayuta 
dvibhryo bahubhryo v sutahna prajyate  

dhanee sahaje jto vikram matimn gu 
km lobh ubhhye ca pphye devanindaka  

dhanee sukhabhvasthe sarvasampatasamanvita 
guru sayute svocce rjatulyo naro bhavet  

dhanee sutabhvasthe jto dhanasamanvita 
dhanoprjanalca jyante tatsut api  

dhanee ripubhvasthe saubhe atruto dhanam 
sappe atruto hnirjaghvaikalyavn bhavet  

dhanee saptame jta paradrarato bhiek 
ppekitayute tasya bhry ca vyabhicri  

dhanee'amage jto bhribhmidhanairyuta 
patnsukha bhavet svalpa jyehabhrtsukha na hi  

dhanee dharmabhvasthe dhanavnudyam pau 
blye rog sukh pact trthadharmavratdikt  

dhanee karmage jta km mn ca paita 
bahudryadhanairyukta kica putrasukhojjhita  

dhanee lbhabhvasthe sarvalbhasamanvita 
sadodyogayuto mn krtimn jyate nara  

dhanee vyayabhvasthe sham dhanavarjita 
parabhgyaratastasya jyehpatyasukha nahi  

lagnage sahajdhe svabhujrjitavittavn 
sevja shas jto vidyhno'pi buddhimn  

dvitye sahajdhe sthlo vikramavarjita 
svalprambh sukh na syt parastrdhanakmuka  

sahaje sahajdhe sahodarasukhnvita 
dhanaputrayuto ho bhunakti sukhamadbhutam  

sukhasthe sahajdhe sukh ca dhanasayuta 
matimn jyate blo duabhrypatica sa  

sutasthe sahajdhe putravn guasayuta 
bhry tasya bhavet krr krragrahayutekite  

ahabhve trtyee bhrtatrurmahdhan 
mtulaica sama vaira mtulnpriyo nara  

saptame sahajdhe rjasevparo nara 
blye dukh sukh cnte jyate n'tra saaya  

aame sahajdhe jtacairo naro bhavet 
dsavttyopajv ca rjadvre mtirbhavet  

navame sahajdhe pitu sukhavivarjita 
strbhirbhgyodayastasya putrdisukhasayuta  

daame sahajdhe jta sarvasukhnvita 
svabhujrjivittaca duastrbharae rata  

lbhage sahajdhe vypre lbhavn sad 
vidyhno'pi medhv shas parasevaka  

vyayasthe sahajdhe kutrye vyayakjjana 
pit tasya bhavet krra strbhirbhgyodayastath  

sukhee dhanage jto vidyguavibhita 
bhmvhanasayukto mtu sukhasamanvita  

sukhee dhanage jto bhog sarvadhannvita 
kuumbasahito mn shas kuhaknvita  

sukhee sahaje jto vikram bhtyasayuta 
udro'rug gu dt svabhujrjitavittavn  

sukhee sukhabhvasthe mantr sarvadhannvita 
catura lavn mn jnavn strpriya sukh  

sukhee putrabhvasthe sukh sarvajanapriya 
viubhakto gu mn svabhujrjitavittavn  

sukhee ripubhvasthe mtu sukhavivarjita 
krodh coro'bhicr ca svecchcraca durman  

sukhee saptame jto bahuvidysamanvita 
pitrrjitadhanatyg sabhy mkavad bhavet  

sukhee randhrabhvasthe ghdisukhavarjita 
pitro sukha bhavedalpa jta klbasamo bhavet  

sukhee bhgyabhvasthe jta sarvajanapriya 
devabhakto gu mn bhavet sarvasukhnvita  

sukhee karmabhvasthe rjamnyo naro bhavet 
rasyan mahho sukhabhog jitendriya  

sukhee lbhage jto guptarogabhaynvita 
udr guavn dt paropakarae rata  

sukhee vyayabhvasthe ghdisukhavarjita 
jto durvyasan mha sad'lasyasamanvita  

sutee lagnage jto vidyn putrasukhnvita 
kadaryo vakracittaca paradravypahraka  

sutee dhanage jto bahuputro dhannvita 
kuumbapoako mn strpriya suya bhuvi  

sutee sahaje bhve jyate sodarapriya 
piunaca kadaryaca svakryanirata sad  

sutee sukhabhvasthe sukh mtsukhnvita 
lakmyukta subuddhica rjo'mtyo'thav guru  

sutee sutabhvaste ubhhye putravn nara 
pphye'patyahno'sau guavn mitravatsala  

sutee ripubhvasthe putra atrusamo bhavet 
mtpatyo'thav jto dattakrtasuto'thav  

sutee saptame mn sarvadharmasamanvita 
putrdisukhayuktaca paropakarae rata  

sutee randhrabhvasthe svalpaputrasukhnvita 
ksavsasamyukta krodh ca sukhavarjita  

sutee bhgyage putro bhapo v tatsamo bhavet 
svaya v granthakart ca vikhyta kuladpaka  

sutee rjyabhvasthe rjayogo hi jyate 
anekasukhabhog ca khytakrtirnaro bhavet  

sutee lbhage jto vidyvn janavallabha 
granthakart mahdako bahuputradhannvita  

sutee vyayabhvasthe jta putrasukhojjita 
dattaputrayuto v'sau krtaputrnvito'thav  

ahee lagnage jto rogavn krtisayuta 
tmaatrurdhan mn shas guavn nara  

ahee dhanabhvasthe shas kulaviruta 
parade sukh vakt svakarmanrata sad  

ahee sahaja jta krodh vikramavarjita 
bhrt atrusamastasya bhtyacottaradyaka  

ahee sukhabhvasthe mtu sukhavivarjita 
manasv piun dve calacitto'tivittavn  

ahee sutago yasya cala tasya dhandikam 
atrut putramitraica sukh svrth daynvita  

ahee ripubhvasthe vaira svajtimaalt 
anyai saha bhaven maitr sukha madhya dhandijam  

ahee drabhvasthe jto drasukhojjhita 
krtimn guavn mn shas dhanasayuta  

ahee'amage jto rog atrurmanim 
paradravybhil ca paradrarato'uci  

ahee bhgyage jta khapavikray 
vyavahre kvaciddhni kvacidvddhica jyate  

ahee daame bhve mnava kulaviruta 
abhaktaca piturvakt videe ca sukh bhavet  

ahee lbhage jta atruto dhanampnuyt 
guavn shas mn kintu putrasukhojjhita  

ahee vyayabhvasthe vyasane vyayakt sad 
vidvaddve bhavejjto jvahissu tatpara  

dree lagnage jta paradreu lampaa 
duo vicakao'dhro jano vtarujnvita  

dree dhanage jto bahustrbhi samanvita 
drayogddhanptica drghastr ca mnava  

dree sahaje jto mtpatyo hi mnava 
kadcijjyate putr yatnt putro'pi jvati  

dree sukhabhvasthe jy nsya vae sad 
svaya satyapriyo dhmn dharmtm dantarogayuk  

dree pacame jto mni sarvagunvita 
sarvad harayuktaca tath sarvadhandhipa  

dree ripubhvasthe bhry tasya rujnvit 
striy sah'tha v vaira svaya krodh sukhojjhita  

dree saptame bhve jto drasukhnvita 
dhro vicakao dhmn kevala vtarogavn  

dree mtyubhvasthe jto drasukhojjhita 
bhry'pi rogayukt'sya dul'pi na cnug  

dree dharmabhvasthe nnstrbhi samgama 
jyhtaman jto bahvrambhakaro nara  

dree karmabhvasthe nsya jy vanug 
svaya dharmarato jto dhanaputrdisayuta  

dree lbhabhvasthe drairarthasamgama 
putrdisukhamalpa ca jana kanyaprajo bhavet  

dree vyayage jto daridra kpao'pi v 
bhrypi vyayal'sya vastrjv naro bhavet  

aamee tanau jtastanusaukhyavivarjita 
devn brhman ca nindako vraasayuta  

aamee dhane bhubalahna prajyate 
dhana tasya bhavet svalpa naa vitta na labhyate  

randhree sahaje bhve bhrtsaukhya na jyate 
slasyo bhtyahnaca jyate balavarjita  

randhree sukhabhvasthe mthno bhavecchiu 
ghabhmisukhairhno mitradroh na saaya  

randhree sutabhvasthe jaabuddhi prajyate 
svalpaprajo bhavejjato drghyuca dhannvita  

randhree ripubhvasthe atrujet bhavejjana 
rogayuktaarraca blye sarpajald bhayam  

randhree drabhvasthe tasya bhrydvaya bhavet 
vypre ca bhavedhnistasmin ppayute dhruvam  

randhree mtyubhvasthe jt drghyu yuta 
nirbale madhyamyu syccauro nindyo'nyanindaka  

aamee tapasthne dharmadroh ca nstika 
duabhrypaticaiva paradravypahraka  

randhree karmabhvaste pitsaukhyavivarjita 
piuna karmahnaca yadi naiva ubhekite

tasmin padatve vijeya madhya turya kramt padam  

yath turyasthite nthe turyameva pada bhavet 
saptame ca sthite nthe vijeya daama padam  

yasmd yvatithe rau khet tadbhavana dvija 
tatastvatitha ri kherha pracakate  

dvinthadvibhayoreva vijeya sabalvadhi 
vigaayya pada vipra tatastasya phala vadet  

ath'ha padamritya phala kicid bruve dvija 
paddekdae sthne grahairyukto'thavekite  

dhanavn jyate blastath sukhasamanvita 
ubhayogt sumrgea dhanpti ppato'ntath  

mirairmira phala jeya svoccamitrdigehagai 
bahudh jyate lbho bahudh ca sukhgama  

padllbhagha yasya payanti sakal grah 
rj v rjatulyo v sa jto ntra saaya  

padllbhagha payed vyaya kacinna payati 
avidhnena sad lbho jyate dvijasattama  

grahadgyogabhulye paddekdae dvija 
srgale cpi tatrpi bahvargalasamgame  

ubhagrahrgale vipra tatrpyuccagrahrgale 
ubhena svmin de lagnabhgydigena v  

jtasya bhgyaprbalya nirdieduttarottaram 
uktayogeu cet khee dvdaa naiva payati  

padasthnd vyaye vipra ubhappayutekite 
vyayabhulyamityeva vieoprjant sad  

ubhagrahe sumrgea kumrgt ppakhecare 
mire miraphala vcyameva lbho'pi lbhage  

padrhd vyaye ukrabhnusvarbhnubhiryute 
rjamld vyayo vcyacandrady vieata  

padrhd vyaye saumye ubhakheayutekite 
jtimadhye vyayo nitya ppadk kalahd vyaya  

padd vyaye surcrye vkite cnyakhecarai 
karamld vyayo vcya svasyaiva dvijasattama  

rhd dvdae saure dharputrea sayute 
anyagrahekite vipra bhrtvargd dhanavyaya  

rhd dvdae sthne ye yog kathit yath 
lbhabhve ca te yog lbhayogakarstath  

rht saptame rhurathav sasthita ikh 
kukivyathyuto bla ikhin pitotha v  

rdht saptame ketu ppakheayutekita 
shas vetake ca vddhalig bhavennara  

padttu saptame sthne guruukranikar 
trayo dvayamathaiko'pi lakmvn jyate jana  

svatuge saptame khea ubho v'pyaubha padt 
rmn so'pi bhavennuna satkrtisahito dvija  

ye yog saptame sthne padca kathit may 
cintystathaiva te yog dvitye'pi sad dvija  

uccastho rauhieyo v jvo v ukra eva v 
evo bal dhanagata riya diati dehina  

ye yogca pade lagne yathvad gadit may 
te yog krake'pi vijey bdhavarjit  

rhd vittabhe saumye sarvadedhipo bhavet 
sarvajo yadi v sa syt kavirvd ca bhrgave  

rdht kendrakoeu sthite drapade dvija 
lagnajypade vpi sabalagrahasayute  

srmca jyate nna dee vikhytimn bhavet 
aheame vyayasthne jto drapade'dhana  

pade tatsaptame vpi kendre vddhau trikoake 
suvrya sasthita kheta bhrybhartsukhaprada  

padddrapade caiva kendre koe ca sasthite 
dvayormaitr bhavennna trike vaira na saaya  

eva lagnapadd vipra tanaydipade sthite 
mitrmitre vijnyllbhlbhau vicakaa  

lagnadrapade vipra mitha kendragate yadi 
trilbhayostrikoe v tath rj dhardhipa  

eva lagnapaddeva dhandipadato dvija 
sthnadvaya samlokya jtakasya phala vadet

              athopapaddhyya  

medskip

athopapadamritya kathaymi phala dvija 
yucchubhatve bhavenn putradrdija sukham  

tanubhvapada vipra pradhna padamucyate
