                 athā'rgalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

bhagavān yā'rgalā proktā śubhadā bhavatā'dhunā 
tāmahaṃ srotumicchāmi salakṣaṇaphalaṃ mune  

maitreya sārgalā nāma yayā bhāvaphalaṃ dṛḍham 
sthiraṃ kheṭaphalaṃ ca syāt sā'dhunā kathyate mayā  

caturthe ca dhane lābhe grahe jñeyā tadargalā 
tadbādhakāḥ kramāt kheṭā vyomariṣphatṛtīyagāḥ  

nirbalā nyūnasaṃkhyā vā bādhakā naiva sammatāḥ 
tṛtīye vyādhikāḥ pāpā yatra maitreya bādhakāḥ  

tatrāpi cārgalā jñeyā viparītā dvijottama 
tathāpi kheṭabhāvānāṃ phalamargalitaṃ viduḥ  

pañcamaṃ cārgalāsthānaṃ navamaṃ tadvirodhakṛt 
tamograhabhavā sā ca vyatyayāj jñāyate dvija  

ekagrahā kaniṣṭhā sā dvigrahā madhyamā smṛtā 
argalā dvyadhikotpannā munibhiḥ kathitottamā  

rāśito grahataścāpi vijñeyā dvividhā'rgalā 
nirbādhakā suphaladā viphalā ca sabādhakā  

yatra rāśau sthitaḥ kheṭastasya pākāntaraṃ yadā 
tasmin kāle phalaṃ jñeyaṃ nirviśaṃkaṃ dvijottama  

argalāṃ pratibandhañca kathamāṃghricaturthayoḥ 
dvitryaṅghrayośca mitho vipra cintayediti me matam  

pade lagne made vāpi nirābhāsārgalā yadā 
tadā jāto'tivikhyāto bahubhāgyayuto bhavet  

yasya pāpaḥ śubho vāpi grahastiṣṭhet śubhārgale 
tena draṣṭrekṣitaṃ lagnaṃ prābalyāyopakalpyate  

sārgale ca dhane vipra dhanadhānyasamanvitaḥ 
tṛtīye sodarādīnāṃ sukhamuktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ  

caturthe sārgale gehapaśubandhukulairyutaḥ 
pañcame putrapautrādisaṃyuto buddhimānnaraḥ  

ṣaṣṭhe ripubhayaṃ kāme dhanadārasukhaṃ bahu 
aṣṭame jāyate kaṣṭaṃ dharme bhāgyodayo bhavet  

daśame rājasammānaṃ lābhe lābhasamanvitaḥ 
sārgale ca vyaye vipra vyayādhikyaṃ prajāyate  

śubhagrahārgalāyāṃ tu saukhyaṃ bahuvidhaṃ bhavet 
madhyaṃ pāpārgalāyāṃ ca miśrāyāmapi cottamam  

lagnapañcamabhāgyeṣu sārgaleṣu dvijottama 
jātaśca jāyate rājā bhāgyavān nātra saṃśayaḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

                atha kārakādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

athā'haṃ sampravakṣyāmi grahānātmādikārakān 
saptaravyādiśanyantān rāhvantān vā'ṣṭasaṃkhyakān  

aṃśaiḥ samaugnahau dvau cedrāhvantan cintayet tadā 
saptaiva kārakānevaṃ kecidaṣṭau pracakṣate  

atmā sūryādikheṭānāṃ madhye hyaṃśādhiko grahaḥ 
aṃśasāmye kalādhikyāt tatsāmye vikalādhikaḥ  

budhau rāśikalādhikyat grāhvo naivātmakārakaḥ 
aṃśādhikaḥ kārakaḥ syādalpabhāgo'ntyakārakaḥ  

madhyāṃśo madhyakheṭaḥ syādupakheṭaḥ sa eva hi 
vilomagamanādrāhoraṃśāḥ śodhyāḥ khavahnitaḥ  

aṃśakramādadho'dhaḥsthāścarākhyāḥ kārakā iti 
ātmākhyakārakasteṣu pradhānaṃ kathyate dvija  

sa eva jātakādhīśo vijñeyo dvijasattama 
yathā bhūmau prasiddho'sti narāṇāṃ kṣitipālakaḥ  

sarvavārtādhikārī ca bandhakṛnmokṣakrat tathā  

yathā rājājñayā viprā putrāmātyādayo janāḥ 
samarthā lokakāryeṣu tathaivānyepi kārakāḥ  

ātmānukūlamevātra bhavanti phaladāyakaḥ 
pratikūle yathā bhūpe sarve'mātyādayo dvija  

karya kartuṃ manuṣyānāṃ na samarthā bhavanti hi 
tathā'tmakārake krūre nā'nye svaśubhadāyakaḥ  

anukūle nṛpe yadvat sarve'mātyādayo dvija 
nāśubhaṃ kurvate tadvanānye svāśubhadāyakāḥ  

ātmākārakabhāgebhyo nyūnāṃśo'mātyakārakaḥ 
tasmānnyūnāṃśako bhrātā tannyūnomātṛsaṃjñakaḥ  

tannyūnāṃśaḥ pitātasmādalpāṃśaḥ putrakārakaḥ 
putrānnyūnāṃśako jñatirjñāternyūnāṃśako hi yaḥ  

sa dārakārako jñeyo nirviśaṃke dvijottama 
carākhyakāralā ete brāhmaṇā kathitāḥ purā  

mātṛkārakamevā'nye vadanti sutakārakam 
dvau grahau bhāgatulyau cejjāyetāṃ yasya janmani  

tadagrakārakasyaivaṃ lopo jñeyo dvijottama 
sthirakārakavaśāttasya phalaṃ jñeyaṃ śubhā'śubham  

adhunā sampravakṣyāmi sthirākhyān karakagrahān 
sa pitṛkārako jñeyo yo balī raviśukrayoḥ  

candrārayorbalī kheṭo mātṛkāraka ucyate 
bhaumato bhaginī śyālaḥ kanīyān jananītyapi  

budhānmātṛsajātīyā mātulādyāśca bāndhavāḥ 
guroḥ pitāmahaḥ śukrāt pitaḥ putraḥ śanaiścarāt  

viprāntevāsinaḥ patnī pitarau śvaśurau tathā 
mātāmahādayaścintyā ete ca sthirakārakā  

athā'haṃ kārakān vakṣye kheṭabhāvavaśāddvija 
ravitaḥ punyabhe tātaścandrānmātā caturthake  

kujāt tṛtīyato bhrātā budhāt ṣaṣthe ca mātulaḥ 
devejyāt pañcamāt putro dārāḥ śukrācca saptame  

mandādaṣṭamato mṛtyuḥ pitrādīnāṃ vicintayet 
iti sarva vicāryaiva budhastattat phalaṃ vadet  

athā'haṃ sampravakṣyāmi prasaṅgādyogakārakān 
kheṭān janmani jātasya miśraḥ sthitivaśād dvija  

svarkṣe svocce ca mitrarkṣe mithaḥ kendragatā grahāḥ 
te sarve kārakāsteṣu karmagastu viśeṣataḥ  

yathā lagne sukhe kāme svorkṣoccasthā grahā dvija 
bhavanti kārakākhyāste viśeṣeṇa ca khe sthitāḥ  

svamitroccarkṣago heturanyo'nyaṃ yadi kendragaḥ 
suhṛt tadguṇasampannaḥ so'pi kāraka ucyate  

nīcānvaye'pi yo jātaḥ vidyamāne ca kārake 
so'pi rājamano vipra dhanavān sukhasaṃyutaḥ  

rājavaṃśasamutpanno rājā bhavati niścayāt 
evaṃ kulānusāreṇa kārakebhyaḥ phalaṃ vadet  

athā'haṃ sampravakṣyāmi viśeṣaṃ bhāvakārakān 
janasya janmalagnaṃ yat vindyādātmakārakam  

dhanabhāvaṃ vijānīyād dārakārakameva hi 
ekādaśe'grajātasya tṛtīye tu kanīyasaḥ  

sute sutaṃ vijānīyāt patnīṃ saptamabhāvataḥ 
sutabhave graho yaḥ syāt so'pi kāraka ucyate  

sūryo guruḥ kujaḥ somo gururbhaubhaḥ sitaḥ śaniḥ 
guruścandrasuto jīvo mandaśca bhavakārakāḥ  

punastanvādayo bhāvaḥ sthāpyāsteṣāṃ śubhā'śubham 
lābhastṛtīyo randhraśca śatrusaṃjñadhanavyayāḥ  

ete bhāvāḥ samākhyātāḥ krūrākhyā dvijasattama 
eṣāṃ yogena yo bhāvastasya hāniḥ prajāyate  

bhāvā bhadrāśca kendrāravyāḥ koṇākhyau dvijasattama 
eṣāṃ saṃyogamātreṇa hvaśubho'pi śubho bhavet  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha kārakāṃśaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

athā'haṃ sampravakṣyāmi kārakāṃśaphalaṃ dvija 
meṣādirāśige svāṃśe yathāvad brahmabhāṣitam  

gṛhe mūṣakamārjārā meṣāṃśe hvātmakārake 
sadā bhayapradā vipra pāpayukte viśeṣataḥ  

vṛṣāṃśakagate svasmin sukhadāśca catuṣpadāḥ 
mithunāṃśagate tasmin kaṇḍvādivyādhisambhavaḥ  

karkāṃśe ca jalādbhītiḥ simhāṃśe śvapadādbhayam 
kaṇḍūḥ sthaulyañca kanyāṃśe tathā vahnikaṇādbhayam  

tulāṃśe ca vaṇig jāto vasrādinirmitau paṭuḥ 
alyaṃśe sarpato bhītiḥ pīḍā mātuḥ payodhare  

dhanuraṃśe kramāduccāt patanaṃ vāhanādapi 
marakāṃśe jalodbhūtairjantubhiḥ khecarastathā  

śaṃkhamuktāpravālādyairlābho bhavati niścitaḥ 
kumbhāṃśe ca taḍāgādikārako jāyate janaḥ  

mīnāṃśe kārake jāto muktibhāg dvijasattama 
nā'śubhaṃ śubhasaṃdṛṣṭe na śubhaṃ pāpavīkṣite  

kārakāṃśe śubhe vipra lagnāṃśe ca śubhagrahe 
śubhasaṃvīkṣite jāto rājā bhavati niścitaḥ  

svāṃśācchubhagrahāḥ kendre koṇe vā pāpavarjitāḥ 
dhanavidyāyuto jāto miśrairmiśraphalaṃ vaded  

upagrahe ca viprendra svoccasvarkṣaṃsubharkṣage 
pāpadṛgrahite cā'ntye kaivalyaṃtasya nirdiśet  

candrā'rabhṛguvargastha kārake pāradārikaḥ 
viparyasthe'nyathā jñeyaṃ phalaṃ sarvaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ  

kārakāṃśe ravau jāto rājakāryaparo dvija 
pūrṇendrau bhogavān vidvān śukradṛṣṭe viśeṣataḥ  

svāṃśe balayute bhaume jātaḥ kantāyughī bhavet 
vahnijīvī naro vā'pi rasavādī ca jāyate  

budhe balayute svāṃśe kalāśilpavicakṣanaḥ 
vāṇijyakuśalaścāpi buddhividyāsamanvitaḥ  

sukarmā jñānaniṣṭhaśca vedavit svāṃśage gurau 
śukre śatendriyaḥ kāmī rājakīto bhavennaraḥ  

śanau svāṃśagate jātaḥ svakulocitakarmakṛt 
rāhau cauraśca dhanuṣko jāto vā lohayantrakṛt  

viṣavaidyo'thavā vipra jāyate nā'tra saṃśayaḥ 
vyayahārī gajādīnāṃ ketau cauraśca jāyate  

ravirāhū yadā svāṃśe sarpād bhītiḥ prajāyate 
śubhadṛṣṭau bhayaṃ naiva pāpadṛṣṭau mṛtibhavet  

śubhaṣaḍvargasaṃyuktau viṣavaidyo bhaven tadā 
bhaumekṣite kārakāṃśe bhānusvarbhānusaṃyute  

anyagrhā na paśyanti svaveśmaparadāhakaḥ 
tasmin budhekṣi te cāpi vahnido naiva jāyate  

pāparkṣe guruṇā dṛṣṭe samīpagṛhadāhakaḥ 
śukradṛṣṭe tu viprendra gṛhadāho na jāyate  

gulikena yute svāṃśe pūrṇacandreṇa vīkṣite 
caurairhṛtadhano jātaḥ svayaṃ cauro'thavā bhavet  

gṛhādṛṣṭe sagulike vipado vā viṣairhataḥ 
budhadṛṣṭe bṛhadvījo jāyate nā'tra saṃśayaḥ  

saketau kārakāṃśe ca pāpadṛṣṭe dvijottama 
jātasya karṇarogo vā karṇacchedaḥ prajāyate  

bhṛguputrekṣite tasmin dīkṣito jāyate janaḥ 
budhārkidṛṣṭe nirvīryo jāyate mānavo dhruvam  

budhaśukrekṣite tasmin dāsīputraḥ prajāyate 
punarbhavāsuto vā'pi jāyate nā'tra saṃśayaḥ  

tapasvī saninā dṛṣṭe jātaḥ preṣyo'thavā bhavet 
śanimātrekṣite tasmin jātaḥ saṃnyāsiveṣavān  

ravisukrekṣite tasmin rājapreṣyo jano bhavet 
itisaṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ kārakāṃśaphalaṃ dvija  

svāṃśāddhane ca śukrāravarge syāt pāradārikaḥ 
tayordṛgyogato jñeyamidamāmaraṇaṃ phalam  

ketau tatpratibandhaḥ syāt gurau tu sraiṇa eva saḥ 
rāhau cā'rthanivṛttiḥ syāt kārakāṃśād dvitīyage  

svāṃśāt tṛtīyage pāpe jātaḥ śūraḥ pratāpavān 
tasmin śubhagrahe jātaḥ kātaro nātra saṃśayaḥ  

svāṃśāccaturthabhāve tu candraśukrayutekṣite 
tatra vā svoccage kheṭe jātaḥ prāsādavān bhavet  

śanirāhuyute tasmain jātasya ca śilāgṛham 
aiṣṭikaṃ kujaketubhyāṃ guruṇā dāravaṃ gṛham  

tārṇa tu raviṇā proktaṃ jātasya bhavanaṃ dvija 
candre tvanāvṛte deśe patnīyoogaḥ prajāyate  

pañcame kujarāhubhyāṃ kṣayarogasya saṃbhavaḥ 
rātrināthena dṛṣṭābhyāṃ niścayena prajāyate  

kujadṛṣṭau tu jātasya piṭakādigado bhavet 
ketudṛṣṭau tu grahaṇī jalarogo'thavā dvija  

sarāhugulike tatra bhayaṃ kṣudaviṣodbhavam 
budhe paramahaṃsaśca laguḍī vā prajāyate  

ravau kheḍgadharo jātaḥ kuje kuntāyudhī bhavet 
śanau dhanurdharo jñeyo rāhau ca lohayantravān  

ketau ca ghaṭikāyantrī mānavo jāyate dvija 
bhārgave tu kavirvāgmī kāvyajño jāyate janaḥ  

svāṃśe tatpañcame vā'pi candrejyābhyāṃ ca granthakṛt 
śukreṇa kiñcidūno'sau tato'pyalpo budhena ca  

guruṇā kevalenaiva sarvavid granthakṛt tathā 
vedavedāntaviccāpi na vāgmī śābdako'pi san  

naiyāyikaḥ kujenāsau jñena mīmāṃsakastathā 
sabhājaḍastu śaninā gītajño raviṇā smṛtaḥ  

candreṇa sāṃkhyayogajñaḥ sāhityajñaśca gāyakaḥ 
ketunā gaṇitajño'sau rāhaṇā'pi tathaiva ca  

sapradāyasya sidhhiḥ syāt gurusambandhato dvija 
svāṃśād dvitīyataḥ kecit phalamevaṃ vadanti hi  

svāṃśāt ṣaṣṭhagate pāpe karṣako jāyate janaḥ 
śubhagrahe'lasaśceti tṛtīye'pi phalaṃ smṛtam  

dyūne candraguru yasya bhāryā tasyātisundarī 
tatra kāmavatī śukre budhe caiva kalāvatī  

ravau ca svakule guptā śanau cāpi vayo'dhikā 
tapasvinī rujāḍhya vā rāhau ca vidhavā smṛtā  

śubhasvāmiyute randhre svāṃśād dīrghāyurucyate 
pāpekṣitayute'lpāyurmadhyāyurmiśradṛgyute  

kārakāṃśācca navame śubhagrahayutekṣita 
satyavādī gurau bhaktaḥ svadharmanirato naraḥ  

svāṃśācca navame bhāve pāpagrahayutekṣite 
svadharmanirato bālye mithyāvādī ca vārdhake  

navame kārakāṃśācca śanirāhuyutekṣite 
gurudrohī bhaved bālaḥ śāstreṣu vimukho naraḥ  

kārakāṃśācca navame gurubhānuyutekṣite 
tadā'pi gurudrohī syāt guruvākyaṃ na manyate  

kārakāṃśācca navame śukrabhaumayutekṣite 
ṣaḍvargādikayoge tu maraṇaṃ pāradārikam  

kārakāṃśācca navame jñenduyuktekṣite dvija 
parastrī saṅgamād bālo bandhako bhavati dhruvam  

navame kevalenaive guruṇā ca yutekṣite 
strīlotupo bhavejjāto viṣayī caiva jāyate  

kārakāṃśācca daśame śubhalheṭayutekṣite 
sthiravitto bhaved bālo gambhīro balabuddhimān  

daśame kārakāṃśācca pāpakheṭayutekṣite 
vyāpāre jāyate hāniḥ pitṛsaukhyena varjitaḥ  

daśame kārakāṃśācca budhaśukrayutekṣite 
vyāpāre bahulābhaśca mahatkarmakaor naraḥ  

kārakāṃśācca daśame ravicandrayutekṣite 
gurudṛṣṭayute vipra jātako rājyabhāg bhavet  

svāṃśādekādaśe sthāne śubhakheṭayutekṣite 
bhrātṛsaukhyayuto bālaḥ sarvakāryeṣu lābhakṛt  

ekādaśe sapāpe tu kumārgāllābakṛnnaraḥ 
vikhyāto vikramī caiva jāyate nā'tra saṃśayaḥ  

kārakāṃśād vyayasthāne sadgrahe sadvyayo bhavet 
asadvyayo'śubhe jñayo grahābhāve ca satphalam  

kārakāṃśād vyayasthāne svabhoccasthe śubhagrahe 
sadgatirjāyate tasya śubhalokamavāpnuyāt  

kārakāṃśād vyaye ketau śubhakheṭayutekṣite 
tadā tu jāyate muktiḥ sāyujyapadamāpnuyāt  

meṣe dhanuṣi vā ketau kārakāṃśāt vyaye sthite 
śubhakheṭena sandṛṣṭe sāyujapadamāpnuyāt  

vyaye ca kevale ketau pāpayuktekṣitepi vā 
na tadā jāyate muktiḥ śubhalokaṃ na paśyati  

raviṇā saṃyute ketau kārakāṃśād vyayasthite 
śivabhaktirbhavesyatta nirviśaṃkaṃ dvijottama  

candreṇa saṃyute ketau kārakāṃśād vyayasthite 
gauryāṃ bhaktirbhavettasya śāktiko jāyate naraḥ  

śukreṇa saṃyute ketau kārakāṃśād vyayasthite 
lakṣmyāṃ sañjāyate bhaktirjātako sau samṛddhimān  

kujena saṃyute ketau skandabhaktau bhavennaraḥ 
vaiṣṇavo budhasauribhyāṃ guruṇā śivabhaktimān  

rāhuṇā tāmasīṃ durgāṃ sevate kṣudradevatām 
bhaktiḥ skande'tha herabhbhe śikhinā kevalena vā  

kārakāṃśād vyaye sauriḥ pāparāśau yadā bhavet 
tadā'pi kṣudradevasya bhaktistasya na saṃśayaḥ  

pāparkṣe'pi śanau sukre tadā'pi kṣudrasevakaḥ 
amātyakārakāt ṣaṣṭheptevameva phalaṃ vadet  

kārakāṃśāt trikoṇasthe pāpakhetadvaye dvija 
mānavo mantratantrajño jāyate nā'tra saṃśayaḥ  

pāpena vīkṣite tatra jāto nigrāhako bhavet 
śubhairnirīkṣite tasmin naro'nugrāhako bhavet  

śukradṛṣṭe vidhau svāṃśe rasavādī bhavennaraḥ 
budhadṛṣṭe ca sadvaidyaḥ sarvarogaharo bhavet  

śukradṛṣṭe sukhe candre pāṇḍuśvitrī bhavennaraḥ 
bhaumadṛṣṭe mahārogī raktapittārdito bhavet  

ketudṛṣṭe sukhe caṃdre nīlakuṣṭhī prajāyate 
caturthe pañcamevā'hi sthitau rāhukujau yadi  

kṣayarogo bhavet tasya candradṛṣṭau tu niścitaḥ 
svāṃśāt sukhe sute vā'pi kevalaḥ saṃsthitaḥ kujaḥ  

piṭkādirbhavet tasya tadā rogo na saṃśayaḥ 
grahaṇī jalarogo vā tatra ketau sthite sati  

khvarbhānugulikau tatra viṣavaidyo viṣārditaḥ 
svāṃśakāt pañcame bhāve kevale saṃsthite śanau  

dhanurvidyāvidā jātā bhavantyatra na saṃśayaḥ 
ketau ca kevale tatra ghaṭikāyantrakārakaḥ  

budhe paramahaṃso vā daṇḍī bhavati mānavaḥ 
lohayantrī tathā rāhau ravau kheḍgadharo bhavet  

kevale ca kuje tatra jātaḥ kuntāstradhārakaḥ 
svāṃśe vā pan'came svāṃśāccandrejyau saṃsthitau tadā  

granthakartā bhavejjātaḥ sarvavidyāviśāradaḥ 
tatra daityagurau kiñcidūnagranthakaro bhavet  

budhe tatra tato'pyūnagranthakarttā prajāyate 
tatra śukre kavirvāgmī kāvyajñaśca prajāyate  

sarvavidgrānthiko jīve na vāgmī ca sabhādiṣu 
śabdajñaśca viśeṣeṇa vedavedāntavit tathā  

sabhājaḍo bhaved bāla uktasthānagate śanau 
mīmāṃsako bhavennūnamuktasthānagate budhe  

svāṃśe vā pañcame bhaume jāto naiyāyiko bhavet 
candre ca sāṃkhyayogajñaḥ sāhityajñaśca gāyakaḥ  

ravau vedāntaviccaiva gītajñaśca prajāyate 
ketau ca gaṇitajñaḥ syājjyotiḥśāstraviśāradaḥ  

sampradāyasya saṃsiddhirgurusambandhato bhavet 
dvitīye ca tṛtīye ca svāṃśādevaṃ vicārayet  

bhāve sūkṣmaphalaṃ jñātvā jātakasya phalaṃ vadet 
ketau svāṃśāddvitīye vā tṛtīye stabdhavāg bhavet  

pāpadṛṣṭe viśeṣeṇa mānavo vaktumakṣamaḥ 
svāṃśāllagnāt padādvā'pi dvitīyāṣṭamabhāvayoḥ  

kemadrumaḥ pāpasāmye candradṛṣṭau viśeṣataḥ 
atrā'dhyāye ca ye yogāḥ saphalāḥ kathitā mayā  

yogakartṛdaśāyānte jñeyāḥ sarve phalapradāḥ 
evaṃ daśāpradādrāśairdvitīyāṣṭamayordvija  

grahasāmye ca vijñeyo yogaḥ kemadrumo'śubhaḥ 
daśāprārambhasamaye salagnān sādhayed grahān  

jñeyastatrāpi yogo'yaṃ pāpasāmye'rtharandhrayoḥ 
evaṃ tanvādibhāvānāṃ sūryādīnāṃ nabhasadām  

tattatsthityanusāreṇa phalaṃ vācyaṃ vipaścitā 
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ kārakāṃśaphalaṃ mayā  

medskiphrulemedskip

           atha yogakārakādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

kārakāṃśavaśādevaṃ phalaṃ proktaṃ mayā dvija 
atha bhāvādhipatyena grahayogaphalaṃ srṛṇu  

kendrādhipatayaḥ saumyā nā diśanti śubhaṃ phalam 
krūrā naivā'śubhaṃ kuryuḥ śubhadāśca trikoṇapāḥ  

lagnaṃ kendratrikoṇatvād viśeṣeṇa śubhapradam 
pañcamaṃ navamaṃ caiva viśeṣadhanamucyate  

saptamaṃ daśamaṃ caiva viśeṣasukhamucyate 
triṣaḍāyādhipāḥ sarve grahāḥ pāpaphalāḥ smṛtāḥ  

vyayadvitīyarandhreśāḥ sāhacaryāt phalapradāḥ 
sthānāntarānurodhātte prabalāścottarottaram  

tatra bhāgyavyayeśatvādrandhreśo na śubhapradaḥ 
trimadāyādhipatve'tho koṇapatve tu satphalaḥ  

ukteṣveṣu balī yogo nirbalasya prabādhakaḥ 
na randhreśatvadoṣo'tra sūryācandramasorbhavet  

guruśukrau śubhau proktau candro madhyama ucyate 
udāsīno budhaḥ khyātaḥ pāpā ravyārkibhūmijāḥ  

pūrṇendujñejyaśukrāśca prabalā uttarottaram 
kṣīṇendvarkārkibhūputrāḥ prabalāśca yathottaram  

kendrādhipatyadoṣoyaḥ śubhānāṃ kathito hi saḥ 
candrajñaguruśukrāṇāṃ prabalāścottarottaram  

kendrakoṇapatī syātāṃ parasparagṛhopagau 
ekabhe dvau sthitau vāpi hyekabhe'nyataraḥ sthitaḥ  

pūrṇadṛṣṭyekṣitau vāpi mitho yogakārau tadā 
yoge'smin jāyate bhūpo vikhyāto vā jano bhavet  

koṇeśatve yadaikasya kendreśatvaṃ ca jāyate 
kendre koṇe sthito vā'sau viśeṣādyogakārakaḥ  

kendreśatvena pāpānāṃ yā proktā śubhakāritā 
sā trikoṇādhipatye'pi na kendreśatvamātrataḥ  

kendrakoṇādhipāveva pāpasthānādhipau yadā 
tayoḥ sambandhamātreṇa na yogaṃ labhate naraḥ  

yadbhāveśayutau vāpi yadyadbhāvasamāgatau 
tattatphalāni prabalau pradiśetāṃ tamoprahau  

yadi kendre trikoṇe vā nivasetāṃ tamograhau 
nāthenātyatareṇāḍhyau dṛṣṭau vā yogakārakau  

kasmillagne prajātasya ke grahā yogakārakāḥ 
ke cā'śubhapradāḥ kheṭāḥ kṛpayā vade me mune  

yathā pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā vipra tathodāharaṇaṃ bruve 
randhreśatve'pi bhūputro bhavecchūbhasahāyavān  

mandasaumyasitāḥ pāpāḥ śubhau gurudivākarau 
na śubhaṃ yogamatreṇa prabhavecchanijīvayoḥ  

pāratantryeṇa jīvasya pāpakarmāpi niścitam 
śukraḥ sākṣānnihantā syānmārakatvena lakṣitaḥ  

mandādayo'pi hantāro bhaveyuḥ pāpino grahāḥ 
meṣalagnodbhavasyaivaṃ phalaṃ jñeyaṃ dvijottama  

jīvaśukrendavaḥ pāpāḥ śubhau śanidivākarau 
rājayogakaraḥ saurirbudhastvalpaśubhapradaḥ  

jīvādayo kujaścāpi santi mārakalakṣaṇāḥ 
vṛṣalagnodbhavasyaivaṃ phalānyūhyāni sūribhiḥ  

bhaumajīvāruṇāḥ pāpāḥ eka eva kaviḥ subhaḥ 
śanaiścaraṇe jīvasya yogo meṣabhavo yathā  

śaśī mukhanihantā'sau sāhacaryācca pākadaḥ 
dvandvalagnodbhavasyaivaṃ phalānyūhyāni paṃḍitaiḥ  

bhārgavendusutau pāpau bhūsutejyendavaḥ śubhāḥ 
pūrṇayogakaraḥ sākṣānmaṃgalo maṃgalapradaḥ  

nihantā'rkasuto'rkastu sāhacaryāt phalapradaḥ 
karkalagnodbhavasyaivaṃ phalaṃ proktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ  

saumyaśukrārkajāḥ pāpāḥ kujejyārkāḥ śubhāvahāḥ 
prabhavedyogamātreṇa na śubhaṃ guruśukrayoḥ  

mārakastu śaniścandraḥ sāhacaryāt phalapradaḥ 
siṃhalagne prajātasya phalaṃ jñeyaṃ vipaścitā  

kujajīvendavaḥ pāpāḥ budhaśukrau śubhāvahau 
bhārgavendusutāveva bhavetāṃ yogakārakau  

mārako'pi kaviḥ sūryaḥ sāhacaryaphalapradaḥ 
kanyālagnodbhavasyaivaṃ phalānyūhyāni sūribhiḥ  

jīvārkabhūsutāḥ pāpāḥ śanaiścarabudhau śubhau 
bhavetāṃ rājayogasya kārakau candratatsutau  

kujo nihanti jīvādyāḥ pāpā mārakalakṣaṇāḥ 
śukraḥ samaḥ phalānyevaṃ vijñeyāni tulodbhave  

sitajñaśanayaḥ pāpāḥ śubhau guruniśākarau 
sūryācandramasāveva bhavetāṃ yogakārakau  

kujaḥ samaḥ sitādyāśca pāpā mārakalakṣaṇāḥ 
evaṃ phalaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ vṛścikodayajanmanaḥ  

eka eva kaviḥ pāpaḥ śubhau bhaumadivākarau 
yogo bhāskarasaumyābhyāṃ nihantā bhāskarātmajaḥ  

guruḥ samaphalaḥ khyātaḥ śukro mārakalakṣaṇaḥ 
dhanurlagnodbhavasyaivaṃ phalaṃ jñeyaṃ vipaścitā  

kujajīvendavaḥ pāpāḥ śubhau bhārgavacandrajau 
mandaḥ svayaṃ na hantā syād hanti pāpāḥ kujādayaḥ  

sūryaḥ samaphalaḥ proktaḥ kavirekaḥ suyogakṛt 
mṛgalagnodbhavasyaivaṃ phalānyūhyāni sūribhiḥ  

jīvacandrakujāḥ pāpāḥ śukrasūryātmajau śubhau 
rājayogakaro jñejaḥ kavireva bṛhaspatiḥ  

sūryo bhaumaśca hantāro budho madhyaphalaḥ smṛtaḥ 
kumbhalagnod bhavasyaivaṃ phalānyūhyāni sūribhiḥ  

mandaśukrāṃśumatsaumyāḥ pāpā bhaumavidhū śubhau 
mahīsutagurū yogakārakau ca mahīsutaḥ  

mārako'pi na hantā'sau mandajñau mārakau smṛtau 
mīnalagnod bhavasyaivaṃ phalāni paricintayet  

evaṃ bhāvādhipatyena janmalagnavaśādiha 
śubhatvamaśubhatva ca grahāṇāṃ pratipāditam  

atyānapi punaryogān nābhasādīn vicintya vai 
dehinā ca phalaṃ vācyaṃ pravakṣyāmi ca tānaham  

medskiphrulemedskip

            atha nābhasayogādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

adhunā nābhasā yogāḥ kathyante dvijasattama 
dvātriṃśāt tatprabhedāstu śataghnāṣṭādaśonmitāḥ  

āśrayākhyāstrayo yogāḥ dalasaṃjñaṃ dvayaṃ tataḥ 
ākṛtirviśatiḥ saṃkhyāḥ sapta yogāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  

rajjuśca musalaścaiva nalaścetyāśrayāstrayaḥ 
mālākhyaḥ sarpasaṃjñaśca dalayogau prakīrtitau  

gadākhyaḥ śakaṭākhyaśca srṛṅgāṭakavihaṃgasau 
halavajrayavāścaiva kamalaṃ vāpiyūpakau  

śaraśaktidaṇḍanaukākūṭacchatradhnūṃṣi ca 
ardhacandrastu cakraṃ ca samudraśceti viṃśatiḥ  

saṃkhyākhyāvallakīdāmapāśakedāraśūlakāḥ 
yugo golaśca saptaite yuktā dantamitā dvija  

sarvaiścare sthitai rajjuḥ sthirasthairmusalaḥ smṛtaḥ 
nalākhyo dvisvabhāvasthairāśrayākhyā ime smṛtāḥ  

kendratrayagataiḥ saumyaiḥ pāpairvā dalasaṃjñakau 
kramānmālābhujaṃgākhyau śubhāśubhaphalapradau  

āsannakendradvayagaiḥ sarvairyogo gadāhvayaḥ 
śakaṭaṃ lagnajāyāsthaiḥ khāmbugairvihagaḥ smṛtaḥ  

yogaḥ srṛṅgāṭakaṃ nāma lagnātmajatapaḥsthitaiḥ 
anyasthānāt trikoṇasthaiḥ sarvairyogo halābhighaḥ  

lagnajāyāsthitaiḥ saumyaiḥ pāpākhyaiḥ khā'mbusaṃsthitaiḥ 
yogo vajrābhidhaḥ proktaḥ vīparītasthitairyavaḥ  

sarvakendragataiḥ sarvairmiśraiḥ kamalasaṃjñakaḥ 
kendrādanyatragaiḥ sarvairyogo vāpīsamāhvayaḥ  

yūpo lagnāccaturbhasthaiḥ śarasturyāccaturbhagaiḥ 
śaktirmadāccaturbhasthairdaṇḍo madhyāccaturbhagaiḥ  

lagnāt saptamagainau kā kūṭasturyācca saptamaiḥ 
chatrākhyaḥ saptamādevaṃ cāpaṃ madhyād bhasaptagaiḥ  

lagnādekāntarasthaiśca ṣaḍbhagaiścakramucyate 
dhanādekāntarasthaistu samudraḥ ṣaḍagṛhāśritai  

ekarāśisthitairgolo yugākhyo dvibhasaṃsthitaiḥ 
śūlastu tribhagaiḥ proktaḥ kedārastu caturbhagaiḥ  

pañcarāśisthataiḥ pāśā dāmākhyaḥ ṣaḍgṛhāśritaiḥ 
vīnā saptabhagaiḥ sarvairvihāyānyānudīritān  

aṭanapriyāḥ surūpāḥ paradeśasvāsthyabhāgino manujāḥ 
krūrāḥ khalasvabhāvā rajjuprabhavāḥ sadā kathitāḥ  

mānajñānadhanādyairyuktā bhūpapriyāḥ khyātāḥ 
bahuputrāḥ sthiracittā musalasamutthā bhavanti narāḥ  

nyūnātiriktadehā dhanasañcayabhāgino'tinipuṇāśca 
bandhuhitāśca surūpā nalayoge samprasūyante  

nityaṃ sukhapradhānā vāhanavastrānnabhogasampannā 
kāntā subahustrīkā mālāyāṃ samprasūtāḥ syuḥ  

vuṣamāḥ krūrā niḥsvā nityaṃ duḥkhārditāḥ sudīnāśca 
parabhakṣapānaniratāḥ sarpaprabhavā bhavanti narāḥ  

satatodyuktārthavaśā yajvānaḥ śāstrageyakuśalāśca 
dhanakanakaratnasampatsaṃyuktā mānavā gadāyāṃ tu  

rogārtāḥ kunakhā mūrkhāḥ śakaṭānujīvino niḥsvā 
mitrasvajanavihīnāḥ śakaṭe jātā bhavanti narāḥ  

bhramaṇarucayovikṛṣṭā dūtāḥ suratānujīvano dhṛṣṭāḥ 
kalahapriyāśca nityaṃ vihage yoge sadā jātāḥ  

priyakalahāḥ samarasahāḥ sukhino nṛpateḥ śubhakalatrāḥ 
āḍhyā yuvatidveṣyāḥ srṛṅgāṭakasambhavā manujāḥ  

bahvāśino daridrāḥ kṛṣīvalā duḥkhitāśca sodvegā 
bandhusuhṛdibhaḥ tyaktāḥ preṣyāḥ halasaṃjñake sadā puruṣāḥ  

ādyantavayaḥsukhinaḥ śūrāḥ subhagā nirīhāścaḥ 
bhāgyavihīnā vajre jātāḥ khalā viruddhāśca  

vrataniyamamaṅgalaparā vayaso madhye sukhārthaputrayutā 
dātāraḥ sthiracittā yavayogabhavāḥ sadā puruṣāḥ  

vibhavaguṇādgyāḥ puruṣāḥ sthirāyuṣo vipulakīrtaya śuddhāḥ 
śubhaśatakāḥ pṛthvīśāḥ kamalabhavāḥ mānavā nityam  

nidhikaraṇe nipuṇadhiyaḥ sthirārthasukhasaṃyutā sutayutāśca 
nayanasukhasamprahṛṣṭā vāpīyogena rājānaḥ  

ātmavidijyānirataḥ striyā yutaḥ sattvasampannaḥ 
vrataniyamaratamanusyo yūpe jāto viśiṣṭaśca  

iṣukārā bandhanapāḥ mṛgayādhanasevitāśca maṃsādā 
hiṃsrāḥ kuśilpakārāḥ śarayoge mānavāḥ prasūyante  

dhanarahitaviphaladuḥkhitanīcalasāścirāyuṣaḥ puruṣāḥ 
saṃgrāmabuddhinipuṇāḥ śaktyāṃ jātāḥ sthirāḥ śubhagāḥ  

hataputradāraniḥsvāḥ sarvatra ca nirdhṛṃṇāḥ svajanabāhyāḥ 
duḥkhitanīcapreṣyā daṇḍaprbhavā bhavanti narāḥ  

salilopajīvivibhavāḥ bahvāśāḥ khyātakīrtayo duṣṭāḥ 
kṛpaṇā malinā lubdhā nausañjātāḥ khalāḥ puruṣāḥ  

anṛtakathanabandhanapā niṣkiñcanāḥ śaṭhāḥ krūrāḥ 
kūṭasamutthā nityaṃ bhavanti giridurgavāsino manujāḥ  

svajanāśrayo dayāvānnānānṛpavallabhaḥ prakṛṣṭamatiḥ 
prathame'ntye vayasi narāḥ sukhavān dīrghāyurātapatrī syāt  

ānṛtikaguptapālāścorāḥ kitavāśca kānane niratāḥ 
kārmukayoge jātā bhāgyavihīnāḥ śubhā vayomadhye  

senāpatayaḥ sarvee kāntaśarīrā nṛpapriyā balinaḥ 
maṇikanakabhūṣaṇayutā bhavanti yoge'rdhacandrākhye  

praṇatā''śeṣanarādhipakirīṭaratnaprabhāsphuritapādaḥ 
bhavati narendro manujaścakre yo jāyate yoge  

bahuratnadhanasamṛddhā bhogayutā dhanajanapriyāḥ sasutā 
udadhisamutthāḥ puruṣāḥ sthiravibhavāḥ sādhuśīlāśca  

priyagītanṛtyavādyā nipuṇāḥ sukhinaśca dhanavantaḥ 
netāro bahubhṛtyā vīṇāyāṃ kīrtitāḥ puruṣāḥ  

dāmni sujanopakārī nayadhanayukto maheśvaraḥ khyātaḥ 
bahusutaratnasamṛddho dhīro jāyeta vidvāṃśca  

pāśe bandhanabhājaḥ kārye dakṣāḥ prapañcakārāśca 
bahubhāṣiṇo viśīlā bahubhṛtyāḥ sampratānāśca  

subahūnāmupayojyāḥ kṛṣīvalāḥ satyavādinaḥ sukhinaḥ 
kedāre sambhūtāścalasvabhāvā dhanairyuktāḥ  

tīkṣṇālasadhanahīnā hiṃsrāḥ subahiṣkṛtā mahāśūrāḥ 
saṃgrāme labdhayaśā śūle yoge bhavanti narāḥ  

pākhaṇḍavādino vā dhanarahitā vā bahiṣkṛtā loke 
sutamātṛdharmarahitā yugayoge ye narā jātāḥ  

balasaṃyuktā vidhanā vadyāvijñānavarjitā malinā 
nityaṃ duḥkhitadīnā gole yoge bhavanti narāḥ  

sarvāsvapi daśasvete bhaveyuḥ phaladāyinaḥ 
prāṇināmiti vijñeyāḥ pravadanti tavāgrajāḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

           atha vividhayogādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

lagne śubhayute yogaḥ śubhaḥ pāpayute'śubhaḥ 
vyayasvagaiḥ śubhaiḥ pāpaiḥ kramādyogau śubhā'śubhau  

śubhayogodbhavo vāgmī rūpaśīlaguṇavanvitaḥ 
pāpayogodbhavaḥ kāmī pāpakarmā parārthayuk  

kendre devagurau lagnāccandrādvā śubhadṛgyute 
nīcāstārigṛhairhīne yogo'yaṃ gajakesarī  

gajakesarīsañjātastejasvī dhanavān bhavet 
medhāvī guṇasampanno rājapriyakaro naraḥ  

daśame'ṅgāttathā candrāt kevalaiśca śubhairyute 
sa yogo'malakītrtyākhyaḥ kīrtirācandratārakī  

rājapūjye mahābhogī dātā bandhujanapriyaḥ 
paropakārī dharmātmā guṇaḍhyo'malakīrtijaḥ  

saptame cā'ṣṭame śuddhe śubhagrahayute'thavā 
kendreṣu śubhayukteṣu yogaḥ parvatasaṃjñakaḥ  

bhāgyavān parvatotpannaḥ vāgmī dātā ca śāstravit 
hāsyapriyo yaśasvī ca tejasvī puranāyakaḥ  

sukheśejyau mithaḥ kendragatau balini lagnape 
kāhalo vā svabhoccasthe sukheśe karmapānvite  

ojasvī sāhasī dhūrtaścaturaṅgabalānvitaḥ 
yatkiñcid grāmanāthaśca kāhale jāyate naraḥ  

lagneśe tuṅgage kendre gurudṛṣṭe tu cāmaraḥ 
śubhadvaye vilagne vā navame daśame made  

rājā vā rājapujyo vā cirajīvī ca paṇḍitaḥ 
vāgmī sarvakalāvid vā cāmare jāyate janaḥ  

savale lagnape putraṣaṣṭhapau kendragau mithaḥ 
śaṃkho vā lagnakarmeśau care balini bhāgyape  

dhanastrīputrasaṃyukto dayāluḥ puṇyavān sudhīḥ 
puṇyakarmā cirañjīvī śaṃkhayogodbhavo naraḥ  

sabale bhāgyape bherī khagaiḥ svāntyodayāstagaiḥ 
sabale bhāgyape vā'sau kendre śukrejyalagnapaiḥ  

dhanastrīputrasaṃyukto bhūpaḥ kīrtiguṇānvitaḥ 
ācāravān sukhī bhogī bherīyoge jano bhavet  

sabale lagnape kheṭāḥ kendre koṇe svabhoccagāḥ 
mṛgaṅgayogo jāto'tra bhūpo vā tatsamaḥ sukhī  

keemeśe karmage tuṅge karmeśe bhāgyapānvite 
yogaḥ śrīnāthasaṃjño'tra jātaḥ śukrasamo nṛpaḥ  

karmeśe sutage kendre budhe'rke sabale svabhe 
candrāt koṇe gurau jñe vā kuje lābhe ca śāradaḥ  

dhanastrīputrasaṃyuktaḥ sukhī vidvān nṛpapriyaḥ 
tapasvī dharmasaṃyuktaḥ śārade jāyate janaḥ  

dharmalagnagate saumye pañcame sadasadyute 
pāpe ca caturasrasthe yogo'yaṃ matsyasaṃjñakaḥ  

kālajñaḥ karuṇāmūrtirguṇadhībalarūpavān 
yaśovidyātapasvī ca matsyayoge hi jāyate  

putrārimadagāḥ saumyāḥ svabhoccasuhṛdaṃśagāḥ 
trilābhodayagāḥ pāpāḥ kūrmayogaḥ svabhoccagāḥ  

kūrmayoge jano bhūpo dhīro dharmaguṇānvitaḥ 
kīrtimānupakārī ca sukhī mānavanāyakaḥ  

bhāgyeśe dhanabhāvāsthe dhaneśe bhāgyabhāvage 
lagneśe kendrakoṇasthe khaḍgayogaḥ sa kathyate  

khaḍgayoge samutpanno dhanabhāgyasukhānvitaḥ 
śāstrajño buddhivīryāḍhyaḥ kṛtajñaḥ kuśalo naraḥ  

kendre mūlatrikoṇaste bhāgyeśe vā svabhoccage 
lagnādhipe balāḍhye ca lakṣmīyogaḥ prakīrtyate  

surūpo guṇavān bhūpo bahuputradhanānvitaḥ 
yaśasvī dharmasampanno lakṣmīyoge jano bhavet  

lagne sthire bhṛgau kendre candrakoṇe śabhānvite 
mānasthānagate saure yogo'yaṃ kusumābhidhaḥ  

bhūpo vā bhūpatulyo vā datā bhogī sukhī janaḥ 
kulamukhyo guṇī vidvān jāyate kusumāhvaye  

dvitīye pañcame jīve budhaśukrayutekṣite 
kṣatre tayorvā samprapte yogaḥ sa ca kalānidhiḥ  

kalānidhisamutpanno guṇavān bhūpavanditaḥ 
rogahīnaḥ sukhī jāto dhanavidyāsamanvitaḥ  

lagneśatadgatarkṣeśatadgatarkṣeśatadaṃśapāḥ 
kendre koṇe svatuṅge vā yogaḥ kalpadrumo mataḥ  

sarvaiśvaryayuto bhūpo dharmātmā balasaṃyutaḥ 
yuddhapriyo dayāluśca pārijāte naro bhavet  

svāntyāṣṭasthairdvitīyeśād hariyogaḥ śubhagrahaiḥ 
kāmeśād bandhudharmāṣṭasthitaiḥ saumyairharābhidhaḥ  

lagneśād bandhukarmāyasthitairbrahmāhvayaḥ smṛtaḥ 
eṣu jātaḥ sukhī vidvān dhanaputrādisaṃyutaḥ  

lagnānmadāṣṭagaiḥ saumyaiḥ pāpadṛgyogavarjitaiḥ 
yogo lagnādhiyogo'smin mahātmā śāstravit sukhī  

lagnape pārijātasthe sukhī vargottame hyaruk 
gopure dhanadhānyāḍhyā bhūpaḥ siṃhāsane sthite  

vidvān pārāvate śrīmān devaloke savāhanaḥ 
airāvatasthite jāto vikhyāto bhūpavanditaḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha candrayogādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

sahasraraśmitacandre kaṇṭakādigate kramāt 
dhanadhīnaipuṇādīni nyūnamadhyottamāni hi  

svāṃśe vā svādhimitrāṃśe sthitaśca divase śaśī 
guruṇā dṛśyate tatra jāto dhanasukhānvitaḥ  

svāṃśe vā svādhimitrāṃśe sthitaśca śaśabhṛnniśi 
śukreṇa dṛśyate tatra jāto dhanasukhānvitaḥ  

etadviparyayasthe ca śukrejyānavalokite 
jāyate'lpadhano bālo yoge'sminnirdhano'thavā  

candrādrandhrārikāmasthai saumyaiḥ syādhiyogakaḥ 
tatra rājā ca mantrī ca senādhīśaśca balakramāt  

candrād vṛddhigataiḥ sarvaiḥ śubhairjāto mahādhanī 
dvābhyāṃ madhyadhano jāta ekenā'lpadhano bhavet  

candrāt svāntyobhayasthe hi grahe sūryaṃ binā kramāt 
sunaphākhto'naphākhyaśca yogo duradharāhvayaḥ  

rājā vā rājatulyo vā dhīdhanakhyātimāñjanaḥ 
svabhujārjitavittaśca sunaphāyogasambhavaḥ  

bhūpo'gadaśarīraśca śīlavān khyātakīrtimān 
surūpaścā'naphājāto sukhaiḥ sarvaiḥ samanvitaḥ  

utpannasukhabhug dātā dhanavāhanasaṃyutaḥ 
sadbhṛtyo jāyate nūnaṃ jano duradharābhavaḥ  

candrādādyadhanā'ntyastho vinā bhānuṃ na cedgrahaḥ 
kaścit syādvā vinā candraṃ lagnāt kendragato'tha vā  

yogaḥ kemadrumo nāma tatra jāto'tigarhitaḥ 
buddhividyāvihīnaśca daridrāpattisaṃyutaḥ  

anyayogaphalaṃ hanti candrayogo viśeṣataḥ 
svaphalaṃ pradadātīti budho yatnād vicintayet  

medskiphrulemedskip

            atha raviyogādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

sūryāt svantyobhayasthaiśca vinā candraṃ kujādibhiḥ 
veśivośisamākhyau ca tathobhayacaraḥ kramāt  

samadṛk satyavāṅ martyo dīrghakāyo'lasastathā 
sukhabhāgalpavitto'pi veśiyogasamudbhavaḥ  

vośau ca nipuṇo dātā yaśovidyābalāvantiḥ 
tathobhayacare jāto bhūpo vā tatsamaḥ sukhī  

śubhagrahabhave yoge phalamevaṃ vicintayet 
pāpagrahasamutpanne yoge tu phalamanyathā  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha rājayogādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

athā'taḥ sampravakṣyāmi rāyayogān dvijottama 
yeṣāṃ vijñānamātreṇa rājapūjyo jano bhavet  

ye yogāḥ śambhunā proktāḥ purā śailasutāgrataḥ 
teṣāṃ sāramahaṃ vakṣye tavāgre dvijanandana  

cintayet kārakāṃśe vā janurlagne'tha vā dvija 
rājayogakarau dvau dvau sphuṭau kheṭau prayatnataḥ  

ātmakārakaputrābhyāṃ yogamekaṃ prakalpayet 
tanupañcamanāthābhyāṃ tathaiva dvijasattama  

lagnaputreśayorātmaputrakārakayordvayoḥ 
sambandhāt pūrṇamardhaṃ vā pādaṃ vīryānusārataḥ  

lagneśe pañcame bhāve pañcameśe ca lagne 
putrātmakārakau vipra lagne ca pañcame sthita  

svocce svaṃśe svabhe vā'pi śubhagrahanirīkṣito 
mahārājākhyayogo'tra jātaḥ khyātaḥ sukhānvitaḥ  

bhāgyeśaḥ kārako lagne pañcame saptame'pi vā 
rājayogapradātārau śubhakheṭayutekṣitau  

lagneśāt kārakāccāpi dhane turye ca pañcame 
śubhakheṭayute bhāve jāto rājā bhaved dhruvam  

tṛtīye ṣaṣṭhabhe tābhyāṃ pāpagrahayutekṣite 
jāto rājā bhavedevaṃ miśre miśraphalaṃ vadet  

svāṃśe vā pañcame śukre jīvenduyutavīkṣite 
lagne lagnapade vā'pi rājavargo bhavennaraḥ  

janmāṅge kālahorāṅge kālaṅge yena kenacit 
ekagraheṇa sandṛṣṭe tritaye rājabhāg janaḥ  

lagnaṣaḍvargake caivamekakheṭayutekṣite 
rājayogo bhavatyeva nirviśaṃka dvijottama  

pūrṇadṛṣṭe pūrnayogamardhadṛṣṭe'rdhameva ca 
pādadṛṣṭe pādayogamiti jñeyaṃ kramāt phalam  

lagnatraye svabhoccasthe kheṭe rājā bhaved dhruvam 
yadvā lagne dṛkāṇeṃ'śe svoccakheṭayute dvija  

pade śubha sacaṃdre ca dhane devagurau tathā 
svoccasthakheṭasandṛṣṭe rājayogo na saṃśayaḥ  

śubhe lagne śubhe tvarthe tṛtīye pāpakhecare 
caturthe ca śubhe prāpte rājā vā tatsamo'pi vā  

svoccastho hariṇāṃko vā jīvo vā śukra eva vā 
budho vā dhanabhāvasthaḥ śriyaṃ diśati dehinaḥ  

ṣaṣṭhe'ṣṭame tṛtīye vā svasvanīcagatā grahāḥ 
lagnaṃ paśyet svabhoccastho lagnapo rājyayogadaḥ  

ṣaṣṭhā'ṣṭamavyayādhīśā nīcasthā ripubhe'sthagāḥ 
svoccasvabhagalagneśo lagnaṃ paśyaṃśca rājyadaḥ  

svoccasvabhastharājyeśo lagnaṃ paśyaṃśca rājyadaḥ 
śubhāḥ kendrasthitā vā'pi rājyadaḥ nā'tra saṃśayaḥ  

śubharāśau śubhāṃśe ca kārako dhanavān bhavet 
tadaṃśakendreṣu śubhe nūnaṃ rājā prajāyate  

lagnārūḍhaṃ dārapadaṃ mithaḥ kendra sthitaṃ yadi 
trilābhe vā trikoṇe vā tadā rājā na saṃśayaḥ  

bhāvahorāghaṭīsaṃjñalagnāni ca prapaśyati 
svoccagrho rājayogo lagnadvayamathāpi vā  

rāśerdreṣkāṇatoṃ'śācca rāśeraṃśādathāpi vā 
yadvā rāśidṛkāṇābhyāṃ lagnadraṣṭā tu yogadaḥ  

pade svoccakhagākrānte candrākrānte viśeṣataḥ 
krānte ca guruśukrābhyāṃ kenāpyuccagraheṇa vā  

duṣṭārgalagrahābhāve rājayogo na saṃśayaḥ 
śubhārūḍhe tatra candre dhane devagurau tathā  

duḥsthāneśo'pi nīcastho yadi lagnaṃ prapaśyati 
tadā'pi rājayogaḥ syāditi jñeyaṃ dvijottama  

caturthadaśamārthāyapatidṛṣṭe vilagnabhe 
padāllābhe tu śukreṇa dṛṣṭe'pyārūḍhabhe śubhe  

rājā vā tatsamo vāpi jātako jāyate dhruvam 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamagate nīce lagnaṃ paśyati vā tathā  

tṛtīyalābhage nīce lagnaṃ paśyati vā tathā 
lagnāṃśakendreṣu śubhe nigrahānugrahakṣamaḥ  

athā'haṃ sampravakṣyāmi rājayogādikaṃ param 
grahāṇāṃ sthānabhedena dṛṣṭiyogavaśāt phalam  

tapaḥsthānādhipo mantrī mantrādhīśo viśeṣataḥ 
ubhāvanyonyasaṃdṛṣṭau jātaścediha rājyabhāk  

yatra kutrāpi saṃyuktau tau vāpi samasaptamau 
rājavaṃśabhavo bālo rājā bhavati niścitam  

vāhaneśastathā māne māneśo vāhane sthitaḥ 
buddhadharmādhipābhyāṃ tu dṛṣṭaścediha rājyabhāk  

sutakarmasuhṛllagnanāthā dharmapasaṃyutāḥ 
yasya janmani bhūpo'sau kīrtyā khyāto digantare  

sukhakarmādipau vāpi mantrināthena saṃyutau 
dharmanāthena vā yuktau jātaścediha rājyabhāk  

suteśe dharmanāthena yute lagneśvareṇa vā 
lagne sukhe'thavā māne sthite jāto nṛpo bhavet  

dharmasthāne sthite jīve svagṛhe bhṛgusaṃyute 
paṃcamādhipayukte vā jātaścediha rājabhāk  

dinārdhācca niśārdhācca paraṃ sārdhadvināḍikā 
śubhā velā tadutpanno rājā syāttatsamo'pi vā  

candraḥ kaviṃ kaviścandramanyo'nyaṃ tribhavasthitaḥ 
mithaḥ paśyati vā kvāpi rājayoga udāhṛtaḥ  

candre vargottamāṃśasthe sabale caturādibhiḥ 
grahairdṛṣṭe ca yo jātaḥ sa rājā bhavati dhruvam  

uttamāṃśagate lagne candrānyaiścaturādibhiḥ 
grahairdṛṣṭe'pi yo jātaḥ so'pi bhūmipatirbhavet  

tryalpairuccasthitaiḥ kheṭe rājā rājakulodbhavaḥ 
anyavaṃśabhavastatra rājatulyo dhanairyutaḥ  

caturbhiḥ pañcabhirvā'pi kheṭaiḥ svoccatrikoṇagaiḥ 
hīnavaṃśabhavaścāpi rājā bhavati niścitaḥ  

ṣaḍbhiruccagataiḥ kheṭaiścakravartitvamāpnuyāt 
evaṃ bahuvidhā rājayogā jñeyā dvijottama  

eko gururbhṛgurvāpi budho vā svoccasaṃsthitaḥ 
śubhagrahayute kendre rājā vā tatsamo bhavet  

kendresthitaiḥ śubhaiḥ sarvaiḥ pāpaiśca triṣaḍāyagaiḥ 
hīnavaṃśo'pi yo jātaḥ sa rājā bhavati dhruvam  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha rājasambandhayogādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

rājyanāthe janurlagnādamātyeśayutekṣite 
amātyakārakeṇāpi pradhānatvaṃ nṛpālaye  

lābheśavīkṣite lābhe pāpadṛgyogavarjite 
rājyabhāve tadā vipra pradhānatvaṃ nṛpālaye  

amātyakārakeṇāpi kārakendreṇa saṃyute 
tīvrabuddhiyuto bālo rājamantrī bhaved dhruvam  

amātyakārake vipra sabale śubhasaṃyute 
svakṣetresvoccage vāpi rājamantrī bhaved dhruvam  

amātyakārake lagne pañcame navame'pi vā 
rājamantrī bhaved bālo vikhyāto nā'trasaṃśayaḥ  

ātmakārakataḥ kendre koṇe vā'mātyakārake 
tadā rājakṛpāyukto jāto rājāśritaḥ sukhī  

kārakācca tathārūḍhāt lagnācca dvijasattama 
tṛtīye ṣaṣṭhabhe pāpaiḥ senādhīśaḥ prajāyate  

kārake kendre koṇeṣu svatuṅge vā svabhe sthite 
bhāgyapena yute dṛṣṭe rājamantrī bhaved dhruvam  

kārake janmarāśīśe lagnage śubhasaṃyute 
mantritve mukhyayogo'yaṃ vārdhakenā'tra saṃśayaḥ  

kārake śubhasaṃyukte pañcame saptame'pi vā 
daśame navame vā'pi dhanaṃ rājāśrayād bhavet  

bhāgyabhāvapade lagne kārake navame'pi vā 
rājasambandhayogo'yaṃ nirviśaṃkaṃ dvijottama  

lābheśe lābhabhāvasthe pāpadṛṣṭivivarjite 
kārake śubhasaṃyukte lābhastasya nṛpālayāt  

lagneśe rājyabhāvasthe rājyeśe lagnasaṃsthite 
prabalo rājasambandhayogo'yaṃ parikīrtitaḥ  

kārakāt turyaṃbhāvasthau sitendū dvijasattama 
yasya janmani jāto'yaṃ rājacihnena saṃyutaḥ  

lagneśe kārake vā'pi pañcameśena saṃyute 
kendre koṇe sthite tasmin rājamitraṃ bhavennaraḥ  

medskiphrule
endindian

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha viśeṣadhanayogā'dhyāyaḥ  

medskip

athā'taḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi dhanayogaṃ viśeṣataḥ 
yasmin yoge samutpanno niścito dhanavān bhavet  

paṇcame bhṛgujakṣetre tasmin śukreṇa saṃyute 
lābhe bhaumena saṃyukte bahudravyasya nāyakaḥ  

paṃcame tu budhakṣetre tasmin budhayuto sati 
candre bhaume gurau lābhe bahudravyasya nāyakaḥ  

paṇcame ca ravikṣetre tasmin raviyute sati 
lābhe śanīndujīvāḍhye bahudravyasya nāyakaḥ  

paṃcame tu śanikṣetre tasmin śaniyute sati 
lābhe ravīndusaṃyukte bahudravyasya nāyakaḥ  

paṃcame tu gurukṣetre tasmin guruyute sati 
lābhe candrasute jāto bahudravyasya nāyakaḥ  

paṃcame tu kujakṣetre tasmin kujayute sati 
lābhasthe bhṛguputre tu bahudravyasya nāyakaḥ  

paṃcame tu śaśikṣetre tasmin śaśiyute sati 
śanau lābhasthite jāto bahudravyasya nāyakaḥ  

bhānukṣetragate lagne tasmin bhānuyute punaḥ 
bhaumena guruṇā yukte dṛṣṭe jāto yuto dhanaiḥ  

candrakṣetragate lagne tasmin candrayute sati 
budhena guruṇā yukte dṛṣṭe jāto dhanī bhavet  

bhaumakṣetre gate lagne tasmin bhaumena saṃyute 
saumyaśukrārkajairyukte dṛṣṭe śrīmānnaro bhavet  

budhakṣetragate lagne tasmin budhayute sati 
śanijīvayute dṛṣṭe jāto dhanayuto bhavet  

gurukṣetragate lagne tasmin guruyute sati 
budhabhaumayute dṛṣṭe jāyate dhanavānnaraḥ  

bhṛgukṣetragate lagne tasmin bhṛguyute sati 
śanisaumyayute dṛṣṭe yo jātaḥ sa dhanī bhavet  

śanikṣetragate lagne tasmin śaniyute sati 
bhaumena guruṇā yukte dṛṣṭe jāto dhanairyutaḥ  

dhanadau dharmadhīnāthau ye vā tābhyāṃ yutā grahāḥ 
te'pi svasvadaśākāle dhanadā nā'tra saṃśayaḥ  

grahāṇāmuktayogeṣu krūrasaumyavibhāgataḥ 
balābalavivekena phalamūhyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ  

kendreśaḥ pārijātasthastadā dātā bhavennaraḥ 
uttame hyuttamo dātā gopure puruṣatvayuk  

siṃhāsane bhavenmānyaḥ śūraḥ pārāvatāṃśake 
sabhādhyakṣo devaloke brahmaloke munirmata 
airāvatāṃśake tṛṣṭo digyogo naiva jāyate  

pārijāte sutādhīśe vidyā caiva kulocitā 
uttame cottamā jñeyā gopure bhuvanāṃkitā  

siṃhāsane tathā vācyā sācivyena samanvitā 
pārāvate ca vijñeyā brahmavidyā dvijottama  

suteśe devalokasthe karmayogaśca jāyate 
upāsanā brahmaloke bhaktistvarāvatāṃśake  

dharmeśe pārijātasthe tīrthakṛttvatra janmani 
pūrvajanmanyapi jñeyastīrthakṛccottamāṃśake  

gaupure makhakartā ca pare caivā'tra janmani 
siṃhāsane bhavedvīraḥ satyavādī jitendriyaḥ  

sarvadharmān parityajya brahmaikapadamāśritaḥ 
pāravate ca paramo haṃaścaivātra janmani  

laguḍī vā tridaṇḍī syāddevaloke na saṃśayaḥ 
brahmaloke śakratadaṃ yāti kṛtvā'śvamedhakam  

airāvate tu dharmātmā svayaṃ dharmo bhaviṣyati 
śrīrāmaḥ kuntiputrādyo yathā jāto dvijottama  

viṣṇusthānaṃ ca kendraṃ syāllakṣmīsthānaṃ trikoṇakam 
tadīśayośca sambandhādrājayogaḥ puroditaḥ  

pārijāte sthitau tau cennṛpo lokānurakṣakaḥ 
uttame cottamo bhūpo gajavājirathādimān  

gopure nṛpaśārdūlaḥ pūjitāṃdhrirnṛpairbhavet 
siṃhāsane cakravartī sarvabhūmiprapālakaḥ  

asmin yoge hariścandro manuścaivottamastathā 
balirvaiśvānaro jātastathānye cakravartinaḥ  

vartamānayuge jātastathā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ 
bhavitā śālivāhādyastathaiva dvijasattama  

pārāvatāṃśake'pyevaṃ jātā manvādayastathā 
viṣṇoḥ sarve'vatārāśca jāyante devalokake  

brahmalokake tu brahmādyā jāyante viśvapālakāḥ 
airāvatāṃśake jātaḥ pūrva svāyaṃbhuvo manuḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

            atha dāridrayyogādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

bahavo dhanadā yogā śrutāstvatto mayā mune 
daridrajanmadān yogān kṛpayā kathaya prabho  

lagneśe ca vyayasthāne vyayeśe lagnamāgate 
mārakeśayute dṛṣṭe nirdhano jāyate naraḥ  

lagneśe ṣaṣṭhabhāvasthe ṣaṣṭheśe lagnamāgate 
mārakeśena yugdṛṣṭe dhanahīnaḥ prajāyate  

lagnendū ketusaṃyuktau lagnape nidhanaṃ gate 
mārakeśayute dṛṣṭe jāto vai nirdhano bhavet  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyayagate lagnape pāpasaṃyute 
dhaneśe ripubhe nīce rājavaṃśyo'pi nirdhanaḥ  

trikeśena samāyukte pāpadṛṣṭe vilagnape 
śaniyukte'dhavā saumyairadṛṣṭe nirdhano naraḥ  

mantreśo dharmanāthaśca kramāt ṣaṣṭhavyayasthitau 
dṛṣṭau cenmārakeśena nirdhano jāyate naraḥ  

pāpagrahe lagnagate rājyadharmādhipau vinā 
mārakeśayute dṛṣṭe jātaḥ syannirdhano bhavet  

trikeśā yatra bhāvasthā tadbhāveśāstrikasthitāḥ 
pāpadṛṣṭayuta bālo duḥkhākrāntaśca nirdhanaḥ  

candrākrāntanavaṃśeśo mārakeśayuto yadi 
mārakasthānago vā'pi jāto'tra nirdhano naraḥ  

lagneśalagnabhāgeśau riśpharandhrārigau yadi 
mārakeśayutau dṛṣṭau jāto'sau nirdhano naraḥ  

śubhasthānagatāḥ pāpāḥ pāpasthānagatāḥ śubhāḥ 
nirdhano jāyate bālo bhojanena prapīḍitaḥ  

koṇeśadṛṣṭihīnā ye trikeśaiḥ saṃyutā grahāḥ 
te sarve svadaśākāle dhanahānikarāḥ smṛtāḥ  

kārakād vā vilagnād vā randhreriṣphe dvijottama 
kārakāṅgapayodṛṣṭyā dhanahīnaḥ prajāyate  

kārakeśo vyayaṃ svasmāt lagneśo lagnato vyayam 
vīkṣate cet tadā bālo vyayaśīlo bhaveddhruvam  

atha dāridryayogāṃst kathayāmi sabhaṅgakān 
dhanasaṃsthau tu bhaumārkī kathitau dhananāśakau  

budhekṣitau mahāvittaṃ kuruto nātra saṃśayaḥ 
niḥsvatāṃ kurute tatra ravirnityaṃ yamekṣitaḥ  

mahādhanayutaṃ khyātaṃ śanyadṛṣṭaḥ karotyasau 
śaniścāpi raverdṛṣṭyā phalamevaṃ prayacchati  

medskiphrulemedskip

            athāyurdāyādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

dhanādhnākhyayogau ca kathitau bhavatā mune 
narāṇāmāyuṣo jñānaṃ kathayasva mahāmate  

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā vipra janānāṃ ca hitecchayā 
kathayāmyāyuṣo jñānaṃ durjñeyaṃ yat surairapi  

āyurjñānavibhedāstu bahubhirbahudhoditāḥ 
teṣāṃ sārāṃśamādāya prvadāmi tavā'grataḥ  

svoccanīcādisaṃsthityā grahā āyuḥpradāyakāḥ 
svasvavīryavaśairnaivaṃ nakṣatrāṇ ca rāśayaḥ  

piṇḍāyuḥ prathamaṃ tatra grahasthitivaśādaham 
kathayāmi dvijaśreṣṭha śraṇuṣvekāgramānasaḥ  

kramāt sūryādikheṭeṣu svasvoccasthānageṣviha 
nandendavastacvamitāstithayo'rkāḥ śarendavaḥ  

prakṛyato viṃśatiścābdā āyuḥpiṇḍāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
nīcageṣvetadardhañca jñeyaṃ madhye'nupātataḥ  

svaccaśuddhau grahaḥ śodhyaḥ ṣaḍbhādūno bhamaṇḍlāt 
svapiṇḍaguṇito bhakto bhādimānena vatsarāḥ  

astagastu haretsvārdha vinā śukraśanaiścarau 
vakracāraṃ vinā tryāṃśāṃ śajñurāśau hared grahaḥ  

sarvārdhatricatuḥpañcaṣaṣṭhabhāgaṃ kramād grahaḥ 
vyayādvāmaṃ sthitaḥ pāpo haret saumyaśca taddalam  

ekabhe tu bahuṣveko haretsvāṃśāṃ balī grahaḥ 
nā'tra kṣīṇasya candrasya pāpatvaṃ munibhiḥ smṛtam  

lagnāṃśaliptikā hatvā pratyekaṃ vihagāyuṣā 
bhājyā maṇḍalaliptābhirlabdhaṃ varṣādi śodhayet  

svāyuṣo lagnage sūrye maṅgale ca śanaiścare 
tadardhaṃ śubhasaṃdṛṣṭe pātayed dvijasattama  

lagnarāśisamāścābdā bhāgādyairanupātataḥ 
māsādikā itīcchanti lagnāyuḥ ke'pi kovidāḥ  

lagnādāyoṃ'śatulyaḥ syādantare cā'nupātataḥ 
tatpatau balasaṃyukte rāśitulyaṃ ca bhāghipe  

atha vipra nisargāyuḥ kheṭānāṃ kathayāmyaham 
candrārajñasitejyārkaśanīnāṃ kramaśobdakā  

ekadvayaṃkanakhā dhṛtyaḥ kṛtiḥ paṃcāśadeva hi 
janmakālāt kramāj jñeyā daśāścaitā nisargajāḥ  

athāṃśāyu salagnānāṃ kheṭānāṃ kathayāmyaham 
navāṃśrāśitulyāni kheṭo varṣāṇi yacchati  

bhādiṃ khagaṃ khagaiḥ sūryairhatvā tadbhagaṇādikam 
kṛtvā'rkraśeṣitaṃ jñeyamabdādyaṃśāyuṣaḥ sphuṭam  

piṇḍāyuriva tatrāpi hāniṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ 
atrā'paro viśeṣo'pi kaimcid vijñairudāhṛtaḥ  

sādhitāyuḥ khage svocce svarkṣe vā triguṇaṃ smṛtam 
dviguṇaṃ svanavāṃśasthe svadreṣkāṇe tathottame  

ubhayatra gate kheṭe kāryaṃ triguṇameva hi 
hānidvaye'rdhahāniḥ syādityāyuḥ prasphuṭaṃ nṛṇām  

evaṃ saṃsādhya cānyeṣāṃ hanyāt svasvaparāyuṣā 
nṛṇāṃ parāyuṣā bhaktvā teṣāmāyuḥ sphuṭaṃ bhavet  

athāyuḥ paramaṃ vakṣye nānājātisamudbhavam 
anantasaṃkhyaṃ devānāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca dvijottama  

gṛdhrolūkśukadhvāṃkṣasarpāṇāṃ ca sahasrakam 
śyenavānarabhallukamaṇḍūkānāṃ śatatrayam  

paṃcaśaduttaraśataṃ rākṣasānāṃ prakīrtitam 
nagaṇāṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ ca viṃśottaraśataṃ tathā  

dvātriṃśad ghoṭakānāñca paṃcaviṃśat kharoṣṭrayoḥ 
vṛṣāṇāṃ mahiṣāṇāṃ ca caturviṃśativatsaram  

viṃśatyāyurmayūrāṇāṃ chāgādīnāṃ ca ṣoḍaśa 
haṃsānāṃ paṃcanava ca pikānāṃ dvādaśābdakāḥ  

śunāṃ pārāvatānāṃ ca kukkuṭānāṃ dvādaśābdakāḥ 
budbudādyaṇḍajānāṃ ca parāyuḥ saptavatsarāḥ  

yadetadadhunā proktaṃ tridhāyudvijasattama 
teṣu kiñca kadā grāhyamiti te kathayāmyaham  

vilagnape balopete śubhadṛṣṭeṃśśasambhavabh 
ravau piṃḍodbhavaṃ grāhyaṃ candre naisargikaṃ tathā  

balasāmye dvayoryogadalamāyuḥ prakīrtitam 
trayāṇāṃ triyutestryaṃśasamaṃ jñeyaṃ dvijottama  

athā'nyadapi vakṣyāmi śrriṇu tvaṃ dvijasattama 
kaiścillagnāṣṭameśābhyāṃ mandendubhyāṃ tathaiva ca  

lagnahorāvilagnābhyāṃ sphuṭamāyuḥ prakīrtitam 
ādau lagnāṣṭameśābhyāṃ yogamekaṃ vicintayet  

dvitīyaṃ mandacandrābhyāṃ yogaṃ paśyed dvijottama 
lagnahorāvilagnābhyāṃ tṛtīyaṃ paricintayet  

cararāśau sthitau dvau cit tadā dīrghamudāhṛtam 
ekaḥ sthire'paro dvandve dīrghamāyustathāpi hi  

ekaścare sthire'nyaścet tadāmadhyamudāhṛtam 
dvau vā dvandve sthitau vipra madhyamāyustathāpi ca  

ekaścare'paro dvandve dvau vā sthiragatau tadā 
jātakasya tadā'lpāyurjñeyamevaṃ dvijottama  

yogatrayeṇa yogābhyāṃ siddhaṃ yad grāhyameva tat 
yogatrayavisaṃvāde lagnahorāvilagnataḥ  

lagne vā saptame candre grāhyaṃ mandendutastadā 
hrāso vṛddhiśca kakṣyāyā vicintyā sarvadā budhaiḥ  

dīrghe yogatrayeṇaivaṃ nakhacandrasamābdakāḥ 
yogadvayena vasvāśā yogaikena rasāṃkakāḥ  

madhye yogatrayeṇaivaṃ khāṣṭatulyābdakāḥ smṛtāḥ 
dvyagā yogadvayenā'trayogaikenābdhiṣaṇmitāḥ  

alpe yogatrayeṇā'tradvātriṃśanmitavatsarāḥ 
yogadvayena ṣaṭtriṃśāt yogaikena ca khābdhayaḥ  

evaṃ dīrghasamālpeṣu khābdhayo rasavahnayaḥ 
khaṇḍā dantamitāstebhyaḥ sphuṭamāyuḥ prasādhayet  

pūrṇa rāśyādige cānte hānirmadhye'nupātataḥ 
yogakārakakheṭāṃśayogastatsaṃkhyayā hṛtaḥ  

labdhāṃśāstu yathāprāptakhaṇḍaghnāstriṃśatoddhṛtāḥ 
labdhavarṣādibhirhīnaṃ prāptāyuḥ prasphuṭaṃ bhavet  

yogahetau śanau kakṣyāhrāso'nyairvṛddhirucyate 
na svarkṣatuṅgage no vā pāpamātrayutekṣite  

lagnasaptamage jīve śubhamātrayutekṣite 
kathitasyāyuṣo vipra kakṣyāvṛddhiḥ prajāyate  

anāyuśced bhavedalpamalpānmadhyaṃ prajāyate 
madhyamājjāyate dīrghaṃ dīrghāyuścettato'dhikam  

yogahetau guravevaṃ kakṣyāvṛddheśca lakṣaṇam 
etasmād vaiparītyena kakṣyāhrāsaḥ śanau bhavet  

āyuṣo bahudhā bhedāḥ kathitā bhavatā'dhunā 
katidhā sā kadā'nāyuramitāyuḥ kadā bhavet  

bālāriṣṭaṃ yogāriṣṭamalpaṃ madhyañca dīrghakam 
divyaṃ caivā'mitaṃ caivaṃ saptadhāyuḥ prakīrtitam  

bālāriṣṭe samā aṣṭau yogāriṣṭe ca viṃśatiḥ 
dvātriṃśad vatrarā alpe catuṣṣaṣṭistu madhyame  

viṃśādhikaśtaṃ dīrghe divye varṣasahasrakam 
tadūrdhvamamitaṃ puṇyairamitairāpyate janaiḥ  

candrejyau ca kulīrāṃge jnasiatu kendrasaṃsthitau 
anye tryāyārigāḥ kheṭā amitāyustadā bhavet  

saumyāḥ kendratrikoṇasthāḥ pāpāstryāyārigāstathā 
śubharāśau sthite randhre divyamāyustadā bhavet  

gopurāṃśe gurau kendre śukre pārāvatāṃśake 
trikoṇe karkaṭe lagne yugāntāyustadā dvija  

devalokāṃśake mande kuje pārāvatāṃśake 
gurau siṃhāsanāṃśe'ṅge jāto munisamo bhavet  

suyogairvardhyate hyāyuḥ kuyogairhīyate tathā 
ato yogānahaṃ vakṣye pūrṇamadhyālpakārakān  

kendre śubhagrahairyukte lagneśe ca śubhānvite 
sandṛṣṭe guruṇā vā'pi pūrṇamāyuyustadā bhavet  

kendrasthite vilagneśe guruśukrasamanvite 
tābhyāṃ nirīkṣite vā'pi pūrṇamāyurvinirdiśet  

uccasthitaistribhiḥ kheṭairlagnarandhraśasaṃyutaiḥ 
aṣṭame pāpahīne ca pūrṇamāyurvinirdiśet  

aṣṭamasthaistribhi kheṭaiḥ svoccamitrasvavargagaiḥ 
lagneśe balasaṃyukte dīrghamāyustadā bhavet  

svabhoccasthena kenāpi nabhaugena samanvitaḥ 
aṣṭameśaḥ śanirvāpi dīrghamāyurvinirdiśet  

triṣaḍāyagataiḥ pāpaiḥ śubhaiḥ kendratrikoṇagaiḥ 
lagneśe balasaṃyukte dīrghamāyurvinirdiśet  

ṣaṭsaptarandhrabhaveṣu śubhakheṭayuteṣu ca 
tribhaveṣu ca pāpeṣu pūrṇamāyurvinirdiśet  

śatruvyayagatāḥ pāpā lagneśo yadi kendragaḥ 
ravimitraṃ ca randhreśaḥ pūrṇamāyustathāpi hi  

āyuḥ sthānasthitāḥ pāpāḥ karmeśaḥ svoccago yadā 
tathāpi dīrghamāyu syāt vijñeyaṃ dvijasattama  

dvisvabhāvagṛhe lagne lagneśe kendrasaṃsthite 
svoccarāśitrikoṇe vā dīrghamāyurvinirdiśet  

dvisvabhāvagṛhe lagne lagneśād balasaṃyutāt 
dvau pāpau yadi kendrasthau dīrghamāyustadā bhavet  

lagnāṣṭameśayormadhye yaḥ kheṭaḥ prabalo bhavet 
tasmin kendragate dīrgha madhyaṃ paṇapharasthite  

āpoklime sthite svalpamāyurbhavati niścitam 
lagneśe ca ravermitre dīrghaṃmāyuḥ same samam  

śatrau svalpaṃ vadeditthamaṣṭameśādapi smṛtam 
mitramadhyā'ribhāvasthe tasminnevaṃ phalaṃ vadet  

sahajādhīśabhūputrau dvau randhreśaśanaiścarau 
astau vā pāpadṛgyuktau svalpamāyuḥ prayacchataḥ  

ṣaṣṭhe'ṣṭame vyaye vā'pi lagneśe pāpasaṃyute 
sva pāyuranapatyo vā śubhadṛgyogavarjite  

catuṣṭyagate pāpe śubhadṛṣṭivivarjite 
balahīne viglaneśe svalpamāyurvinirdiśet  

vyayārthau pāpasaṃyuktau śubhadṛgyogavarjitau 
svalpamāyustadā jñeyaṃ nirviśaṃkaṃ dvijottama  

lagnarandhreśayorevaṃ duḥsthayorbalahīnayoḥ 
svalpamāyurbudhairjñeyaṃ miśrayogācca madhyamam  

medskiphrulemedskip

            atha mārakabhedādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

bahudhā''yurbhavā yogāḥ kathitā bhavatā'dhunā 
nṛṇāṃ mārakabhedāśca kathyantāṃ kṛpayā mune  

tṛtīyamaṣṭamasthānamāyuḥsthānāṃ dvayaṃ dvija 
mārakaṃ tadvyayasthānaṃ dvitīyaṃ saptamaṃ tathā  

tatrāpi saptamasthānād dvitīyaṃ balavattaram 
tayorīśau tatra gatāḥ pāpinastena saṃyutāḥ  

ye kheṭāḥ pāpinaste ca sarve mārakasaṃjñakāḥ 
teṣāṃ daśāvipākeṣu sambhave nidhanaṃ nṛṇām  

alpamadhyamapūrṇāyuḥ pramāṇamiha yogajam 
vijñāya prathamaṃ puṃsāṃ mārakaṃ paricintayet  

alābhe punareteṣāṃ sambandhena vyayeśituḥ 
kvacicchubhānāṃ ca daśasvaṣṭameśadaśāsu ca  

kevalānāṃ ca pāpānāṃ daśāsu nidhanaṃ kvacit 
alpanīyaṃ budhairnṛṇāṃ mārakāṇāmadarśane  

satyapi svena sambandhe na hanti śubhabhuktiṣu 
hanti satyapyasambandhe mārakaḥ pāpabhuktiṣu  

mārakagrahasambandhānnihantā pāpakṛcchaniḥ 
atikramyetarān sarvān bhavatyatra na saṃśayaḥ  

athā'nyadapi vakṣyāmi dvija mārakalakṣaṇaṃ 
trividhāścāyuṣo yogāḥ svalpāyurmadhyamottamāḥ  

dvāviṃśāt pūrvamalpāyurmadhyamāyustataḥ param 
catuṣṣaṣṭyāḥ purastāt tu tato dīrghamudāhṛtam  

uttamāyuḥ śatādūrdhvaṃ jñātavyaṃ dvijasattama 
janairviṃśativarṣāntyamāyurjñātaṃ na śakyate  

japahomacikitsādyairbālarakṣāṃ hi kārayet 
mriyante pitṛdoṣaiśca kecinmātṛgrahairapi  

kecit svāriṣṭyogācca trividhā bālamṛtyavaḥ 
tataḥ paraṃ nṛṇāmāyurgaṇayed dvijasattama  

athā'nyadapi vakṣyāmi nṛṇāṃ mārakalakṣaṇam 
alpāyuryogajātasya vipbhe ca mṛtirbhavet  

madhyāyuryogajasyaivaṃ pratyarau ca mṛtirbhavet 
dīrghāyuryogajātasya vadhabhe tu mṛtirbhavet  

dvāviṃśatryaṃśapaścaiva tathā vaināśikādhipaḥ 
vipattārāpratyarīśā vadhabheśaṃstathaiva ca  

ādyāntapau ca vijñeyau candrākrāntagṛhād dvija 
mārakau pāpakheṭau tau śubhau cedrogadau smṛtau  

ṣaṣṭhādhipadaśāyāṃ ca nṛṇāṃ nidhanasambhavaḥ 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭariṣphanāthānāmapahāre mṛtirbhavet  

mārakā bahavaḥ kheṭā yadi vīryasamanvitāḥ 
tattaddaśāntare vipra rogakaṣṭādisaṃbhavaḥ  

uktā ye mārakāsteṣu prabalo mukhyamārakaḥ 
tadavasthānusāreṇa mṛtiṃ vā kaṣṭamādiśet  

rahuścedathavā keturlagne kāme'ṣṭame vyaye 
mārakeśānmade vā'pi mārakeśena saṃyutaḥ  

mārakaḥ sa ca vijñeyaḥ svadaśāntardaśāsvapi 
makare vṛścike janma rāhustasya mṛtipradaḥ  

ṣaṣṭhā'ṣṭariṣphago rāhustaddaye kaṣṭado bhavet 
śubhagrahayuto dṛṣṭo na tadā kaṣṭakṛnmataḥ  

lagnāt tṛtīyabhāve tu balinā raviṇā yute 
rājahetuśca maraṇaṃ tasya jñeyaṃ dvijottama  

tritīye cendunā yukte dṛṣṭe vā yakṣmaṇā mṛtiḥ 
kujena vraṇaśastrāgnidāhādyairmaraṇaṃ bhavet  

tṛtīye śanirāhubhyāṃ yukte dṛṣṭe'pi vā dvija 
viṣārtito mṛtirvācyā jalādvā vahnipīḍanāt  

gartāduccāt prapatanād bandhanād vā mṛtirbhavet 
tṛtīye candramāndibhyāṃ yukte vā vīkṣite dvija  

kṛmikuṣṭhādinā tasya maraṇaṃ bhavati dhruvam 
tṛtīye budhasaṃyukte vīkṣite vāpi tena ca  

jvareṇa maraṇaṃ tasya vijñeyaṃ dvijasattama 
tṛtīye guruṇā yukte dṛṣṭe śophādinā mṛtiḥ  

tṛtīye bhṛguyugdṛṣṭe meharogeṇa tanmṛtiḥ 
bahukheṭayute tasmin bahurogabhavā mṛtiḥ  

tṛtīye ca śubhairyukte śubhadeśe mṛtirbhavet 
pāpaiśca kīkaṭe deśe miśrairmiśrasthale mṛtiḥ  

tṛtīye guruśukrābhyāṃ yukte jñānana vai mṛtiḥ 
ajñānenā'nyakheṭaiśca mṛtirjñeyā dvijottama  

cararāśau tṛtīyasthe paradeśe mṛtirbhavet 
sthirarāśau svagehe ca dvisvabhāve pathi dvija  

lagnādaṣṭamabhāvācca nimittaṃ kathitaṃ budhaiḥ 
sūrye'ṣṭame'gnito mṛtyuścandre mṛtyurjalena ca  

śāstrād bhaume jvarāj jñe ca gurau rogāt kṣudhā bhṛgau 
pipāsayā śanau mṛtyurvijñeyo dvijasattama  

aṣṭame śubhadṛgyukte dharmape ca śubhairyute 
tīrthe mṛtistadā jñeyā pāpākhyairanyathā mṛtiḥ  

agnyambumiśratryaṃśairjñeyo mṛtyurgṛhāśritaiḥ 
pariṇāmaḥ śavasyā'tra bhasmasaṃkledaśoṣakaiḥ  

vyālavargadṛkāṇaistu viḍambo bhavati dhruvam 
śavasya śvaśṛgālādyairgṛdhrakākādipakṣibhiḥ  

karkaṭe madhyamo'ntyaśca vṛścikādyadvitīyakau 
mīne'ntimastribhāgaśca vyālavargāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  

raviścandrabalākrāntatryaṃśanāthe gurau janaḥ 
devalokāt samāyāto vijñeyo dvijasattama  

śukrendvoḥ pitṛlokāttu martyācca ravibhaumayoḥ 
budhā''rkyornarakādevaṃ janmakālād vadet sudhiḥ  

guruścandrasitau sūryabhaumau jñārkī yathākramam 
devendubhūmyadholokān nayantyastārirandhragāḥ  

atha tatra grahabhāve randhrāritryaṃśanāthayoḥ 
yo balī sa nijaṃ lokaṃ nayatyante dvijottama  

tasya svoccādi saṃsthityā varamadhyā'dhamāḥ kramāt 
tattalloke'pi sañjātā vijñeyā dvijasattama  

anyān mārakabhedāṃśca rāśigrahakṛtān dvija 
daśādhyāyaprasaṃgeṣu kathayiṣyāmi suvrata  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha grahāvasthādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

avasthāvaśataḥ proktaṃ grahāṇāṃ yat phalaṃ mune 
kā sā'vasthā muniśreṣṭha katidhā ceti kathyayām  

avasthā vividhāḥ santi grahāṇāṃ divajasattama 
sārabhūtāśca yāstāsu bālādyāstā vadāmyaham  

kramād bālaḥ kumāro'tha yuvā vṛddhastathā mṛtaḥ 
ṣaḍaṃśairasame kheṭaḥ same jñeyo viparyayāt  

phalaṃ pādamitaṃ bāle phalārdhaṃ ca kumārake 
yūni pūrṇaṃ phalaṃ jñeyaṃ vṛddhe kiñcit mṛte ca kham  

svabhoccayoḥ samasuhṛdbhayoḥ śatrubhanīcayoḥ 
jāgratsvapnasuṣuptyākhyā avasthā nāmadṛkphalāḥ  

jāgare ca phalaṃ pūrṇaṃ svapne madhyaphalaṃ tathā 
suṣuptau tu phalaṃ śūnyaṃ vijñeyaṃ dvijasattama  

dīptaḥ svasthaḥ pramuditaḥ śānto dīno'tha duḥkhitaḥ 
vikalaśca khalaḥ ko'pītyavasthā navadhā'parāḥ  

svoccasthaḥ khecaro dīptaḥ svarkṣe svastho'dhimitrabhe 
mudito mitrabhe śāntaḥ samabhe dīna ucyate  

śatrubhe duḥkhitaḥ prokto vikalaḥ pāpasaṃyutaḥ 
khalaḥ khalagṛhe jñeyaḥ kopī syādarkasaṃyutaḥ  

yādṛśo janmakāle yaḥ kheṭo yadbhāvago bhavet 
tādṛśaṃ tasya bhāvasya phalamuhyaṃ dvijottama  

lajjito garvitaścaiva kṣudhitastṛṣitastathā 
muditaḥ kṣobhitaścaiva grahabhāvāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  

putragehagataḥ kheṭo rāhuketuyuto'thavā 
ravimandakujairyukto lajjito graha ucyate  

tuṅgasthānagato vā'pi trikoṇe'pi bhavetpunaḥ 
garvitaḥ so'pi gadito nirviśaṃkaṃ dvijottama  

śatrugehī śatruyukto ripudṛṣṭo bhavedyadi 
kṣudhitaḥ sa ca vijñeyaḥ śaniyukto yathā tathā  

jalarāśau sthitaḥ kheṭaḥ śatruṇā cā'valokitaḥ 
śubhagrahā na paśyanti tṛṣitaḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ  

mitragehī mitrayukto mitreṇa ca vilokitaḥ 
guruṇā sahito yaśca muditaḥ sa prakīrtitaḥ  

raviṇā sahito yaśca pāpā paśyanti sarvathā 
kṣobhitaṃ taṃ vijānīyācchatruṇā yadi vīkṣitaḥ  

yeṣu yeṣu ca bhāveṣu grahāstiṣṭhanti sarvathā 
kṣudhitaḥ kṣobhito vāpi tadbhāvaphalanāśanaḥ  

evaṃ krameṇa boddhavyaṃ sarvabhāveṣu paṇḍitaiḥ 
balā'balavicāreṇa vaktavyaḥ phalanirṇayaḥ  

anyonyaṃ ca mudā yuktaṃ phalaṃ miśraṃ vadetpunaḥ 
balahīne tadā hāniḥ sabale ca mahāphalam  

karmasthāne sthito yasya lajjitastṛṣitastathā 
kṣudhitaḥ kṣobhito vāpi sa naro duḥkhabhājanam  

sutasthāne bhavedyasya lajjito graha eva ca 
sutanāśo bhavettasya ekastiṣṭhati sarvadā  

kṣobhitastṛṣitaścaiva saptame yasya vā bhavet 
mriyate tasya nārī ca satyamāhurdvijottama  

navālayārāmasukhaṃ nṛpatvaṃ kalāpaṭutvaṃ vidadhāti puṃsām 
sadārthalābhaṃ vyavahāravṛddhiṃ phalaṃ viśeṣādiha garvitasya  

bhavati muditayoge vāsaśālāviśālā 
vimalavasanabhūṣābhūmiyoṣāsu saukhyam 
svajanajanavilāso bhūmipāgāravāso 
ripunivahavināśo buddhividyāvikāśaḥ  

diśati lajjitabhāvavaśādratiṃ vigatarāmamatiṃ vimatikṣayam 
sutagadāgamanaṃ gamanaṃ vṛthā kalikathābhiruciṃ na ruciṃ śubhe  

saṃkṣobhitasyāpi phalaṃ viśeṣāddridrajātaṃ kumatiṃ ca kaṣṭam 
karoti vittakṣayamaṃdhribādhāṃ dhanāptibādhāmavanīśakopāt  

kṣudhitakhagavaśādvai śokamohādipātaḥ 
parijanaparitāpādādhibhītyā kṛśatvam 
kalirapi ripulokairarthabādhā narāṇā 
makhilabbalanirodho buddhirodho viṣādāt  

tṛṣitakhagabhave svādaṃganāsaṃgamadhye 
bhavati gadavikāro dṛṣṭakāryādhikāraḥ 
nijajanaparivādādarthahāniḥ kṛśatvaṃ 
khalakṛtaparitāpo mānahāniḥ sadaiva  

śayanaṃ copaveśaṃ ca netrapāṇiprakāśanam 
gamanāgamanaṃ cā'tha sabhāyāṃ vasatiṃ tathā  

āgamaṃ bhojanaṃ caiva nṛtyaṃ lipsāṃ ca kautukam 
nidrāṃ grahāṇāṃ ceṣṭāṃ ca kathayāmi tavāgritaḥ  

yasminnṛkṣe bhavetkheṭastena taṃ paripūrayet 
punaraṃśena sampūrya svanakṣatraṃ niyojayet  

yātadaṇḍaṃ tathā lagnamekīkṛtya sadā budhaḥ 
ravibhistu hared bhāgaṃ śeṣaṃ kārye niyojayet  

nākṣatrikadaśārītyā punaḥ pūraṇamācaret 
nāmādyasvarasaṃkhyāḍhyaṃ hartavyaṃ ravibhistataḥ  

ravau pañca tathā deyāścandre dadyāddvayaṃ tathā 
kuje dvayaṃ ca saṃyktaṃ budhe trītri niyojayet  

gurau bāṇāḥ pradeyāśca trayaṃ dadyācca bhārgave 
śanau trayamatho deyaṃ rāhau dadyāccatuṣṭayam  

tribhirbhaktaṃ ca śeṣāṃkaiḥ sā punastribidhā smṛtā 
daṣṭiśceṣṭā viceṣṭā ca tatphalaṃ tathayāmyaham  

dṛṣṭau madhyaphalaṃ jñeyaṃ ceṣṭāyāṃ vipulaṃ phalam 
viceṣṭāyāṃ phalaṃ svalpamevaṃ dṛṣṭiphalaṃ viduḥ  

śubhā'śubhaṃ grahāṇāṃ ca samīkṣyā'tha balā'balam 
tuṅgasthāne viśeṣeṇa balaṃ jñeyaṃ tathā budhaiḥ  

mandāgnirogo bahudhā narāṇāṃ sthūlatvamanṅ ghrerapipittakopaḥ 
vraṇaṃ gude śūlamuraḥpradeśe yadoṣṇabhānuḥ śayanaṃ prayātaḥ  

daridratābhāravihārāśālī vivādavidyābhirato naraḥ syāt 
kathoracittaḥ khalu naṣṭavittaḥ sūryo yadā cedupaveśanasthaḥ  

naraḥ sadānandadharo vivekī paropakārī balavittayuktaḥ 
mahāmukhī rājakṛpābhimānī divādhinātho yadi netrapānau  

udāracittaḥ paripūrṇavittaḥ sabhāsu vaktā bahupuṇyakarttā 
mahābalī sundarararūpaśālī prakāśane janmani padimanīśe  

pravāsaśālī kila duḥkhamālī sadālasī dhīdhanavarjitaśca 
bhayāturaḥ kopaparo viśeṣāddivādhināthe gamane manuṣyaḥ  

paradārarato janatārahito bahudhāgamane gamanābhiruciḥ 
khalatākuśalo malino divasādhipatau manujaḥ kumatiḥ kṛpaṇaḥ  

sabhāgate hite naraḥ paropakāratatparaḥ 
sadārtharatnapūrito divākare guṇākaraḥ 
vasundharānavāṃbarālayānvito mahābalī 
vicitramitravatsalaḥ kṛpākalādharaḥ paraḥ  

kṣobhito ripugaṇaiḥ sadā naraścañcalaḥ khalamatiḥ kṛśastathā 
dharmakarmarahito madoddhataścāgame dinapatau tadā tadā  

sadāṅgasandhivedanāparāṅganādhanakṣayo 
balakṣayaḥ pade pade yadā yadā hi bhojane 
asatyatā śirovyathā tathā vṛthānnabhojanaṃ 
ravāvasattathāratiḥ kumārgagāminī mati  

vijñalokaiḥ sdā maṇḍitaḥ paṇḍitaḥ kāvyavidyānavadyapralāpānvitaḥ 
rājapūjyo dharāmaṇḍale sarvadā nṛtyalipsāgate padminīnāyake  

sarvadānandadhartā jano jñānavān yajñakartā dharādhīśasadmasthitaḥ 
padmabandhāvarāterbhayaṃ svānanaḥ kāvyavidyāpralāpī mudā kautuke  

nidrābharāraktanibhe bhavetāṃ nidrāgate locanapadmayugme 
ravau videśe vasatirjanasya kalatrahāniḥ kātidhārthanāśaḥ  

jānuḥkāle kṣapānāthe śayanaṃ cedupāgate 
mānī śītapradhānaśca kāmī vittavināśakaḥ  

rogārdito mandamatirviśeṣādvittena hīno manujaḥ kaṭhoraḥ 
akāryakārī paravittahārī kṣapākare cedupaveśanasthe  

netrapāṇau kṣapānāthe mahārogī naro bhavet 
analpajalpako dhūrtaḥ kukarmanirataḥ sadā  

yadā rākānāthe gatavati vikāśaṃ ca janane 
vikāśaḥ saṃsāre vimalaguṇarāśeravanipāt 
navāśāmālā syātkarituragalakṣmyā parivṛtā 
vibhūṣā yoṣābhiḥ sukhamanudinaṃ tīrthagamanam  

sitetare pāparato niśākare  viśeṣataḥ krūrakaro naro bhavet 
sadākṣirogaiḥ paripīḍyamāno valakṣapakṣe gamane bhayāturaḥ  

vidhāvāgamage mānī pādarogī naro bhavet 
guptapāparato dīno matitoṣavivarjitaḥ  

sakalajanavadānyo rājarājendramānyo 
ratipatisamākāntiḥ śāntikṛtkāminīnām 
sapadi sadasi yāte cārubimbe śaśaṃke 
bhavati paramarītiprītivijño guṇajñaḥ  

vidhāvāgamake matyoṃ vāvālo dharmapūritaḥ 
kṛṣṇapakṣe dvibhāryaḥ syādrogī duṣṭataro haṭhī  

bhojane januṣi pūrṇacandramā mānayānajanatāsukhaṃ nṛṇām 
ātanoti vanitāsutāsukhaṃ sarvameva na sitetare śubham  

nṛtyalipsāgate candre sabale balavānnaraḥ 
gītajño hi rasajñaśca kṛṣṇe pāpakaro bhavet  

kautakabhavanaṃ gatavati candre bhavati nṛpatvaṃ vā dhanapatvam 
kāmakalāsu sadā kuśalatvaṃ vāravadhūratitamaṇapaṭutvam  

nidrāgate janmani mānavānāṃ kalādhare jīvayute mahattvam 
hīne'ṅganāsañcitavittanāśaḥ śivālaye rauti vicitramuccaiḥ  

śayane vasudhāputre vraṇayukto jano bhavet 
bahunā kaṇḍunā yukto dadruṇā ca viśeṣataḥ  

balī sadā pāparato naraḥ syādasatyavādī nitarāṃ pragalbhaḥ 
dhanena pūrṇo nijadharmahīno dharāsutaścedupaveśanasthaḥ  

yadā bhūmisuto lagne netrapāṇimupāgataḥ 
daridratā tadā puṃsāmanyabhe nagareśatā  

prakāśo guṇasyāpi vāsaḥ prakāśe dharādhīśabhratuḥ sadā mānavṛddhiḥ 
sute bhūsute putrakāntāviyogo bhavedrāhuṇā dāruṇo vā nipātaḥ  

gamane gamanaṃ kurute'nudinaṃ vraṇajālabhayaṃ vanitākalahaḥ 
bahudadrukakaṇḍubhayaṃ bahudhā vasudhātanayo vasuhānikaraḥ  

āgamane guṇaśālī maṇimālīvā karālakaravālī 
gajahantā ripuhantā parijanasantāpahārako bhaume  

tuṅge yuddhakalākalāpakuśalo dharmadhvajo vittapaḥ 
koṇe bhūmisute sabhāmupagate vidyāvihīnaḥ pumān 
ante'patyakalatramitrarahitaḥ proktetarasthānage 
'vaśyaṃ rājasabhābudho bahudhanī mānī ca dānī janaḥ  

āgame bhavati bhūmije jano dharmakarmarahito gadāturaḥ 
karṇamūlaguruśūlarogavāneva kātaramatiḥ kusaṅgamī  

bhojane miṣṭabhojī ca janane sabale kuje 
nīcakarmakaro nityaṃ manujo mānavarjitaḥ  

nṛtyalipsāgate bhūsute janmināmindirārāśirāyāti bhūmīpateḥ 
svarnaratnapravālaiḥ sadā maṇḍitā vāsaśālā narāṇāṃ bhavetsarvadā  

kautukī bhavti kautuke kuje mitraputraparipūrito janaḥ 
uccage nṛpatigehamaṇḍitaḥ pūjito guṇavarairguṇākaraiḥ  

nidrāvasthāṃ gate bhaume krodhī dhīdhanavarjitaḥ 
dhūrto dharmaparibhraṣṭo manuṣyo gadapīḍitaḥ  

kṣudhāturo bhavedaṃge khañjo guñjānibhekṣaṇaḥ 
anyabhe lampaṭo dhūrto manujaḥ śayane budhe  

śaśāṃkaputre januraṇgagehe yadopaveśe guṇarāśipūrṇaḥ 
pāpekṣite pāpayute daridro hite śubhe vittasukhī manuṣyaḥ  

vidyāvivekarahito hitatoṣahīno manī 
janobhavati candrasute'kṣi pāṇau 
putrālaye sutakalatrasukhena hīnaḥ kanyā 
prajā nṛpatigehabudho varārthaḥ  

dātā dayāluḥ khalu puṇyakartā vikāśane candrasute manuṣyaḥ 
anekavidyārṇavapāraṅgatā vivekapūrṇaḥ khalavargahantā  

gamanāgamane bhavato gamane bahudhā vasudhādhipaterbhavane 
bhavanaṃ ca vicitramalaṃ ramayā vidi nuśca januḥsamaye nitarām  

sapadi vidi janānāmuccage janmakāle 
sadasi dhanasamṛddhiḥ sarvadā puṇyavṛddhiḥ 
dhanapatisamatā vā bhūpatā maṃtritā vā 
hariharapadabhaktiḥ sāttvikī muktilabdhiḥ  

āgame januṣi janmināṃ yadā candraje bhavati hīnasevayā 
arthasiddhirapi putrayugmatā bālikā bhavati mānadāyikā  

bhojane candraje janmakāle yadā janminānarthahāniḥ sadā vādataḥ 
rājabhītyā kṛśatvaṃcalatvaṃ materaṅgasaṅgo na jāyā na jāyāsukham  

nṛtyalipsāgate candraje mānavo mānayānapravālavrajaiḥ saṃyutaḥ 
mitraputrapratāpaiḥ sabhāpaṇḍitaḥ pāpabhe vāravāmārato lampaṭaḥ  

kautuke candraje janmakāle nṛṇāmaṃgabhe gītavidyā'navadyā bhavet 
saptame naidhane vāravadhvā ratiḥ puṇyabhe puṇyayuktā matiḥ sadgatiḥ  

nidrāśrite candrasute na nidrāsukhaṃ sadā vyādhisamādhiyogaḥ 
sahotthavaikalyamanalpatāpo nijena vādo dhanamānanāśaḥ  

vacasāmadhipe tu januḥsamaye śayane balavānapi hīnaravaḥ 
atigauratanuḥ khaludīrghahanuḥ sutarāmaribhītiyuto manujaḥ  

upaveśaṃ gatavati yadi jīve vācālo bahugarvaparītaḥ 
kṣoṇīpatiripujanapatirtaptaḥ padajaṃghāsyakaravraṇayuktaḥ  

netrapāṇiṃ gate devarājārcite rogayukto viyukto varārthaśriyā 
gītanṛtyapriyaḥ kāmukaḥ sarvadā gauravarṇo vivarṇodbhavaprītiyuk  

guṇānāmānandaṃ vimalasukhakandaṃ vitanute 
sadā tejaḥpuñjaṃ vrajapatinikuñjaṃ pratigamam 
prakāśaṃ ceducce drutamupagato vāsavaguru 
rgurutvaṃ lokānāṃ dhanapatisamatvaṃ tanubhṛtām  

sāhasī bhavati mānavaḥ sadā mitravargasukhapūrito mudā 
paṇḍito vividhavittamaṇḍito devavidyadi gurau gamaṃ gate  

āgamane janatā varajāyā yasya januḥsamaye harimāyā 
muñcati nālamihālayamaddhā devagurau paritaḥ paribaddhā  

suragurusamavaktā śubhramuktāphalāḍhyaḥ 
sadasi sapadi pūrṇo vittamāṇikyamānaiḥ 
gajaturagarathāḍhyo devatādhīśapūjyo 
januṣi vividhavidyāgarvito mānavaḥ syāt  

nānāvāhanamānayānapaṭalīsaukhyaṃ gurāvāgame 
bhṛtyāpatyakalatramitrajasukhaṃ vidyā'navadyā bhavet 
kṣoṇīpālasamānatānavarataṃ cā'tīva hṛdyā matiḥ 
kāvyānandaratiḥ sadā hinagatiḥ sarvatra mānonnatiḥ  

bhojane bhavati devatāgurau yasya tasya satataṃ subhojanam 
naiva muñcati ramālayaṃ tadā vājivāraṇarathaiśca maṇḍitam  

nṛtyalipsāgate rājamānī dhanī devatādhīśavandyaḥ sadā dharmavit 
tantravijño budhairmaṇḍitaḥ paṃḍitaḥ śabdavidyānavidyo hi sadyo janaḥ  

kutūhalī sakautuke māhādhanī janaḥ sadā 
nijānvaye ca bhāskaraḥ kṛpākalādharaḥ sukhī 
nilimparājapūjite sutena bhūnayena vā 
yuto mahābalī dharādhipendrasadmapaṇḍitaḥ  

gurau nidrāgate yasya mūrkhatā sarvakarmaṇi 
daridratāparikrantaṃ bhavaneṃ puṇyavarjitam  

jano balīyānapidantarogī bhṛgau mahāroṣasamanvitaḥ syāt 
dhanena hīnaḥ śayanaṃ prayāte vārāṃganāsaṃgamalampaṭaśca  

yadi bhaveduśanā upaveśane navamaṇivrajakāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ 
sukhamajasramarikṣaya ādarādavanipādapi mānasamunnatiḥ  

netrapāṇiṃgate lagnagehe kavau saptame mānabhe yasya tasya dhruvam 
netrapāte nipāto dhanānāmalaṃ cānyabhe vāsaśālā viśālā bhavet  

svālaye tuṃgabhe mitrabhe bhārgave tuṃgamātaṃgalīlākalāpī janaḥ 
bhūpatestulya eva prakāśaṃ gate kāvyavidyākalākaitukī gītavit  

gamane janane śukre tasya mātā na jīvati 
ādhiyogo viyogaśca janānāmaribhītitaḥ  

āgamanaṃ bhṛguputre gatavati vitteśvaro manujaḥ 
satterthabhramaśālī nityotsāhī karāṃghrirogī ca  

anāyāsenālaṃ sapadi mahasā yāti sahasā 
pragalbhatvaṃrājñaḥ sadasi guṇavijñaḥ kila kavau 
sabhāyāmāyāte ripunivahahantā dhanapateḥ 
samatvaṃ vā dātā balaturagagantā naravaraḥ  

āgame bhārgave māgamo janmināmartharāśerarāteratīva kṣatiḥ 
putrapāto nipāto janānāmapivyādhibhītiḥ priyābhogahānirbhavet  

kṣudhāturo vyādhinipīḍitaḥ syādanekadhārātibhayardditaśca 
kavau yadā bhojanage yuvatyā mahādhanī paṇḍitamaṇḍitaśca  

kāvyavidyānavadyā ca hṛdyā matiḥ sarvadā nṛtyalipsāgate bhārgave 
śaṃkhavīṇāmṛdaṃgādigānadhvanivrātanaipuṇyametasya vittonnatiḥ  

kautukabhavanaṃ gatavati śukre śakreśatvaṃ sadasi mahattvam 
hṛdyā vidyā bhaviti ca puṃsaḥ padamā nivasati sadamārataḥ  

parasevārato nityaṃ nidrāmupagate kavau 
paranindāparo vīro vācālo bhramate mahīm  

kṣutpipāsāparikrānto viśrāntaḥ śayane śanau 
vayasi prathame rogī tato bhāgyavatāṃ varaḥ  

bhānaoḥ sute cedupaveśanasthe karālakārātijanānutaptāḥ 
apāyuśālī khalu dadrumālī narobhimānī nṛpadaṇḍayuktaḥ  

nayanapāṇigate ravinandane paramayā ramayā ramayāyutaḥ 
nṛpatito hitato mahitoṣakṛdbahukalākalito vimaloktikṛt  

nānāguṇaprāmadhanādhiśālī sadā naro buddhivinodamālī 
prakāśane bhānusute subhānuḥ kṛpānutakto harapādabhaktaḥ  

mahādhanī nandanananditaḥ syādapāyakārī ripubhūmihārī 
game śanau paṇḍitarājābhāvaṃ dharāpaterāyātane prayāti  

āgamane gardabhapadayuktaḥ putrakalatrasukhena vimuktaḥ 
bhānusute bhramate bhuvi nityaṃ dīnamanā vijanāśrayabhāvam  

ratnāvalīkāñcanamauktikānāṃ vrātena nityaṃ vrajati pramodam 
sabhāgate bhānusute nitāntaṃ nayena pūrṇo manujo mahaujāḥ  

āgame gadasamāgamo nṛṇāmabjabandhutanaye yadā tadā 
mandameva gamanaṃ dharāpateryācanāvirahitā matiḥ sadā  

saṃgate januṣi bhānunandane bhojanaṃ bhavati bhojanaṃ rasaiḥ 
saṃyutaṃ nayanamandatā tatā mohatāpaparitāpitā matiḥ  

nṛtyalipsāgate mande dharmātmā vittapūritaḥ 
rājapūjyo naro dhīro mahāvīro raṇāṅgaṇe  

bhavati kautakabhāvamupāgate ravisute vasudhāvasupūritaḥ 
atisukhī sumukhīsukhapūritaḥ kavitayāmalayā kalayānaraḥ  

nidrāgate vāsaranāthaputre dhanī sadā cāruguṇairupetaḥ 
parākramī caṇḍavipakṣahantā suvārakāntāratirītivijñaḥ  

yadāgamo janmani yasya rāhau kleśādhikatvaṃ śayanaṃ prayāte 
vṛṣe'tha yugme'pi ca kanyakāyāmaje samājo dhanadhānyarāśeḥ  

upaveśanamiha gatavati rāhau dadrugadena janaḥ paritaptaḥ 
rājasamājayuto bahumānī vittasukhena sadā rahitaḥ syāt  

netrapāṇāvagau netre bhavato rogapīḍite 
duṣṭavyālāricaurāṇāṃ bhayaṃ tasya dhanakṣayaḥ  

prakāśane śubhāsane sthitiḥ kṛtiḥ śubhā nṛṇāṃ 
dhanonnatirguṇonnatiḥ sadā vidāmagāviha 
dharādhipādhikāritā yaśolatā tatā bhave 
nnavīnanīradākṛtirvideśato mahonnatiḥ  

gamane ca yadā rāhau bahusantānavānnaraḥ 
paṇḍito dhanavān dātā rājapūjyo naro bhavet  

rāhāvāgamane krodhī sadā dhīdhanavarjitaḥ 
kuṭilaḥ kṛpaṇaḥ kāmī naro bhavati sarvathā  

sabhāgato yadā rāhuḥ paṇḍitaḥ kṛpaṇo naraḥ 
nānāguṇaparikrānto vitta saukhyasamanvitaḥ  

cedagāvāgamaṃ yasya yāte tadā vyākulatvaṃ sadārātibhītyā bhayam 
mahadbandhuvādo janānāṃ nipāto bhavedvittahāniḥ śaṭhatvaṃ kṛśatvaṃ  

bhojane bhojanenālaṃ vikalo manujo bhavet 
mandabuddhiḥ kriyābhīruḥ strīputrasukhavarjitaḥ  

nṛtyalipsāgate rāhau mahāvyādhivivarddhanam 
netrarogī riporbhītirdhanadharmakṣayo nṛṇām  

kautuke ca yadā rāhau sthānahīno naro bhavet 
paradārarato nityaṃ paravittāpahārakaḥ  

nidrāvasthāṃ gate rāhau guṇagrāmayuto naraḥ 
kāntāsantānavān dhīro garvito bahuvittavān  

meṣe vṛṣe'tha vā yugme kanyayāṃ śayanaṃ gate 
ketau dhanasamṛddhiḥ syādanyabhe rogavardhanam  

upaveśaṃ gatau ketau dadrurogavivarddhanam 
arivātanṛpavyālacairaśaṃkā samantataḥ  

netrapāṇiṃ gate ketau netrarogaḥ prajāyate 
duṣṭasarpādibhītiśca ripurājakulādapi  

ketau prakāśane saṃjñe dhanavān dhārmikaḥ sadā 
nityaṃ pravāsī cotsāhī sāttviko rājasevakaḥ  

gamecchāyāṃ bhavetketurbahuputro mahādhanaḥ 
paṇḍito guṇavān dātā jāyate ca narottamaḥ  

āgamane ca yadā keturnānārogo dhanakṣayaḥ 
dantaghātī mahārogī piśunaḥ paranindakaḥ  

sabhāvasthāṃ gate ketau vācālo bahugarvitaḥ 
kṛpaṇo lampaṭaścaiva dhūrtaviddyāviśāradaḥ  

yadāgame bhavetketuḥ ketuḥ syātpāpakarmaṇām 
bandhuvādarato duṣṭo ripuroganipīḍitaḥ  

bhojane tu jano nityaṃ kṣudhayā paripīḍitaḥ 
daridro rogasaṃtaptaḥ ketau bhrāmati medinīm  

nṛtyalipsāṅgate ketau vyādhinā vikalo bhavet 
budbudākṣo durāgharṣo dhūrto'narthakaro naraḥ  

kautukī kautuke ketau naṭavāmāratipriyaḥ 
sthānabhraṣṭo durācārī daridro bhramate mahīm  

nidrāvasthāṃ gate ketau dhanadhānyasukhaṃ mahat 
nānāguṇavinodena kālo gacchati janminām  

śayane dvija bhāveṣu yatra tiṣṭhanti sadgrahāḥ 
nityaṃ tasya śubhajñānaṃ nirviśaṃkaṃ vadet budhaḥ  

bhojane yeṣu bhāveṣu pāpāstiṣṭhanti sarvathā 
tadā sarvavināśe'pi nā'tra kāryā vicāraṇā  

nidrāyāṃ ca yadā pāpo jāyāsthāne śubhaṃ vadet 
yadi pāpagrahairdṛṣṭo na śubhaṃ ca kadācana  

sutasthāne sthitaḥ pāpo nidrāyāṃ śayane'pi vā 
tadā śubhaṃ vadettasya nā'tra kāryā vicāraṇā  

mṛtyusthānasthitaḥ pāpo nidrāyāṃ śayane'pi vā 
tadā tasyā'pamṛtyuḥ syādrājataḥ paratastathā  

śubhagrahairyadā yuktaḥ śubhairvā yadi vīkṣitaḥ 
tadā tu maraṇaṃ tasya gaṅgādau ca viśeṣataḥ  

karmasthāne yadā pāpaḥ śayane bhojane'pi vā 
tadā karmavipākaḥ syānnānāduḥkhapradāyakaḥ  

daśamastho niśānāthaḥ kautuke ca prakāśane 
tadaiva rājayogaḥ syānnirviśakaṃ dvijottama  

balā'balavicāreṇa jñātavyañca śubhā'śubham 
evaṃ krameṇa boddhavyaṃ sarvābhāveṣu buddhiman
