sarvajño'si maharṣe tvaṃ kṛpayā dīnavatsala 
daśāḥ katividhāḥ santi tanme kathaya tattvataḥ  

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ svayā vipra lokānugrahakāriṇā 
kathayāmi tavāgre'haṃ daśabhedānanekaśaḥ  

daśābahuvidhāstāsu mukhyā viṃśottarī matā 
kaiścidaṣṭottarī kaiścit kathitā ṣoḍaśottarī  

dvādaśābdottarī vipra daśā pañcottarī tathā 
daśā śatasamā tadvat caturāśītivatsarā  

dvisaptatisamā ṣaṣṭisamā ṣaḍtriṃśavatsarā 
nakṣatrādhārikāścetāḥ kathitāḥ pūrvasūribhiḥ  

athā kāladaśā cakradaśā proktā munīśvaraiḥ 
kālacakradaśā cā'yā mānyāsarvadaśāsu yā  

daśā'tha caraparyāyā sthirākhyā ca daśā dvija 
kendrādya ca daśā jñeyā kārakādigrahodbhavā  

brahmagrahāśritarkṣādyā daśā proktā tu kenacit 
māṇḍūkī ca daśā nāma tathā sthūladaśā smṛtā  

yogārdhajadaśā vipra dṛgdaśā ca tataḥ param 
trikoṇākhyā daśā nāma tathā rāśidaśā smṛtā  

pañcasvaradaśā vipra vijñeyā yoginīdaśā 
daśā paiṇḍī tathāṃśī ca naisargikadaśā tathā  

aṣṭavargadaśa sandhyādasā pācakasaṃjñikā 
anyāstārādaśādyāśca na svargāḥ sarvasammatāḥ  

kṛttikātaḥ samārabhya trirāvṛtya daśādhipāḥ 
ācaṃkurāguśabukeśupūrvā vihagāḥ kramāt  

vahnibhājjanmabhaṃ yāvad yā saṃkhyā navataṣṭitā 
śeṣāddaśādhipo jñeyastamārabhya daśāṃ nayet  

viṃśottaraśataṃ pūrṇamāyuḥ pūrvamudāhṛtam 
kalai viṃśottarī tasmād daśā mukhyā dvijottama  

daśāsamāḥ kramādeṣāṃ ṣaḍ daśā'śvā gajendavaḥ 
nṛpālā navacandrāśca navacandrā nagā nakhāḥ  

daśāmanāṃ bhayātaghnaṃ bhabhogena hṛtaṃ phalam 
daśāyā bhuktavarṣādya bhogyaṃ mānād viśodhitam  

lagneśāt kendrakoṇasthe rāhau lagnaṃ vinā sthite 
aṣṭottarī daśā vipra vijñeyā raudrabhāditaḥ  

catuṣkaṃ tritayaṃ tasmāt catuṣkaṃ tritayaṃ punaḥ 
evaṃ svajanmabhaṃ yāvad vigaṇayya yathākramam  

sūryaścandraḥ kujaḥ saumyaḥ śanirjīvastamo bhṛguḥ 
ete daśādhipā vipra jñeyāḥ ketuṃ vinā grahāḥ  

rasāḥ pañcendavo nāgāḥ saptacandrāśca khendavaḥ 
go'bjāḥ sūryāḥ kunetrāśca ravyādīnāṃ daśāsamāḥ  

daśābdāṃghriśca pāpānāṃ śubhānāṃ tryaṃśa eva hi 
ekaikabhe daśāmānaṃ vijñeyaṃ dvijasattama  

tatastadyātabhogādhyāṃ bhuktaṃ bhogyaṃ ca sādhayet 
viṃśottarīvadevātra tatastatphalamādiśet  

kṛṣṇapakṣe divā janma śuklapakṣe tathā niśi 
tadā hyaṣṭottarī cintyā phalārthañca viśeṣataḥ  

candrahorāgate kṛṣṇe sūryahorāgate sitee 
lagne nṛṇāṃ phalajñaptyai vicintyā ṣoḍaśottarī  

puṣyabhājjanmabhaṃ yāvad yā saṃkhyā gajataṣṭitā 
ravirbhaumo gururmandaḥ ketuścandro budho bhṛguḥ  

iti kramād daśādhīśāḥ jñeyā rāhuṃ vinā grahāḥ 
rudrādyekottarāḥ saṃkhyā dhṛtyantaṃ vatsarāḥ kramāt  

śukrāṃśake prajātasya vicintyā dvādaśottarī 
janmabhāt pauṣṇabhaṃ yāvat saṃkhyā hi vasutaṣṭitā  

sūryo guruḥ śikhī jño'guḥ kujo mando niśākaraḥ 
vinā śukraṃ daśādhīśā dvicayāt saptataḥ samāḥ  

arkāṃśa karkalagne pañcottarī matā 
mitrarkṣājjanmabhaṃ yāvat saṃkhyā saptavibhājitā  

ekādiśeṣe vijñyāḥ kramātsaptadaśādhipāḥ 
ravirjño'rkasuto bhaumaḥ śukraścandro vṛhaspatiḥ  

ekottarācca vijñeyā dvādaśādyāḥ kramātsamāḥ 
dhṛtyantāḥ saptakheṭānāṃ rāhuketū vinā dvija  

vargottamagate lagne daśā cintyā śatābdikā 
pauṣṇbhājjanmaparyantaṃ gaṇayet saptabhirbhajet  

śeṣāṅke ravito jñeyā daśā śatasamāhvayā 
raviścandro bhṛgurjñaśca jīvo bhaumaḥ śanistathā  

kramadete daśādhīśā bāṇā bāṇā diśo daśa 
nakhā nakhāḥ kharāmāśca samājñeyā dvijottama  

karmeśe karmage jñeyā caturāśītikā daśā 
pavanājjanmabhaṃ yāvad yā saṇkhyā saptabhājitā  

śeṣe ravīndubhaumajñā guruśukraśanaiścarāḥ 
daśādhīśāḥ kramādeṣāṃ jñeyā dvādaśavatsarāḥ  

mūlājjanmarkṣaparyantaṃ gaṇayedaṣṭabhirbhajet 
śeṣāddaśādhīpā jneyā aṣṭau ravyādayaḥ kramāt  

nava varṣāṇi sarveṣāṃ viketūnāṃ nabhaḥsadām 
lagneśe saptame yasya lagne vā saptamādhipe  

cintanīyā daśā tasya dvisaptatisamāhvayā 
viṃśottarīvadatrā'pi bhuktaṃ bhogyaṃ ca sādhayet  

yadārko lagnarāśisthaścintyā ṣaṣṭisamā tadā 
dāsrāt trayaṃ catuṣkaṃ ca trayaṃ ceti punaḥ punaḥ  

gurvarkabhūsutānāṃ ca daśā daśa daśābdakāḥ 
tataḥ śaśijñaśukrārkaputrāgūnāṃ rasābdakāḥ  

śravaṇājjanmabhaṃ yāvat saṃkhyā vasuvibhājitā 
śeṣe candraravījyārabudhārkibhṛgurāhavaḥ  

kramāddaśādhipāsteṣāmekādyekottarāḥ samā 
lagne dine'rkahorāyāṃ candrahorāgate niśi  

sūryasyā'rdhāstayaḥ pūrvaṃ parastādūdayādapi 
pañca pañca ghaṭī sandhyā daśanāḍī prakīrtitā  

sandhyādvayañca viṃśatyā nāḍikābhiḥ prakīrtitam 
dinasya viṃśatirghaṭyaḥ pūrṇasaṃjñā udāhṛtāḥ  

niśāyāḥ mugdhasaṃjñāśca ghaṭikā viṃśatiśca yāḥ 
sūryodaye ca yā sandhyā khaṇḍākhyā dasanāḍikā  

astakāle ca yā sandhyā sudhākhyā daśanāḍikā 
pūrṇamugdhaghaṭīmāne dviguṇe tithibhirbhajet  

tathā khaṇḍasudhāghaṭyau caturghne tithibhirbhajet 
labdhaṃ varṣādikaṃ mānaṃ sūryādīnāṃ khacāriṇām  

ekādisaṃkhyayā nighnaṃ daśāmānaṃ pṛthak kramāt 
rāhuketuyutānāṃ ca navānāṃ kālasaṃjñakam  

rātrau lagnāśritādrāśerdine lagneśvarāśritām 
sandhyāyāṃ vittabhāvasthānneyā cakradaśā budhaiḥ  

daśā varṣāṇi rāśīnāmekaikasya daśāmitiḥ 
kramāccakrasthitānāñca vijñātavyā dvijottama  

athā'haṃ śaṅkaraṃ natvā kālacakradaśāṃ bruve 
pārvatyai kathitā pūrvaṃ sādaraṃ yā pinākinā  

tasyāḥ sāraṃ samuddhṛtya tavāgre dvijamandana 
śubhā'śubhaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ yathā jānanti paṇḍitāḥ  

dvādaśāraṃ likheccakraṃ tiryagūrghvasamānakam 
gṛhā dvādaśa jāyante savye'savye dvidhā dvija  

dvitīyādiṣu koṣṭheṣu rāśīn meṣādikān likhet 
evaṃ dvādaśarāśyākhyaṃ kālacakramudīritam  

aśvinyāditrayaṃ savyamārge cakre vyavasthitam 
rohiṇyāditrayaṃ caivamapasavye vyavisthitam  

evamṛkṣavibhāgaṃ hi kṛtvā cakraṃ samuddharet 
aśvinyaditihastakṣemūlaproṣṭhapadābhidhāḥ  

vahnivātādiviśvarkṣarevatyaḥ savyatārakāḥ 
etaddaśoṣupādānāmaśvinyādau ca vīkṣayet  

dehajīvau kathaṃ vīkṣyau nakṣatrāṇāṃ padeṣu ca 
viśadaṃ tatprakāraṃ ca maitreya kathayāmayaham  

dehajīvau meṣacāpau dāsrādyacaraṇasya ca 
meṣādyāścāpaparyantaṃ rāśipāśca daśādhipāḥ  

mṛgayugme dehajīvau dvitīyacaraṇe smṛtau 
kramāt mithunaparyantaṃ rāśipāśca daśādhipāḥ  

dāsrādidaśatārāṇāṃ tṛtīyacaraṇe dvija 
gaurdeho mithunaṃ jīvo dvyekārkeśadaśāṅkapāḥ  

kvakṣirāmarkṣanāthāśca daśādhipatayaḥ kramāt 
aśvinyādidaśauḍūnāṃ caturthacaraṇe tathā  

karkamīnau dehajīvau karkādinavarāśipāḥ 
daśādhīśāśca vijñeyā navaite dvijasattama  

yamejyacitrātoyarkṣā'hīrbudhnyāḥ savyatārakāḥ 
etatpañcoḍupādānāṃ bharaṇyādau vicintayet  

yāmyaprathamapādasya dehajīvāvalirjhaṣaḥ 
nāgāgartupayodhīṣurāmākṣīndvarkabheśvarāḥ  

yāmyadvitīyapādasya dehajīvau ghaṭāṅgane 
rudradiṅnandacandrākṣirāmābdhīṣvaṅgabheśvarāḥ  

yāmyatṛtīyapādasya dehajīvau tulāṅgane 
saptāṣṭāṅkadigīśārkagajādriramabheśvarāḥ  

karko deho dhanurjīvo yāmyaturyapade dvija 
vedabāṇāgninetrendusūryeśāśāṅkabheśvarāḥ  

saptamevaṃ vijānīyādasavyaṃ kathayāmyaham 
dvādaśārāṃ likheccakaṃ pūrvavad dvijasattama  

dvitīyādiṣu koṣṭheṣu vṛścikād vyastamālikheet 
rohiṇī ca maghā dvīśaḥ karṇaśceti catuṣṭayam  

uktaṃ cā'savyanākṣatraṃ pūrvācāryairdvijottama 
etadvedoḍupādānāṃ rohinīvannirīkṣayet  

rohiṇyādipade dehajīvau karkidhanurdharau 
navadigrudrasūryendunetrāgnoṣvabdhibheśvarāḥ  

dhātṛdvitīcaraṇe dehajīvau tulastriyau 
aṅkāgavasusūryeśadigaṅkavasujūkapāḥ  

tṛtīyacaraṇe brāhma deehajīvau ghaṭāṅgane 
ṣaḍbāṇabdhiguṇakṣīndunandadigrudrabheśvarāḥ  

rohiṇyantapade dehajīvāvalijaṣau smṛtau 
sūryendudviguṇeṣvabdhitarkaśailāṣṭabheśvarāḥ  

cāndraraudrabhagāryamṇamitrenduvasuvāruṇam 
etattārāṣṭakaṃ vijñairvijñeyaṃ cāndravat kramāt  

karko deho jhaṣo jīvo mṛgādyacaraṇe dvija 
vyastānmīnādikarkāntarāśipāśca daśādhipāḥ  

gaurdeho mithunaṃ jīvo dvitīyacaraṇe mṛge 
tridvyekāṅkadiśīśārkacandrākṣibhavanādhipāḥ  

dehajīvau nakrayugme tṛtīyacaraṇe mṛge 
tribāṇābdhirasāgāṣṭasūryeśadaśabheśvarāḥ  

meṣo deho dhanurjīvo caturthacaraṇe mṛge 
vyastāccāpādimeṣāntarāśipāśca daśādhipāḥ  

apasavyagaṇe tvevaṃ dehajīvadaśādikam 
pārvatyai śambhunā proktamidāvīṃkathitaṃ mayā  

keṣāṃ ca kati varṣāṇi daśeśānāṃ mahāmune 
daśāyā bhuktabhogyādyaṃ tadārambha pracakṣva me  

bhūtaikaviṃśagirayo navadikṣoḍaśābdhayaḥ 
sūryādīnāṃ daśābdhāḥ syū rāśīnāṃ svāmino vaśāt  

narasya janmakāle vā praśnakāle yadaṃśakaḥ 
tadādinavarāśināmabdāstasyāyurucyate  

sampūrṇāyurbhavedādāvardhamaṃśasya madhyake 
aṃśānte paramaṃ kaṣṭamityāhurapare budhāḥ  

jñātvaivaṃ sphuṭasiddhāntaṃ rāśyaṃśaṃ gaṇayed budhaḥ 
anupātena vakṣyāmi tadupāyamataḥ param  

gatatārāstribhirbhaktāḥ śeṣaṃ caiva caturguṇam 
vartamānapadenāḍhyaṃ rāśīnāmaṃśako bhavet  

meṣe śataṃ vṛṣe'kṣāṣṭau mithune trigajāḥ samāḥ 
karkaṭe'ṅgagajāḥ proktāstāvantastattrikoṇayoḥ  

jano yatrāṃśake jāto gatanāḍīpalādibhiḥ 
tadāṃśasya hatāḥ svābdāḥ pañcabhūmivibhājitāḥ  

evaṃ mahādaśārambho bhavedaṃśādyathā kramāt 
gaṇayennavaparyantaṃ tattadāyuḥ prakīrtitam  

padasya bhuktaghaṭyādyaiḥ svābdamānaṃ hataṃ tataḥ 
bhabhogāṃghrihṛtaṃ bhuktaṃ bhogyaṃ mānād viśodhitam  

candrāṅkāṃśakalā bhuktāḥ svābdamānahatā hṛtāḥ 
dviśatyā bhuktavarṣādyaṃ jñeyaṃ bhogyaṃ tato budhaiḥ  

savyākhye prathamāṃśo yaḥ sa deha iti kathyate 
antyāṃśo jīvasaṃjñaḥ syād vilomamapasavyake  

dehādiṃ gaṇayet savye jīvādimapasavyake 
evaṃ vijñāya daivajñastatastatphalamādiśet  

kālacakragatiḥ proktā tridhā pūrvamaharṣibhiḥ 
maṇḍūkākhyā gatiścaikā markaṭīsaṃjñakā'parā  

siṃhāvalokanākhyā ca tṛtīyā parikīrtitā 
utplutya gamanaṃ vijñā maṇḍūkākhyaṃ pracakṣate  

pṛṣṭhato gamanaṃ nāma markaṭīsaṃjñakaṃ tathā 
vāṇācca navaparyantaṃ gatiḥ siṃhāvalokanam  

kanyākarkaṭayoḥ siṃhayugmayormaṇḍūykī gatiḥ 
karkakesariṇorevaṃ kathyate markaṭīṃ gatiḥ  

mīnavṛścikayoścāpameṣayoḥ saiṃhikī gatiḥ 
iti sañcintya vijñeyaṃ kālacakradaśāphalam  

maṇḍūkagatikāle hi savye bandhujane bhayam 
pitrorvā viṣaśastrāgnijvaracorādijaṃ bhayam  

kesarīyugmamaṇḍūke māturmaraṇmādiśet 
svamṛtiṃ rājabhitiṃ vā sannipātabhayaṃ bhavet  

markaṭīgamane savye dhanadhānyapaśukṣayaḥ 
piturmaraṇamālasyaṃ tatsamānāṃ ca va mṛtiḥ  

savye siṃhāvaloke tu paśubhītirbhavennṛṇām 
suhṛtsnehādināśaśca samānajanapīḍanam  

patanaṃ vāpi kūpādau viṣaśasrtāgnijaṃ bhayam 
vāhanāt patanaṃ vāpi jvarārtiḥ sthānanāśanam  

maṇḍūkagamane vāme strīsutādiprapīḍanam 
jvaraṃ ca śvāpadād bhītiṃ vaded vijñaḥ padacyutim  

markaṭīgamane vā'pi jalabhītiṃ padacyutim 
piturnāśaṃ nṛpakrodhaṃ durgāraṇyāṭanaṃ vadet  

siṃhāvalokane vāme padabhraṃśaḥ piturmṛtiḥ 
tatsamānamṛtirvā'pi phalamevaṃ vicintayet  

mīnāt tu vṛścike yāte jvaro bhavati niścitaḥ 
kanyātaḥ karkaṭe yāte bhrātṛbandhuvināśanam  

siṃhāttu mithune yāte striyā vyādhirbhaved dhruvam 
karkaṭācca harau yāte vadho bhavati dehinām  

pitṛbandhumṛtiṃ vidyāccāpānmeṣe gate punaḥ 
bhayaṃ pāpakhagairyukte śubhakheṭayute śubham  

śubhaṃ vā'pyaśubhaṃ vā'pi kālacakradaśāphalam 
rāśidikbhāgato vāpi pūrvādidigtabhaścarāt  

taddigāvabhāge vaktavyaṃ taddaśāsamaye nṛṇām 
yathopadeśamārgeṇa sarveṣāṃ dvijasattama  

kanyātaḥ karkaṭe yāte pūrvabhāge mahatphalam 
uttaraṃ deśamāśritya śubhā yātrā bhaviṣyati  

siṃhāttu mithune yāte pūrvabhāgaṃ vivarjayet 
kāryānte'pi ca naiṛtyāṃ sukhaṃ yātrā bhaviṣyati  

karkaṭāt siṃhabhe yāte kāryahāniśca dakṣiṇe 
dakṣiṇāṃ diśamāśritya pratyagāgamanaṃ bhavet  

mīnāttu vṛścike yāte udag gacchati saṅkaṭam 
cāpācca makare yāte saṅkaṭaṃ jāyate dhruvam  

cāpānmeṣe tu yātrāyāṃ vyādhirbandho mṛtirbhavet 
vṛścike tu sukhaṃ sampat strīprāptiśca dvijottama  

siṃhācca karkaṭe yāte pascimāṃ varjayeddiśam 
śubhayoge śubhaṃ brūyādaśubhe tvaśubhaṃ phalam  

śūraścauraśca meṣāṃśe lakṣmīvāṃśca vṛṣāṃśake 
mithunāṃśe bhavejjñānī karkāṃśe nṛpatirbhavet  

siṃhāṃśe rājamānyaśca kanyāṃśe paṇḍito bhavet 
tulāṃśe rājamantrī syād vṛścikāṃśe ca nirdhanaḥ  

cāpāṃśe jñānasampanno marakāṃśe ca pāpakṛt 
kumbhāṃśe ca vaṇikkarmā mīnāṃśe dhanadhānyavān  

deho jīvo'thavā yukto ravibhaumārkirāhubhiḥ 
ekaikayoge mṛtyuḥ syād bahuyoge tu kā kathā  

krūrairyukte tanau rogaṃ jīve yukte mahad bhayam 
ādhī rogo bhaved dvābhyāmapamṛtyusrtibhirbhavet  

caturbhirmṛtimāpanno dehe jīve'śubhairyute 
yugapaddehajīvau ca krūragrahayutau tadā  

rājacorādibhītiśca mṛtiścāpi na saṃśayaḥ 
vahnivādhā ravau jñeyā kṣīṇendau ca jalād bhayam  

kuje śastrakṛtā pīḍā vāyuvādhā budhe bhavet 
gulmavādhā śanau jñeyā rāhau ketau viṣād bhayam  

dehajīvagṛhe yāto budho jīvo'thavā bhṛguḥ 
sukhasmpatkarāḥ sarve rogaśokavināśanāḥ  

miśragṛhaiśca saṃyukte miśraṃ phalamavāpnuyāt 
pāpakṣetradaśākāle dehajīvau tu duḥkhitau 
śubhakṣetradaśākāle śubhaṃ bhavati niścitam  

śubhayuktāśubhakṣetradaśā miśraphalā smṛtā 
krūrayuktaśubhakṣetradaśā miśraphalā tathā  

janānāṃ janmakāle tu yo rāśistanubhāvagaḥ 
tasya cakradaśākāle dehārogyaṃ sukhaṃ mahat  

śubhe pūrṇasukhaṃ pāpe dehe rogādisambhavaḥ 
svoccādigatakheṭāḍhye rājyamānadhanāptayaḥ  

dhanabhāve ca yo rāśistasya cakradaśā yadā 
tadā subhojanam putrastrisukhaṃ ca dhanāptayaḥ  

vidyāptirvākpaṭutvaṃ ca sugoṣṭhyā kālayāpanam 
śubharkṣe phalamevaṃ syāt pāpabhe phalamanyathā  

tṛtīyabhāvarāśestu kālacakradaśā yadā 
tadā bhrātṛsukhaṃ śauryaṃ dhairyaṃ cāpi mahatsukham  

svarṇābharaṇavastrāptiḥ sammānaṃ rājasaṃsadi 
śubharkṣe phalamevaṃ syāt pāparkṣe phalamanyathā  

sukhabhāvagatarkṣasya kālacakradaśā yadā 
tadā bandhusukhaṃ bhūmigṛharājyasukhāptayaḥ  

ārogyamarthalābhaśca vastravāhanajaṃ sukham 
śubharkṣe śobhanaṃ jñeyaṃ pāpabhe phalamanyathā  

sutabhāvagatarkṣasya kālacakradaśā yadā 
sutastrīrājyasaukhyāptirārogyaṃ mitrasaṃgamaḥ  

vidyābuddhiyaśolābho dhairyaṃ ca vikramodayaḥ 
śubharāśau śubhaṃ pūrṇaṃ pāparkṣe phalamanyathā  

ripubhāvagatarkṣasya kālacakradaśā yadā 
tadā corādibhūpāgniviṣaśastrabhayaṃ mahat  

pramehagulmapaṇḍvādirogāṇāmapi saṃbhavaḥ 
pāparkṣe phalamevaṃ syāt śubharkṣe miśramādiśet  

jāyābhāvagatarkṣasya kālacakradaśā yadā 
tadā pāṇigrahaḥ patnīputralābhādikaṃ sukham  

kṛṣiyodhanavastrāptirnṛpapūjā mahadyaśaḥ 
śubharāśau phalaṃ pūrṇaṃ pāparāśau ca taddalam  

mṛtyubhāvasthitarkṣasya kālacakradaśā tadā 
sthānanāśaṃ mahad duḥkhaṃ bandhunāśaṃ dhanakṣayam  

dāridryamannavidvopamaribhītiṃ ca nirdiśet 
pāparāśau phalaṃ pūrṇaṃ śubharāśau ca taddalam  

dharmabhāvagatarkṣasya kālacakradaśā yadā 
tadā putrakalatrārthakṛṣigehasukhaṃ vadet  

satkarmadharmasaṃsiddhiṃ mahajjanaparigraham 
śubharāśau śubhaṃ pūrṇaṃ pāparāśau ca taddalam  

karmabhāvagatarkṣasya kālacakradaśā yadā 
rājyāptirbhūpasammānaṃ putradārādijaṃ sukham  

satkarmaphalamaiśvaryaṃ sadgoṣṭhyā kālayāpanam 
śubharāśau phalaṃ pūrṇaṃ pāparāśau ca miśritam  

lābhabhāvasthitarkṣasya kālacakradaśā yadā 
putrastrībandhusaukhyāptirbhūpaprītirmahatsukham  

dhanavastrāptirārogyaṃ satāṃ saṅgaśca jāyate 
śubharāśau phalaṃ pūrṇaṃ pāparāśau ca khaṇḍitam  

vyayabhāvagatarkṣasya kālacakradaśā tadā 
udyogabhaṅgamālasyaṃ dehapīḍāṃ padacyutim  

dāridyaṃ karmavaiphalyaṃ tathā vyarthavyayaṃ vadet 
pāparāśau phalaṃ tvevaṃ śubharāśau ca taddalam  

lagnādivyayaparyantaṃ bhānāṃ caradaśāṃ bruve 
tasmāt tadīśaparyantaṃ saṃkhyāmatra daśāṃ viduḥ  

meṣāditritribhairjñeyaṃ padamojapade kramāt 
daśābdānayane kāryā gaṇanā vyutkramāt same  

vṛścikādhipatī dvau ca ketubhaumau smṛtau dvija 
śanirāhu ca kumbhasya svāminau parikīrtito  

dvināthakṣetrayoratra kriyate nirṇayo'dhunā 
dvāvevādhipatī vipra yuktau svarkṣe sthitau yadi  

varṣa dvādaśakaṃ tatra na cedekādi cintayet 
ekaḥ svakṣetrayo'nyastu paratra yadi saṃsthitaḥ  

tadā'nyatra sthitaṃ nāthaṃ parigṛhya daśāṃ nayet 
dvāvapyanyarkṣagau tau cet tamormadhye ca yo balī  

tata eva daśā grāhyā kramād votkramato dvijaḥ 
balasyā'tra vicāre syādagrahāt sagraho balī  

dvāveva sagrahau tau cet balī tatrādhikagrahaḥ 
grahayogasamānatve jñeyaṃ rāśibalād balam  

jñeyāścarasthiradvandvāḥ kramato balaśālinaḥ 
rāśisattvasamānatve bahuvarṣo balī bhaved  

ekaḥ svoccagataścā'nyaḥ paratra yadi saṃsthitaḥ 
gṛhṇīyāduccakheṭasthaṃ rāśimanyaṃ vihāya vai  

uccakheṭasya sadbhāve varṣamekaṃ ca nikṣipet 
tathaiva nīcakheṭasya varṣamekaṃ viśodhayet  

evaṃ sarvaṃ samālocya jātakasya phalaṃ vadet  

kramādutkramato vā'pi dharmabhāvapadakramāt 
lagnarāśiṃ samārabhya vijñaścaradaśāṃ nayet  

athā'haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sthirasaṃjñāṃ daśāṃ dvija 
care sapta sthire cā'ṣṭau dvandve nava samāḥ smṛtāḥ  

sthiratvācca daśābdānāṃ sthirākhyeti nigadyate 
brahmakheṭāśritarkṣādirdaśeyaṃ parivartate  

yo'sau brahmagrahaḥ proktaḥ kathaṃ sa jñāyate mune 
iti spaṣṭataraṃ brūhi kṛpā'sti yadi te mayi  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭavyayanātheṣu yo balī viṣamarkṣagaḥ 
pṛṣṭhasthito bhaved brahmāṃ balino lagnajāyayoḥ  

kārakādaṣṭameśo vā brahmā'pyaṣṭabhāvagaḥ 
śanau pāte ca brahmattve brahmā tatṣaṣṭhakhecaraḥ  

bahavo lakṣaṇakrāntā jñeyasteṣvadhikāṃśakaḥ 
aṃśasāmye balādhikyād vijñeyo brahmakhecaraḥ  

yogārdhe ca daśāmānaṃ dvayoryogārdhasammitam 
lagnasaptamaprāṇyādirdaśeyaṃ ca pravartate  

lagnasaptamayormadhye yo rāśirbalavān bhavet 
tataḥ kendrādisaṃsthānāṃ rāśīnāñca balakramāt  

kārakādapi rāśīnāṃ kheṭānāṃ caivameva hi 
daśābdāścaravajjñeyāḥ kheṭānāṃ ca svabhāvadhi  

dvirāśyadhipakṣeṭasya gaṇyedubhayāvadhi 
ubhayordhika saṃkhyā kārakasya daśā samāḥ  

ātmakārakamārabhya kārakākhyadaśā kramāt 
lagnāt kārakaparyantaṃ saṃkhyāmatra daśāṃ viduḥ  

maṇḍūkāparaparyāyā trikūṭākhyadaśā dvija 
lagnasaptamayormadhye yo rāśirbalavān bhavet  

tataḥ krameṇaujarāśau same neyā tatho'tkramāt 
trikūṭānāṃ ca vijñeyāḥ sthiravacca daśā samāḥ  

niryāṇasya vicārārthaṃ kaiścichūladaśā smṛtā 
lagnasaptamato mṛtyubhayoryo balavān bhavet  

tadādirviṣame vipra kramādutkramataḥ same 
daśābdāḥ sthiravattatra balimārakabhe mṛtiḥ  

janmalagnatrikoṇeṣu yo rāśirbalavān bhavet 
tamārbhya nayed dhīmān cariparyāyavad daśām  

kramādutkramato grāhyaṃ trikoṇaṃ viṣame same 
trikoṇākhyadaśā proktā samā nāthāvasānakāḥ  

lagnād dharmasya taddṛṣṭarāśīnāṃ ca daśāstataḥ 
daśamasya ca taddṛṣṭarāśīnāṃ ca nayet punaḥ  

ekādaśasya taddṛṣṭarāśīnāṃ sthiravat samāḥ 
pravṛttā dṛg vaśādyasmād dṛgdaśeyaṃ tataḥ smṛtā  

care vyutkramato grāhyā dṛgyogyāḥ sthirabhe kramāt 
viṣame kramato dvandve rāśayo vyutkramāt same  

ṛkṣe lagnādirāśīnāṃ daśā rāśidaśā smṛtā 
bhayātaṃ ravibhirnighnaṃ bhabhogavihṛtaṃ phalam  

rāśyādyaṃ lagnarāśyādau yojyaṃ dvādaśaśeṣitam 
tadārabhya kramādoje daśā jñeyotkramāt same  

daśābdā bhuktabhāgaghnā triṃśatā vihṛtāh phalam 
bhuktaṃ varṣādikaṃ jñeyaṃ bhogyaṃ mānād viśodhitam  

akārādīn svarān pañca prathamaṃ vinyaset kramāt 
kādihāntāṃllikhed varṇān svarādho ṅañaṇojjhitān  

tiryak paṃktikrameṇaiva pañcapañcavibhāgataḥ 
na proktā ṅañaṇā varṇā nāmādau santi te nahi  

ced bhavanti tadā jñeyā gajaḍāste yathākramāt 
yatra svare svanāmādyavarṇaḥ syāt tatsvarādayaḥ  

kramāt paṃca daśādhīśāḥ dvādaśadvādaśābdakāḥ 
svarāṇāṃ ca kramājjñeyāḥ daśāsvantardaśādayaḥ  

pūrvameva mayā proktā varṇadākhyā daśā dvija 
idānīṃ śambhunā proktā kathyate yoginī daśā  

maṅgalā piṅgalā dhanyā bhrāmarī bhadrikā tathā 
ulkā siddhā saṃkaṭā ca yoginyo'ṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ  

maṅgalāto'bhavaccandraḥ piṅgalāto divākaraḥ 
dhanyāto devapūjyo'bhūd bhrāmarīto'bhavat kujaḥ  

bhardikāto budho jātastatholkātaḥ śanaiścaraḥ 
siddhāto bhārgavi jātaḥ saṃkaṭātastamo'bhavad  

janmarkṣa ca tribhiryuktaṃ vasubhirbhāgamāharet 
ekādiśeṣe vijñeyā yoginyoḥ maṅgalādikāḥ  

ekādyekottarā jñeyāḥ kramādāsāṃ daśāsamāḥ 
nakṣatrayātabhogābhyāṃ bhuktaṃ bhogyaṃ ca sādhayet  

yeṣāṃ yadāyuḥ saṃproktaṃ paiṇḍamāṃśaṃ nisargajam 
takṣat teṣāṃ daśā jñeyā paiṇḍī cāṃśī nisargajā  

balī lagnārkacandrāṇāṃ yattasya prathamā daśā 
tatkendrādigatānāṃ ca jñeyā balavaśāttataḥ  

aṣṭavargabalenaiṣāṃ phalāni paricintayet 
aṣṭavargadaśāścaitāḥ kathitāḥ pūrvasūribhiḥ  

parāyurdvādaśo bhāgastasya sandhyā prakīrtitā 
tanmitā lagnabhādīnāṃ kramāt sandhyādaśā smṛtā  

sandhyā rasaguṇā kāryā candravahnihṛtā phalam 
saṃsthāpyaṃ prathame koṣṭhe tadardhaṃ triṣu vinyaset  

tribhāgaṃ vasukoṣṭheṣu vinyasya tatphalaṃ vadet 
evaṃ dvādaśabhāveṣu pācakāni prakalpayet  

viṃśattaridaśevā'tra kaiścit tārādaśā smṛtā 
āśaṃkurāguśabukeśvādisthāneṣu tārakāḥ  

anmasampatvipatkṣemapratyariḥ sādhako badhaḥ 
maitraṃ paramamaitraṃ ca kendrasthabalino grahāt  

jñeyā tārādaśā vipra nāmatulyaphalapradā 
yasya kendre sthitaḥ kheṭo daśeyaṃ tasya kīrtitā  

iti te kathitā vipra daśa bhedā anekadhā 
etadantardaśābhedān kathayiṣyāmi cāgrataḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

            atha daśāphalādyāyaḥ  

medskip

śrutāśca bahudhā bhedā daśānāṃ ca mayā mune 
phalaṃ ca kīdṛśaṃ tāsāṃ kṛpayā me taducyatām  

sādhāraṇaṃ viśiṣṭañca daśānāṃ dvividhaṃ phalam 
grahāṇāṃ ca svabhāvena sthānasthitivaśena ca  

grahavīryānusāreṇa phalaṃ jñeyaṃ daśāsu ca 
ādyadreṣkāṇage kheṭe daśārambhe phalaṃ vadet  

daśāmadhye phalaṃ vācyaṃ madhyadreṣkāṇage khage 
ante phalaṃ tṛtīyasthe vyastaṃ kheṭe ca vakrage  

daśārambhe daśādīśe lagnage śubhadṛgyute 
svocce svabhe svamaitre vā śubhaṃ tasya daśāphalam  

ṣaṣṭhā'ṣṭamavyayasthe ca nīcāstaripubhasthite 
aśubhaṃ tatphalaṃ cā'tha bruve sarvadaśāphalam  

mūlatrikoṇe svakṣetre svocce vā paramoccage 
kendratrikoṇalābhasthe bhāgyakarmādhipairyute  

sūrye balasamāyukte nijavargabalairyute 
tasmindāye mahat saukhyaṃ dhanalābhādikaṃ śubham  

atyantaṃ rājasanmānamaśvāṃdolyādikaṃ śubham 
sutādhipasamāyukte putralābhaṃ ca vindati  

dhaneśasya ca sambandhe gajāntaiśvaryamādiśet 
vāhanādhipasambandhe vāhanātrayalābhakṛt  

nṛpalatuṣṭirvittāḍhyaḥ senādhīśaḥ sukhī naraḥ 
vastravāhanalābhaśca daśāyāṃ balino raveḥ  

nīce ṣaḍaṣṭake  riḥphe durbale pāpasaṃyute 
rāhuketusamāyukte duhsthānādhipasaṃyute  

tasmindāye mahāpīḍā dhanadhānyavināśakṛta 
rājakopaḥ pravāsaśca rājadaṇḍo dhanakṣayaḥ  

jvarapīḍā yaśohānirbandhumitravirodhakṛta 
pitṛkṣayabhayaṃ caiva gṛhe tvaśubhameva ca  

pitṛvarge manastāpaṃ jandveṣaṃ ca vindati 
śubhadṛṣṭiyute sūrye madhye tasmin kvacitsukham 
pāpagrheṇa sandṛṣṭe vadetpāpaphalaṃ budhaḥ  

evaṃ sūryaphalaṃ vipra saṃkṣepāduditaṃ mayā 
viṃśottarīmatenātha bruve candradaśāphalam  

svocce svakṣetrage caiva kendre lābhatrikoṇage 
śubhagraheṇa saṃyukte pūrṇe candrebalairyute  

karmabhāgyādhipairyukte vāhaneśabalairyute 
ādyantaiśvaryasaubhāgyadhanadhānyādilābhakṛta  

gṛhe tu śubhakāryāṇi vāhanaṃ rājadarśanam 
yatnakāryārthasiddhiḥ syād gṛhe lakṣmīkaṭākṣakṛt  

mitraprabhuvaśādbhāgyaṃ rājyalābhaṃ mahatsukham 
aśvāndolyādilābhaṃ ca śvetavastrādikaṃ labhet  

putralābhādisantoṣaṃ gṛhagodhanasaṃkulam 
dhanasthānagate candre tuṅge svakṣetrage'pi vā  

anekadhanalābhaṃ ca bhāgyavṛddhirmahatsukham 
nikṣeparājasanmānaṃ vidyālābhaṃ ca vindati  

nīce vā kṣīṇacandre vā dhanahānirbhaviṣyati 
duścikye balasaṃyukte kvacitsaukhyaṃ kvaciddhanam  

durbale pāpasaṃyukte dehajāḍyaṃ manorujam 
bhṛtyapīḍā vittahānirmātṛvargajanādvadhaḥ  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye candre durbale pāpasaṃyute 
rājadveṣo manoduḥkhaṃ dhanadhānyādināśanam  

mātṛkleṣaṃ manastāpaṃ dehajāḍyaṃ manorujam 
duḥsthe candre balairyukte kvacillābhaṃ kvacitsukham 
dehajāḍyaṃ kvaciccaiva śāntyā tatra śubhaṃ diśet  

svabhoccādigatasyaivaṃ nīcaśatrubhagasya ca 
bravīmi bhūmipurtasya śubhā'śubhadaśāphalam  

paramoccagate bhaume svocce mūlatrikoṇage 
svarkṣe kendratrikoṇe vā lābhe vā dhanage'pi vā  

sampūrṇabalasaṃyukte śubhadṛṣṭe śubhāṃśake 
rājyalābhaṃ bhūmilābhaṃ dhanadhānyādilābhakṛt  

ādhikyaṃ rājasammānaṃ vāhanāmbarabhūṣaṇam 
videśe sthānalābhaṃ ca sodarāṇāṃ sukhaṃ labhet  

kendre gate sadā bhaume duścikye balasaṃyute 
parākramādvittalābho yuddhe śatrujayo bhavet  

kalatraputravibhavaṃ rājasammānameva ca 
daśādau sukhamāpnoti daśānte kaṣṭamādiśet  

nīcādiduṣṭabhāvasthe bhaume balavivarjite 
pāpayukte pāpadṛṣṭe sā daśā neṣṭadāyikā  

evaṃ rāhośca ketośca kathayāmi gṛhādikam 
tayordaśāphalajñaptyai tavā'gre dvijanandana  

rāhostu vṛṣabhaṃ ketorvṛścikaṃ tuṅgasaṃjñakam 
mūlatrikoṇakaṃ jñeyaṃ yugmaṃ cāpaṃ krameṇa ca  

kumbhālī ca gṛhau proktau kanyāmīnau ca kenacit 
taddāye bahusaukhyaṃ ca dhanadhānyādisampadām  

mitrprabhuvaśādiṣṭaṃ vāhanaṃ putrasambhavaḥ 
navīnagṛhanirmāṇaṃ dharmacintā mahotsavaḥ  

videśarājasanmānaṃ vastrālaṅkārabhūṣaṇam 
śubhayukte śubhairdṛṣṭe yogakārakasaṃyute  

kendratrikooṇalābhe vā duścikye śubharāśige 
mahārājaprasādena sarvasampatsukhāvaham  

yavanaprabhusanmānaṃ grhe kalyāṇasambhavam 
randhre vā vyayage rāhau taddāye kaṣṭamādiśet  

pāpagraheṇa sambandhe mārakagrhasaṃyute 
nīcarāśigate vāpi sthānabhraṃśo manovyathā  

vināśo dāraputrāṇāṃ kutsitānnaṃ ca bhojanam 
daśādau dehapīḍā ca dhanadhānyaparicyutiḥ  

daśāmadhye tu saukhyaṃ syāt svadeśe dhanalābhakṛt 
daśānte kaṣṭamāpnoti sthānabhraṃśo manovyathā  

yaḥ sarveṣu nābhogeṣu budhairatiśubhaḥ smṛtaḥ 
tasya devendrapūjyasya kathayāmi daśāphalam  

svocce svakṣetrage jīve kendre lābhatrikoṇage 
mūlatrikoṇalābhe vā tuṃgāṃśe svāṃśage'pi vā  

rājyalābhaṃ mahāpauruṣaṃ rājasanmānakīrtanam 
gajavājisamāyuktaṃ devabrāhmaṇapūjanam  

dāraputrādisaukhyaṃ ca vāhanāṃbaralābhajam 
yajñādikarmasiddhiḥ syādvedāntaśravaṇādikam  

mahārājaprasādenā'bhīṣṭasiddhiḥ sukhāvahā 
āndolikādilābhaśca kalyāṇaṃ ca mahatsukham  

putradārādilābhaśca annadānaṃ mahatpriyam 
nīcāstapāpasaṃyukte jīvai riṣphāṣṭasaṃyute  

sthānabhraṃśaṃ manastāpaṃ putrapīḍāmahadbhayam 
paśvādidhanahāniśca tīrthayātrādikaṃ labhet  

ādau kaṣṭaphalaṃ caiva catuṣpājjīvalābhakṛt 
madhyānte sukhamāpnoti rājasammānavaibhavam  

atha sarveṣu kheṭeṣu yo'tihīnaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
tasya bhāskaraputrasya kathayāmi daśāphalam  

svocce svakṣetrage mande mitrakṣetre'tha vā yadi 
mūlatrikoṇe bhāgye vā tuṃgāṃśe svāṃśage'pi vā  

duścikye lābhage caiva rājasammānavaibhavam 
satkīrtirdhanalābhaśca vidyāvādavinodakṛt  

mahārājaprasādena gajavāhanabhūṣaṇam 
rājayogaṃ prakurvīta senādhīśānmahatsukham  

lakṣmīkaṭākṣacihnāni rājyalābhaṃ karoti ca 
gṛhe kalyāṇasampattirdāraputrādilābhakṛt  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye mande nīce vā'staṅgate'pi vā 
viṣaśastrādipīḍā ca sthābhraṃśaṃ mahadbhayam  

pitṛmātṛviyogaṃ ca dāraputrādipīḍanam 
rājavaisḥamyakāryāṇi hyaniṣṭaṃ bandhanaṃ tathā  

śubhayuktekṣite mande yogakārakasaṃyute 
kendratrikoṇalābhe vā mīnage kārmuke śanau  

rājyalābhaṃ mahotsāhaṃ gajaśvāmbarasaṃkulam  

atha sarvanabhogeṣu yaḥ kumāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
tasya tāreśaputrasya kathayāmi daśāphalam   

svocce svakṣetrasaṃyukte kendralābhatrikoṇage 
mitrakṣetrasamāyukte saumye dāye mahatsukham  

dhanadhānyādilābhaṃ ca satkīrtidhanasampadām 
jñānādhikyaṃ nṛpaprītiṃ satkarmaguṇavarddhanam  

putradārādisaukhyaṃ ca dehārogyaṃ mahatsukham 
kṣīreṇa bhojanaṃ saukhyaṃ vyāpārāllabhate dhanam  

śubhadṛṣṭiyute saumye bhāgye karmādhipe daśā 
ādhipatye balavatī sampūrṇphaladādikā  

pāpagrahayute dṛṣṭe rājadveṣaṃ manorujam 
bandhujanavirodhaṃ ca videśagamanaṃ labhet  

parapreṣyaṃ ca kalahaṃ mūrtakṛrcchānmahanbhayam 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye saumye lābhabhogārthanāśanam  

vātapīḍāṃ dhanaṃ caivaṃ pāṇḍurogaṃ vinirdiśet 
nṛpacaurāgnibhītiṃ ca kṛṣigobhūmināśanam  

daśādau dhanadhānyaṃ ca vidyālābhaṃ mahatsukham 
putrakalyāṇasampattiḥ sanmārge dhanalābhakṛt  

madhye narendrasanmānamante duḥkhaṃ bhaviṣyati  

yastamograhayormadhye kabandhaḥ kathyate budhaiḥ 
tasya ketoridānīṃ te katheyāmi daśāphalam  

kendre lābhe trikoṇe va śubharāśau śubhekṣite 
svocce vā śubhavarge vā rājaprītiṃ manonugam  

deśāgrāmādhipatyaṃ ca vāhanaṃ putrasambhavam 
deśāntaraprayāṇaṃ ca nirdiśet tat sukhāvaham  

putradārasukhaṃ caiva catuṣpājjīvalābhakṛt 
duścikye ṣaṣṭhalābhe vā keturdāye sukhaṃ diśet  

rājyaṃ karoti mitrāṃśaṃ gajavājisamanvitam 
daśadau rājayogaśca daśāmadhye mahadbhayam  

ante dūrāṭanaṃ caiva dehaviśramaṇaṃ tathā 
dhane randhre vyaye ketau pāpadṛṣṭiyutekṣite  

nigaḍaṃ bandhunāśaṃ ca sthānabhraṃśaṃ manorujam 
śūdrasaṅgādilābhaṃ ca kurute rogasaṃkulam  

atha bhūteṣu yaḥ śukrā madarūpeṇa tiṣṭhati 
tasya daityagurorvipra kathayāmi daśāphalam  

paramoccagate śukre svocce svakṣetrakendrage 
nṛpā'bhiṣekasamprāptirvāhanā'mbarabhūṣaṇam  

gajāśvapaśulābhaṃ ca nityaṃ miṣṭhānnabhojanam 
akhaṇḍamaṇḍalādhīśārājasanmānavaibhavam  

mṛdaṅgavādyaghoṣaṃ ca gṛhe lakṣmīkaṭākṣakṛt 
trikoṇasthe nije tasmin rājyārthagṛhahasampadaḥ  

vivāhotsavakāryāṇi putrakalyāṇavaibhavam 
senādhipatyaṃ kurute iṣṭabandhusamāganam  

naṣṭarājyāddhanaprāptiṃ gṛhe godhanasaṅgraham 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye śukre nīce vā vyayarāśige  

ātmabandhujanadveṣaṃ dāravargādipīḍanam 
vyavasāyātphlaṃ naṣṭaṃ gomahiṣyādihānikṛt  

dāraputrādipīḍā vā ātmabandhuviyogakṛt 
bhāgyakarmādhipatyena lagnavāhanarāśige  

taddaśāyāṃ mahatsaukhyaṃ deśagrāmādhipālatā 
devālayataḍāgādipuṇyakarmasu saṃgrahaḥ  

annadāne mahatsaukhyaṃ nityaṃ miṣṭhānnabhojanam 
utsāhaḥ kīrtisampattī strīputradhanasampadaḥ  

svabhuktau phalamevaṃ syādbalānyanyāni bhuktiṣu 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehapīḍā bhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ rudraṃ vā tryambakaṃ japet 
svetāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ davyādārogyaṃ ca tato bhavet  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha viśeṣanakṣatradaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

sthānasthitivaśenaivaṃ phalaṃ proktaṃ purātanaiḥ 
mitho bhāveśasambandhātphalāni kathayāmyaham  

lagneśasya gaśākāle satkītirdehajaṃ sukham 
dhaneśasya daśāyāṃ tu kleśo vā mṛtyuto bhayam  

sahajeśadaśākāle jñeyaṃ pāpaphalaṃ nṛṇām 
sukhādhīśadaśāyāṃ tu gṛhabhūmisukhaṃ bhavet  

pañcameśasya pāke ca vidyāptiḥ putrajaṃ sukham 
rogeśasya daśākāle dehapīḍā riporbhayam  

saptameśasya pāke tu strīpīḍā mṛtyuto bhayam 
aṣṭameśadaśākāle mṛtyubhītirdhanakṣatiḥ  

dharmaśasya daśāyāṃ ca bhūrillābho yaśaḥsukham 
daśameśadaśākāle sammānaṃ nṛpasaṃsadi  

lābheśasya daśākāle lābhe bādhā rujobhayam 
vyayeśasya daśā nṛṇāṃ bahukaṣṭapradā dvija  

daśārambhe śubhasthāne sthitasyāpi śubhaṃ phalam 
aśubhasthānagasyaivaṃ śubhasyāpi na śobhanam  

pañcameśena yuktasya karmeśasya daśā śubhā 
navameśena yuktasya karmeśasyātiśabhanā  

pañcameśena yuktasya grahasyāpi daśā śubhā 
tathā dharmapayuktasya daśā paramaśobhanā  

sukheśasahitasyāpi dharmeśasya daśā śubhā 
pañcamasthānagasyāpi māneśasya daśāśubhā  

evaṃ trikoṇanāthānāṃ kendrasthānāṃ daśāḥ śubhāḥ 
tathā koṇasthitānāṃ ca kendreśānāṃ daśāḥ śubhāḥ  

kendreśaḥ koṇabhāvasthaḥ koṇeśaḥ kendrago yadi 
tayordaśāṃ śubhāṃ prāhurjyotiḥśāstravido janāḥ  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyayādhīśā api koṇeśasaṃyutā 
teṣāṃ daśā'pi śubhadā kathitā kālakovidaiḥ  

koṇeśo yadi kemdrasthaḥ kendreśo yadi koṇagaḥ 
tābhyāṃ yuktasya kheṭasya dṛṣṭiyuktasya caitayoḥ  

daśāṃ śubhapradāṃ prāhurvidvāṃso daivacintakāḥ 
lagneśo dharmabhāvastho dharmeśo lagnago yadi  

etayostu daśākāle sukhadharmasamudbhavaḥ 
karmeśo lagnarāśistho lagneśaḥ karmabhāvagaḥ  

tayordaśāvipāke tu rājyalābho bhaveddhruvam 
triṣaḍāyagatānāṃ ca triṣaḍāyādhipairyujam  

śubhānāmapi kheṭānāṃ daśā pāpaphalapradā 
mārakasthānagānāṃ ca mārakeśayujāmapi  

randhrasthānagatānāṃ ca daśā'niṣṭaphalapradā 
evaṃ bhāveśasambandhādūranīyaṃ daśāphalam  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha kālacakradaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

kathayāmyatha viprendra kālacakradaśāphalam 
tatrādau rāśināthānāṃ sūryādīnāṃ phalaṃ bruve  

raktapittādito vyādhiṃ nṛṇāmarkaphalaṃ vadet 
dhanakīrtiprajāvṛddhivastrābharaṇadaḥ śaśī  

jvaramāśu diśet paittyaṃ granthisphoṭaṃ kujastathā 
prajānāṃ ca dhanānāṃ ca sadā vṛddhiṃ budho diśet  

dhanaṃ kīrtiṃ prajāvṛddhiṃ nānābhogaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ 
vidyāvṛddhirvivāhaśca gṛhaṃ dhānyaṃ bhṛgoḥ phalam  

tāpādhikyaṃ mahadduḥkhaṃ bandhunāśaḥ śaneḥ phalam 
evamarkādiyogena vadedrāśidaśāphalam  

meṣe tu raktapīḍā ca vṛṣabhe dhānyavarddhanam 
mithune jñānasampānnaścāndre dhanapatirbhavet  

sūryakṣe śatrubādhā ca kanyā strīṇāṃ ca nāśanaṃ 
tālike rājamantritvaṃ vṛścike maraṇaṃ bhavet  

arthalābho bhaveccāpe meṣasya navabhāgake 
makare pāpakarmāṇi kumbhe vāṇijyameva ca  

mīne sarvārthasiddhiśca vṛścikeṣvagnito bhayam 
taulike rājapūjyaśca kanyāyāṃ śatruvardhanam  

śaśibhe dārasambādhā siṃhe ca tvakṣirogakṛt 
mithune vṛttibādhā syādvṛṣabhasya navāṃśake  

vṛṣabhe tvarthalābhāśca meṣe tu jvararogakṛt 
mīne tu mātulaprītiḥ kumbhe śatrupravarddhanam  

mṛge caurasya sambādhā dhanuṣi śastravardhanam 
meṣe tu śastrasaṃghāto vṛṣabhe kalaho bhavet  

mithune sukhamāpnoti mithunasya navāṃśake 
karkaṭe saṅkaṭaprāptiḥ siṃhe rājaprakopakṛt  

kanyāyāṃ bhrātṛpūjā va taulike priyakṛnnaraḥ 
vṛścike pitṛbādhā syāt cāpe jñānadhanodayaḥ  

makare jalabhītiḥ syāt kumbhe dhānyavivardhanam 
mīne ca sukhasampattiḥ karkaṭasya navāṃśake  

vṛścike kalaḥ pīḍā taulike hyadhikaṃ phalam 
kanyāyāmatilābhaśca śaśāṃke mṛgabādhikā  

siṃhe ca putralābhaśca mithune śatruvarddhanam 
vṛṣeḥ catuṣpadāllābho meṣāṃśe paśuto bhayam 
mīne tu dīrghayātrā syāt siṃhasya navabhāgake  

kumbhe tu dhanalābhaśca makare dravyalābhakṛt 
dhanuṣi bhrātṛsaṃsargo meṣe mātṛvivarddhanam  

vṛṣabhe putravṛddhiḥ syānmithune śatruvarddhanam 
śaśibhe tu striyāṃ prītiḥ siṃhe vyādhivivarddhanam  

kanyāyāṃ putravṛddhiḥ syātkanyāyā navamāṃśake 
tulāyāmarthalābhaśca vṛścike bhrātṛvarddhanam  

cāpe ca tātasaukhyaṃ ca mṛge mātṛvirodhitā 
kumbhe putrārthalābhaśca mīne śatruvirodhitā  

alau jāyāvirodhaśca tule ca jalabādhatā 
kanyāyāṃ dhanavṛddhiḥ syāt tulāyā navabhāgake  

karkaṭe hyarthanāśaśca siṃhe rājavirodhitā 
mithune bhūmilābhaśca vṛṣabhe cā'rthalābhakṛt  

meṣe sarpādibhītiḥ syānmīne caiva jalād bhayam 
kumbhe vyāpārato lābho makare'pi rujo bhayam  

cāpe tu dhanalābhaḥ syād vṛścikasya navāṃśake 
meṣe tu dhanalābhaḥ syād vṛṣe bhūmivivarddhanam  

mithune sarvasiddhiḥ syātkarkaṭe sarvasiddhikṛt 
siṃhe tu pūrvavṛddhiḥ syātkanyāyāṃ kalaho bhavet  

taulike cārthalābhaḥ syād vṛścike roogamāpnuyāt 
cāpe tu sutavṛddhiḥ syāccāpasya navamāṃśake  

makare putralābhaḥ syātkumbhe dhānyavivarddhanam 
mīne kalyāṇamāpnoti vṛścike viṣabādhitā  

taulike tvarthalābhaśca kanyāyāṃ śatruvarddhanam 
śaśibhe sriyamāpnoti siṃhe tu mṛgabādhitā  

mithune vṛkṣabādhā ca mṛgasya navabhāgake 
vṛṣabhe tvarthalābhaśca meṣabhe tvakṣirogakṛt  

mīne tu dīrghayātrā syātkumbhe dhanavivarddhanam 
makare sarvasiddhiḥ syāccāpe śatruvivarddhanam  

meṣe saukhyavināśaśca vṛṣabhe maraṇaṃ bhavet 
yugme kalyāṇamāpnoti kumbhasya navamāṃśake  

karkaṭe dhanavṛddiḥ syāt siṃhe tu rājapūjanam 
kanyāyāmarthalābhastu tulāyāṃ lābhamāpnuyāt  

vṛścike jvaramāpnoti cāpe śatruvivarddhanam 
mṛge jāyāvirodhaśca kumbhe jalavirodhatā  

mīne tu sarvasaubhāgyaṃ mīnasya navabhāgake 
daśāaṃśakrameṇaivaṃ jñātvā sarvaphalaṃ vadet  

krūragrahadaśākāle śāntiṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ 
yat proktaṃ rājayogādau saṃjñādhyāye ca yat phalam  

tatsarvaṃ catrakāle hi subuddhyā yojayed budhaḥ 
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ kālacakradaśāphalam  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha carādidaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

carasthirādisaṃjñā yā daśāḥ proktāḥ purā dvija 
śubhā'śubhaphalaṃ tāsāṃ kathayāmi tavā'grataḥ  

lagnādidvādaśāntānāṃ bhāvānāṃ phalakīrtane 
tattadrāśīśavīryeṇa yathāyogyaṃ prayojayet  

balayukte ca rāśīśe pūrṇaṃ tasya tadā phalam 
phalaṃ madhybale madhyaṃ balahīne viparyayaḥ  

yo yo daśāprado rāśistasya randhratrikoṇake 
pāpakheṭayute vipra taddaśā duḥkhadāyikā  

tṛtīyaṣaṣṭhage pāpe jyādiḥ parikīrtitaḥ 
śubhakheṭayute tatra jāyate ca parājayaḥ  

lābhasthe ca śubhe pāpe lābho bhavati niścitaḥ 
yadā daśāprado rāśiḥ śubhakheṭayuto dvija  

śubhakṣetre hi tadrāśeḥ śubhaṃ jñeyaṃ daśāphalam 
pāpayukte śubhakṣetre pūrvaṃ śubhamasatpare  

pāparkṣe śubhasaṃyukte pūrvaṃ saukhyaṃ tato'śubham 
pāpakṣetre pāpayukte sā daśā sarvadukhadā  

śubhakṣetradaśā rāśau yukte pāpaśubhairdvija  

pūrvaṃ kaṣṭaṃ sukhaṃ paścānnirviśaṅkaṃ prajāyate 
śubhakṣetre śubhaṃ vācyaṃ pāparkṣe tvaśubhaṃ phalam  

dvitīye pañcame saumye rājaprītirjayo dhruvam 
pāpe tatra gate jñeyamaśubhaṃ taddaśāphalam  

caturthe tu śubhaṃ saukhyamārogyaṃ tvaṣṭame śubhe 
dharmavṛddhirgurujanātsaukhyaṃ ca navame śubhe  

viparīte viparyāso miśre miśraṃ prakīrtitam 
pāke bhoge ca pāpāḍhye dehapīḍā manovyathā  

saptame pākabhogābhyāṃ pāpe dārārtirīritā 
caturthe sthānahāniḥ syātpañcame putrapīḍanam  

daśame kīrtihāniḥ syānnavame pitṛpīḍanam 
pākādrudrāgate pāpe pīḍā sarvāpyabādhikā  

uktasthānagate saumye tataḥ saukhyaṃ vinirdiśet 
kendrasthānagate saumye lābhaḥ śatrujapapradaḥ  

janmakālagrahasthityā sagocagagrahairapi 
vicāritaiḥ pravaktavyaṃ tattadrāśidasāphalam  

yaśca rāśiḥ śubhākānto yasya paścācchubhagrahāḥ 
taddaśā śubhadā proktā viparīte viparyayaḥ  

trikoṇarandhrariṣphasthaiḥ śubhapāpaiḥ śubhā'śubham 
taddaśāyāṃ ca vaktavyaṃ phalaṃ daivavidā sadā  

meṣakarkatulānakrarāśīnāṃ ca yathākramam 
bādhā stānāni samproktā kubhagosiṃhavṛścikāḥ  

pākeśākrāntarāśau vā bādhāsthāne śubhetare 
sthite sati mahāśoko bandhanavyasanāmayāḥ  

uccasvarkṣagrhe tasmiñchubhaṃ saukhyaṃ dhanāgamaḥ 
tacchūnyaṃ cedasaukhyaṃ syāttaddaśā na phalapradā  

bādhakavyayaṣaḍarandhre rāhuyukte mahadbhayam 
prasthāne bandhanaprāptī rājapīḍā ripobhayam  

ravyārarāhuśanayo bhuktirāśau sthitā yadi 
tadrāśibhiktau patanaṃ rājakopān mahadbhayam  

bhuktirāśitrikoṇe tu nīcakheṭaḥ sthito yadi 
tadrāśau vā yute nīce pāpe mṛtyubhayaṃ vadet  

bhuktirāśau svatuṅgasthe trikoṇe vāpi khecare 
yadā bhuktidaśā prāptā tadā saukhyaṃ labhennaraḥ  

nagaragrāmanāthatvaṃ putralābhaṃ dhanāgamam 
kalyāṇaṃ bhūribhāgyaṃ ca senapatyaṃ mahonnatam  

pākeśvaro jīvadṛṣṭaḥ śubharāśisthito yadi 
taddaśāyāṃ dhanaprāptirmaṅgalaṃ putrasambhavam  

sitāsitabhayugmāśca sūryasya ripurāśayaḥ 
kaurpitaulighaṭāścendrorbhaumasya ripurāśayaḥ  

ghaṭamīnanṛyultaulikanyā jñasya tataḥ param 
karkamīnālikumbhāśca rāśayo ripavaḥ smṛtāḥ  

vṛṣataulinṛyukkanyārāśayo ripavo guroḥ 
siṃhālikarkacāpāśca śukasya ripurāśayaḥ  

meṣasiṃhadhanuḥkaurpikarkaṭā śaniśatravaḥ 
evaṃ grāhantaradāśāṃ cintayetkovido dvija  

ye rājayogadā ye ca śubhamadhyamatā grahāḥ 
yasmādvā dvitrituryasthāḥ grahāḥ śubhaphalapradāḥ  

taddaśānāṃ śubhaṃ brūyādrājayogādisambhavam 
śubhadvayāntaragataḥ pāpo'pi śubhadaḥ smṛtaḥ  

gatā śubhadaśāmadhyaṃ daśā saumyasya śobhanā 
śubhā yasya trikoṇasthastaddaśāpi śubhapradā  

ārambhānto mitraśubharāśyoryadi phalaṃ śubham 
pratirāśyaivamavdādyaṃ vibhajya tatphalaṃ vadet  

ārambhāttattrikoṇe tu saumye tu śubhabhāvahet 
śubharāśau śubhārambhe daśā syādatiśobhanā  

śubhādirāśau pāpaśceddaśārambhe śubhā smṛtā 
śubhārambhe kathā keti prārambhasya phalaṃ vadet  

ārambhe pāparāśau vā yadīśo durbalo dvija 
nīcādau taddaśādyante vadedbhāgyaviparyayam  

yatra sthito nīcakheṭastrikoṇe vā'tha nīcagaḥ 
tathā rāśīśvare nīce sambandho nīcakheṭakaiḥ  

bhāgyasya viparītatvaṃ karotyeva dvijottama 
dhanadhānyādihāniśca dehe rogabhayaṃ tathā  

rāhoḥ ketośca kumbhādi vṛścikādi catuṣṭayam 
svabhaṃ tatra samārambhastaddaśāyāṃ śubhaṃ bhavet  

yaddaśāyāṃ śubhaṃ brūyātsa cenmārakasaṃsthitaḥ 
yasmin rāśaudaśāntaḥsyāttasmin dṛṣṭe yute'pi vā  

śukreṇa vidhunā vā syādrājakopāddhanakṣayaḥ 
daśāntaścedarikṣetre rāhudṛṣṭayute'pi vā  

idaṃ phalaṃ śaneḥ pāke na vicintyaṃ dvijottama 
daśāprade nakrarāśau na vicintyamidaṃ phalam  

rāhurdaśānte sarvasvanāśo maraṇabandhane 
daśānnirvāsanaṃ vā syātkaṣṭaṃ vā mahadaśnute  

tattrikoṇagate pāpe niścayādduḥkhamādiśet 
evaṃ śubhāśubhaṃ sarvaṃ niścayena vaded budhaḥ  

rāhvādyāśritarāśistu bhavedyadi daśāpradaḥ 
tatra kāle'pi pūrvoktaṃ cintanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ  

dasārambho daśānto vā mārake cenna śobhanam 
tasminneva ca rāhuścannarodho dravyanāśanaḥ  

yatra kvāpi ca bhe rāhau daśārambhe vināśanam 
gṛhabhraṃśaḥ samuddiṣṭo dhane rāhudhanārtikṛt  

candrśukrau dvādaśa cedrājakopo bhaveddhruvam 
bhaumaketū tatra yadi vadho'gnermahatī vyathā  

cendraśukrau dhane vipra yadi rājyaṃ prayacchataḥ 
daśārambhe daśānte ca dvitīyasthamidaṃ phalam  

evamargalabhāvānāṃ phalaṃ vijñaiḥ pradarśitam 
yasya pāpaḥ śubho vā'pi grahastiṣṭhecchubhārgale  

tena draṣṭrekṣite lagnaṃ pābalyāyopakalpyate 
yadi paśyedgrahastanna viparītārgalasthitaḥ  

tadbhāvasya daśāyāstu viparītaphalaṃ bhavet 
saddṛṣṭe'pi śubhaṃ brūyānnirviśaṃkaṃ dvijottama  

yasminbhāve śubhasvāmisambandhastuṅgakhecaraḥ 
syāttadbhāvadaśāyāṃ tu antyaiśvaryamakhaṇḍitam  

yadbhāveśaḥ svārtharāśimadhitiṣṭhati paśyati 
syātadbhāvadaśākāle dhanalābho mahattaraḥ  

yasmādvyayagato yastu taddaśāyāṃ dhanakṣayaḥ 
yasmāttrikoṇagāḥ pāpāstatrātmaśubhanāśanam  

putrahāniḥ pituḥ pīḍā manastāpo mahān bhavet 
yasmāttrikoṇgā riḥpharandhreśārkārasūryajāḥ  

putrapīḍā dravyahānistatra ketvahisaṅgame 
videśabhramaṇaṃ kleśo bhayaṃ caiva pade pade  

tasmātṣaṣṭhāṣṭame krūranīcakheṭādayaḥ sthitāḥ 
rogaśatrunṛpālebhyo muhuḥ pīḍā suduḥsahā  

yasmāccaturthaḥ krūraḥ syādbhūgṛhakṣetranāśanam 
paśuhānistatra bhaume gṛhadāhaḥ pramādakṛt  

śanau hṛdayaśūlaṃ syātsūrye rājaprakopanam 
sarvasvaharaṇaṃ rāhau viṣacaurādijaṃ bhayam  

yasmād daśamabhe rāhuḥ puṇyatīrthāṭanaṃ bhavet 
yasmātkarmāyabhāgyarkṣagataḥ śobhanakhecarāḥ  

vidyārthadharmasatkarmakhyātipauruṣasiddhayaḥ 
yataḥ pañcamakāmārigatāḥ svoccaśubhagrahāḥ  

putradārādisaṃprāptirnṛpapūjā mahttarā 
yasmānputrāyakarmāmbunavalagnādhipāḥ sthitāḥ  

tattadbhāvārthasiddhiḥ syācchreyo yogānusārataḥ 
yasmin gururvā śukrovā śubheśo vāpi saṃsthitaḥ  

kalyāṇaṃ sarvasaṃpattir devabrāhmaṇatarpanam 
yatcaturthe tuṅgakheṭāḥ śubhasvāmī grahaśca vā  

vāhanagrāmalābhaśca paśuvṛddhiśca bhūyasī 
tatra candre ca lābhaḥ syādbahudhānyarasānvitaḥ  

pūrṇe vidhau nidhiprāptirlabhedvā maṇisañjayam 
tatra sukre bhṛdaṅgādivādyagānapuraskṛtaḥ  

āndolikāptirjīve tu kanakāṃdolikā dhruvam 
lagnakarmeśabhāgyeśatuṅgasthaśubhayogataḥ  

sarvotkarṣamahaiśvaryasāmrājyādimahatphalam 
evaṃ tattadbhāvadāyaphalaṃ yatsyādvicintayet  

ekaikoḍudaśā svīyairguṇairaṣṭādaśātmabhi 
bhinnaṃ phalavipākaṃ tu kuryādvai citrasaṃyutam  

paramocce tuṅgamātre tadarvāktaduparyapi 
mūlatrikoṇabhe svarkṣe svādhimitragrahasya bhe  

tatkālasuhṛdo gehe udāsīnasya bhe tathā 
śartorbhe'dhiriporbhe ca nīcāntādūrdhvadeśabhe  

tasmādarvāṅ nīcamātra nīcānte paramāṃśake 
nīcārivarge sakhale svavarge kendrakoṇabhe  

vyavasthitasya kheṭasya samare pīḍitasya ca 
gāḍhapūḍhasya ca daśāpacitiḥ svaguṇaiḥ phalam  

paramoccagato yastu yo'tivīryasamanvitaḥ 
sampūrṇākhyā daśā tasya rājyabhoogyaśubhapradā  

lakṣmīkaṭākṣacihnānāṃ ciravāsagṛhapradā 
tuṅgamātragatasyāpi tathā vīryādhikasya ca  

pūrṇākhyā bahulaiśvaryadāyinyāpi rujapradā 
atinīcagatasyāpi durbalasya grahasya tu  

riktā tvaniṣṭaphaladā vyādhyanarthamṛtipradā 
atyucce'pyatinīcasthe madhyagasyāvarohiṇī  

mitroccabhāvaprāptasya madhyākhyā hyarthadā daśā 
nīcāṃtāduccabhāgāntaṃ bhaṣaṭke madhyagasya ca  

daśā cārohiṇī nīcaripubhāṃśagatasya ca 
adhamākhyā bhayakleśavyādhiduḥkhavivardhinī  

nāmānurūpaphaladāḥ pākakāle daśā imāḥ 
bhāgyeśagurusambandho yogadṛkkendrabhādibhiḥ  

pareṣāmapi dāyeṣu bhagyopakramamunnayet 
jātako yastu phalado bhagyayogaprado'tha yaḥ  

saphalo vakrimādūrdhvamanyānapi ca khecarān 
durbalānasamarthāṃśca phaladāneṣu yāgataḥ  

tāratamyātsusambandhā daśā hyetāḥ phalapradāḥ 
svakendrādijuṣāṃ teṣāṃ pūrṇārddhāṃghrivyavasthayā  

śīrṣodayabhagāḥ svasvadaśādau svaphalapradāḥ 
ubhayodayarāśisthadaśā madhyaphalapradā  

pṛṣṭhodayarkṣagāḥ kheṭāḥ svadaśānte phalapradāḥ 
nisargataśca tatkāle suhṛdāṃ haraṇe śubham  

sampādayettadā kaṣṭaṃ tadviparyayagāminām 
daśeśākrāṃtabhāvarkṣādārabhya dvādaśarkṣakam  

bhaktvā dvādaśarāśīnāṃ daśābhukti prakalpayet 
ekaikarāśeryā tatra suhṛtsvakṣetragāminī  

tasyāṃ rājyādisampattipūrvakaṃ śubhamīrayet 
duḥsthānaripugehasthanīcakrūrayutā ca yā  

tasyāmanarthakalahaṃ rogamṛtyubhayādikam 
bindubhūyastvaśūnyatvavaśāt svīyāṣṭavargake  

vṛddhiṃ hāniṃ ca tadrāśibhāvasya svagṛhātkramāt 
bhāvayojanayā vidyātsutastryādiśubhā'śubham  

dhātvādirāśibhedācca dhātvādigrahayogataḥ 
śubhapāpanaśābhedācchubhapāpayutairapi  

iṣṭāniṣṭasthānabhedāt phalabhedāt samunnayet 
evaṃ sarvagrahāṇāṃ ca svāṃ svāmantardaśāmapi  

svarāśito rāśibhuktiṃ prakalpya phalamīrayet 
antarantardaśāṃ svīyāṃ vibhajyaivaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
