medskiphrulemedskip

          athā'ntardaśādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

daśābdāḥ svasvamānaghnāḥ sarvāyuryogabhājitāḥ 
pṛthagantardaśā evaṃ pratyantaradaśādikāḥ  

ādāvantardaśā pākapatestatkramato'parāḥ 
evaṃ pratyantarādau ca kramo jñeyo vicakṣaṇaiḥ  

bhuktirnavānāṃ tulyā syād vibhājyā navadhā daśā 
ādau daśāpaterbhuktistatkendrādiyujāṃ tataḥ  

vidyāt krameṇa bhuktyaṃśānevaṃ sūkṣmadaśādikam 
balakramāt phalaṃ vijñairvaktavyaṃ pūrvarītitaḥ  

kṛtvā'rkadhā rāśidaśāṃ rāśerbhuktiṃ kramād vadet 
pratyantardaśādyevaṃ kṛtvā tattatphalaṃ vadet  

ādyasaptamayormadhye yo rāśirbalavāṃstataḥ 
oje daśāśraye gaṇyāḥ kramādutkramataḥ same  

atrā'paro viśeṣo'sti bravīmi tamahaṃ dvija 
care'nujjhitamārgaḥ syāt ṣaṣṭhaṣaṣṭhādikāḥ sthire  

ubhaye kaṇṭakāj jñeyā lagnapañcamabhāgyataḥ 
carasthiradvisvabhāveṣvojeṣuḥ prāk kramo mataḥ  

teṣveva triṣu yugmeṣu grāhyaṃ vyutkramato'khilam 
evamullikhito rāśi pākarāśirudīryute  

sa eva bhogarāśiḥ syāt paryāye prathame smṛtaḥ 
ādyād yāvatithaḥ pākaḥ paryāye yatra dṛśyate  

tasmāt tāvatitho bhogaḥ paryāye tatra gṛhyatām 
tadidaṃ caraparyāyasthiraparyāyayordvayoḥ  

trikoṇākhyadaśāyāṃ ca pākabhogaprakalpanam 
pāke bhoge ca pāpāḍhye depapīḍā namovyathā  

piṇḍatrikadaśāyāṃ tu bravimyantardaśāvidhim 
pūrṇa daśāpatirdadyāt tadardhaṃ tena saṃyutaḥ  

trikoṇagastṛtīyāṃśaṃ turyāṃśaścaturasragaḥ 
smaragaḥ saptamaṃ bhāgaṃ bahuṣveko balī grahaḥ  

evaṃ salagnakāḥ kheṭāḥ pācayanti mithaḥ sthitāḥ 
samacchedīkṛtāḥ prāptā aṃsāśchedavivarjitāḥ  

daśābdāḥ pṛthagaṃśaghnā aṃśayogavibhājitāḥ 
antardaśā bhavantyevaṃ tatpratyantardaśādikāḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

       atha viṃśottarīmatena sūryadaśāntardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

svocce svbhe sthitaḥ sūryo lābhe kendre trikoṇake 
svadaśāyāṃ svabhuktau ca dhanadhānyādilābhakṛt  

nīcādyaśubharāśistho viparītaṃ phalaṃ diśet 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe'rke tvapamṛtyubhayaṃ vadet  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ mṛtyuñjayajapaṃ caret 
sūryaprītikarīṃ śāntiṃ kuryādārogyalabdhaye  

sūryasyā'ntargate candre lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
vivāhaṃ śubhakāryaṃ ca dhanadhānyasamṛddhikṛt  

gṛhakṣetrābhivṛddhiṃ ca paśuvāhanasampadām 
tuṅge vā svarkṣage vā'pi dārasaukhyaṃ dhanāgamam  

putralābhasukhaṃ caiva saukhyaṃ rājasamāgamam 
mahārājaprasādena iṣṭasiddhisukhavāham  

kṣīṇe vā pāpasaṃyukte dāraputrādipoḍanam 
vaiṣamyaṃ janasaṃvādaṃ bhṛtyavargavināśanam  

virodhaṃ rājakalahaṃ dhanadhānyapaśukṣayam 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye candre jalabhītiṃ manorujam  

bandhanaṃ rogapīḍāṃ ca sthānavicyutikārakam 
duḥsthānaṃ cāpi cittena dāyādajanavigraham  

nirdiśet kutsitānnaṃ ca caurādinṛpapīḍanam 
mūtrakṛcchādirogaśca dehapīḍā tathā bhavet  

dāyeśāllabhabhāgye ca kendre vā śubhasaṃyute 
bhogabhāgyādisantoṣadāraputrādivarddhanam  

rājyaprāptiṃ mahatsaukhyaṃ sthānaprāptiṃ ca śāśvartām 
viviāhaṃ yajñadīkṣāṃ ca sumālyāmabarabhūṣaṇam  

vāhanaṃ putrapautrādi labhate sukhavarddhanam 
dāyeśādripurandhrasthe vyaye vā balavarjite  

akāle bhojanaṃ caiva deśāddeśaṃ gamiṣyati 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe ca hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati 
śvetāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ gadyācchānti kuryātsukhāptaye  

sūryasyāntargate bhaume svocce svakṣetralābhage 
lagnātkendratrikoṇe vā śubhakāryaṃ samādiśet  

bhūlābhaṃ kṛṣilābhaṃ ca dhanadhānyavivardhanam 
gṛhakṣetrādi lābhaṃ ca raktavastrādilābhakṛt  

lagnādhipena saṃyukte saukhyaṃ rājapriyaṃ vadet 
bhāgyalābhādhipairyukte lābhaścaiva bhaviṣyati  

bahusenādhipatyaṃ ca śatrunāśaṃ manodṛḍham 
ātmabandhusukham caiva bhrātṛvarddhanakaṃ tathā  

dāyeśādvyayarandhrasthe pāpairyukte ca vīkṣite 
ādhipatyabalairhīne krūrabuddhiṃ manorujam  

kārāgṛhe praveśaṃ ca kathayed bandhunāśanam 
bhrāṛvagavirodhaṃ ca karmanāśamathāpi vā  

nīce vā durbale bhaume rājamūlāddhanakṣayaḥ 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehe jāḍyaṃ manorujam  

subrahmajapadānaṃ ca vṛṣotsargaṃ tathaiva ca 
śāntiṃ kurvīta vidyivadāyurārogyasiddhidām  

sūryasyāntargate rāhau lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
ādau dvimāsaparyantaṃ dhananāśo mahadbhayam  

caurādivraṇabhītiśca dāraputrādipīḍanam 
tatparaṃ sukhamāpnoti śubhayukte śubhāṃśake  

dehārogyaṃ manastuṣṭi rājaprītikaraṃ sukham 
lagnādupacaye rāhau yogakārakasaṃyute  

dāyeśācchubharāśisthe rājasanmānamādiśet 
bhāgyavṛddhiṃ yaśolābhaṃ dāraputrādipīḍanam  

putrotsavādisantoṣaṃ gṛhe kalyāṇaśobhanaṃ 
dāyeśādatha riṣphasthe randhre vā balavarjite  

bandhanaṃ sthānanāśaśca kārāgṛhaniveśanam 
caurādivraṇabhītiśca dāraputrādivarddhanam  

catuṣpājjīvanāśaśca gṛhakṣetrādināśanaṃ 
gulmakṣayādirogaśca hyatisārādipīḍanaṃ  

dvisphasthe tathā rāhau tatsthānādhipasaṃyute 
apamṛtyubhayaṃ caiva sarpabhītiśca sambhavet  

durgājapaṃ ca kurvīt chāgadānaṃ samācaret 
kṛṣṇāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyacchāntimāpnotyasaṃśayam  

sūryasyāntargate jīve lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
svocce mitrasya vargasthe vivāhaṃ rājadarśanam  

dhanadhānyādilābha ca putralābhaṃ mahatsukhaṃ 
mahārājaprasādena iṣṭakāryārthalābhakṛt  

brāhmaṇpriyasanmānaṃ priyavastrādilābhakṛt 
bhāgyakarmādhipavaśādrājyalābhaṃ vaded dvija  

naravāhanayogaśca sthānādhikyaṃ mahatsukham 
dāyeśācchubharāśisthe bhāgyavṛddhiḥ sukhāvahā  

dīnadharmakriyāyukto devatārādhanapriyaḥ 
gurubhaktirmanaḥsiddhiḥ puṇyukarmādisaṃgrahaḥ  

rāśeśādripurandhrasthe nīce vā pāpasaṃyute 
dāraputrādipīḍā ca dehapīḍā mahadbhayam  

rājakopaṃ prakurute'bhīṣṭavastuvināśnam 
pāpamūladdravyanāśaṃ dehabhraṣṭaṃ manorujam  

svarṇadānaṃ prakurvīta sveṣṭajāpyaṃ ca kārayet 
gavāṃ kapilavarṇānāṃ dānenārogyamādiśet  

sūryasyāntargate mande lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
śatrunāśo mahatsaukhyaṃ svalpadhānyārthalābhakṛt  

vivāhādisukāryañca gṛhe tasya śubhāvaham 
svocce svakṣetrage mande suhṛdgrahasamanvite  

gṛhe kalyāṇasampattirvivāhādiṣu satkriyā 
rājasanmānakīrtiśca nānāvastradhanāgamam  

dāyeśādatha randhrasthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute 
vātaśūlamahāvyādhijvarātīsārapīḍanam  

bandhanaṃ kāryahāniśca vittanāśo mahadbhayam 
akaśmātkalahaścaiva dāyādajanavigrahaḥ  

bhuktyādau mitrahāniḥsyānmadhye kiñcitsukhāvaham 
ante kleśakaraṃ caiva nīce teṣāṃ tathaiva ca  

pitṛmātṛviyogaśca gamanāgamamaṃ tathā 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu apamṛtyubhayaṃ bhavet  

kṛṣṇāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyānmṛtyuñjayajapaṃ caret 
chāgadānaṃ prakurvīta sarvasampatpradāyakam  

sūryāsyāntargate saumye svocce vā svarkṣage'pi vā 
kendratrikoṇalābhasthe budhe vargabalairyute  

rājyalābho mahotsāho dāraputrādisaukhyakṛt 
mahārajaprasādena vāhanāmbarabhūṣaṇaṃ  

puṇyatīrthaphalāvāptirgṛhe godhanasaṃkulam 
bhāgyalābhādhipairyukte lābhavṛddhikoro bhavet  

bhāgyapaṃcamakarmasthe sanmāno bhavati dhruvam 
sukarmadharmabuddhiśca gurudevadvijārjanam  

dhanadhānyādisaṃyukto vivāhaḥ putrasambhavaḥ 
dāyeśācchubharāśisthe saumyayukte mahatsukham  

vaivāhikaṃ yajñakarma dānadharmajapādikam 
svanāmāṅkitapadyāni nāmadvayamathā'pi vā  

bhojanāmbarabhūṣāptiramareśo bhavennaraḥ 
dāyeśādripurandhrasthe riṣphage nīcage'pi vā  

dehapīḍā manastāpo dāraputrādipīḍanam 
bhuktyādau duḥkhamāpnoti madhye kiñcitsukhāvaham  

ante tu rājabhītiśca gamanāgamanaṃ tathā 
dvitīye dyūnanāthe tu dehajāḍyaṃ jvarādikam  

viṣṇunāmasahasraṃ ca hyannadānaṃ ca kārayet 
rajatapratimādānaṃ kuryādārogyasiddhaye  

sūryasyāntargate ketau dehapīḍā manovyathā 
arthavyayaṃ rājakopaṃ svajanāderupadravam  

lagnādhipena saṃyukte ādau saukhyaṃ dhanāgamam 
madhye tatkleśamāpnoti mṛtavārtāgamaṃ vadet  

athāṣṭamavyaye caivaṃ dāyeśātpāpasaṃyute 
kapoladantarogaśca mūtrakṛrcchasya sambhavaḥ  

sthānavicyutirarthasya mitrahāniḥ piturmṛtiḥ 
videśagamanaṃ caiva śatrupīḍā mahadbhayam  

lagnādupacaye ketau yogakārakasaṃyute 
śubhāṃśe śubhavarge ca śubhakarmaphalodayaḥ  

putradārādisaukhyaṃ ca santoṣaṃ priyavarddhanam 
vicitravastralābhaśca yaśovṛddhiḥ sukhāvahā  

dvitīyādyūnanāthe vā hyapamṛtyubhayaṃ vadet 
durgājapaṃ ca kurvīta chāgadānaṃ sukhāptaye  

sūryasyāntargate śukre trikoṇe kendrage'pi vā 
svocce mitrasvavargasthe'bhīṣṭastrībhogyasampadaḥ  

grāmāntaraprayāṇaṃ ca bhāhmaṇaprabhudarśanam 
rājyalābho mahotsāhaśchatracāmaravaibhavam  

gṛhe kalyāṇasampattirnityaṃ miṣṭhānnabhojanam 
vidrumādiratnalābho muktāvastrādi lābhakṛt  

catuṣpājjīvalābhaḥ syādbahudhānyadhanādikam 
utsāhaḥ kīrtisampattirnaravāhanasampadaḥ  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye śukre dāyeśādbalavarjite 
rājakopo manaḥkleśaḥ putrastrīdhananāśanam  

bhuktyādau madhyamaṃ madhye lābhaḥ śubhakaro bhavet 
ante yaśonāśanaṃ ca sthānabhraṃśamathāpi vā  

bandhudveṣaṃ vaded vāpi svakulādbhoganāśanam 
bhārgave dyūnanāthe tu dehe jāḍyaṃ rujobhayam  

randhrariṣphasamāyukte hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ mṛtyurjayajapaṃ caret  

śvetāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyādrudrajāpyaṃ ca kārayet 
tataḥ śāntibhavāpnoti śaṅkarasya prasādataḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha candrāntardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

svocce svakṣetrage candre trikoṇe lābhage'pi vā 
bhāgyakarmādhipairyukte gajāśvāmbarasaṃkulam  

devatāgurubhaktiśca puṇyaślokādikīrtanam 
rājyalābho mahatsaukhyaṃ yaśovṛddhiḥ sukhāvahā  

pūrṇe candre balaṃ pūrṇaṃ senāpatyaṃ mahatsukham 
pāpayukte'thavā candre nīce vā riṣphaṣaṣṭhage  

atakāle dhananāśaḥ syātsthānacyutirathāpi vā 
dehalasyaṃ manastapo rājamantrivirodhakṛt  

mātṛkleśo manoduḥkhaṃ nigaḍaṃ bandhunāśanam 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu randhrariṣpheśasaṃyute  

dehajāḍyaṃ mahābhaṅgamapamṛtyobhayaṃ vadet 
śvetāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyāt svadaśāntargate vidhau  

candrasyāntargate bhaume lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
saubhāgyaṃ rājasanmānaṃ vastrabharaṇabhūṣaṇam  

yatnāt kāryārthasiddhistu bhaviṣyati na samśayaḥ 
gṛhakṣetrābhivṛddhiśca vyavahāre jayo bhavet  

kāryalābho mahatsaukhyaṃ svocce svakṣetrage phalam 
tathā'ṣṭamavyaye bhaume pāpayukte'tha vā yadi  

dāyaśādaśubhasthāne dehārtiḥ paravīkṣite 
gṛhakṣetrādihāniśca vyavahāre tathā kṣatiḥ  

mṛtyuvargeṣu kalaho bhūpālasya virodhanam 
ātmabandhuviyogaśca nityaṃ niṣṭhurabhāṣaṇam  

dvitīye dyūnanāthe tu randhre randhrādhipo yadā 
tattoṣaparihārārthaṃ brāhmaṇasyā'rcanaṃ caret  

candrasyāntargate rāhau lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
ādau svalphalaṃ jñeyaṃ śatrupīḍā mahadbhayam  

caurāhirājabhītiśca catuṣpājjivapīḍanam 
bandhunāśo mitrahānirmānahānirmanovyathā  

śubhayukte śubhairdṛṣṭe lagnādupacaye'pi vā 
yogakārakasambandhe sarvakāryārthasiddhikṛt  

nairṛtye paścime bhāve kvacitprabhusamāgamaḥ 
vāhanāmabaralābhaśca sveṣṭakāryārthasiddhikṛt  

dāyeśādatha randhrathe vyaye vā balavarjite 
sthānabhraṃśo manodukhaṃ putrakleśo mahadbhayam  

dārapīḍā kvacijjñeyā kvacitsvāṅge rujobhayam 
vṛścikādiviṣādbhītiścaurāhinṛpapīḍanam  

dāyeśātkendrakoṇe va duścikye lābhage'pi vā 
puṇyatīrthaphalāvāptirdevatādarśanaṃ mahat  

paropakārakarmādipuṇyakarmādisaṃprahaḥ 
dvitīyadyūnarāśiathe dehabādhā bhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ rudrajāpyaṃ samācaret 
chāgadānaṃ prakurvīta dehārogyaṃ prajāyate  

candrasyāntargate jīve lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
svagehe lābhage svocce rājyalābho mahotsavaḥ  

vastrā'laṅkārabhūṣāptī rājaprītirdhanāgamaḥ 
iṣṭadevaprasādena garbhādhānādikaṃ phalam  

tathā śobhanakāryāṇi gṛhe lakṣmīḥ kaṭākṣakṛt 
rājāśrayaṃ dhanaṃ bhūmigajavājisamanvitam  

mahārājaprasādena sveṣṭasiddhiḥ sukhāvahā 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye jīve nīca vāstaṅgate yadi  

pāpayukte'śubhaṃ karma guruputrādināśanam 
sthānabhraṃśo manoduḥkhamakasmātkalaho dhruvam  

gṛhakṣetrādināśaśca vāhanāmbaranāśanam 
dāyeśātkendrakoṇe vā duścikye lābhage'pi vā  

bhojanāmbaraparavādilābhaṃ saukhyaṃ karoti ca 
brhātrādisukhasampattiṃ dhairyaṃ vīryaparākramam  

yajñavratavivāhādirājyaśrīdhanasampadaḥ 
dāyeśādripurandhrasthe vyaye vā balavarjite  

karoti kutsinānnaṃ ca videśagamanaṃ tathā 
bhuktyādau śobhanaṃ proktamante kleśakaraṃ bhavet  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe ca hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ śivasāhasrakaṃ japet 
svarṇadānamiti proktaṃ sarvakaṣṭanivārakam  

candrasyāntargate mande lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
svakṣetre svāṃśage caiva mande tuṅgāṃśasaṃyute  

śubhadṛṣṭayute vā'pi lābhe vā balasaṃyute 
putramitrārthasampattiḥ śūdraprabhusamāgamāt  

vyayasāyātphalādhikyaṃ gṛhe kṣetrādivṛddhidam 
putralābhaśca kalyāṇaṃ rājānugrahavaibhavam  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye mande nīce vā dhanage'pi vā 
tadbhuktyādau puṇyatīrthe snānaṃ caiva tu darśanam  

anekajanatrāsaśca śastrapīḍā bhaviṣyati 
dāyeśātkendrarāśisthe trikoṇe balage'pi vā  

kvacitsaukhyaṃ dhanāptiśca dāraputravirodhakṛt 
dvitīyadyūnarandhrasthe dehabādhā bhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ mṛtyuñjayajapaṃ caret 
kṛṣṇāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyāddānemārogyamādiśet  

candrasyāntargate saumye kendralābhatrikoṇage 
svarkṣe nijāṃśake saumye tuṅge vā balasaṃyute  

dhanāgamo rājamānapriyavastrādilābhakṛt 
vidyāvinodasadgoṣṭhī jñānavṛddhiḥ sukhāvahā  

santānaprāptiḥ santoṣo vāṇijyāddhanalābhkṛt 
vāhanacchatrasaṃyuktanānālaṅkāralābhakṛt  

dāyeśātkendrakoṇe vā lābhe vā dhanage'pi vā 
vivāho yajñadīkṣā ca dānadharmaśubhādikam  

rājaprītikaraścaiva vidvajjanasamāgamaḥ 
muktāmaṇipravālāni vāhanāmbarabhūṣaṇam  

ārogyaprītisaukhyaṃ ca somapānādikaṃ sukham 
dāyeśādripurandhrasthe vyaye vā nīcage'pi vā  

tadbhuktau dehabādhā ca kṛrṣigobhūmināśanam 
kārāgṛhapraveśāśca dāraputrādipīḍanam  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu jvarapīḍā mahadbhayam 
chāgadānaṃ prakurvīta viṣṇusāhasrakaṃ japet  

candrasyāntargate ketau kendralābhatrikoṇage 
duścikye balasaṃyukte dhanalābhaṃ mahatsukham  

putradārādisaukhyaṃ ca vidhikarma karoti ca 
bhuktyādau dhanahāniḥ syānmadhyage sukhamāpnuyāt  

dāyeśātkendralābhe vā trikoṇe balasaṃyute 
kvacitphalaṃ daśādau tu dadyāt saukhyaṃ dhanāgamam  

gomahiṣyādilābhaṃ ca bhuktyante cārthanāśanam 
pāpayukte'thavā dṛṣṭe dāyeśādrandhrariḥphage  

śatrutaḥ kāryahāniḥ syādakasmātkalaho dhruvam 
dvitīyadyūnarāśistyhe hyanārogyaṃ mahadbhayam  

mṛtyuñjayajapaṃ kuryāt sarvasampatpradāyakam 
tataḥ śāntimavāpnoti śaṅkarasya prasādataḥ  

candrasyāntargate śukre kendralābhatrikoṇage 
svocce svakṣetrage vāpi rājyalābhaṃ karoti ca  

mahārājaprasādena vāhanāmbarabhūṣaṇam 
catuṣpājjivalābhaḥ syāddāraputrādivardhanam  

nūtanāgāranirmāṇaṃ nityaṃ miṣṭhānnabhojanaṃ 
sugandhapuṣpamālyādiramyastryārogyasampadam  

daśādhipena saṃyukte dehasaukhyaṃ mahatsukham 
satkīrtisukhasampattigṛhakṣetrādivṛddhikṛt  

nīce vā'staṅgate śukre pāpagrahayutekṣite 
bhūnāśaḥ putramitrādināśanaṃ patnināśanam  

catuṣpājjivahāniḥ syādrājadvāre virodhakṛt 
dhanasthānagate śukre svacce svakṣetrasaṃyute  

nidhilābhaṃ mahatsaukhyaṃ bhū lābhaṃ putrasambhavam 
bhāgyalābhādipairyukte bhāgyavṛddhiḥ karotyasau  

mahārājaprasādena sveṣṭasiddhiḥ sukhāvahā 
devabrāhmaṇabhaktiśca muktavidrumalābhakṛt  

dāyaśāllābhage śukre trikoṇe kendrage'pi vā 
gṛhakṣetrābhivṛddhiśca vittalābho mahatsukham  

dāyeśādripurandhrasthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute 
videśavāsaduḥkhārtimṛtyucaurādipīḍanam  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu apamṛtyubhayaṃ bhavet 
taddoṣavinivṛttyarthaṃ rudrajāpyaṃ ca kārayet  

śvetāṃ gāṃ rajataṃ dadyācchantimāpnotyasaṃśayaḥ 
śaṅkarasya prasādena nā'tra kāryā vicāraṇā  

candrasyāntargate bhānau svocce svakṣetrasaṃyute 
kendre trikoṇe lābhe vā dhane vā sodarālaye  

naṣṭarājyadhanaprāptirgṛhe kalyāṇaśobhanam 
mitrarājaprasādena grāmabhūmyādilābhkṛt  

garbhādhānaphalaprāptirgṛhe lakṣmīḥ kaṭākṣakṛt 
bhuktyante deha ālasyaṃ jvarapīḍā bhaviṣyati  

dāyeśādapi randhrasthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute 
nṛpacaurāhibhītiśca jvararogādisambhavaḥ  

videśagamane cārti labhate na saṃśayaḥ 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu jvarapīḍā bhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ śivapūjāṃ ca kārayet 
tataḥ śāntibhavāpnoti śāṅkarasya prasādataḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha kujadaśāntardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

kuje svāntargate vipra lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
lābhe vā śubhasaṃyukte duṣcikye dhanasaṃyute  

lagnādhipena saṃyukte rājā'nugrahavaibhavam 
lakṣmīkaṭokṣacihnāni naṣṭarājyārthalābhakṛt  

putrotsavādisantoṣo gṛhe gokṣīrasaṅkalam 
svocce vā svarkṣage bhaume svāṃśe vā balasaṃyute  

gṛhakṣetrābhivṛddhiśca gomahiṣyādilābhakṛt 
mahārājaprasādena sveṣṭasiddhiḥ sukhāvahā  

athā'ṣṭamavyaye bhaume pāpadṛgyogasaṃyute 
mūtrakṛrcchādirogaśca kaṣṭādhikyaṃ vraṇādbhayam  

caurāhirājapīḍā ca dhanadhānyaparukṣayaḥ 
dvitīye dyūnanāthe tu dehajāḍyaṃ manovyathā  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ rudrajāpyaṃ ca kārayet 
anaḍvāhaṃ pradadvācca kujadoṣanivṛttaye  

tena tuṣṭo bhaved bhaumaḥ śaṅkarasya prasādataḥ 
ārogyaṃ kurute tasya sarvasampattidāyakam  

kujasyāntargate rāhau svocce mūlatrikoṇage 
śubhairyukte śubhairdṛṣṭe kendralābhatṛkoṇage  

tatkāle rājasammānaṃ gṛhabhūmyādilābhakṛt 
kalatraputralābhaḥ syādvyavasāyātphalādhikam  

gaṅgāsnānaphalāvāptiṃ videśagamanaṃ tathā 
tathā'ṣṭamavyaye rāhau pāpayukte'tha vīkṣite  

caurāhivraṇabhītiśca catuṣpājjīvanaśanam 
vātapittarujobhītiḥ kārāgṛhaniveśanam  

dhanasthānagate rāhau dhananāsaṃ mahadbhayam 
saptamasthānage vā'pi hyapamṛtyubhayaṃ mahat  

nāgapūjāṃ prakurvīta devabrāhmaṇabhojanaṃ 
mṛtyuñjayajapaṃ kuryādāyurārogyalabdhaye  

kujasyāntargate jīve trikoṇe kendrage'pi vā 
lābhe vā dhanasaṃyukte tuṅgāṃśe svāṃśagepi vā  

satkīrtī rājasammānaṃ dhanadhānyasya vṛddhikṛt 
gṛhe kalyāṇasampattirdāraputrādilābhakṛt  

dāyeśātkendrarāśisthe trikoṇe lābhage'pi vā 
bhāgyakarmādhipairyukte vāhanādhipasaṃyute  

lagnādhipasamāyukte śubhāṃśe śubhavargage 
gṛhakṣetrābhivṛddhiśca gṛhe kalyāṇasampadaḥ  

dehārogyaṃ mahatkīrtigṛhe gokulasaṃgrahaḥ 
catuṣpājjīvalābhaḥ syādvyavasāyātphalādhikam  

kalaputrasaukhyaṃ ca rājasammānavaibhavam 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye jīve nīce vāstaṃgate sati  

pāpagraheṇa saṃyukte dṛṣṭe vā durbale sati 
caurāhinṛpabhītiśca pittarogādisambhavam  

pretabādhā bhṛtyanāśaḥ sodarāṇāṃ vināśanam 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu hyapamṛtyujvarādikam 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ śivasāhasrakaṃ japet  

kujasyāntargate mande svarkṣe kendratrikoṇage 
mūlatrikoṇakendre vā tuṅgāṃśe svāṃśage sati  

lagnādhipatinā vāpi śubhadṛṣṭiyute'site 
rājyasaukhyaṃ yaśovṛddhiḥ svagrāme dhānyavṛddhikṛt  

putrapautrasamāyukto gṛhe godhanasaṃgrahaḥ 
svavāre rājasammānaṃ svamāse putravṛddhikṛt  

nīcādikṣetrage mande tathā'ṣṭavyayarāśige 
mlecchavargaprabhubhayaṃ dhanadhanyādināśanam  

nigaḍe bandhanaṃ vyādhirante kṣetranāśakṛt 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu pāpayukte mahadbhayam  

dhananāśaśca sañcāre rājadveṣo manovyathā 
caurāgninṛpapīḍā ca sahodaravināśanam  

bandhudveṣaḥ pramādyaiśca jīvahāniśca jāyate 
akasmācca mṛterbhītiḥ putradārādipīḍanam  

kārāgṛhādibhīdiśca rājadaṇḍo mahadbhayam 
dāyeśātkendrarāśisthe lābhasthe vā trikoṇage  

videśayānaṃ labhate duṣkīrtirvividhā tathā 
pāpakarmarato nityaṃ bahujīvādihiṃsakaḥ  

vikrayaḥ kṣetrahāniśca sthānabhraṃśo manovyathā 
raṇe parājayaścaiva mūtrakṛrcchānmahadbhayam  

dāyeśādatha randhre vā vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute 
tadbhuktau maraṇaṃ jñeyaṃ nṛpacaurādipīḍanam  

vātapīḍā ca śūlādijñātiśtrubhayaṃ bhavet  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ mṛtyuñjayajapaṃ caret 
tataḥ sukhamavāpnoti śaṅkarasya prasādataḥ  

kujasyāntargate saumye lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
satkathāścā'japādānaṃ dharmabuddhirmahadyaśaḥ  

nītimārgaprasaṅgaśca nityaṃ miṣṭānnabhojanam 
vāhanāmbarapaśvādirrājakarma sukhāni ca  

kṛṣikarmaphale siddhirvāraṇāmbarabhūṣaṇam 
nīce vāstaṅgate vāpi ṣaṣṭhāṣṭavyayage'pi vā  

hṛdrogaṃ mānahāniśca nigaḍaṃ bandhunāśanam 
dāraputrārthanāśaḥ syāccatuṣpājjīvanāśanam  

daśādhipena saṃyukte śatruvṛddhirmahadbhayam 
videśagamanaṃ caiva nānārogāstathaiva ca  

rājadvāre virodhaśca kalahaḥ svajanairapi 
dāyeśātkendratrikoṇe vā svocce yuktārthalābhakṛt  

anekadhananāthatvaṃ rājasammanameva ca 
bhūpālayogaṃ kurute dhanambaravibhūṣaṇam  

bhūravādyamṛdaṃgādi senāpatyaṃ mahatsukham 
vidyāvinodavimalā vastravāhanabhūṣaṇam  

dāraputrādivibhavaṃ gṛhe lakṣmīḥ kaṭākṣakṛt 
dāyeśātṣaṣṭhariḥphasthe randhre vā pāpasaṃyute  

taddāye mānohāniḥ syātkrūrabuddhistu krūravāk 
caurāgninṛpapīḍā ca mārge dasyubhayādikam  

akasmātkalahaścaiva budhamuktau na saṃśayaḥ 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu mahāvyādhirbhayaṅkaraḥ  

aśvadānaṃ prakurvīta viṣṇornāmasahasrakam 
sarvasampatpradaṃ vipra sarvāriṣṭapraśāntaye  

kujasyāntargate ketau trikoṇe kendrage'pi vā 
diścikye lābhage vā'pi śubhayukte śubhekṣite  

rājānugrahaśāntiśca bahusaukhyaṃ dhanāgamaḥ 
kiñcitphalaṃ daśādau tu bhūlābhaḥ putralābhakṛt  

rājasaṃlābhakāryāṇi catuṣpājjīvalābhakṛt 
yogakārakasaṃsthāne balavīryasamanvite  

putralābho yaśovṛddhirgṛhe lakṣmīḥ kaṭākṣakṛt 
bhṛtyavargadhanaprāptiḥ senāpatyaṃ mahatsukham  

bhūpālamitraṃ kurute yāgāmbarādibhūṣaṇam 
dāyeśātṣaṣṭhariḥphasthe randhre vā pāpasaṃyute  

kalaho dantarogaśca cauravyāghrādipīḍanam 
jvarātisārakuṣṭhādidāraputrādipīḍanam  

dvitīyasaptamasthāne dehe vyādhirbhaviṣyati 
apamānamanastāpo dhanadhānyādipracyutim  

kujasyāntargate śukre kendralābhatrikoṇage 
svocce vā svarkṣage vā'piśubhasthānādhipe'thavā  

rājyalābho mahatsaukhyaṃ gajāśvāmbarabhūṣaṇam 
lagnādhipena sambandhe putradārādivardhanam  

āyuṣo vṛddhiraiśvaryaṃ bhāgyavṛddhisukhaṃ bhavet 
dāyeśātkendrakoṇasthe lābhe vā dhanage'pi vā  

tatkāle śriyamāpnoti putralābhaṃ mahatsukham 
svaprabhośca mahatsaukhyaṃ dhanavastrādilābhakṛt  

mahārajaprasādena grāmabhūmyādilābhadam 
bhuktyante phalamāpnoti gītanṛtyādilābhakṛt  

puṇyatīrthasnānalābhaṃ karmādhipasamanvite 
puṇyadharmadayākūpataḍāgaṃ kārayiṣyati  

dāyeśādrandhrariṣphasthe ṣaṣṭhe vā pāpasaṃyute 
karoti duḥkhabāhulyaṃ dehapīḍāṃ dhanakṣayaṃ  

rājacaurādibhītiñca gṛhe kalahameva ca 
dāraputrādipīḍāṃ ca gomahiṣyādināśakṛt  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehabādhā bhaviṣyati 
śvetāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyādāyurārogyavṛddhaye  

kujasyāntargate sūrye svocce svakṣetrakendrage 
mūlatrikoṇalābhe vā bhāgyakarmeśasaṃyute  

tadbhuktau vāhanaṃ kīrtiṃ putralābhaṃ ca vindati 
dhanadhānyasamṛddhiḥ syād gṛhe kalyāṇasampadaḥ  

kṣemārogyaṃ mahaddhairyaṃ rājapūjyaṃ mahatsukham 
vyavasāyātphalādhikyaṃ videśe rājadarśanam  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭhariṣphe vā vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute 
dehapīḍā manastāpaḥ kāryahānirmahadbhayam  

śirorogo jvarādiśca atisāramathāpi vā 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu sarpajvaraviṣādbhayam  

sutapīḍābhayaṃ caiva śānti kuryādyathāvidhi 
dehārogyaṃ prakurute dhanadhānyacayaṃ tathā  

kujasyāntargate candre svocce svakṣetrakendrage 
bhāryavāhanakarmeśalagnādhipasamanvite  

karoti vipulaṃ rājyaṃ gandhamālyāmbarādikam 
taḍāgaṃ gopurādīnāṃ puṇyadharmādisaṃgraham  

vivāhotsavakarmāṇi dāraputrādisaukhyakṛt 
pitṛmātṛsukhāvāptiṃ gṛhe lakṣmīḥ kaṭākṣakṛt  

mahārajaprasādena sveṣṭasiddhisukhādikam 
pūrṇe candre pūrṇaphalaṃ kṣīṇe svalpaphalṃ bhavet  

nīcāristha'ṣṭame ṣaṣṭhe dāyeśādripurandhrake 
maraṇaṃ dāraputrāṇāṃ kaṣṭaṃ bhūmivināśanam  

paśudhānyakṣayaścaiva caurādiraṇabhītikṛt 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati  

dehajāḍyaṃ manoduḥkhaṃ durgā lakṣmījapaṃ caret 
śvetāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyādanemārogyamādiśet  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha rahvantardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

kulīre vṛścike rāhau kanyatyāṃ cāpage'pi vā 
tadbhukto rājasammānaṃ vastravāhanabhūṣaṇam  

vyavasāyātphalādhikyaṃ catuṣpājjīvalābhakṛt 
prayāṇaṃ paścime bhāge vāhanāmbaralābhakṛt  

lagnādupacaye rāhau śubhagrahayutekṣite 
mitrāṃśe tuṅgabhāgāṃśe yogakārakasaṃyute  

rājyalābhaṃ mahotsāhaṃ rājaprītiṃ śubhāvaham 
karoti sukhasampattiṃ dāraputrādivarddhanam  

lagnāṣṭme vyaye rāhau pāpayukte'tha vīkṣite 
caurādivraṇapīḍā ca sarvatraivaṃ bhaveddvija  

rājadvārajanadveṣa iṣṭabandhuvināśanam 
dāraputrādipīḍā ca bhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe vā saptamasthānamāśrite 
sadā rogo mahākaṣṭaṃ śāntiṃ kuryādyathāvidhi 
ārogyaṃ sampadaścaiva bhaviṣyanti tadā dvija  

rāhurantargate jīve lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
svocce svakṣetrage vāpi tuṅgasvarkṣāṃśage'pi vā  

sthānalābhaṃ manodhairyaṃ śatrunāśaṃ mahatsukham 
rājaprītikaraṃ saukhyaṃ jano'tīva samaśnute  

dinedine vṛddhirapi sitapakṣe śaśī yathā 
vāhanādidhanaṃ bhūri gṛhe godhanasaṃkulam  

nairṛtye paścime bhāge prayāṇaṃ rājadarśanam 
yuktakāryārthasiddhiḥ syātsvadeśe punareṣyati  

upakāro brāhmaṇānāṃ tīrthayātrādikarmaṇām 
vāhanagrāmalābhaśca devabrāhmaṇapūjanam  

putrotsavādisantoṣo nityaṃ miṣṭhānnabhojanam 
nīce vā'staṅgate vāpi ṣaṣṭhāṣṭavyayarāśige  

śatrukṣetre pāpayukte dhanahānirbhaviṣyati 
karmavighno bhavettasya mānahāniśca jāyate  

kalatraputrapīḍā ca hṛdrogo rājakārakṛt 
dāyeśātkendrakoṇe vā lābhe vā dhanage'pi vā  

duścikye balasampūrṇe gṛhakṣetrādivṛddhikṛt 
bhojanāmbarapaśvādidānadharmajapādikam  

bhuktyante rājakopācca dvimāsaṃ dehapīḍanam 
jyeṣṭhabhrāturvināśaśca mātṛpitrādipīḍanam  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭharandhre vā riḥphe vā pāpasaṃyute 
tadbhuktau dhanahāniḥ syāddehapīḍā bhaviṣyati  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe vā hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati 
svarṇasya prtimādānaṃ śivapūjaṃ ca kāryate  

srīśambhośca prasādena grahastuṣṭo dvijottama 
dehārogyaṃ prakurute śāntiṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇam  

rāhorantargate mande lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
svocce mūlatrikoṇe vā duścikye lābharāśige  

tadbhuktau nṛpateḥ sevā rājaprītikarī śubhā 
vivāhotsavakāryāṇi kṛtvā puṇyāni bhūriśaḥ  

ārāmakaraṇe yukto taḍāgaṃ kārayiṣyati 
śūdraprabhuvaśādiṣṭalābho godhanasaṃgrahaḥ  

prayāṇaṃ paścime bhāge prabhumūlāddhanakṣayaḥ 
dehālasyaṃ phalālpatvaṃ svadeśe punareṣyati  

nīcārikṣetrage mande randhre vā vyayage'pi vā 
nīcārirājabhītiśca dāraputrādipīḍanam  

ātmabandhumanastāpaṃ dāyādajanavigraham 
vyavahāre ca kalahamakasmādbhūṣaṇaṃ labhet  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭhariṣphe vā randhre vā pāpasaṃyute 
hṛdrogo mānahāniśca vivādaḥ śatrupīḍanam  

anyadeśādisañcāro gulmavadvayādhibhāgbhavet 
kubhojanaṃ kodravādi jātiduḥkhādbhayaṃ bhavet  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati 
kṛṣṇāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyāddānemārogyamādiśet  

rāhorantargate saumye bhāgye vā svarkṣage'pi vā 
tuṅge vā kendrarāśisthe putre vā balage'pi vā  

rājayogaṃ prakurute gṛhe kalyāṇavarddhanam 
vyāpāreṇa dhanaprāptividyāvāhanamuttamam  

vivāhotsavakāryāṇi catuṣpājjīvalābhakṛt 
saumyamāse mahatsaukhyaṃ svavāre rājadarśanam  

sugandhapuṣpaśayyādi strīsaukhyaṃ cātirobhanam 
mahārājaprasādena dhanalābho mahadyaśaḥ  

dāyeśātkendralābhe vā duścikye bhāgyakarmage 
dehārogyaṃ hṛdutsāha iṣṭasiddhiḥ sukhāvahā  

puṇyaślokādikīrtiśca purāṇaśravaṇādikam 
vivāho yajñadīkṣā ca dānadharmadayādikam  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye saumye mandenāpi yutekṣite 
dāyeśātṣaṣṭhariḥphe vā randhre vā pāpasaṃyute  

devabhāhmaṇanindā ca bhogabhāgyavivarjitaḥ 
satyahīnaśca durbuddhiścaurāhinṛpapīḍanam  

akasmātkalahaścaiva guruputrādināśanam 
arthavyayo rājakopo dāraputrādipīḍanam  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe vā hyapamṛtyubhayaṃ vadet 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ viṣṇusāhasrakaṃ japet  

rāhorantargate ketau bhramaṇaṃ rājato bhayam 
vātajvarādirogaśca catuṣpājjīvahānikṛt  

aṣṭamādhisaṃyukte dehajāḍyaṃ manovyathā 
śubhayukte śubhairdṛṣṭe dehasaukhyaṃ dhanāgamaḥ 
rājasammānabhūṣāptirgṛhe śubhakaro bhavet  

lagnādhipena sambandhe iṣṭasiddhiḥ sukhāvahā 
lagnādhipasamāyukte lābho vā bhavati dhruvam  

catuṣpājjivalābhaḥ syātkendre vātha trikoṇage 
randhrasthānagate ketau vyaye vā balavarjite  

tadbhuktau bahurogaḥ syāccorāhivraṇapīḍanam 
pitṛmātṛviyogaśca bhātṛdveṣo manorujā  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehabādhā bhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ chāgadānaṃ ca kārayet  

rāhorantargate śukre kagnātkendgatrikoṇage 
lābhe vā balasaṃyukte yogaprābalyamādiśet  

vipramūlāddhanaprāptirgomahiṣyādilābhakṛt 
putrotsavādisantoṣo gṛhe kalyāṇasambhavaḥ  

sammānaṃ rājasammanaṃ rājyalābho mahatsukham 
svocce vā svarkṣage vāpi tuṅgāṃśe svāṃśage'pi vā  

nūtanaṃ gṛhanirmāṇaṃ nityaṃ miṣṭhānnabhojanaṃ 
kalatraputravibhavaṃ mitrasaṃgaḥ subhojanam  

annadānaṃ priyaṃ nityaṃ dānadharmādisaṃgrahaḥ 
mahārājaprasādena vāhanāmbarabhūṣaṇaṃ  

vyavasāyātphalādhikyaṃ vivāho mauñjibandhanam 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye śukre nīce śatrugṛhe sthite  

mandāraphaṇisaṃyukte tadbhuktau rogamādiśet 
akasmātkalahaṃ caiva pitṛputraviyogakṛt  

svabandhujanahāniśca sarvatra janapīḍanam 
dāyādakalahaścaiva svaprabhoḥ svasya mṛtyukṛt  

kalatraputrapīḍā ca śūlarogādisambhavaḥ 
dāyeśātkendrarāśisthe trikoṇe vā samanvite  

lābhe vā karmarāśisthe kṣetrapālamahatsukham 
sugandhavastraśayyādi gānavādyasukhaṃ bhavet  

chatracāmarabhūṣāptiḥ priyavastusamanvitā 
dāyeśādripurandhrasthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute  

viprāhinṛpacaurādimūtrakṛcchrānmahadbhayam 
pramehādraudhiro rogaḥ kutsitānnaṃ śirovyathā  

kārāgṛhapraveśaśca rājadaṇḍāddhanakṣayaḥ 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe vā dāraputrādināśanam  

ātmapīḍā bhayaṃ caiva hyapamṛtyubhayaṃ bhavet 
durgālakṣmījapaṃ kuryāt tataḥsukhamavāpnuyāt  

rāhorantargate sūrye svocce svakṣetrakendrage 
trikoṇe lābhage vā'pi tuṅgāṃśe svāṃśage'pi vā  

śubhagraheṇa sandṛṣṭe rājaprītikaraṃ śubham 
dhanadhānyasamṛddhiśca hyalpamāna sukhavāham  

alpagrāmādhipatyaṃ ca svalpalābho bhaviṣyati 
bhāgyalagneśasaṃyukte karmeśena nirīkṣite  

rājāśrayo mahākīrtirvideśagamanaṃ tathā 
deśādhipatyayogaśca gajaśvāmbarabhūṣaṇam  

mano'bhiṣṭapradānaṃ ca putrakalyāṇasambhavam 
dayeśādriḥpharandhrasthe ṣaṣṭhe vā nīcage'pi vā  

jvarātisārarogaśca kalaho rājavigrahaḥ 
prayāṇaṃ śatruvṛddhiśca nripacaurāgnipīḍanam  

dāyeśātkendrakoṇe vā daścikye lābhage'pi vā 
videśe rājasammānaṃ kalyāṇaṃ ca śubhāvaham  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu mahārogo bhaviṣyati 
sūryapraṇāmaṃ śāntiṃ ca kuryādārogyasambhavām  

rāhorantargate candre svakṣetre svoccage'pi vā 
kendratrikoṇalābhe vā mitrarkṣe śubhasaṃyute  

rājatvaṃ rājapūjyatvaṃ dhanārthaṃ dhanalābhakṛt 
ārogyaṃ bhūṣaṇṃ caiva mitrastrīputrasampadaḥ  

pūrṇe candre phalaṃ pūrṇaṃ rājaprītyā śubhāvaham 
aśvavāhanalābhaḥ syadgṛhakṣetrādivṛddhikṛt  

dāyeśātsukhabhāgyasthe kendre vā lābhage'pi vā 
lakṣmīkaṭākṣacihnāni gṛhe kalyāṇasambhavaḥ  

sarvakāryasiddhiḥ syāddhanadhānyasukhāvahā 
satkīrtilābhasammānaṃ devyārādhanamācaret  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭharandhrasthe vyaye vā balavarjite 
piśācakṣudravyāghrādysirgṛhakṣetrārthanāśanam  

mārge caurabhayaṃ caiva vraṇādhikya mahodayam 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu apamṛtyustadā bhavet  

śvetāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyād viprāyārogyasiddhaye 
tataḥ saukhyamavāpnoti candragrahaprasādataḥ  

rāhorantargate bhaume lagnāllābhatrikoṇage 
kendre vā śubhasaṃyukte svocce svakṣetrage'pi vā  

naṣṭarājyadhanprāptirgṛhakṣetrābhivṛddhikṛt 
iṣṭadevaprasādena santānasukhabhāgbhavet  

kṣiprabhojyānmahatsaukhyaṃ bhūṣaṇaśvāmbarādikṛt 
dāyeśātkendrakoṇe vā duścikye lābhage'pi vā  

raktavastrādilābhaḥ syātprayāṇaṃ rājadarśanam 
putravargeṣu kalyāṇaṃ svaprabhośca mahatsukham  

senapatyaṃ mahotsāho bhrātṛvargadhanāgamaḥ 
dāyeśādrandhrariḥphe vā ṣaṣṭhe pāpasamanvite  

putradārādihāniśca soodarāṇāṃ ca pīḍanam 
sthānabhraṃśo bandhuvargadāraputravirodhanam  

caurāhivraṇabhītiśca svadehasya ca pīḍanam 
ādau kleśakaraṃ caiva madhyānte saukhamāpnuyāt  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehālasyaṃ mahadbhayam 
anaḍvāhaṃ ca gāṃ dadyādārogyasukhalabdhaye  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha jīvāntardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

svocce svakṣetrage jīve lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
anekarājadhīśo vā sampanno rājapūjitaḥ  

momahiṣyādilābhaśca vastravāhanabhūṣaṇam 
nūtanasthānanirmāṇaṃ harmyaprākārasaṃyutam  

gajāntaiśvaryasampattirbhāgyakarmaphalaodayaḥ 
brāhmaṇaprabhusammānaṃ samānaṃ prabhudarśanam  

svaprabhoḥ svaphalādhikya dāraputrādilābhakṛt 
nīcāṃśe nīcarāśisthe ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyayarāśige  

nīcasaṅgo mahāduḥkhaṃ dāyādajanavigrahaḥ 
kalaho na vicārosya svaprabhuṣvapamṛtyukṛt  

putradāraviyogaśca dhanadhānyārthahānikṛt 
saptamādhipadoṣeṇa devavādhā bhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ śivasāhasrakaṃ japet 
rudrajāpyaṃ ca godānaṃ kuryāt svā'bhīṣṭalabdhaye  

jīvasyāntargate mande svocce svakṣetramitrabhe 
lagnātkendratrikoṇasthe lābhe vā balasaṃyute  

rājyalābho mahatsaukhyaṃ vastrābharaṇasaṃyutam 
dhanadhānyādilābhaśca strīlābho bahusaukhyakṛt  

vāhanāmbarapaśvādibhūlābhaḥ sthānalābhakṛt 
putramitrādisaukhyaṃ ca naravāhanayogakṛt  

nīlavastrādilābhaśca nīlāśvaṃ labhate ca saḥ 
paścimāṃ diśamāśritya prayāṇaṃ rājadarśanam  

anekayānalābhaṃ ca nirdiśenmandabhuktiṣu 
lagnātṣaṣṭhāṣṭame mande vyaye nīce'stage'pyarau  

dhanadhānyādināśaśca jvarapīḍā manorujaḥ 
strīputrādiṣu pīḍā vāvraṇārtyādikamudbhavet  

gṛhe tvaśubhakāryāṇi bhrtyavargādipīḍanam 
gomahiṣyādihāniśca bandhudveṣī bhaviṣyati  

dāyeśātkendrakoṇasthe lābhe vā dhanage'pi vā 
bhūrābhaścārthalābhaśca putralābhasukhaṃ bhavet  

gomahiṣyādilābhaśca śūdramūlāddhanaṃ tathā 
dāyeśādripurandhrasthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute  

dhanadhānyādināśaśca bandhumitravirodhakṛt 
udyogabhaṅgo dehārtiḥ svajanānāṃ mahadbhayam  

dvisaptamādhipe mande hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ viṣṇusāhasrakaṃ japet  

kṛṣṇāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyādanenārogyamādiśet 
mandagrahaprasādena satyaṃ satyaṃ dvijottama  

jīvasyāntargate saumye kendralābhatrikoṇage 
svocce vā svarkṣage vāpi daśādhipasamanvite  

arthalābho dehasaukhyaṃ rājyalābho mahatsukham 
mahārājaprasādena sveṣṭasiddhiḥ sukhāvahā  

vāhanāmbarapaśvādigodhanaiśaṃkulaṃ gṛham 
mahīsutena saṃdṛṣṭe śatruvṛddhiḥ sukhakṣayaḥ  

vyavasāyātphalaṃ niṣṭaṃ jvarātīmārapīḍanam 
dāyeśādbhāgyakoṇe vā kendre vā tuṅgarāśige  

svadeśe dhanalābhaśca pitṛmātṛsukhāvahā 
gajavājisamāyukto rājamitraprasādataḥ  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭharandhrasthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute 
śubhadṛṣṭivihīne ca dhandhānyaparicyutiḥ  

videśagamanaṃ caiva mārge caurabhayaṃ tathā 
vraṇadāhākṣirogaśca nānādeśaparibhramaḥ  

lagnātṣaṣṭhāṣṭamabhāve vā vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute 
aksamātkalahaścaiva gṛhe miṣṭhurabhāvaṇam  

catuṣpājjīvahāniśca vyavahāre tathaiva ca 
apamṛtyubhayaṃ caiva śatrūṇāṃ kalaho bhavet  

śubhadṛṣṭe śubhairyukte dārasaukhyaṃ dhanāgamaḥ 
ādau śubhaṃ dehasaukhyaṃ vāhanāmbaralābhakṛt  

ante tu dhanahāniścetsvātmasaukhyaṃ na jāyate 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe vā hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ viṣṇusāhasrakaṃ japet 
āyurvṛddhikaraṃ caiva sarvasaubhāgyadāyakam  

jīvasyāntargate ketau śubhagrahasamanvite 
alpasaukhyadhanavyāptiḥ kutsitānnasya bhojanam  

parānnaṃ caiva śrāddhānnaṃ pāpamūlāddhanāni ca 
dāyeśādripurandhrasthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute  

rājakopo dhanacchedo bandhanaṃ rogapīḍanam 
balāhāniḥ pitṛdveṣo bhrātṛdveṣo manorujam  

dāyeśātsutabhāgyasthe vāhane karmage'pi vā 
naravāhanayogaśca gajāśvāmbarasaṅkulam  

mahārājaprasādena sveṣṭakāryārthalābhakṛt 
vyavasāyātphalādhikyaṃ gomahiṣyādilābhakṛt  

yavanaprabhumūlādvā dhanavastrādilābhakṛt 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehavādhā bhaviṣyati  

chāgadānaṃ prakurvīta mṛtyuñjayajapaṃ caret 
sarvadoṣopaśamanīṃ śāntiṃ kuryādvidhānataḥ  

jīvasyāntargate śukre bhāgyakendreśasaṃyute 
lābhe vā sutarāśisthe svakṣetre śubhasaṃyute  

naravāhanayogaśca gajāśvāmbarasaṃyutaḥ 
mahārajaprasādena lābhādhikyaṃ mahatsukham 
nīlāmbarāṇāṃ raktānāṃ lābhaścaiva bhaviṣyati  

pūrvasyāṃ diśi viprendra prayāṇaṃ dhanlābhadam 
kalyāṇaṃ ca mahāprītiḥ pitṛmātṛsukhāvahā  

devatāgurubhaktiśca annadānaṃ mahattathā 
taḍāgagopurādīni diśet puṇyāni bhūriśaḥ  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye nīce dāyeśādvā tathaiva ca 
kalho bandhuvaiṣamyaṃ dāraputrādipīḍanam  

mandārarāhusaṃyukte kalaho rājato bhayam 
strīmūlātkalahaścaiva śvasurātkalahastathā  

sodareṇa vivādaḥ syāddhanadhānyaparicyutiḥ 
dāyeśātkendrarāśisthe dhane vā bhāgyage'pi vā  

dhanadhānyādilābhaśca srīlābho rājadarśanam  

vāhanaṃ putralābhaśca paśuvṛddhirmahatsukham 
gītāvādyaprasaṅgādirvidvajjanasamāgamaḥ  

divyānnabhojanaṃ saukhyaṃ svabandhujanapoṣakam 
dvisaptamādhipe śukre taddaśānāṃ dhanakṣatiḥ  

apamṛtyubhayaṃ tasya strīmūlādauṣadhāditaḥ 
tasya rogasya śāntyarthaṃ śāntikarma samācaret  

śvetāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyādāyurārogyavṛddhaye 
śukragrahaprasādena tataḥ sukhamavāpnuyāt  

jīvasyāntargate sūrye svocce svakṣetrage'pi vā 
kendre vā'thatrikoṇe ca duścikye lābhage'pi vā  

dhane vā balasaṃyute dāyeśādvā tathaiva ca 
tatkāle dhanalābhaḥ syādrājasammānavaibhavam  

vāhanāmbarapaśvādibhūṣaṇaṃ putrasambhavaḥ 
mitraprabhuvaśādiṣṭaṃ sarvakārye śubhāvaham  

lagnādaṣṭamavyaye sūrye dāyeśādvā tathaiva ca 
śirorogādipīḍā ca jvarapīḍā tathaiva ca  

satkarmasu tadā hīnaḥ pāpakarmacayastathā 
sarvatra janavidveṣo hyātmabandhuviyogakṛt  

akasmātkalahaścaiva jīvasyāntargate ravau 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehapīḍā bhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthamādityahṛdayaṃ japet 
sarvapīḍopaśamanaṃ śrīsūryasya prasādataḥ  

jīvasyāntargate candre kendre lābhatrikoṇage 
svocce vā svarkṣarāśisthe pūrṇe caiva balairyute  

dāyeśācchubharāśisthe rājasammānavaibhavam 
dāraputrādisaukhyaṃ ca kṣīrāṇaṃ bhojanaṃ tathā  

satkarma ca tathā kīrtiḥ putrapautrādivṛddhidā 
mahārājaprasādena sarvasaukhyaṃ dhanāgamaḥ  

anekajanasaukhyaṃ ca dānadharmādisaṃgrahaḥ 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye candre sthite vā pāpasaṃyute  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭharandhre vā vyaye vā balavarjite 
mānārthabandhuhāniśca videśaparivicyutiḥ  

nṛpacaurādipīḍā ca dāyādajanavigrahaḥ 
mātulādiviyogaśca mātṛpīḍā tathaiva ca  

dvitīyaṣaṣṭhayorīśe dehapīḍā bhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ durgāpāṭhaṃ ca kārayet  

jīvasyāntargate bhaume lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
svocce vā svarkṣage vāpi tuṅgāṃśe svāṃśage'pi vā  

vidyāvivāhakāryāṇi grāmabhūmyādilābhakṛt 
janasāmarthyamāpnoti sarvakāryārthasiddhidam  

dāyeśātkendrakoṇasthe lābhe vā dhanage'pi vā 
śubhayukte śubhairdṛṣṭe dhanadhānyādisampadaḥ  

miṣṭhānnadānavibhavaṃ rājaprītikaraṃ śubham 
strīsaukhyaṃ ca sutavāptiḥ puṇyatīrthaphalaṃ tathā  

dāyeśādrandhrabhāve vā vyaye vā nīcage'pi vā 
pāpayutekṣite vāpi dhānyārthagṛhanāśanam  

nānarogabhayaṃ duḥkhaṃ netrarogādisambhavaḥ 
pūrvārddhe kaṣṭamadhikamaparārddhe mahatsukham  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehajāḍyaṃ manorujaḥ 
vṛṣabhasya pradānaṃ tu sarvasampatpradāyakam  

jīvasyāntargate rāhau svocce vā kendrage'pi vā 
mūlatrikoṇe bhāgye ca kendrādhipasamanvite  

śubhayutekṣite vāpi yogaprītiṃ samādiśet 
bhuktyādau pañcamāsāṃśca dhanadhānyādikaṃ labhet  

deśagrāmādhikaṃ ca yavanaprabhudarśanam 
gṛhe kalyāṇasampattirbahusenādhipatyakam  

dūrayātrādigamanaṃ puṇyadharmādisaṃgrahaḥ 
setusnānaphalāvāptiriṣṭasiddhiḥ sukhāvahā  

dāyeṣādrandhrabhāve vā vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute 
caurāhivraṇabhītiśca rājavaiṣamyameva ca  

gṛhe karmakalāpena vyākulo bhavati dhruvam 
sodareṇa virodhaḥ syāddāyādajanavigrahaḥ  

gṛhe tvaśubhakāryāṇi duḥsvapnādibhayaṃ dhruvam 
akasmātkalahaścaiva kṣūdraśūnyādirogakṛt  

dvisaptamasthite rāhau dehavādhāṃ vinirdiśet 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ mṛtyuñjayajapaṃ caret  

chāgadānaṃ prakurvīta sarvasaukhyamavāpnuyāt 
devapūyaprasādena rāhutuṣṭyā dvijottama  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha śanyantardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

mūlatrikoṇe svarkṣe vā tulāyāmuccage'pi vā 
kendratrikoṇalābhe vā rājayogādisaṃyute  

rājyalābho mahatsaukhyaṃ dāraputrādivardhanam 
vāhanatrayasaṃyuktaṃ gajāśvāmbarasaṅkulam  

mahārājaprasādena senāpatyādilābhakṛt 
catuṣpājjīvalābhaḥ syādgrāmabhūmyādilābhakṛt  

tathā'ṣṭame vyaye mande nīce vā pāpasaṃyute 
tadbhuktyādau rājabhītirviṣaśastrādipīḍanam  

raktastrāvo gulmarogo hyatimārādipīḍanam 
madhye caurādi bhītiśca deśatyāgo manorujaḥ  

ante śubhakarī caiva śanerantardaśā dvija 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ mrṭyuñjayajapaṃ caret 
tataḥ śāntimavāpnoti śaṅkarasya prasādataḥ  

mandasyāntargate saumye trikoṇe kendrage'pi vā 
sammānaṃ ca yaśaḥ kīrtiṃ vidyālābhaṃ dhanāgamam  

svadeśe sukhamāpnoti vāhanādiphalairyutam 
yajñādikarmasiddhiśca rājayogādisambhavam  

dehasaukhyaṃ hṛdutsāhaṃ gṛhe kalyāṇasambhavam 
setusnānaphalāvāptistīrthayātrādikarmaṇā  

vāṇijyāddhanalābhaśca purāṇaśravaṇādikam 
annadānaphalaṃ caiva nityaṃ miṣṭhānnabhojanam  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye saumye nīce vāstaṃgate sati 
ravyāraphaṇisaṃyukte dāyeśādvā tathaiva ca  

nṛpābhiṣekamarthāptirdeśagrāmādhipatyatā 
phalamīdṛśamādau tu madhyānte rogapīḍanam  

naṣṭāni sarvakāryāṇi vyākulatvaṃ mahadbhayam 
dvitīyasaptamādhiśe dehabādhā bhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ viṣṇusāhasrakaṃ japet 
annadānaṃ prakurvīta sarvasampatpradāyakam  

mandasyāntargate ketau śubhadṛṣṭiyutekṣite 
svocce vā śubharāśisthe yogakārakasaṃyute  

kendrakoṇagate vāpi sthānabhraṃśo mahadbhayam 
daridrabandhanaṃ bhītiḥ putradārādināśanam  

svaprabhośca mahākaṣṭaṃ videśagamanaṃ tathā 
lagnādhipena saṃyukte ādau saukhyaṃ dhanāgamaḥ  

gaṅgādisarvatīrbheṣu snānaṃ daivatadarśanam 
dāyeśātkendrakoṇe vā tṛtīyabhavarāśige  

samartho dharmabuddhiśca saukhyaṃ nṛpasamāgamaḥ 
tathā'ṣṭame vyaye ketau dāyeśādvā tathaiva ca  

apamṛtyubhayaṃ caiva kutsitānnasya bhojanam 
śītajvarātisāraśca vraṇacaurādipīḍanam  

dāraputraviyogaśca saṃsāre bhavati dhruvam 
dvitiyadyūnarāśisthe deha pīḍā bhaviṣyati  

chāgadānaṃ prakurvīta hyapamṛtyunivāraṇam 
ketugrahaprasādena sukhaśāntimavāpnuyāt  

mandasyāntargate śukre svocce svakṣetrage'pi vā 
kendre vā śubhasaṃyukte triokoṇe lābhage'pi vā  

dāraputradhanaprāptirdehārogyaṃ mahotsavaḥ 
gṛhe kalyāṇsampatti rājyalābhaṃ mahatsukham  

mahārājaprasādena hīṣṭasiddhiḥ sukhāvahā 
śammānaṃ prabhusammānaṃ priyavastrādilābhakṛt  

dvipāntarādvastralābhaḥ śvetāśvo mahiṣī tathā 
gurucāravaśādbhāgyaṃ saukhyaṃ ca dhanasampadaḥ  

śanicārānmanuṣyo'sau yogamāpnotyasaṃśayam 
śatrunīcāstage śukre ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyayarāśige  

dāranāśo manaḥkleśaḥ sthānanāśo manorujaḥ 
dārānāṃ svajanakleśaḥ santāpo janavigrahaḥ  

dāyeśādbhāgyage caiva kendre vā lābhasaṃyute 
rājaprītikaraṃ caiva mano'bhīṣṭapradāyakam  

dānadharmadayāyuktaṃ tīrthayātrādikaṃ phalam 
sāsrtārthakāvyaracanāṃ vedāntaśravaṇādikam  

dāraputrādisaukhyaṃ ca labhate nā'tra saṃśayaḥ 
dāyeśādvyayage śukre ṣaṣṭhe vā hyaṣṭame'pi vā  

netrapīḍā jvarabhayaṃ svakulācāravarjitaḥ 
kapole dantaśūlādi hṛdi guhye ca pīḍanam  

jalabhītirmanastāpo vṛkṣātpatanasambhavaḥ 
rājadvāre janadveṣaḥ sodhareṇa virodhanam  

dvitīyasaptamādhīśe ātmakleśo bhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ durgādevījapaṃ caret  

śvetāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyādāyurārogyavṛddhidām 
jagadambāprasādena tataḥ sukhamavāpnuyāt  

mandasyāntargate sūrye svocce svakṣetrage'pi vā 
bhāgyādhipena saṃyukte kendralābhatrikoṇage  

śubhadṛṣṭiyute vāpi svaprabhośca mahatsukham 
gṛhe kalyāṇasampattiḥ putrādisukhavarddhanam  

vāhanāmbarapaśvādigokṣīraiśaṃkulaṃ gṛham 
lagnāṣṭamavyaye sūrye dāyeśādvā tathaiva ca  

hṛdrogo mānahāniśca sthānabhraṃśo manorujā 
iṣṭbandhuviyogaśca udyogasya vināśanam  

tāpajvarādipīḍā ca vyākulatvaṃ bhayaṃ tathā 
ātmasambandhimaraṇamiṣṭavastuviyogakṛt  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehabādhā bhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ sūryapūjāṃ ca kārayet  

mandasyāntargate candre jīvadṛṣṭisamanvite 
svocce svakṣetrakendrasthe trikoṇe lābhage'pi vā  

pūrṇe śubhagrahairyukte rājaprītisamāgamaḥ 
mahārājaprasādena vāhanāmbarabhūṣaṇam  

saubhāgyaṃ sukhavṛddhiṃ ca bhṛtyānāṃ paripālanam 
pitṛmātṛkule saukhyaṃ paśuvṛddhiḥ sukhāvahā  

kṣīṇe vā pāpasaṃyukte pāpadṛṣṭe vā nīcage 
krūrāṃśakagate vāpi krūrakṣetragate'pi vā  

jātakasya mahatkaṣṭaṃ rājakopo dhanakṣayaḥ 
pitṛmātṛviyogaśca putrīputrādirogakṛt  

vyavasāyātphalaṃ neṣṭaṃ nānāmārge dhanavyayaḥ 
akāle bhojanaṃ caiva mauṣadhasya ca bhakṣaṇam  

phalametadvijānīyādādau saukhyaṃ dhanāgamaḥ 
dāyeśātkendrarāśisthe trikoṇe lābhage'pi vā  

vāhanāmbarapaśvādibhrātṛvṛddhiḥ sukhāvahā 
pitṛmātṛsukhāvāptiḥ strīsaukhyaṃ ca dhanāgamaḥ  

mitraprabhuvaśādiṣṭaṃ sarvasaukhyaṃ śubhāvaham 
dāyeśāddvādaśa bhāve randhre vā balavarjite  

śayanaṃ rogamālasyaṃ sthānabhraṣṭaṃ sukhāpaham 
śatruvṛddhivirodhaṃ ca bandhudveṣamavāpnuyāt  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehālasya bhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaśamanārthaṃ ca tilahomādikaṃ caret  

guḍaṃ ghṛtaṃ ca dadhnāktaṃ taṇḍulaṃ ca yathāvidhi 
śvetāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyādāyurārogyavṛddhaye  

mandasyāntargate bhaume kendralābhatrikoṇage 
tuṅge svakṣetrage vāpi daśādhipasamanvite  

lagnādhipena saṃyukte ādau saukhyaṃ dhanāgamaḥ 
rājaprītikaraṃ saukhyaṃ vāhanāmbarabhūṣaṇam  

senāpatyaṃ nṛpaprītiḥ kṛṣigodhānyasampadaḥ 
nūtanasthānanirmāṇaṃ bhrātṛvargeṣṭasaukhyakṛt  

nīce cāstaṅgate bhaume lagnādaṣṭavyayasthite 
pāpadṛṣṭiyute vāpi dhanahānirbhaviṣyati  

caurāhivraṇaśastrādigranthirogādipīḍanam 
bhrātṛpitrādipīḍā ca dāyādajanavigrahaḥ  

catuṣpājjīvahāniśca kutsitānnasya bhojanam 
videśagamanaṃ caiva nānamārge dhanavyayaḥ  

aṣṭamadyūnanāthe tu dvitīyasthe'tha vā yadi 
apamṛtyubhayaṃ caiva nānākaṣṭaṃ parābhavaḥ  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ śāntihomaṃ ca kārayet 
vṛṣadānaṃ prakurvīta sarvāriṣṭanivāraṇam  

mandasyāntargate rāhau kalahaśca manovyathā 
dehapīḍā manastāpaḥ putradveṣo rujobhayam  

arthavyayo rājabhayaṃ svajanādivirodhitā 
videśagamanaṃ caiva gṛhakṣetrādināśanam  

lagnādhipena saṃyukte yogakārakasaṃyute 
svocce svakṣetrage kendre dāyeśāllābharāśige  

ādau saukhyaṃ dhanāvāptiṃ gṛhakṣetrādisampadam 
devabrāhmaṇabhaktiṃ ca tīrthayātrādikaṃ labhet  

catuṣpājjīvalābhaḥ syādgṛhe kalyāṇvarddhanam 
madhye tu rājabhītiśca putramitravirodhanam  

meṣe kanyāgate vāpi kulīre vṛṣabhe tathā 
mīnakodaṇḍasiṃheṣu gajāntaiśvaryamādiśet  

rājasammanabhūṣāptiṃ mṛdulābharasaukhyakṛt 
dvisaptamādhipairyukte dehabādhā bhaviṣyati  

mṛtyuñjayaṃ prakurvīta chāgadānaṃ ca kārayet 
vṛṣadānaṃ prakurvīta sarvasampatsukhāvaham  

mandasyāntargate jīve kendre lābhatrikoṇage 
lagnādhipena saṃyukte svocce svakṣetrage'pi vā  

sarvakāryārthasiddhiḥ syācchobhanaṃ bhavati dhruvam 
mahārājaprasādena dhanavāhanabhūṣaṇam  

sanmānaṃ prabhusammānaṃ priyavastrārthalābhakṛt 
devatāgurubhaktiśca vidvajjanasamāgamaḥ  

dāraputrādilābhaśca putrakalyāṇavaibhavam 
ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye jīve nīce vā pāpasaṃyute  

nijasambandhimaraṇaṃ dhanadhānyavināśanam 
rājasthāne janadveṣaḥ karyahānirbhaviṣyati  

videśagamanaṃ caiva kuṣṭharogādisambhavaḥ 
dāyeśātkendrakoṇe vā dhane vā lābhage'pi vā  

vibhavaṃ dārasaubhāgyaṃ rājaśrīdhanasampadaḥ 
bhojanāmbarasaukhyaṃ ca dānadharmādikaṃ bhavet  

brahmaprtiṣṭhāsiddhiśca kratukarmaphalaṃ tathā 
annadānaṃ mahākīrtirvedāntaśravaṇādikam  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭharandhre vā vyaye vā balavarjite 
bandhudveṣo manoduḥkhaṃ kalahaḥ padavicyuti  

kubhojanaṃ karmahānī rājadaṇḍāddhanavyaya 
kārāgṛhapraveśaśca putradārādipīḍanam  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehavādhā manorujaḥ 
ātmasambandhamaraṇaṃ bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ śivasāhasrakaṃ japet 
svarṇadānaṃ prkurvīta hyārogyaṃ bhavati dhruvam  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha budhāntardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

muktāvidrumalābhaśca jñānakarmasukhādikam 
vidyāmahattvaṃ kīrtiśca nūtanaprabhudarśanam  

vibhavaṃ dāraputrādi pitṛmātṛsukhāvaham 
svoccādisthe'tha nīce'ste ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyayarāśige  

pāpayukte'thavā dṛṣṭe dhanadhānyapaśukṣayaḥ 
ātmabandhuvirodhaśca śūlaroogādisambhavaḥ  

rājakāryakalāpena vyākulo bhavti dhruvam 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dārakleśo bhaviṣyati  

ātmasambandhimaraṇaṃ vātaśūlādisambhavaḥ 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ viṣṇusāhasrakaṃ japet  

budhasyāntargate ketau lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
śubhayukte śubhairdṛṣṭe lagnādhipasamanvite  

yogakārakasambandhe dāyeśātkendralābhage 
dehasaukhyaṃ dhanālpatvaṃ bandhusnehamathādiśet  

catuṣpājjīvalābhaḥ syātsaṃcāreṇa dhanāgamaḥ 
vidyākīrtirprasaṅgaśca samānaprabhudarśanam  

bhojanāmbarasaukhyaṃ ca hyādau madhye sukhāvaham 
dāyeśādyadi randhrasthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute  

vāhanātpatanaṃ caiva putrakleśādisambhavaḥ 
caurādirājabhītiśca pāpakarmarataḥ sadā  

vṛścikādiviṣādbhītirnīcaiḥ kalahasaṃbhavaḥ 
śokarogādiduḥkhaṃ ca nīcasaṅgādikaṃ bhavet  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehajāḍyaṃ bhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārāya chāgadānaṃ tu kārayet  

saumyasyāntargate śukre kendre lābhe trikoṇage 
satkathāpuṇyadharmādisaṃgrahaḥ puṇyakarmakṛt  

mitraprabhuvaśādiṣṭaṃ kṣetralābhaḥ sukhaṃ bhavet 
daśādhipātkendragate trikoṇe lābhage'pi vā  

tatkāle śriyamāpnoti rājaśrīdhanasampadaḥ 
vāpīkūpataḍāgadidānadharmādisaṃgrahaḥ  

vyavasāyātphalādhikyaṃ dhanadhānyasamṛddhikṛt 
dāyeśātṣaṣṭharandhrasthe vyaye vā balavarjite  

hṛdrogo mānahāniśca jvarātīsārapīḍanam 
ātmabandhuviyogaśca saṃsāre bhavati dhruvam  

ātmakaṣṭaṃ manastāpadāyakaṃ dvijasattama 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ durgādevījapaṃ caret 
jagadambāprasādena tataḥ śāntimavāpnuyāt  

saumyasyāntargate sūrye svocce svakṣetrakendrage 
trikoṇe dhanalābhe tu tuṅgāṃśe svāṃśage'pi vā  

rājaprasādasubhāgyaṃ mitraprabhuvaśātsukham 
bhūmyātmajena saṃdṛṣṭe ādau bhūlābhamādiśet  

lagnādhipena saṃdṛṣṭe bahusaukhyaṃ dhanāgamam 
grāmabhūmyādilābhaṃ ca bhojanāmbarasaukhyakṛt  

lagnāṣṭamavyaye vāpi śanyāraphaṇisaṃyute 
dāyeśādripurandhrasthe vyaye vā balavarjite  

caurādiśastrapīḍā ca pittādhikyaṃ bhaviṣyati 
śiroruṅmanasastāpa iṣṭabandhuviyogakṛt  

dvitīyasaptamādhīśe hyapamṛtyurbhaviśyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ śāntiṃ kuryādyathāvidhi  

saumyasyāntargate candre lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
svocce vā svarkṣage vāpi gurudṛṣṭisamanvite  

yogasthānādhipatyena yogaprābalyamādiśet 
strīlābhaṃ putralābhaṃ ca vastravāhanabhūṣaṇam  

nūtanālayalābhaṃ ca nityaṃ miṣṭhānnabhojanam 
gītavādyaprasaṃgaṃ ca śāstravidyāpariśramam  

dakṣiṇāṃ diśamāśritya prayāṇaṃ ca bhaviṣyati 
dvīpāntarādivastrāṇāṃ lābhaścaiva bhaviṣyati  

muktāvidrumaratnāni dhautavastrādikaṃ labhet 
nīcārikṣetrasaṃyukte dehabādhā bhaviṣyati  

dāyeśātkendrakoṇasthe duścikye lābhage'pi vā 
tadbhuktyādau puṇyatīrthasthānadaivatadarśanam  

manodhairyaṃ hṛdutsāho videśadhanalābhakṛt 
dāyeśātṣaṣṭharandhre vā vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute  

corāgninṛpabhītiśca strīsamāgamato bhavet 
duṣkṛtirdhanahāniśca kṛṣigośvādināśakṛt  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehabādhā bhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ durgādevījapaṃ caret  

vastradānaṃ prakurvīta āyurvṛddhisukhāvaham 
jagadambāprasādena tataḥ sukhamavāpnuyāt  

saumyasyāntargate bhaume lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
svocce vā svarkṣage vāpi lagnādhipasamanvite  

rājānugrahaśāntiṃ ca gṛhe kalyāṇasambhavam 
lakṣmīkaṭākṣacihnāni naṣṭarājyārthamāpnuyāt  

putrotsavādisantoṣaṃ gṛhe godhanasaṃkulam 
gṛhakṣetrādilābhaṃ ca gajavājisamanvitam  

rājaprītikaraṃ caiva strīsaukhyaṃ cātiśobhanam 
nīcakṣetrasamāyukte hyaṣṭame vā vyaye'pi vā  

pāpadṛṣṭiyute vāpi dehapīḍā manovyathā 
udyogabhaṅgo daśādau svagrāme dhānyanaśanam  

graṃthiśastravraṇādīnāṃ bhayaṃ tāpajvarādikam 
dāyeśātkendrage bhaume trikoṇe lābhage'pi vā  

śubhadṛṣṭe dhanaprāptirdehasaukhyaṃ bhavenṛṇām 
putralābho yaśovṛddhirbhrātṛvargo mahāpriyaḥ  

dāyeśādatha randhrasthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute 
tadbhuktyādau mahākleśo bhrātṛvarge mahadbhayam  

nṛpāgnicaurabhītiśca putramitravirodhanam 
sthānabhraṃśo bhavedādau madhye saukhyaṃ dhanāgamaḥ  

ante tu rājabhītiḥ syātsthānabhraṃśohyathāpivā 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu hyapamṛtyubhayaṃ bhavet  

godānaṃ ca prakurvīta mṛtyuñjayajapaṃ caret 
śaṅkarasya prasādena tataḥ sukahmavāpnuyāt  

budhasyāntargate rāhau kendralābhatrikoṇage 
kulīre kumbhage vāpi kanyāyāṃ vṛṣabhepi vā  

rājasammānakīrtiṃ ca dhanaṃ ca prabhaviṣyati 
puṇyatīrthasthānalābho devatādarśanaṃ tathā  

iṣtāpūrte ca mahato mānaścāmbaralābhakṛt 
bhuktyādau dehapīḍā ca tvante saukhyaṃ vinirdiśet  

lagnāṣṭavyayarāśisthe tadbhuktau dhananāśanam 
bhuktyādau dehanāśaśca vātajvaramajīrṇakṛt  

lagnādupacaye rāhau śubhagrahasamanvite 
rājasaṃlāpasantoṣo nūtanaprabhudarśanam  

dāyeśāddvādaśe vāpi hyaṣṭame pāpasaṃyute 
niṣṭhuraṃ rājakāryāṇi athānabhraṃśo mahadbhayam  

bandhanaṃ rogapīḍā ca nijabandhumanovyathā 
hṛdrogo mānahāniśca dhanahānirbhaviṣyati  

dvitīyasaptamasthe vā hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ durgālakṣmījapaṃ caret  

śvetāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyādāyuārogyadāyinīm 
jagadambāprasādena tataḥ sukhamavāpnuyāt  

budhasyāntargate jīve lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
svocce vā svarkṣage vāpi lābhe vā dhanarāśige  

dehasaukhyaṃ dhanāvāptī rājaprītistathaiva ca 
vivāhotsavakāryāṇi nityaṃ miṣṭhānnabhojanam  

gomahiṣyādilābhaśca purāṇasravaṇādikam 
devatāgurubhaktiśca dānadharmamakhādikam  

yajñakarmapravṛddhiśca śivapūjāphalaṃ tathā 
nīce vāstaṃgate vāpi ṣaṣṭhāṣṭavyayage'pi vā  

śanyāradṛṣṭasaṃyukte kalaho rājavigrahaḥ 
caurādidehapīḍā ca pitṛmātṛvināśnam  

mānahāni rājadaṇḍo dhanahānirbhaviṣyati 
viṣāhijvarapīḍā ca kṛṣibhūmivināśanam  

dayeśātkendrakoṇe vā lābhe vā balasaṃyute 
bandhuputrahṛdutsāho śubhaṃ ca dhanasaṃyutam  

paśuvṛddhiryaśovṛddhirannadānādikaṃ phalam 
dāyeśātṣaṣṭharandhre vā vyaye vā balavarjite  

aṅgatāpaśca vaikalyaṃ dehabādhā bhviṣyati 
kalatrabandhuvaiṣamyaṃ rājakopo dhanakṣayaḥ  

akasmātkalahādbhītiḥ pramādo dvijato bhayam 
dvitīyasaptamasthe vā dehabādhā bhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ śivasāhasrakaṃ japet 
gobhūriraṇyadānena sarvāriṣṭaṃ vyapohati  

saumyasyāntargate mande svocce svakṣetrakendrage 
trikoṇalābhage vāpi gṛhe kalyāṇavarddhanam  

rājyalābhaṃ mahotsāhaṃ gṛhaṃ godhanasaṃkulam  

śubhasthānaphalavāptiṃ tīrthavāsaṃ tathādiśet 
aṣṭame vā vyaye mande dāyeśādvā tathaiva ca  

arātiduḥkhabāhulyaṃ dāraputrādipīḍanam 
buddhibhraṃśo bandhunāśaḥ karmanāśo manorujaḥ  

videśagamanaṃ caiva duḥsvapnādipradarśanam 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ mṛtyuñjayajapaṃ caret 
kṛṣṇāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyādāyurārogyavṛddhaye  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha ketvantardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

kendre trikoṇalābhe vā ketau lagneśasaṃyute 
bhāgyakarmasusambandhe vāhaneśasamanvite  

tadbhuktau dhanadhānyādi catuṣpājjīvalābhakṛt 
putradārādisaukhyaṃ ca rājaprītimanorujaḥ  

grāmabhūmyādilābhaśca gṛhaṃ godhanasaṃkulam 
nīcāstakheṭasaṃyukte hyaṣṭame vyayage'pi vā  

hṛdrogo mānahāniśca dhanadhānyapaśukṣayaḥ 
dāraputrādipīḍā ca manaścāṃcalyameva ca  

dvitīyadyūnanāthena sambandhe tatra saṃsthite 
anārogyaṃ mahatkaṣṭamātmabandhuviyogakṛt  

durgādevījapaṃ kuryānmṛtyuñjayajapaṃ caret 
evaṃ svāntargate ketau tataḥ sukhamavāpnuyāt  

ketorantargate śukre svocce svakṣetrasaṃyute 
kendratrikoṇalābhe vā rājyanāthena saṃyute  

rājaprītiṃ ca saubhāgyaṃ diśātsvāmbarasaṃkulam 
tatkāle śriyamāpnoti bhāgyakarmeśasaṃyute  

naṣṭarājyadhanaprāptiṃ sukhavāhanasuttamam 
setusnānādikaṃ caiva devatādarśanaṃ mahat  

mahārājaprasādena grāmabhūmyādilābhakṛt 
dāyeśātkendrakoṇe vā duścikye lābhage'pi vā  

dehārogyaṃ śubhaṃ caiva gṛhe kalyāṇaśobhanam 
bhojanāmbarabhūṣāptirathadolādilābhakṛt  

dāyeśādripurandhrasthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute 
akasmātkalahaṃ caiva paśudhānyādipīḍanam  

nīcasthe kheṭasaṃyukte lagnātṣaṣṭhāṣṭarāśige 
svabandhujanavaiṣamyaṃ śirokṣivraṇapīḍanam  

hṛdrogaṃ mānahāniṃ ca dhanadhānyapaśukṣayam 
kalatraputrapīḍāyāḥ sañcāraṃ ca samādiśet  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehajāḍyaṃ manorujam 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ durgādevījapaṃ caret 
śvetāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyādāyuārogyavṛddhaye  

ketorantargate sūrye svocce svakṣetrage'pi vā 
kendratrikoṇalābhe vā śubhayuktanirīkṣite  

dhanadhānyādilābhaśca rājānugrahavaibhavam 
anekaśubhakāryāṇi ceṣṭasiddhiḥ sukhāvahā  

aṣṭamavyayarāśisthe pāpagrahasamanvite 
tadbhuktau rājabhītiśca pitṛmātṛviyogakṛt  

videśagamanaṃ caiva caurāhiviṣapīḍanam 
rājamitravirodhaśca rājadaṇḍāddhanakṣayaḥ  

śokarogabhayaṃ caiva uṣṇādhikyaṃ jvaro bhavet 
dāyeśātlendrakoṇe vā lābhe vā dhanasaṃsthite  

dehasaukhyaṃ cārthalābha putralābho manodṛḍham 
sarvakāryārthasiddhiḥ syātsvalpagrāmādhipatyayuk  

dāyeśādrandhrariḥphe vā sthite vā pāpasaṃyute 
annavighno manobītirdhanadhānyapaśukṣayaḥ  

ādau madhye mahākleśānante saukhyaṃ vinirdiśet 
dvitīyasaptamādhīśe hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati  

tasya śāntiṃ prakurvīta svarṇaṃ dhenuṃ pradāpayet 
bhāskarasya prasādena tataḥ sukhamavāpnuyāt  

ketorantargate candre svocce svakṣetrage'pi vā 
kendratrikoṇalābhe vā dhane śubhasamanvite  

rājaprītirmahotsāhaḥ kalyāṇaṃ ca mahatsukham 
mahārājaprasādena gṛhabhūmyādilābhakṛt  

bhojanāmbarapaśvādivyavasāye'dhikaṃ phalam 
aśvavāhanalābhaśca vastrabharaṇabhūṣaṇam  

devālayataḍāgādipuṇyadharmādisaṅgraham 
putradārādisaukhyaṃ ca pūrṇacandraḥ prayacchati  

kṣīṇe vā nīcage candre ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyayarāśige 
ātmasaukhyaṃ manastāpaṃ kāryavighnaṃ mahadbhayam  

pitṛmātṛviyogaṃ ca dehajāḍyaṃ manovyathām 
vyavasāyātphalaṃ kaṣṭaṃ paśunāśaṃ bhayaṃ vadet  

dāyeśātkendrakoṇe vā lābhe vā balasaṃyute 
kṛṣigobhūmilābhaṃ ca iṣṭabandhusamāgamam  

tasmātsvakāryasiddhiṃ ca gṛhe gokṣīrameva ca 
bhuktyādau śubhamārogyaṃ madhye rājapriyaṃ śubham  

ante tu rājabhītiṃ ca videśagamanaṃ tathā 
dūrayātrādisañcāraṃ sambandhijanapūjanam  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭhariḥphe vā randhre vā balavarjite 
dhanadhānyādihāniśca manovyātkulameva ca  

svabandhujanavairaṃ ca bhrātṛpīḍā tathaiva ca 
nidhanādhipadoṣeṇa dvisaptapatisaṃyute  

apamṛtyubhayaṃ tasya śāntiṃ kuryādyathāvidhi 
candraprītikarīṃ caiva hyāyurārogyasiddhaye  

ketorantargate bhaume lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
svocce svakṣetrage vā'pi śubhagrahayutekṣite  

ādau śubhaphalaṃ caiva grāmabhūmyādilābhakṛt 
dhanadhānyādilābhaśca catuṣpājjīvalābhakṛt  

gṛgārāmakṣetralābho rājānugrahavaibhavam 
bhāgye karmeśasambandhe bhūlābhaḥ saukhyameva ca  

dāyeśātkendrakoṇe vā duścikye lābhage'pi vā 
rājaprītiyaśolābhaḥ putramitrādisaukhyakṛt  

tathā'ṣṭamavyaye bhaume dāyeśāddhanage'pi vā 
drutaṃ karoti maraṇaṃ videśe cāpadaṃ bhramam  

pramehamūtrakṛcchrādicaurādinṛpapīḍanam 
kalahādi vyathāyuktaṃ kiñcitsukhavivarddhanam  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu tāpajvaraviṣādbhayam 
dārapīḍā manaḥkleśamapamṛtyubhayaṃ bhavet  

anḍvāhaṃ pradadyāttu sarvasampatsukhāvaham 
tataḥ śāntimavāpnoti bhaumagrahaprasādataḥ  

ketorantargate rāhau svocce mitrasvarāśige 
kendratrikoṇe lābhe vā duścikye dhanasaṃjñake  

tatkāle dhanalābhaḥ syātsañcāro bhavati dhruvam 
mlecchaprabhuvaśātsaukhyaṃ dhandhānyaphalādikam  

catuṣpājjīvalābhaḥ syādgrāmabhūmyādilābhakṛt 
bhuktyādau kleśamāpnoti madhyānte saukhyamāpnuyāt  

randhre vā vyayage rāhau pāpasaṃdṛṣṭasaṃyute 
bahumūtraṃ kṛśaṃ deehaṃ śītajvaraviṣādbhayam  

cāturthikajvaraṃ caiva kṣudropadravapīḍanam 
akasmātkalahaṃ caiva pramehaṃ śūlamādiśet  

dvitīyasaptamasthe vā tadā kleśaṃ mahadbhayam 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ durgādevījapaṃ caret  

ketorantargate jīve kandre lābhe trikoṇage 
svocce svakṣetrage vāpi lagnādhipasamanvite  

karmabhāgyādhipairyukte dhanadhānyārthasaṃpadam 
rājaprītiṃ tadotsāhamaśvāṃdolyādikaṃ diśet  

gṛhe kalyāṇasampattiṃ putralābhaṃ mahotsavaham 
puṇyatīrthaṃ mahotsāhaṃ satkarma ca sukhāvaham  

iṣṭadevaprasādena vijayaṃ kāryalābhakṛt 
rājasaṃllāpakāryāṇi nūtanaprabhudarśanam  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye jīve dāyeśānnīcage'pi vā 
caurāhivraṇabhītiṃ ca dhanadhānyādināśanam  

putradārāviyogaṃ ca tvatīvakleśasambhavam 
ādau subhaphalaṃ caiva ante kleśakaraṃ vadet  

dāyeśātkendrakoṇe vā duścikye lābhage'pi vā 
śubhayukte nṛpaprītirvicitrāmbarabhūṣaṇam  

dūradeśaprayāṇaṃ ca svabandhujanapoṣaṇam 
bhojanāmbarapaśvādi bhuktyādau dehapīḍanam  

ante tu sthānacalanamakasmātkalaho bhavet 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ śivasāhasrakaṃ japet 
mahāmṛtyuñjayaṃ jāpyaṃ sarvopadravanāśanam  

ketorantargate mande svadaśāyāṃ tu pīḍanam 
bandhoḥ kleśo manastāpaścatuṣpājjīvalābhakṛt  

rājakāryakalāpena dhananāśo mahadbhayam 
sthānāccyutiḥ pravāsaśca mārge caurabhayaṃ bhavet  

ālasyaṃ manaso hāniścāṣṭame vyayarāśige 
mīnatrikoṇage mande tulāyāṃ svarkṣage'pi vā  

kendratrikoṇalābhe vā duścikye vā śubhāṃśake 
śubhadṛṣṭayute caiva sarvakāryārthasādhanam  

svaprabhośca mahatsaukhyaṃ bhramaṇaṃ ca sukhāvaham 
svagrāme sukhasampattiḥ svavarge rājadarśanam  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭhariḥphe vā aṣṭame pāpasaṃyute 
dehatāpo manastāpaḥ kārye vighno mahadbhayam  

ālasyaṃ mānahāniśca pitṛmātrorvināśanam 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu hyapamṛtyubhayaṃ bhavet  

taddoṣapairhārārthaṃ tilahomaṃ ca kārayet 
kṛṣṇāṃ gāṃ mahiṣīṃ dadyādāyurārogyavṛddhaye  

ketorantargate saumye kendralābhatrikoṇage 
svocce svakṣetrasaṃyukte rājyalābho mahatsukham  

satkathāśravaṇaṃ dānaṃ dharmasiddhiḥ sukhāvahā 
bhūlābhaḥ putralābhaśca śubhagoṣṭhīdhanāgamaḥ  

ayatnāddharmalabdhiśca vivāhaśca bhaviṣyati 
gṛhe śubhakaraṃ karma vastrābharaṇabhūṣaṇam  

bhāgyakarmādhipairyukte bhāgyavṛddhiḥ sukhāvahā 
vidvadgoṣṭhīkathābhiśca kālakṣepo bhaviṣyati  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye saumye mandārāhiyutekṣite 
virodho rājavargaiśca paragehanivāsanam  

vāhanāmbarapaśvādidhanadhānyādināśakṛt 
bhuktyādau śobhanaṃ proktaṃ madhye saukhyaṃ dhanāgamaḥ  

ante kleśakaraṃ caiva dāraputrādipīḍanam 
dāyeśātkendrage saumye trikoṇe lābhage'pi vā  

dehārogyaṃ mahāṃllābhaḥ putrakalyāṇavaibhavam 
bhojanāmbarapaśvādivyavasāye'dhikaṃ phalam  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭharandhre vā vyaye vā balavarjite 
tadbhuktyādau mahākleśo dāraputrādipīḍanam  

rājabhītikaraścaiva madhye tīrthakaro bhavet 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu hyapamṛtyurbhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ viṣṇusāhasrakaṃ japet 
tataḥ sukhamavāpnoti śrīhareśca prasādataḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha śukrāntardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atha svāntargate śukre lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
lābhe vā balasaṃyukte tadbhuktau ca śubhaṃ phalam  

vipramūlāddhanaprāptirgomahiṣyādilābhakṛt 
putrotsavādisantoṣo gṛhe kalyāṇasambhavaḥ  

sanmānaṃ rājasammānaṃ rājyalābho mahatsukham 
svocce vā svarkṣage vāpi tuṅgāṃśe vāṃśage'pi vā  

nūtanālayanirmāṇaṃ nityaṃ miṣṭhānnabhojanam 
kalatraputravibhavaṃ mitrasaṃyuktabhojanam  

annadānaṃ priyaṃ nityaṃ danadharmādisaṅgrahaḥ 
mahārājaprasādena vāhanāmbarabhūṣaṇam  

vyavasāyātphalādhikyaṃ catuṣpājjīvalābhakṛt 
prayāṇaṃ paścime bhāge vāhanāmbaralābhakṛt  

lagnādyupacaye śukre śubhagrahayutekṣite 
mitrāṃśe tuṅgalābheśayogalārakasaṃyute  

rājyalābho mahotsāho rājaprītiḥ śubhāvahā 
gṛhe kalyāṇasampattirdāraputrādivarddhanam  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyaye śukre pāpayukte'tha vīkṣite 
caurādivraṇabhītiśca sarvatra janapīḍanam  

rājadvāre janadveṣa iṣṭabandhuvināśanam 
dāraputrādipīḍā ca sarvatra janapīḍanam  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu sthite cenmaraṇaṃ bhavet 
tarta durgājapaṃ kuryāddhanudānaṃ ca kārayet  

śukrasyāntargate sūrye santāpo rājavigrahaḥ 
dāyādakalahaścaiva svoccanīcavivarjite  

śukrasyāntargate sūrye santāpo rājabhiḥ kaliḥ 
dāyādāt kalahaścaiva śubhakṣetrātya rāśige   

svocce svakṣetrage sūrye mitrarkṣe kendrakoṇage 
dāyeśātkendrakoṇe vā lābhe vā dhanage'pi vā  

tadbhuktau dhanalābhaḥ syādrājyastrīdhanasampadaḥ 
svaprabhośca mahatsaukhyamiṣṭabandhoḥ samāgamaḥ  

pitṛmātroḥ sukhaprāptiṃ bhrātṛlābhaṃ sukhāvaham 
satkīrtiṃ sukhasaubhāgyaṃ putralābhaṃ ca vindati  

tathāṣṭame vyaye sūrye ripurāśisthite'pi vā 
nīce vā pāpavargasthe dehatāpo manorujaḥ  

svajanoparisaṃkleśo nityaṃ niṣṭhurabhāṣaṇam 
pitṛpīḍā bandhuhānī rājadvāre virodhakṛt  

vraṇapīḍāhibādhā ca svagṛhe ca bhayaṃ tathā 
nānārogabhayaṃ caiva gṛhakṣetrādināśanam  

saptamādhipatau sūrye grahabādhā bhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ sūryaprītiṃ ca kārayet  

śukrasyāntargate candre kendralābhatrikoṇage 
svocce svakṣetrage caiva bhāgyanāthenasaṃyute  

śubhayukte pūrṇacandre rājyanāthena saṃyute 
tadbuktau vāhanādīnāṃ lābhaṃ gehe mahatsukham  

mahārājaprasādena gajāntaiśvaryamādiśet 
mahānadīsnānapuṇyaṃ devabrāhmaṇapūjanam  

gītavādyaprasaṅgādividvajjanavibhūṣaṇam 
gomahiṣyādivṛddhiśca vyavasāye'dhikaṃ phalam  

bhojanāmbarasaukhyaṃ ca bandhusaṃyuktabhojanam 
nīce vātsaṅgate vāpi ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamavyayarāśige  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭhage vāpi randhre vā vyayarāśige 
tatkāle dhananāśaḥ syātsañcareta mahadbhayam  

dehāyāso manastāpo rājadvāre virodhakṛt 
videśagamanaṃ caiva tīrthayātrādikaṃ phalam  

dāraputrādi pīḍā ca nijabandhuviyogakṛt 
dāyeśātkendralābhasthe trikoṇe sahaje'pi vā  

rājaprītikarī caiva deśagrāmādhipatyatā 
dhairyaṃ yaśaḥ sukhaṃ kīrtirvāhanāmbarabhūṣaṇam  

kūpārāmataḍāgadinirmāṇaṃ dhanasaṅgrahaḥ 
bhuktayādau dehasaukhyaṃ syādante kleśastathā bhavet  

śukrasyāntargate bhaume lagnātkendratrikoṇage 
svocce vā svarkṣage bhaume lābhe vā balasaṃyute  

lagnādhipena saṃyukte karmabhāgyeśasaṃyute 
tadbhuktau rājayogādisampadaṃ śobhanāṃ vadet  

vastrābharaṇabhūmyāderiṣṭasiddhiḥ sukhāvahā 
tathā'ṣṭame vyaye vā'pi dāyeśādvā tathaiva ca  

śītajvarādipīḍā ca pitṛmātṛbhayāvahā 
jvarādyadhikarogāśca sthānabhraṃśo manorujā  

svabandhujanahāniśca kalaho rājavigrahaḥ 
rājadvārajanadveṣo dhanadhānyavyayo'dhikaḥ  

vyavasāyātphalaṃ neṣṭaṃ grāmabhūmyādihānikṛt 
dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehavādhā bhaviṣyati  

śukrasyāntargate rāhau kendralābhatrikoṇage 
svocce vā śubhasaṃdṛṣṭe yogakārakasaṃyute  

tadbhuktau bahusaukhyaṃ ca dhanadhānyādilābhakṛt 
iṣṭabandhusamākīrṇaṃ bhavanaṃ ca samādiśet  

yātuḥ kāryārthasiddhiḥ syāt paśukṣetrādisambhavaḥ 
lagnādyupacaye rāhau tadbhuktiḥ sukhadā bhavet  

śatrunāśo mahotsāho rājaprītikarī śubhā 
bhuktyādau śaramāsāṃśca ante jvaramajīrṇakṛt  

kāryavighnamavāpnoti sañcare ca manovyathā 
paraṃ sukhaṃ ca saubhāgyaṃ mahārāja ivā'śnute  

naiṛtīṃ diśamāśritya prayāṇaṃ prabhudarśanam 
yātuḥ kāryārthasiddhiḥ syātsvadeśe punareṣyati  

upakāro brāhmaṇānāṃ tīrthayātrāphalaṃ bhavet 
dāyeśādrandhrabhāvasthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute  

aśubhaṃ labhate karma pitṛmātṛjanāvadhi 
sarvatra janavidveṣaṃ nānārūpaṃ dvijottama  

dvitīye saptame vāpi dehālasya vinirdiśet 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ mṛtyuñjayajapaṃ caret  

śukrasyāntargate jīve svocce svakṣetrakendrage 
dāyeśācchubharāśisthe bhāgye vā putrarāśige  

naṣṭarājyāddhanaprāptimiṣṭārthāmbarasampadam 
mitraprabhośca sanmānaṃ dhanadhānyaṃ labhennaraḥ  

rājasammānakīrtiṃ ca aśvāndolādilābhakṛt 
vidvatprabhusamākīrṇaṃ śāstrāpariśramam  

putrotsavādisantoṣamiṣṭabandhusamāgamam 
pitṛmātṛsukhaprāptiṃ putrādisaukhyamādiśet  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭharāśisthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute 
rājacaurādipīḍā ca dehapīḍā bhaviṣyati  

ātmarugbandhukaṣṭaṃ syātkalahena manovyathā 
sthānacyutiṃ pravāsaṃ ca nānārogaṃ samāpnuyāt  

dvitīyasaptamādhīśe dehabādhā bhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ mahāmṛtyuñjayaṃ caret  

śukrasyāntargate mande svocce tu paramoccage 
svarkṣakendratrikoṇasthe tuṅgāṃśe svāṃśage'pi vā  

tadbhuktau bahusaukhyaṃ syādiṣṭabandhusamāgamaḥ 
rājadvāre ca sammānaṃ putrikājanmasambhavaḥ  

puṇyatīrthaphalavāptirdānadharmādipuṇyakṛt 
svaprabhośca padāvāptiḥ nīcasthe kleśabhāgyabhavet  

dehālasyamavāpnoti tathā'yādadhikavyayam 
tathāṣṭame vyaye mande dāyeśādvā tathaiva ca  

bhuktyādau vividhā pīḍā pitṛmātṛjanāvadhi 
dāraputrādipīḍā ca paradeśādivibhramaḥ  

vyavasāyātphalaṃ naṣṭaṃ gomahiṣyādihānikṛt 
dvitīyasaptamādhīśe dehabādhā bhaviṣyati  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ tilahomaṃ ca kārayet 
mṛtyuñjayajapaṃ kuryāccaṇḍīpāṭhamāthapi vā  

svayaṃ vā brāhmaṇadvārā yathāśakti yathāvidhi 
tataḥ śāntimavāpnoti śivāśambhuprasādataḥ  

śukrasyāntargate saumye kendre lābhatrikoṇage 
svocce vā svarkṣage vāpi rājaprītikaraṃ śubham  

saubhāgyaṃ putralābhaśca sanmārgeṇa dhanāgamaḥ 
purāṇadharmaśravaṇaṃ śṛṅgārijanasaṃgamaḥ  

iṣṭabandhujanākīrṇaṃ śobhitaṃ tasya mandiram 
svaprabhośca mahatsaukhyaṃ nityaṃ miṣṭhānnabhojanam  

dāyeśātṣaṣṭharandhre vā vyaye vā balavarjite 
pāpadṛṣṭe pāpayukte catuṣpājjīvahānikṛt  

anyālayanivāsaśca manovaikalyasambhavaḥ 
vyāpāreṣu ca sarveṣu hānireva na saṃśayaḥ  

bhuktyādau śobhanaṃ proktaṃ madhye madhyaphalaṃ diśet 
ante kleśakaraṃ caiva śītavātajvarādikam  

saptamādhīśadoṣeṇa dehapīḍā bhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ viṣṇusāhasrakaṃ japet  

śukrasyāntargate ketau svocce vā svarkṣage'pi vā 
yogakārakasambandhe sthānavīryasamanvite  

bhuktyādau śubhamādhikyānnityaṃ miṣṭhānnabhojanam 
vyavasāyātphalādhikyaṃ gomahoṣyādivṛddhikṛt  

dhanadhānyasamṛddhiśca saṃgrāme vijayo bhavet 
bhuktyante hi sukhaṃ caiva bhuktyādau madhyamaṃ phalam  

madhye madhye mahatkaṣṭaṃ paścādārogyamādiśet 
dāyeśādrandhrabhāvasthe vyaye vā pāpasaṃyute  

caurāhivraṇapīḍā ca buddhināśo mahadbhayam 
śirorujaṃ manastāpamakarmakalahaṃ vadet  

pramehabhavarogaṃ ca nānāmārge dhanavyayaḥ 
bhāryāputravirodhaśca gamanaṃ kāryanāśanam  

dvitīyadyūnanāthe tu dehabādhā bhaviṣyati 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ mṛtyuñjayajapaṃ caret  

chāgadānaṃ prakurvīta sarvasampatpradāyakam 
śukraprītikarīṃ śāntiṃ tataḥ sukhamavāpnuyāt
