medskiphrulemedskip

         atha pratyantardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

pṛthak svasvadaśāmānairhanyādantardaśāmitim 
bhyetsarvadaśāyogaiḥ phalaṃ pratyantaraṃ kramāt  

vivādo vittahāniśca dārārtiḥ śirasi vyathā 
ravyantare budhairjñeyaṃ tasya pratyantare phalam  

udvegaḥ kalahaścaiva vittahānirmanovyathā 
ravyantare vijānīyāt candrapratyantare phalam  

rājabhītiḥ śastrabhītirbandhanaṃ bahusaṃkaṭam 
satruvahnikṛtā pīḍā kujapratyantare phalam  

śleṣmavyādhiḥ śastrabhītiedhanahānirmahadbhayam 
rājabhaṅgastathā trāso rāhupratyantare phalam  

śatrunāśo jayo vṛddhirvastrahemādibhūṣaṇam 
aśvayānādilābhaśca gurupratyantare phalam  

dhanahāniḥ paśoḥ pīḍā mahodvego mahārujaḥ 
aśubhaṃ sarvamāpnoti śanipratyantare janaḥ  

vidyālābho bandhusaṅga bhojyaprāptirdhanāgamaḥ 
dharmalābho nṛpātpūjā bidhapratyantare bhavet  

prāṇabhītirmahāhānī rājabhītiśca vigrahaḥ 
śatruṇāñca mahāvādo ketoḥ pratyantare bhavet  

dināni samarūpāṇi lābho'pyalpo bhavediha 
svalpā ca sukhasampattiḥ śukrapratyantare bhavet  

bhūmojyadhanasamprāptī rājapūjāmahatsukham 
lābhaścandrāntare jñeyaṃ candrapratyantare phalam  

mativṛddhirmahāpūjyaḥ sukhaṃ bandhujanaiḥ saha 
dhanāgamaḥ śatrubhayaṃ kujapratyantare bhavet  

bhavetkalyāṇasampattī rājavittasamāgamaḥ 
aśubhairalpamṛtyuaśca rāhupratyantare dvija  

vastralābho mahātejo brahmajñānaṃ ca sadguroḥ 
rājyālaṃkaraṇāvāptirgurupratyantare phalam  

durdine labhate pīḍāṃ vātapittādviśeṣataḥ 
dhanadhānyayaśohāniḥ śanipratyantare bhavet  

putrajanmahayaprāptirvidyālābho mahonnatiḥ 
śuklavastrānnalābhaśca budhapratyantare bhavet  

brāhmaṇena samaṃ yuddhamapamṛtyuḥ sukhakṣayaḥ 
sarvatra jāyate kleśaḥ ketoḥ pratyantare bhavet  

dhanalābho mahatsaukhyaṃ kanyājanma subhojanam 
prītiśca sarvalokebhyo bhṛgupratyantare vidhoḥ  

annāgamo vastralābhaḥ śatruhāniḥ sukhāgamaḥ 
sarvatra vijayaprāptiḥ sūryapratyantare vidhoḥ  

śatrubhītiṃ kaliṃ ghoraṃ raktasrāvaṃ mṛterbhayam 
kujasyāntardaśāyāṃ ca kujapratyantare vadet  

bandhanaṃ rājabhaṅgaśca dhanahāniḥ kubhojanam 
kalahaḥ śatrubhirnityaṃ rāhupratyantare bhavet  

matināśastathā duḥkhaṃ santāpaḥ kalaho bhavet 
viphalaṃ cintitaṃ sarvaṃ guroḥ pratyantare bhavet  

svāmināśastathā pīḍā dhanahānirnmahābhayam 
vaikalyaṃ kalahastrāso śaneḥ pratyantare bhavet  

sarvathā buddhināśaśca dhanahānirjvarastanau 
vastrānnasuhṛdāṃ nāśo budhapratyantare bhavet  

ālasya ca śiraḥpīḍā pāparogo'pamṛtyukṛt 
rājabhītiḥ śastraghāto ketoḥ pratyantare bhavet  

cāṇḍālātsaṅkaṭastrāso rājaśāstrabhayaṃ bhavet 
atisārā'tha vamanaṃ bhṛgoḥ pratyantare bhavet  

bhūmilābho'rthasampattiḥ santoṣo mitrasaṅgatiḥ 
sarvatra sukhamāpnoti raveḥ pratyantare janaḥ  

yāmyāṃ diśi bhavellābhaḥ sitavastravibhūṣaṇam 
saṃsiddhiḥ sarvakāryāṇāṃ vidhoḥ pratyantare bhavet  

bandhanaṃ bahudhā rogo bahughātaḥ suhṛdbhayam 
rāhvantardaśāyāṃ ca jñeyaṃ rāhvantare phalam  

sarvatra labhate mānaṃ gajāśvaṃ ca dhanāgamam 
rāhorantardaśāyāṃ ca guroḥ pratyantare janaḥ  

bandhanaṃ jāyate ghoraṃ sukhahānirmahadbhayam 
pratyahaṃ vātapīḍā ca śaneḥ pratyantare bhavet  

sarvatra bahudhā lābhaḥ strīsaṅgācca viśeṣataḥ 
paradeśabhavā siddhirbudhapratyantare bhavet  

buddhināśo bhayaṃ vighno dhanahānirmahadbhayam 
sarvatra kalahodvegau ketoḥ pratyantare phalam  

yoginībhyo bhayaṃ bhūyādaśvahāniḥ kubhojanam 
strīnāśaḥ kulajaṃ śokaṃ śukrapratyantare bhavet  

jvararogo mahābhītiḥ putrapautrādipīḍanam 
alpamṛtyuḥ pramādaśca raveḥ pratyantare bhavet  

udvegakalaho cintā mānahānirmahadbhayam 
piturvikalatā dehe vidyoḥ raveḥ pratyantare bhavet  

bhagandarakṛtā pīḍā raktapittaprapīḍanam 
arthahānirmahodvegaḥ kujapratyantare phalam  

hemalābho dhānyavṛddhi kalyāṇaṃ suphalodayaḥ 
gurorantardaśāyāṃ ca bhaved gurvantare phalam  

gobhūmihayalābhaḥ syātsarvatra sukhasādhanam 
saṃgraho hyannapānādeḥ śaneḥ pratyantare bhavet  

vidyālābho vastralābho jñānalābhaḥ samauktikaḥ 
suhṛdāṃ saṅgamaḥ sneho budhapratyantare bhavet  

jalabhītistathā cauryaṃ bandhanaṃ kalaho bhavet 
apamṛtyurbhayaṃ ghoraṃ ketoḥ pratyantare dvija  

nānāvidyārthasamprāptirhemavastravibhūṣaṇam 
labhate kṣemasantoṣaṃ bhṛgoḥ pratyantare janaḥ  

nṛpāllābhastathā mitrātpitṛto mātṛto'pi vā 
sarvatra labhate pūjāṃ raveḥ pratyantare janaḥ  

sarvaduḥkhavimokṣaśca muktalābho hayasya ca 
siddhyanti sarvakāryāṇi vidho pratyantare dvija  

śastrabhītirgade pīḍā vahnimāddyamajīrṇatā 
pīḍā śatrukṛtā bhūrirbhaumapratyantare bhavet  

cāṇḍālena viradhaḥ syādbhayaṃ tebhyo dhanakṣatiḥ 
kaṣṭaṃ jīvāntare jñeyaṃ rāhoḥ pratyantare dhruvam  

dehapīḍā kalerbhītirbhayamantyajalokataḥ 
duḥkhaṃ śanyantare nānā śaneḥ prtyantare bhavet  

buddhināśaḥ kalerbhītirannapānādihānikṛt 
dhanhānirbhayaṃ śatroḥ saneḥ pratyantare budhe  

bandhaḥ śatrorgṛhe jāto varṇahānirbahukṣudhā 
citte cintā bhayaṃ trāsaḥ keto pratyantare bhavet  

cintitaṃ phalitaṃ vastu kalyāṇaṃ svajane sadā 
manuṣyakṛtito lābhaḥ bhṛgiḥ pratyantare dvija  

rājatejo'dhikāritvaṃ svagṛhe jāyate kaliḥ 
jvarādivyādhipīḍā ca raveḥ pratyantare bhavet  

sphītabuddhirmahārambho mandatejā bahuvyayaḥ 
bahustrībhiḥ samaṃ bhogo vidhoḥ pratyantare śanau  

tejohāni putraghāto vahnibhītī riporbhayam 
vātapittakṛtā pīḍā kujapratyantare bhavet  

dhananāśo vastrahānirbhūmināśo bhayaṃ bhavet 
videśagamanaṃ mṛtyuḥ rāho pratyantare śanau  

gṛheṣu svīkṛtaṃ chidraṃ hyasamartho nirīkṣaṇe 
atha vā kalimudvegaṃ guroḥ pratyantare vadet  

buddhirvidyārthalābho vā vastralābho mahatsukham 
budhāsyāntardaśāyāñca budhapratyantare bhavet  

kaṭhinānnasya samprāptirudare rogasambhavaḥ 
kāmalaṃ raktapittaṃ ca ketoḥ pratyantare bhavet  

uttarasyāṃ bhavellābho hāniḥ syāttu catuṣpadāt 
adhikāro nṛpāgāre bhṛgoḥ prtyanatare bhavet  

tejohānirbhavedrogastanupīḍā yadā kadā 
jāyate cittavaikalyaṃ raveḥ pratyantare budhe  

strīlābhaścārthasampattiḥ kanyālābho mahaddhanam 
labhate sarvataḥ saukhyaṃ vidhoḥ prtyantare janaḥ  

dharmadhīdhanasamprāptiścaurāgnyādiprapīḍanam 
raktavastraṃ śastraghātaṃ bhaumapratyantare bhavet  

kalaho jāyate strībhirakasmādbhayasambhavaḥ 
rājaśastrākṛtā bhītiḥ rāhiḥ prtyantare dvija  

rājyaṃ rājyādhikāro vā pūjā rājasamudbhavā 
vidyābuddhisamṛddhiśca guroḥ pratyantare bhavet  

vātapittamahāpīḍā dehaghātasamudbhavā 
dhananāśamavāpnoti śaneḥ pratyantare janaḥ  

āpatsamudbhavo'kasmāddeśantarasamāgamaḥ 
ketvantare'rthahāniśca ketoḥ pratyantare bhavet  

mlecchabhīrarthanāśo vā netrarogaḥ śirovyathā 
hāniścatuṣpadānāṃ ca bhṛgoḥ pratyantare bhavet  

mitraiḥ saha virodhaśca svalpamṛtyuḥ parājayaḥ 
matibhraṃśo vivādaśca raveḥ prtyantare bhavet  

annanāśo yaśohānirdehapīḍā matibhramaḥ 
āmavātādivṛddhiścavidhoḥ prtyantare bhavet  

śastraghātena pātena pīḍito vahnipīḍayā 
nīcādbhītī ripoḥ śaṅkā kujapratyantare bhavet  

kāminībhyo bhayaṃ bhūyāttathā vairisamudbhavaḥ 
kṣudrādapi bhavedbhītī rāhoḥ pratyantare bhavet  

dhanahānirmahotpāto sastramitravināśanam 
sarvatra labhate kleśaṃ guroḥ pratyantare phalam  

gomahiṣyādimaraṇaṃ dehapīḍā suhṛdvadhaḥ 
svalpālpalābhakaraṇaṃ śaneḥ pratyantare phalam  

buddhināśo mahodvego vidyāhānirmahābhayam 
kāryasiddhirna jāyate jñasya pratyantare phalam  

śvetāśvavastramuktādyaṃ divyastrījaṅgajaṃ sukham 
labhate śukrantare prāpte śukrapratyantare janaḥ  

vātajvaraḥ śiraḥpīḍā rājñaḥ pīḍā riporapi 
jāyate svalpalābho'pi raveḥ pratyantare phalam  

kanyājanma nṛpāllābho vastrābharaṇasaṃyutaḥ 
rājyādhikārasaṃprāptiḥ candrapratyantare bhavet  

raktapittādirogaśca kalahastāḍanaṃ bhavet 
mahānkleśo bhavedata kujapratyantare dvija  

kalaho jāyate strībhirakasmādbhayasambhavaḥ 
rājataḥ śatrutaḥ pīḍā rāhoḥ pratyantare bhavet  

mahaddravyaṃ mahadrājyaṃ vastrmuktādibhūṣaṇam 
gajāśvādipadaprāptiḥ guroḥ pratyantare bhavet  

kharoṣṭrachāgasamprāptirlohamāṣatilādikam 
labhate svalpapīḍādi śaneḥ pratyantare janaḥ  

dhanajñānamahallābho rājarājyādikāritā 
nikṣepāddhanalābho'pi jñasya pratyantare bhavet  

apamṛtyubhayaṃ jñeyaṃ deśāddeśāntarāgamaḥ 
lābho'pi jāyate madhye ketoḥ pratyantare dvija  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha sūkṣmāntardaśādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

guṇyā svasvadaśāvarṣaiḥ pratyantaradaśāmitiḥ 
khārkraibhaktā pṛthaglabdhiḥ sūkṣmāntaradaśā bhavet  

nijabhūmiparityāgo prāṇanāśabhayaṃ bhavet 
sthānanāśo mahāhāniḥ nijasūkṣmagate  ravau  

devabrāhmaṇbhaktiśca nityakarmaratastathā 
suprītiḥ sarvamitraścaiva raveḥ sūkṣmagate vidhau  

krūrakarmaratistigmaśatrubhiḥ paripīḍanam 
raktasrāvādirogaśca raveḥ sūkṣmagate kuje  

caurāgniviṣabhītiśca raṇe bhaṅgaḥ parājayaḥ 
dānadharmādihīnaśca raveḥ sūkṣmagate hyagau  

nṛpasatkārarājārhaḥ sevakaiḥ paripūjitaḥ 
rājacakṣurgataḥ śāntaḥ sūryasūkṣmagate gurau  

cauryasāhasakarmārthaṃ devabrāhmaṇapīḍanam 
sthānacyutiṃ manodukhaṃ raveḥ sūkṣmagate śanau  

divyāmbarādilabdhiśca divyastrīparibhogitā 
acintitārthasiddhiśca raveḥ sūkṣmagate budhe  

gurutārthavināśaśca bhṛtyadārabhavastathā 
kvacitsevakasambandho raveḥ sūkṣmagate dhvaje  

putramitrakalatrādisākhyasampanna eva ca 
nānāvidhā ca sampattī raveḥ sūkṣmagate bhṛgau  

bhūṣaṇaṃ bhūmilābhaśca sammānaṃ nṛpapūjanam 
tāmasattvaṃ gurutvaṃ ca nijasūkṣmagate vidhau  

duḥkhaṃ śatruvirodhaśca kukṣirogaḥ piturmṛtiḥ 
vātapittakaphodrekaḥ vidhoḥ sūkṣmagate kuje  

krodhanaṃ mitrabandhūnāṃ deśatyāgo dhanakṣayaḥ 
videśānnigaḍaprāptirvidhoḥ sūkṣmagatepyagau  

chatracāmarasaṃyuktaṃ vaibhavaṃ putrasampadaḥ 
sarvatra sukhamāpnoti vidhoḥ sūkṣmagate gurau  

rājopadravabhītiḥ syādvyavahāre dhanakṣayaḥ 
caurarvaṃ viprabhītiśca vidhoḥ sūkṣmagate śanau  

rājamānaṃ vastulābho videśādvāhanādikam 
putrapautrsamṛddhiśca vidhoḥ sūkṣmagate budhe  

ātmano vṛttihananaṃ sasyaśṛṅgavṛṣādibhiḥ 
agnisūryādibhītiḥ syādvidhoḥ sūkṣmagate dhvaje  

vivāho bhūmilābhaśca vastrābharaṇavaibhavam 
rājyalābhaśca kīrtiśca vidhoḥ sūkṣmagate bhṛgau  

kleśātkleśaḥ kāryanāśaḥ paśudhānyadhanakṣayaḥ 
gātravaiṣamyabhūmiśca vidhoḥ sūkṣmagate ravau  

bhūmihānirmanaḥkhedo hyapasmārī ca bandhuyuk 
purokṣobhamanastāpo nijasūkṣmagate kuje  

aṅgadoṣo janādbhītiḥ pramadāvaṃśanāśanam 
vahnisarpabhayaṃ ghoraṃ bhaume sūkṣmagate'pyahau  

devapūjāratiścātra mantrābhyutthānatatparaḥ 
loke pūjā pramodaśca bhaume sūkṣmagate gurau  

bandhanānmucyate baddho dhanadhānyaparicchadaḥ 
bhṛtyārthabahulaḥ śrīmān bhaume sūkṣmagate śanau  

vāhanaṃ chātrasaṃyuktaṃ rājyabhogaparaṃ sukham 
kāmaśvāsādikā pīḍā bhaume sūkṣmagate budhe  

parapretitabuddhiśca sarvatrā'pi ca garhitā 
aśuciḥ sarvakāleṣu bhaume sūkṣmagate dhvaje  

iṣṭastrībhogasampattiriṣṭabhojanasaṃgrahaḥ 
iṣṭārthasyāpi lābhaśca bhaume sūkṣmagate bhṛgau  

rājadveṣo dvijātkleśaḥ kāryābhiprayavaṃcakaḥ 
loke'pi nindyatāmeti bhaume sūkṣmagate ravau  

śuddhatvaṃ dhanasamprāptirdevabhāhmaṇvatsalaḥ 
vyādhinā paribhūyet bhaume sūkṣmagate vidhau  

lokopadravabuddhiśca sarvakārye mativibhramaḥ 
śūnyatā cittadoṣaḥ syāt svīye sūkṣmagate'pyagau  

dīrgharogī daridraśca sarveṣāṃ priyadarśanaḥ 
dānadharmarataḥ śasto rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate gurau  

kumārgātkutsitorthaśca duṣṭaśca parasevakaḥ 
asatsaṅgamatirmūḍho rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate śanau  

strīsambhogamatirvāgmī lokasambhāvanāvṛtaḥ 
annamicchaṃstanuglānī rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate budhe  

mādhuryaṃ mānahāniśca bandhanaṃ cāpramākaram 
pāruṣyaṃ jīvahāniśca rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate dhvaje  

bandhanānmucyate baddhaḥ sthānamānārthasañcayaḥ 
kāraṇād dravyalābhaśca rāhau sūkṣmagate bhṛgau  

vyaktārśo gulmarogaśca krodhahānistathaiva ca 
vāhanādisukhaṃ sarvaṃ rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate ravau  

maṇiratnadhanavāptirvidyopāsanaśīlavān 
devārcanaparo bhaktyā rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate vidhau  

nirjite janavidrāvo jane krodhaśca bandhanam 
cauryaśīlaratirnityaṃ rāhoḥ sūkṣmagate kuje  

śokanāśo dhanādhikyamagnihotraṃ śivārcanam 
vāhanaṃ chatrasaṃyuktaṃ svīye sūkṣmagate gurau  

vratabhaṅgo manastāpo videśe vasunāśanam 
virodho bandhuvairgaśca guroḥ sūkṣmagate śanau  

vidyābuddhivivṛddhiśca sasammānaṃ dhanāgamaḥ 
gṛhe sarvavidhaṃ saukhyaṃ guroḥ sūkṣmagate budhe  

jñānaṃ vibhavapāṇḍitye śāstraśrotā śivārcanam 
agnihotraṃ gurorbhaktirguroḥ sūkṣmagate dhvaje  

rogānmuktiḥ sukhaṃ bhogo dhanadhānyasamāgamaḥ 
putradārādisaukhyaṃ ca guroḥ sūkṣmagate bhṛgau  

vātapittaprakopaśca śleṣmodrekastu dāruṇaḥ 
rasavyādikṛtaṃ śūlaṃ guroḥ sūkṣmagate ravau  

chatracāmarasaṃyuktaṃ vaibhavaṃ putrasampadaḥ 
netrakukṣigatā pīḍā guroḥ sūkṣmagate vidhau  

srtījanācca viṣotpattirbandhanaṃ ca rujobhayam 
deśāntaragamo bhrāntirguroḥ sūkṣmagate kuje  

vyādhibhiḥ paribhūtaḥsyāccaurairapahṛtaṃ dhanam 
sarpavṛścikabhītiśca guroḥ sūkṣmagate'pyagau  

dhanahānirmahāvyādhiḥ vātapīḍā kulakṣayaḥ 
bhinnāhārī mahāduḥkhī nijasūkṣmagate śanau  

vāṇijyavṛtterlābhaśca vidyāvibhavameva ca 
strīlābhaśca mahīprāptiḥ śaneḥ sūkṣmagate budhe  

cauropadravakuṣṭhādivṛttikṣayavigumphanam 
sarvāṅgapīḍanaṃ vyādhiḥ śaneḥ sūkṣmagate dhvaje  

aiśvaryamāyudhābhyāsaḥ putralābho'bhiṣecanam 
ārogyaṃ dhanakāmau ca śaneḥ sūkṣmagate bhṛgau  

rājatejovikāratvaṃ svagṛhe jāyate kaliḥ 
kiñcitpīḍā svadehotthā śaneḥ sūkṣmagate ravau  

sphītabuddhirmahārambho mandatejā bahuvyayaḥ 
strīputraiśca samaṃ saukhyaṃ śaneḥ sūkṣmagate vidhau  

tejohānirmahodvego vahnimāndyaṃ bhramaḥ kaliḥ 
vātapittakṛtā pīḍā śaneḥ sūkṣmagate kuje  

pitṛmātṛvināśaśca manoduḥkhaṃ guruvyayam 
sarvatra viphalatvaṃ ca śaneḥ sūkṣmagate'pyahau  

sanmudrābhogasammānaṃ dhanadhānyavivarddhanam 
chatracāmarasamprāptiḥ śaneḥ sūkṣmagate gurau  

saubhāgyaṃ rājasammānaṃ dhanadhānyādisampadaḥ 
sarveṣāṃ priyadarśī ca nijasūkṣmagate budhe  

bālagrahognibhīstāpaḥ strīgadodbhavadoṣabhāk 
kumārgī kutsitāśī ca baudhe sūkṣmagate dhvaje  

vāhanaṃ dhanasampattirjalajānnārthasambhavaḥ 
śubhakīrtirmahābhogo baudhe sūkṣmagate bhṛgau  

tāḍanaṃ nṛpavaiṣamyaṃ buddhiskhalanarogabhāk 
hānirjanāpavādaṃ ca baudhe sūkṣmagate ravau  

subhagaḥ sthirabuddhiśca rājasanmānasampadaḥ 
suhṛdāṃ gurusaṃcāro baudhe sūkṣmagate vidhau  

agnidāho viṣotpattirjaḍatvaṃ ca daridratā 
vibhramaśca mahodvego baudhe sūkṣmagate kuje  

agnisarpanṛpādbhītiḥ kucchrādiriparābhavaḥ 
bhūtāveśabhramādbhrāntirbaudhe sūkṣmagatepyahau  

gṛhopakaraṇaṃ bhavyaṃ dānaṃ bhogādivaibhavam 
rājaprasādasampattirbaudhe sūkṣmagate gurau  

vāṇijyavṛttilābhaśca vidyāvibhavameva ca 
strīlābhaśca mahāvyāptirbaudhe sūkṣmagate śanau  

putradārādijaṃ duḥkhaṃ gātravaiṣamyameva ca 
dāridryād bhikṣuvṛttiśca naije sūkṣmagate dhvaje  

roganāśa'rthalābhaśca guruviprānuvatsalaḥ 
saṅgamaḥ svajanaiḥ sārddhaketoḥ sūkṣmagate bhṛgau  

yuddhaṃ bhūmivināśaśca vipravāsaḥ svadeśataḥ 
suhṛdvipātirārtiśca ketoḥ sūkṣmagate ravau  

dāsīdāsasamṛddhiśca yuddhe labdhirjayastathā 
lalitā kīrtirutpannā ketoḥ sūkṣmagate vidhau  

āsane bhayamaśvādeścauraduṣṭādipīḍanam 
gulmapīḍā śirorogaḥ ketoḥ sūkṣmagate kuje  

vināśaḥ strīgurūṇāṃ ca duṣṭastrīsaṅgamāllaghuḥ 
vamanaṃ rudhiraṃ pittaṃ ketoḥ sūkṣmagate'pyagau  

riporvirodhaḥ sampattiḥ sahasā rājavaibhavam 
paśukṣetravināśārtiḥ ketoḥ sūkṣmagate gurau  

mṛṣā pīḍā bhavetkṣudramukhotpattiśca laṅghanam 
strīvirodhaḥ satyahāniḥ ketoḥ sūkṣmagate śanau  

nānāvidhajanāptiśca viprayogo'ripīḍanam 
arthasampatsamṛddhiśca ketoḥ sūkṣmagate budhe  

śatruhānirmahatsaukhyaṃ śaṅkarālayanirmitiḥ 
taḍāgakūpanirmāṇaṃ nijasūkṣmagate bhṛgau  

urastāpo bhramaścaiva gatāgataviceṣṭitam 
kvacillābhaḥ kvaciddhānirbhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate ravau  

ārogyaṃ dhanasampāttiḥ kāryalābho gatāgataiḥ 
buddhividyāvivṛddhiḥ syād bhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate vidhau  

jaḍatvaṃ ripuvaiṣamyaṃ deśabhraṃśo mahadbhayam 
vyādhiduḥkhasamṛtpattirbhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate kuje  

rājyāgnisarpajā bhītirbandhunāśo guruvyathā 
sthānacyutirmahābhītirbhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate'pyahau  

sarvatra kāryalābhaśca kṣetrārthavibhavonnatiḥ 
vaṇigvṛttermahālabdhirbhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate gurau  

śatrupīḍā mahadduḥkhaṃ catuṣpādavināśanam 
svagotraguruhāniḥ syād bhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate śanau  

bāṇdhavādiṣu sampattirvyavahāro dhanonnatiḥ 
putradārāditaḥ saukhyaṃ bhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate budhe  

agnirogo mahāpīḍā mukhanetraśirovyathā 
sañcitārthātmanaḥ pīḍā bhṛgoḥ sūkṣmagate dhvaje  

medskiphrulemedskip

           atha prāṇadaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

pṛthak khagadaśāvarṣairhanyāt sūkṣmadaśāmitim 
khasūryairvibhajellibdharjñeya prāṇadaśāmitiḥ  

pāūṃścalyaṃ viṣajā bādhā caurāgninṛpajaṃ bhayam 
kaṣṭaṃ sūkṣmadaśākāle ravau prāṇadaśāṃ gate  

sukhaṃ bhojanasampattiḥ saṃskāro nṛpavaibhavam 
udārādikṛpābhiśca raveḥ prāṇagate vidhau  

bhūpopadravamanyārthe dravyanāśo mahadbhayam 
mahatyapacayaprāptī raveḥ prāṇagate kuje  

annodbhavā mahāpīḍā viṣotpattirviśeṣataḥ 
arthāgnirājabhiḥ kleśo raveḥ prāṇagate'pyahau  

nānāvidyārthasampattiḥ kāryalābho gatāgataiḥ 
nṛpaviprāśrame sūkṣme raveḥ prāṇagate gurau  

bandhanaṃ prāṇanāśaśca cittodvegastathaiva ca 
bahubādhā mahāhānī raveḥ prāṇagate śanau  

rājānnabhogaḥ satataṃ rājalāñchānatatpadam 
ātmā santarpayedeevaṃ raveḥ prāṇagate budhe  

anyo'nyaṃ kalahaścaiva vasuhāniḥ parājayaḥ 
gurustrībandhuvirgaiśca sūryaprāṇagate dhvaje  

rājapūjā dhanādhikyaṃ strīputrādibhavaṃ sukham 
annapānādibhogādi sūryaprāṇagate bhṛgau  

strīputrādisukhaṃ dravyaṃ labhate nūtanāmbaram 
yogasiddhiṃ samādhiñca nijaprāṇagate vidhau  

kṣayaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ bandhunāśaṃ raktasrāvānmahadbhayam 
bhūtāveśādi jāyate vidhoḥ prāṇagate kuje  

sarpabhītiviśeṣāṇa bhūtopadravān sadā 
dṛṣṭikṣobho matibhraṃśo vidhoḥ prāṇagate'pyahau  

dharmavṛddhiḥ kṣamāprāptirdevabrāhmaṇapūjanam 
saubhāgyaṃ priyadṛṣṭiśca candraprāṇagate gurau  

sahasā dehapatanaṃ śatrūpadravavedanā 
andhatvaṃ ca dhanaprāptiścandraprāṇagate śanau  

cāmaracchatrasamprāptī rājyalābho nṛpāttataḥ 
samatvaṃ sarvabhūteṣu candraprāṇagate budhe  

śastrāgniripujā pīḍā viṣāgniḥ kukṣirogatā 
putradāraviyogaśca candraprāṇagate dhvaje  

putramitrakalatrāptivideśācca dhanāgamaḥ 
sukhasampattirarthaśca candraprāṇagate bhṛgau  

krūratā kopavṛddhiśca prāṇahānirmanovyathā 
deśatyāgo mahābhītiścandraprāṇagate ravau  

kalaho ripubhirbandhaḥ raktapittādirogabhīḥ 
nijasūkṣmadaśāmadhye kuja prāṇagate phalam  

vicyutaḥ sutadāraiśca bandhūpadravapīḍitaḥ 
prāṇatyāgo viṣeṇaiva bhaumaprāṇagate'pyahau  

devārcanaparaḥ srīmānmantānuṣṭhānatatparaḥ 
putrapautrasukhāvāptirbhaumaprāṇagate gurau  

agnibādhā bhavenmṛtyurarthanāśaḥ padacyutiḥ 
bandhubhibandhutāvāptirbhaumaprāṇagate śanau  

divyāmbarasamutpattirdivyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
divyāṅganāyāḥ samprāptirbhaumaprāṇagate budhe  

patanotpātipīḍā ca netrakṣobho mahadbhayam 
bhujaṅgād dravyahāniśca bhaumaprāṇagate dhvaje  

dhanadhānyādisampattirlokapūjā sukhāgamā 
nānābhogairbhavedbhogī bhaumaprāṇagate bhṛgau  

jvaronmādaḥ kṣayo'rthasya rājavisnehasambhavaḥ 
dīrgharogī daridraḥ syādbhaumaprāṇagate ravau  

bhojanādisukhaprāptirvastrābharaṇajaṃ sukham 
śītoṣṇavyādhipīḍā ca bhaumaprāṇagate vidhau  

annāśane viraktaśca viṣabhītistathaiva ca 
sāhasāddhananāśaśca rāhau prāṇagate bhavet  

aṅgasaukhyaṃ vinirbhītirvāhanādeśca saṅgatā 
nīciḥ kalahasamprāptī rāhoḥ prāṇagate gurau  

gṛhadāhaḥ śarīre ruṅ nīcairapahṛta dhanam 
tathā bandhanasamprāptī rāhoḥ prāṇagate śanau  

gurūpadeśavibhavo gurusatkāravarddhanam 
guṇavāñchīlavāṃścāpi rāhoḥ prāṇagate budhe  

strīputrādivirodhaśca gṛhānniṣkramaṇādapi 
sāhasātkāyahāniśca rāhoḥ prāṇagate dhvaje  

chatravāhanasampattiḥ sarvārthaphalasañcayaḥ 
śivārcanagṛhārambho rāhoḥ prāṇagate bhṛgau  

arśādirogabhītiśca rājyopadravasambhavaḥ 
catuṣpādādihāniśca rāhoḥ prāṇagate ravau  

saumanasyaṃ ca sadbuddhiḥ satkāro gurudarśanam 
pāpādbhītirmanaḥsaukhyaṃ rāhoḥ prāṇagate vidhau  

cāṇḍālāgnivaśādbhītiḥ svapadacyutirāpadaḥ 
malinaḥ śvādivṛttiśca rāhoḥ prāṇagate kuje  

harṣāgamo dhanādhikyamagnihotraṃ śivārcanam 
vāhanaṃ chatrasaṃyuktaṃ nija prāṇagate gurau  

vratahānirviṣādaśca videśe dhananāśanam 
virodho bandhuvargaiśca guroḥ prāṇagate śanau  

vidyābuddhivivṛddhiśca loke pūjā dhanāgamaḥ 
strīputrādisukhaprāptirguroḥ prāṇagate budhe  

jñānaṃ vibhavapāṇḍityaṃ śāstrajñānaṃ śivārcanam 
agnihotraṃ gurorbhaktirguroḥ prāṇagate dhvaje  

rogānmuktiḥ sukhaṃ bhogo dhanadhānyasamāgamaḥ 
putradārādijaṃ saukhyaṃ guroḥ prāṇagate bhṛgau  

vātapittaprakopaṃ ca śleṣmodrekaṃ tu dāruṇam 
rasavyādhikṛtaṃ śūlaṃ guroḥ prāṇagate ravau  

chatracāmarasaṃyuktaṃ vaibhavaṃ putrasampadaḥ 
netrakukṣigatā pīḍā guroḥ prāṇagate vidhau  

strījanācca viṣotpattirbandhanaṃ cātinigrahaḥ 
deśāntaragamo bhrāntirguroḥ prāṇagate kuje  

vyādhibhiḥ paribhūtaḥ syāccaurairapahṛtaṃ dhanam 
sarpavṛścikabhītiśca guroḥ prāṇagate'pyahau  

jvareṇa jvalitā kāntiḥ kuṣṭharogodarādiruk 
jalāgnikṛtamṛtyuḥ syānnijaprāṇagate śanau  

dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ ca māṅgalyaṃ vyavahārābhipūjanam 
devabrāhmaṇabhaktiśca śaneḥ prāṇagate budhe  

mṛtyuvedanaduḥkhaṃ ca bhūtopadravasambhavaḥ 
paradārābhibhūtatvaṃ śaneḥ prāṇagate dhvaje  

putrārthavibhavaiḥ saukhyaṃ kṣitipālāditaḥ sukham 
agnihotraṃ vivāhaśca śaneḥ prāṇagate bhṛgau  

akṣipīḍā śirovyādhiḥ sarpaśatrubhayaṃ bhavet 
arthahānirmahākleśaḥ śaneḥ prāṇagate ravau  

ārogyaṃ putralābhaśca śāntipauṣṭikavardhanam 
devabrāhmaṇabhaktiśca śaneḥ prāṇagate vidhau  

gulmarogaḥ śatrubhītirmṛgayā prānanāśanam 
sarpāgniviṣato bhītiḥ śaneḥ prāṇagate kuje  

deśatyāgo nṛpādbhītirmohanaṃ viṣabhakṣaṇam 
vātapittakṛtā pīḍā śaneḥ prāṇagate'pyahau  

senāpatyaṃ bhūmilābhaḥ saṃgamaḥ svajanaiḥ saha 
gauravaṃ nṛpasammānaṃ śaneḥ prāṇagate gurau  

ārogyaṃ sukhasampattirdharmakarmādisādhanam 
samatvaṃ sarvabhuteṣu nijaprāṇagate budhe  

vahnitaskarato bhītiḥ paramādhirviṣodbhavaḥ 
dehāntakaraṇaṃ duḥkhaṃ budhaprāṇagate dhvaje  

prabhutvaṃ dhanasampattiḥ kīrtirdharmaḥ śivārcanam 
putradārādikaṃ saukhyaṃ budhaprāṇagate bhṛgau  

antardāho jvaronmādau bāndhavānāṃ rati striyāḥ 
prāpyate steeyasampattirbudhaprāṇagate ravau  

strīlābhaścārthasampattiḥ kanyālābho dhanāgamaḥ 
labhate sarvataḥ saukhyaṃ budhaprāṇagate vidhau  

patitaḥ kukṣirogī ca dantanetrādijā vyathā 
arśāṃsi prāṇasandeho budhaprāṇagate kuje  

vastrābharaṇasampattirviyogo vipravairitā 
sannipātodbhavaṃ dukhaṃ budhaprāṇagate'pyahau  

gurutvaṃ dhanasampattirvidyā sadguṇasaṃgrahaḥ 
vyavasāyena sallābho budhaprāṇagate gurau  

cauryeṇa nidhanaprāptirvidhanatvaṃ daridratā 
yācakatvaṃ viśeṣeṇa budhaprāṇagate śanau  

aśvapātena ghātaśca śatrutaḥ kalahāgamaḥ 
nirvicāravadhotpattirnijaprāṇagate dhvaje  

kṣetralābho vairināśo hayalābho manaḥsukham 
paśukṣetradhanāptiśca ketoḥ prāṇagate bhṛgau  

steyāgniripubhītiśca dhanahānirmanovyathā 
prāṇāntakaraṇaṃ kaṣṭaṃ ketoḥ prāṇagate ravau  

devadvijaguroḥ pūjā dīrghayātrā dhanaṃ sukham 
karṇe vā locane rogaḥ ketoḥ prāṇagate vidhau  

pittarogo nasāvṛddhirvibhramaḥ sannipātajaḥ 
svabandhujanavidveṣaḥ ketoḥ prāṇagate kuje  

virodhaḥ strīsutādyaiśca gṛhānniṣkramaṇaṃ bhavet 
svasāhasātkāryahāniḥ ketoḥ prāṇagate'pyahau  

sastravraṇairmahārogo hṛtpīḍādisamudbhavaḥ 
sutadāraviyogaśca ketoḥ prāṇagate gurau  

mativibhramatīkṣṇatvaṃ krūrakarmaratiḥ sadā 
vyavasanādbandhanaṃ duḥkhaṃ ketoḥ prāṇagate śanau  

kusumaṃ śayanaṃ bhūṣā lepanaṃ bhojanādikam 
saukhyaṃ sarvāṅgabhogyaṃ ca ketoḥ prāṇagate budhe  

jñānamīśvarabhaktiśca santoṣaśca dhanāgamaḥ 
putrapautrasamṛddhiśca nijaprāṇagate bhṛgau  

lokaprakāśakīrtiśca sutasaukhyavivarjitaḥ 
uṣṇādirogajaṃ dukhaṃ śukraprāṇagate ravau  

devārcane karmaratirmantratoṣaṇatatparaḥ 
dhanasaubhāgyasampattiḥ śukraprāṇagate vidhau  

jvaro masūrikāsphoṭakaṇḍūcipiṭakādikāḥ 
devabrāhmaṇapūjā ca śukraprāṇagate kuje  

nityaṃ śatrukṛtā pīḍā netrakukṣirujādayaḥ 
virodhaḥ suhṛdāṃ pīḍā śukraprāṇagate'pyahau  

āyurārogyamaiśvaryaṃ putrastrīdhanavaibhavam 
chatravāhanasaṃprāptiḥ śukraprāṇagate gurau  

rājopadravajā bhītiḥ sukhahānirmahārujaḥ 
nīcaiḥ saha vivādaśca bhṛgoḥ prāṇagate śanau  

santoṣo rājasammānaṃ nānādigbhūmisampadaḥ 
nityamutsāhavrddhiḥ syācchukraprāṇagate budhe  

jīvitātmayaśohānirdhanadhānyaparikṣayaḥ 
tyāgabhogadhanāni syuḥ śukraprāṇagate dhvaje  

evamṛkṣadaśānāṃ hi sāntarāgāṃ mayā dvija 
phalāni kathitānyatra saṃkṣepādeva te'grataḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha kālacakrāntardaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

jagaddhitāya proktāni purā yāni purāriṇā 
tāni cakrāntardaśāphalāni kathayāmyaham  

meṣāṃśe svāntare bhaume jvaraśca vraṇasambhavaḥ 
budhaśukrendujīveṣu sukhaṃ śatrubhayaṃ ravau  

vṛṣāṃśe svāntare saure kalaho rogasambhavaḥ 
vidyālābhastanau saukhyaṃ gurau tatra gate phalam  

deśatyāgo mṛtirvāpi śastraghāto jvaro'thavā 
vṛṣabhasvāṃśake vipra kuje tatra gate phalam  

vastrābharaṇalābhaśca strīsuyogo mahat sukham 
śukrendusutacandreṣu vṛṣabhasvāṃśake phalam  

nṛpād bhayaṃ pitṛmṛtiḥ svavadādyairbhayaṃ ravau 
mithune svāṃśake śukre dhanavastrasamāgamaḥ  

pitṛmātṛmṛterbhītirjvaraśca vraṇasambhavaḥ 
dūradeśaprayāṇaṃ ca mithune svāṃśake kuje  

buddhividyāvivṛddhiśca mahāvibhavasambhavaḥ 
loke mānaśca prītiśca mithene svāṃśake gurau  

videśagamanaṃ vyādhirmaraṇaṃ dhananāśanam 
bandhunāśo'thavā vipra mithune svāṃśake śanau  

vidyāvastrādilābhaśca dāraputrādijaṃ sukham 
sarvatra mānamāpnoti mithune svāṃśake budhe  

karka svāṃśagate candre putradārasukhaṃ mahat 
aiśvaryaṃ labhate loke mānaṃ prītiṃ tathaiva ca  

śatrubhyaśca paśubhyaśca bhayaṃ rājakulāt tathā 
ādhivyādhibhayaṃ caiva karke svāṃśagate ravau  

putradārasuhṛtsaukhyaṃ dhanavṛddhistathaiva ca 
loke mānaṃ yaśaścaiva karkāṃśe budhaśukrayoḥ  

viṣaśastramṛterbhītiṃ jvararogādisambhavām 
pīḍāṃ caiva samāpnoti karke svāṃśagate kuje  

vibhavasyātilābhaśca śarīre'pi sukhaṃ tathā 
nṛpāt sammānalābhaśca karke svāṃśagate gurau  

vādavyādhibhayaṃ ghoraṃ sarpavṛścikato bhayam 
nānākaṣṭamavāpnoti karke svāṃśagate śanau  

siṃhāṃśe svāṃśage bhaume mukharogabhayaṃ diśet 
pittajvarakṛtāṃ vādhāṃ śastrakṣatamathāpi vā  

dhanavastrādilābhaśca strīputrādisukhaṃ tathā 
budhabhārgavayorvipra siṃhāṃśe svāntarasthayoḥ  

uccāt patanabhītiśca svalpadravyasamāgamaḥ 
videśagamanaṃ caiva siṃhe svāntargate vidhau  

bhayaṃ śatrujanebhyaśca jvarādivyāddhisambhavaḥ 
jñānahānirmṛterbhītiḥ siṃhe svāntargate ravau  

dhanadhānyādilābhaṃ ca prasādaṃ dvijabhūpayoḥ 
vidyāvṛddhimavāpnoti siṃhe svāntargate gurau  

kanyāyāṃ svāṃśage saure kaṣṭaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ 
drayāṇaṃ ca jvaraṃ caiva kṣudbhavaṃ vaiklavaṃ tathā  

nṛpaprasādamaiśvaryaṃ suhṛdbandhusamāgamam 
vidyāvṛddhimavāpnoti kanyāyāṃ svāṃśake gurau  

pittajvarabhavā pīḍā videśe gamanaṃ tathā 
śastraghāto'gnibhītiśca kanyāyāṃ svāntare kuje  

bhṛtyaputrārthalābhaśca nānāsukhasamāgamaḥ 
bandhubhārgavacandreṣu kanyāsvāṃśagateṣu ca  

prayāṇaṃ rogabhītiśca kalaho bandhubhiḥ saha 
śastraghātabhayaṃ caiva kanyāṃśe svāṃśage ravau  

tule svāntargate śukre sadbuddhiśca sukhodayaḥ 
strīputradhananavastrādilābho bhavati niścitaḥ  

pitṛkaṣṭaṃ suhṛdvairaṃ śirorogo jvarodayaḥ 
viṣaśastrāgnibhītiśca tule svāntargate kuje  

dravyaratnādilābhaśca dharmakāryaṃ nṛpādayaḥ 
sarvatra sukhasamprāptistule svāṃśagate gurau  

prayāṇaṃ ca mahāvyādhiḥ kṣetradeḥ kṣatireva ca 
śatruvādhā ca kāryeṣu tule svāṃśagate śanau  

putrajanma dhanaprāptiḥ strīsukhaṃ ca manaḥpriyam 
bhāgyodayaśca vijneyastule svāntargate budhe  

śaśāṅkabudhaśukreṣu vṛścike svāṃśageṣu ca 
nānādhānyadhanaprāptirvyādhivināśo mahat sukham  

śatrukṣobhabhayaṃ vyādhimarthanāśaṃ piturbhayam 
śvāpadād bhayamāpnoti vṛścike svāṃśage ravau  

vātapittabhayaṃ caiva masūrīvraṇamādiśet 
agniśastrādibhītiśca vṛścike svāṃśage kuje  

dhanaṃ dhānyañca ratnaṃ ca devabrāhmaṇapūjanam 
rājaprasādamāpnoti vṛścike svāṃśage gurau  

dhanabandhuvināśaśca jāyate mānasī vyathā 
śatruvādhā mahāvyādhirvṛścike svāṃśage śanau  

atidāhaṃ jvaraṃ chardi mukharogaṃ viśeṣataḥ 
nānākleśamavāpnoti cāpāṃśe svāṃśage kuje  

śriyaṃ vidyāṃ ca saubhāgyaṃ śatrunāśaṃ nṛpāt sukham 
bhārgavenducandrāṇāṃ cāpe svasvāṃśake diśet  

bhāryāvittavināśaṃ ca kalahaṃ ca nṛpād bhayam 
dūrayātrāmavāpnoti cāpāṃśe svāṃśage ravau  

dānadharmatapolābhaṃ rājapūjanamāpnuyāt 
bhāryāvibhavalābhaṃ ca cāpe svāṃśagate gurau  

dvijadevanṛpodbhūtaṃ kopaṃ bandhuvināśanam 
deśatyāgamavāpnoti makarasvāṃśage śanau  

devārcanaṃ tapodhyānaṃ sammānaṃ bhūpateḥ kule 
bhārgavajñendujīvānāṃ mṛgāṃśe'ntardaśāphalam  

śirorogaṃ jvaraṃ caiva karapādakṣataṃ diśet 
raktapittātisārāṃśca mṛgasvāṃśagate kuje  

vināśaṃ pitṛbandhūnāṃ jvararogādikaṃ diśet 
nṛpaśatrubhayaṃ caiva mṛgāṃśasvāṃśage śanau  

nānāvidyārthalābhaśca putrastrīmitrajaṃ sukham 
śarīrārogyamaiśvaryaṃ kumbhe svāṃśagate bhṛgau  

jvarāgnicorajā pīḍā śatruṇāṃ ca mahad bhayam 
manovyathāmavāpnoti ghaṭāṃśasvāntare kuje  

nairujyaṃ ca sukhaṃ caiva sammānaṃ bhūpateḥ dvijāt 
manaḥprasādamāpnoti kumbhāṃśasvāṃśage gurau  

dhātutrayaprakopaṃ ca kalahaṃ deśavibhramam 
kṣayavyādhimavāpnoti kuṃbhāṃśasvāṃśage śanau  

putramitradhanastrīṇāṃ lābhaṃ caiva manaḥpriyam 
saubhāgyavṛddhimāpnoti kumbhāṃśasvāṃśage budhe  

vidyāvṛddhimavāpnoti strīsukhaṃ vyādhināśanam 
suhṛtsaṅgaṃ manaḥprītiṃ mīnāṃśasvāṃśage vidhau  

bandhubhiḥ kalahaṃ caiva caurabhītiṃ manovyathām 
sthānabhraṃśamavāpnoti mīnāṃśasvāṃśage ravau  

raṇe vijayamāpnoti paśubhūmisutāgamam 
dhanavṛddhiśca mīnāṃśe svāṃśayorbudhaśukrayoḥ  

pittarogaṃ vivādañca svajanairapi mānavaḥ 
śatruṇāṃ bhayamāpnoti mīnāṃśasvāṃśage kuje  

dhanavastrakalatrāṇāṃ lābho bhūpasamādaraḥ 
pratiṣṭhā bahudhā loke mīnāṃśasvāṃśage gurau  

dhananāśo manastāpo veśyādīnāṃ ca saṅgamāt 
deśatyāgo bhavedvāpi mīnāṃśasvāṃśage śanau  

evaṃ prājñaiśca vijñeyaṃ kālacakradaśāphalam 
antardaśāphalaṃ caiva vāmarkṣe'pyevameva ca  

idaṃ phalaṃ mayā proktaṃ dharmā'dharmakṛtaṃ purā 
tatsarvaṃ pāṇibhirnityaṃ prāpyate nā'tra saṃśayaḥ  

suhṛdo'ntardaśā bhavyā pāpasyāpi dvijottama 
śubhasyāpi ripoścaivamaśubhā ca prakīrtitā  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha kālacakranavāṃśadaśāphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

meṣe tu raktajā pīḍā vṛṣabhe dhānyavarddhanam 
mithune jñānavṛddhiśca karke dhanapatirbhavet  

siṃhabhe śatrubādhā syāt kanyāyāṃ strījanāt sukham 
tulabhe rājamantritvaṃ vṛścike mṛtyuto bhayam  

arthalābho bhaveccāpe meṣasya navabhāgake 
phalamevaṃ vijānīyaṃ daśākāle dvijottama  

makare pāpakarmāṇi kumbhe vāṇijyato dhanam 
mīne sarvārthasiddhiśca vṛścike vahnito bhayam  

tulabhe rājapūjā ca kanyāyāṃ śatruto bhayam 
karke patnījane kaṣṭaṃ siṃhabhe netrapīḍanam  

mithune viṣato bhītirvṛṣasya navamāṃśake 
vṛṣabhe dhanalābhaḥ sthānmeṣe tu jvarasaṃbhavaḥ  

mīne ca mātulaprītiḥ kumbhe śatrupravardhanam 
makare corato bhītiścāpe vidyāvivardhanam  

meṣe tu śastrasaṃghāto vṛṣe tu kalaho bhavet 
mithune sukhamāpnoti mithunāṃśe phalaṃ tvidam  

karkaṭe sukhamāpnoti siṃhe bhūpālato bhayam 
kanyāyāṃ bandhutaḥ saukhyaṃ tulabhe kīrtimāpnuyāt  

vṛścike ca pituḥ kaṣṭaṃ cāpe jñānadhanāgamaḥ 
makare tvayaśo loke kumbhe vāṇijyataḥ kṣatiḥ  

mīne sukhamāpnoti karkāṃśe phalamīdṛśam 
vṛścike kalahaḥ pīḍā tulabhe sukhasampadaḥ  

kanyāyāṃ dhanadhānyāni karke paśugaṇād bhayam 
siṃhe sukhaṃ ca duḥkhaṃ ca mithune śatruvardhanam  

vṛṣe ca sukhasampattiḥ meṣe kaṣṭamavāpnuyāt 
mīne tu dīrghayātrā syāt siṃhāṃśe phalamīdṛśam  

kumbhabhe dhanalābhaḥ syānmakare'pi dhanāgamaḥ 
cāpe bhrātṛjanāt saukhyaṃ meṣe mātṛsukhaṃ vadet  

vṛṣabhe putrasaukhyaṃ ca mithune śatruto bhayam 
karke dārajanaiḥ prītiḥ siṃhe vyādhivivardhanam  

kanyāyāṃ ca sutotpattiḥ kanyāṃśe phalamīdṛśam 
tulabhe dhanasampattirvṛścike bhrātṛtaḥ sukham  

pitṛvargasukhaṃ cāpe mātṛkaṣṭaṃ mṛge vadet 
kumbhe vāṇijyato lābhaṃ mīne ca sukhasampadam  

vṛścike ca strīyāḥ pīḍā tule ca jalato bhayam 
kanyāyāṃ sukhasampattistulāṃśe phalamīdṛśam  

karkabhe dhanahāniḥ syāt siṃhe bhūpālato bhayam 
mithune bhūmilābhaśca vṛśabhe dhanasampadaḥ  

meṣe tu raktajā pīḍā mīne ca sukhamādiśet 
kumbhe vāṇijyato lābho makare ca dhanakṣitaḥ  

cāpe ca sukhasampattirvṛścikāṃśe phalaṃ tvidam 
meṣe ca dhanalābhaḥ syāt vṛṣe bhūmivivarddhanam  

mithune sarvasiddhiḥ syāt karkabhe sukhasampadaḥ 
siṃhe sarvasukhotpattiḥ kanyāyāṃ kalahāgamaḥ  

tule vāṇjyato lābho vṛścike rogajaṃ bhayam 
cāpe putrasukhaṃ vācyaṃ dhanuraṃśe phalaṃ tvidam  

makare putralābhaḥ syāt kumbhe dhanavivardhanam 
mīne kalyāṇamāpnoti vṛścike paśuto bhayam  

tulabhe tvarthalābhaḥ syāt kanyāyāṃ śatruto bhayam 
karkaṭe śriyamāpnoti siṃhe śatru janād bhayam  

mithune viṣato bhītirmṛgāṃśe phalamīdṛśam 
vṛśabhe dhanasampattirmeṣe netrarujo bhayam  

mīnabhe dīrghayātrā syāt kumbhe dhanavivardhanam 
makare sarvasiddhiḥ syāccāpe jñānavivardhanam  

meṣe saukhyavināśaḥ syāt vṛṣabhe maraṇaṃ bhavet 
mithune sukhasampattiḥ kumbhāṃśe phalamīdṛśam  

karkaṭe dhanavṛddhiḥ syāt siṃhe rājāśrayaṃ vadet 
kanyāyāṃ dhanadhānyāni tule vāṇijyato dhanam  

vṛścike jvarajā pīḍā cāpe jñānasukhodayaḥ 
makare strīvirodhaḥ syāt kumbhe ca jalato bhayam  

mīne tu sarvasaubhāgyaṃ mīnāṃśe phalamīdṛśam 
daśādyaṃśakrameṇaiva jñātvā sarvaphalaṃ vadet  

krūragrahadaśākāle śāntiṃ kuryād vidhānataḥ 
tataḥ śubhamavāpnoti taddaśāyāṃ na saṃśayaḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

           athāṣṭakavargādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

bhagavan bhavatā'khyātaṃ grahabhāvādijaṃ phalam 
bahunāmṛṣivaryāṇāmācāryāṇāṃ ca sammatam  

saṃkarāt tatphalānāṃ ca grahāṇāṃ gatisaṅkarāt 
itthameveti no sarve jñātvā vaktumalaṃ narāḥ  

kalau pāparatānāṃ ca mandā buddhiryuto nṛṇām 
ato'lpabuddhigamyaṃ yat śāstrametad vadasya me  

tattatkālagrahasthityā mānavānāṃ parisphuṭam 
sukhaduḥkhaparijñānamāyuṣo nirṇayaṃ tathā  

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā brahman kathayāmi tavāgrataḥ 
lokeyātrāparijñānamāyuṣo nirṇayaṃ tathā  

saṃkarasyāvirodhañca śāstrasyāpi prayojanam 
janānāmupakārārthaṃ sāvadhānamanāḥ śṛṇu  

lagnādivyayaparyantaṃ bhāvā saṃjñānurūpataḥ 
phaladāḥ śubhasaṃdṛṣṭā yuktā vā śobhanā matāḥ  

te tūccādibhagaiḥ kheṭairna cāstāribhanīcagaiḥ 
pāpairdṛṣṭayutā bhāvāḥ kalyāṇetaradāyakāḥ  

tairaḥtāribhanīcasthairna ca mitrasvabhoccagaiḥ 
evaṃ samānyataḥ proktaṃ horāśāstrajñasūribhiḥ  

mayaiyat sakalaṃ proktaṃ pūrvācāryānuvartinā 
āyuśca lokayātrāṃ ca śāstrasyāsyate prayojanam  

niścetuṃ tanna saknoti vasiṣṭho vā bṛhaspatiḥ 
kiṃ punarmanujāstatra viśeṣāttu kalau yuge  

sāmānyāṃśo viśeṣāṃśo jyotiḥśāstraṃ dvidhoditam 
proktaḥ sāmānyabhāgastu niścayāṃśastu kathyate  

yathā lagnācca candrācca grahāṇāṃ bhāvajaṃ phalam 
tathā'nyebhyo'pi kheṭebhyo vicintyaṃ daivavidvaraiḥ  

ato ravyādikheṭānāṃ salagnānāṃ pṛthak pṛthak 
aṣṭānāṃ sarvabhāvotthaṃ yathoktamaśubhaṃ śubham  

jñātvā'dau karaṇaṃ sthānaṃ bindurekhopalakṣitam 
kramādaṣṭakavargasya vācyaṃ spaṣṭaphalaṃ yathā  

tatusvāyustririṣpheṣu pañca kāme sukhe'rṇavāḥ 
arau bhāgye trayaḥ putre ṣaṭ karau khe bhave ca bhūḥ  

lagnendujīvaśukrajñāstanau sve maraṇe'pi ca 
ravibhaumārki candrāryā vyaye jñendusitāyakāḥ  

sukhe horenduśukrāśca dharme'rkārkikujā arau 
horājñāryendavaḥ kāme bhave daityendrapūjitaḥ  

sahaje'rkārkiśukrāryabhaumāḥ khe gurubhārgavau 
sute'rkārkīndulagnāraśukrāḥ syuḥ karaṇaṃ raveḥ  

bhāgyasvayośca ṣaḍ veśmamṛtihorāsu pañca ca 
mānaduścikyayorekaḥ sute vedā aristriyoḥ  

trayo vyayeṣṭāvāye ca śūnyaṃ śītakarasya tu 
horārkārārkibhṛgavoṅgajñārkendvārkabhārgavāḥ  

jīvorkārkīndulagnārā horendugurubhāskarāḥ 
sitajñāryāḥ kujatanumandāste sitaśītagū  

horārkārārkivijjīvāḥ śaniḥ khaṃ sakalāḥ kramāt 
vyayaveśmasutastrīṣu ṣaḍ sapta dhanadharmayoḥ  

horāmṛtyuvoḥ śarā vedā vikrame khe trayaḥ kṣate 
dvau bhave śūnyamevaṃ syāt karaṇaṃ bhūmijasya tu  

kujasyārkenduvijjīvasita lagnaśanī ca tu 
sitāragurumandāḥ syurdharmokteṣu kujaṃ vinā  

candrāraguruśukrārkilagnāni kujabhāskarī 
jñendvarkasitalagnāryā eṣu śukraṃ vinā tataḥ  

vinā śaniṃ sapta dharme sitendujñā viyattataḥ 
arkārkijñendulagnārāḥ karaṇaṃ procyate kramāt  

tanusvagṛhakarmāridharmeṣvagnirmṛgau karau 
bhrātṛstriyo rasā lābhe śūnyaṃ putre vyaye śarāḥ  

budhāsyarkenduguravo gurusūryabudhāḥ kramāt 
lagnārkārārkicandrāryā jñārkāryā hi budhasya tu  

jīvārendvārkilagnāni śukramannadharāsutāḥ 
jñendulagnārkaśukrāryā jñārkau jīvendulagnakāḥ  

arkāryaśukraḥ śūnyaṃ ca horendvārārkibhārgavāḥ 
rūpaṃ dhanāyayoḥ khe dvau vyaye sapta kṣate'rṇavāḥ  

mṛtivikramayo pañca guroḥ śeṣeṣu vanhiyaḥ 
lagne śukrendumandāḥ sve āye mandaśca vikrame  

lagnārendujñabhṛgavaḥ suterkāryakujā gṛhe 
śukramandendavo dyūne budhaśukraśanaiścarāḥ  

jīvārārkendavaḥ śatrau sarve mandaṃ vinā vyaye 
karmaṇīnduśanī dharme mandāraguravo mṛgau  

lagnārkisitacandrajñāḥ karaṇaṃ ca guroridam 
sutāyurvikrameṣvakṣi tanusvavyayakheṣviṣuḥ  

aṣṭau striyāmarau ṣaḍ bhūrdharme mitre'kṣi khaṃ bhave 
lagne sve'rkāravijjīvamandāḥ sarve ca kāmabhe  

arkāryau vikramasthāne sute'rkārau śubhe raviḥ 
sukhe'kabudhajīvāḥ syurbhaumajñau mṛtibhe dvaja  

śukrārkendvārkilagnāryāḥ śatrau śūnyaṃ bhave vyaye 
horārkibudhaśukrāryāstanvārajñendvināśca khe  

svastrīdharmeṣu saptāṅgaṃ mṛtihorāgṛheṣu ca 
ājñābhrātṛvyaye vedā rūpaṃ śatrau sute śarāḥ  

āye śūnyaṃ śanerevaṃ karaṇaṃ procyate budhaiḥ 
gṛhe tanau ca lagnārkau svastriyośca raviṃ vinā  

hitvā dharme budhaṃ māne lagnāraravicandrajān 
tato bhrātari jīvārkabudhaśukrāḥ kṣate raviḥ  

vyaye lagnendumandārkāḥ sitārkandujñalagnakāḥ 
sute mṛtau budhārkau ca hitvā'ye khaṃ śanervidaḥ  

uktā'nye sthānadātāra iti sthānaṃ vidurbudhāḥ 
atha sthānagrahān vakṣye sukhabodhāya suriṇām  

svāyastanuṣu mandārasūryā jīvabudhau sute 
vikrame jñendulagnāni lagnārkārkikujā gṛhe  

te ca jñendū khabhe cā'ye sarve śukraṃ vinā vyaye 
lagnaśukrabudhāḥ śatrau te ca jīvasudhākarau  

dyūne'rkārārkiśukrāśca dharmerkārārkividguruḥ 
jñendujīvāḥ kujāryau jñārkendvārārkitanūśanāḥ  

jīvaśukrabudhā bhaumabudhaśukraśanaiścarāḥ 
ravīndvārārkilagnāni ravīndvāryajñabhārgavāḥ  

arkajñajīvāḥ śukrendū te ca tau lagnabhūsutau 
sarve śūnyaṃ kramātproktaṃ sthānaṃ śītakarasya ca  

lagnamandakujā bhaumo horājñendudinādhipāḥ 
mandārau jñaravī jñendujīvārkatanubhārgavāḥ  

mandārau tau sita ścārkiḥ kujārkāryārkilagnakāḥ 
sarve gurusitau sthānaṃ bhaumastaivaṃ vidurbudhāḥ  

lagnamandāraśukrajñā lagnārendusitārkajāḥ 
śukrajñau lagnacandrārkisitārā jñārkabhārgavāḥ  

jīvajñārkendulagnāni bhūmiputraśanaiścarau 
tau ca lagnendu śakrāryā mandārārkajñabhārgavāḥ  

lagnamandāraviccandrāḥ sarve jīvajñabhāskarāḥ 
gurorlagne sukhe jīva lagnārākrabudhā dhane  

candraśukrau ca duścikye mandāryārkāḥ śanirvyaye 
sute śukrendulagnajñamandāścandraṃ vinā tvarau  

lagnārāryā'rkendavo'ste mṛgau jīvārkabhūsutāḥ 
dharme śukrārkalagnendubudhā mandaṃ vinā'yabhe  

māne gurubudhārārkaśukrahorāstathā viduḥ 
lagnaśukrendava ste te jñārkyā rāste jñavarjitāḥ  

sutabhe laghnaśaśijaśaśāṅkāryārkibhārgavāḥ 
jñārau śūnyaṃ sitā'rkendugurulagnaśanaiścarāḥ  

sarve raviṃ vinā śukragurumandāśca mānabhe 
sarve kujenduravayaḥ kramāt bhṛgusutasya ca  

śane ravitanū sūryo lagnendukujasūryajāḥ 
lagnārkau jīvamandārāḥ sarve sūryaṃ vinā kṣate  

arko'rkajñau budho'rkāratanujñāḥ sakalāstataḥ 
kujajñaguruśukrāśca kramāt sthānamidaṃ viduḥ  

tanau turye ca vahniḥ syād duścikye dvau dhane śarāḥ 
buddhimṛtyaṃkariḥpheṣu ṣaṭ kheśakṣatarāśiṣu  

rūpaṃstriyāṃ guruṃ tyaktvā lagnasya karaṇaṃ tvidam 
horāsūryendavo lagne lagnārendvinasūryajāḥ  

gurujñau lagnacandrārā lasūcaṃmaṃbusaurayaḥ 
kṣate śukrastathā caikaḥ kāme sarve guruṃ vinā  

mṛgau bhṛgubudhau tyaktvā dharme gurusitau vinā 
karmaṇyāye tathā śukrovyaye sūryenduvarjitāḥ  

lagnasyedaṃ tu saṃproktaṃ karaṇaṃ dvijapuṅgava 
atha sthānaṃ pravakṣyāmi lagnasya dvijapuṅgava  

ārkijñaśukragurvārāḥ saumyadevejyabhārgavāḥ 
hitvā saumyagurū śeṣāḥ sūjñejyabhṛgusūryajāḥ  

tathā jīvabhṛgū buddhau sarve śukraṃ vinā kṣate 
jīva ekastathā dyūne mṛgau saumyabhṛgū tathā  

dharme gurusitāveva khe bhave śukramantarā 
sūryacandrau tathā riṣphe sthānaṃ lagnasya kīrtitam  

karaṇaṃ binduvat lekhyaṃ sthānaṃ rekhāsvarūpakam 
karaṇaṃ tvaśubhadaṃ proktaṃ sthānaṃ śubhaphalapradam  

daśārekhā likhedūrdhvāstiryag rekhāścaturdaśa 
nageśakoṣṭhasaṃyuktaṃ cakramevaṃ prajāyate  

tiryagaṣṭasu koṣṭheṣu vilagnasahitān khagān 
ādyeṣūrdhvādhareṣvevaṃ bhāvasaṃkhyā likhed budhaḥ  

yathoktaṃ vinyaset tatra karaṇaṃ sthānameva vā 
tataḥ śubhā'śubhaṃ jñātvā jātakasya phalaṃ vadet  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha trikoṇaśodhanādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

evaṃ salagnakheṭānāṃ vidhāyāṣṭakavargakam 
trikoṇaśodhanaṃ kuryādādau sarvaṃṣu rāśiṣu  

trikoṇaṃ kathyate vipra meṣasiṃhadhanūṃṣyatha 
vṛṣakanyāmṛgasyāśca yugmataulighaṭāstathā  

karkavṛścikamīnāśca trikoṇāḥ syuḥ parasparam 
adho'dhaḥ sarvarāśīnāmaṣṭavargaphalaṃ nyaset  

trikoṇeṣu ca yannyūnaṃ tattulyaṃ triṣu śodhayet 
ekasmin bhavane śūnyaṃ tat trikoṇaṃ na śodhayet  

samatve sarvageheṣu sarvaṃ saṃśodhayed budhaḥ 
paścāt vipaścitā kāryamekādhipatiśodhanam  

medskiphrulemedskip

          athaikādhipatyaśodhanādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

pūrvaṃ trikoṇaṃ saṃśodhya rāśīnāṃ sthāpayet phalam 
pṛthak pṛthak tataḥ kuryādekādhipatiśodhanam  

kṣetradvaye phalani syustadā saṃśodhayed yathā 
kṣīṇena saha cānyasmin śudhayed grahavarjite  

ubhayorgrahasaṃyoge na saṃśodhyaḥ kadācan 
grahayukte phalairhīne grahābhāve phalādhike  

ūnena samamanyasmin śodhayed grahavarjite 
phalādhike grahairyukte cānyasmin sarvamutsṛjet  

ubhayatra grahabhāve samatve sakalaṃ tyajet 
sagrahāgrahayostulye sarvaṃ saṃśodhyamagrahe  

kulīrasiṃhayo rāśyoḥ pṛthak kṣetraṃ pṛthak phalam 
saṃśodhyaikādhipatyaṃ hi tataḥ piṇḍaṃ prasādhayet  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha piṇḍasādhanādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

evaṃ śodhyāvaśeṣāṅkaṃ rāśimānena varddhayet 
grahayukte ca tadrāśau grahamānena varddhayet  

sarveṣāṃ ca punaryogaḥ piṇḍākhyaḥ kathyate dvija 
gosiṃhau daśabhirguṇyau vasubhiryugmavṛścikau  

saptabhistulameṣau ca mṛgakanye ca pañcabhiḥ 
śeṣāḥ svasaṃkhyayā guṇyā grahamānamathocyate  

jīvāraśukrasaumyānāṃ daśāṣṭanagasāyakāḥ 
pañca śeṣagrahāṇāṃ ca mānaṃ proktamidaṃ kramāt  

medskiphrulemedskip

        athā'ṣṭakavargaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

ātmasvabhāvaśaktiśca pitṛcintā raveḥ phalam 
manobuddhiprasādaśca mātṛcintā mṛgāṅkataḥ  

bhrātṛsattvaṃ guṇaṃ bhūmiṃ bhaumenaiva vicintayet 
vāṇijyakarma vṛttiśca suhṛdaṃ ca budhena tu  

guruṇā dehapuṣṭiñca vidyā putrārthasampadaḥ 
bhṛgorvivāhakarmāṇi bhogasthāna ca vāhanam  

veśyāstrījanasaṃyogaṃ śukreṇa ca nirīkṣayet 
āyuśca jīvanopāyaṃ duḥkhaśoka bhayāni ca  

sarvakṣayaṃ ca maraṇaṃ mandenaiva nirīkṣayet 
tattadbhāvaphalāṅkena guṇayed yogapiṇḍakam  

saptaviṃśaodhṛtaṃ śeṣatulyarkṣe yāti bhānujaḥ 
yadā tadā tasya tasya bhāvasyārti vinirdiśet  

arkāśritarkṣānnavamo rāśiḥ pitṛ gṛhaṃ smṛtam 
tadrāśiphalasaṃkhyābhirvardhayed yogapiṇḍakam  

vibhajet saptaviṃśatyā śeṣarkṣe yāti bhānujaḥ 
yadā tadā pitṛkleśo bhavatīti na saṃśayaḥ  

tattrikoṇagate vāpi pitā pitṛsamo'pi vā 
maraṇaṃ tasya jānīyāt pīḍāṃ vā mahatīṃ vadet  

guṇayed yogapiṇḍaṃ vā tadrāśiphalasaṃkhyayā 
arkoddhṛtāvaśeṣarkṣe yadā gacchati bhānujaḥ  

tattrikoṇarkṣakaṃ vāpi pitṛkaṣṭaṃ tadā vadet 
riṣṭapradadaśāyāṃ tu maraṇaṃ kaṣṭamanyadā  

arkāttu turyage rāhau mande vā bhūminandane 
guruśukrekṣaṇamṛte pitṛhā jāyate naraḥ  

lagnāt candrād gurusthāne yāte sūyrasute'thavā 
pāpairdṛṣṭe yute vāpi pitṛnāśaṃ vaded budhaḥ  

lagnāt sukheśvarāriṣṭadaśākāle pitṛkṣayaḥ 
anukūladaśākāle neti cintyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ  

pitṛjanmāṣṭame jātastadīśe lagnage'pi vā 
karoti pitṛkāryāṇi sa evātra na saṃśayaḥ  

sukhanāthadaśāyāntu sukhaprāpteśca saṃbhavaḥ 
sukheśe lagnalābhasthe candrasthānād viśeṣataḥ 
pitṛgehasamāyukte jātaḥ pitṛvaśānugaḥ  

pitṛjanmatṛtīyarkṣe jātaḥ pitṛdhanāśritaḥ 
pitṛkarmagṛhe jātaḥ pitṛtulyaguṇānvitaḥ  

tadīśe lagnasaṃsthe'pi pitṛśreṣṭho bhavennaraḥ 
evaṃ pūrvaktasāmānyaphalaṃ cātrāpi cintayet  

sūryāṣṭavarge yanchūnyaṃ tanmāse vastare'pi ca 
vivāhavratacūḍādi śubhakarma parityajet  

yatra rekhādhikā tatra māse saṃvacare'pi ca 
aniṣṭe'pi ravau jīve śubhakarma samācaret  

evaṃ candrāṣṭavarge ca yatra śūnyaṃ bhaved bahu 
tatra tatra gate candre śubhaṃ karmaṃ parityajet  

candrāccaturtho mātṛprasādagrāmacintanam 
candrāt sukhaphalaṃ piṇḍaṃ varddhayed bhaiśca sambhajet  

śeṣamṛkṣaṃ śanau yāte mātṛhāniṃ vinirdiśet 
tattrikoṇagate cāpi śanau mātṛrujaṃ vadet  

bhaumāṣṭavarge saṃcintyaṃ bhrātṛvikramadhairyakam 
kujāśritāt tṛtīyarkṣaṃ budhairbhrātṛgṛhaṃ smṛtam  

trikoṇaśodhanaṃ kṛtvā yatra syādadhikaṃ phalam 
bhūmerlābho'tra bhāryāyā bhrātṛṇāṃ sukhamuttamam  

bhaumo balavihīnaścad dīrghāyurbhātṛko bhavet 
phalāani yatra kṣīyante tatra bhaume gate kṣatih  

tṛtīyarkṣaphalenātha piṇḍaṃ sambardhya pūrvavat 
śeṣamṛkṣaṃ śanau yāte bhrātṛkaṣṭaṃ vinirdiśet  

budhātturye kuṭumbaṃ ca mātulaṃ mitrameva ca 
budhe phalādhike rāśau gate teeṣāṃ sukhaṃ diśet  

budhāṣṭavargaṃ saṃśodhya śeṣamṛkṣaṃ gate śanau 
kaṣṭaṃ kuṭumbamitrāṇāṃ mātulānāṃ ca nirdiśet  

jīvāt pañcamato jñānaṃ dharmaṃ putraṃ ca cintayet 
tasmin phalāadhike rāśau santānasya sukhaṃ diśet  

bṛhaspateḥ sutasthāne phalaṃ yatsaṃkhyakaṃ bhavet 
śatrunīcagrahaṃ tyaktvā tāvatī santatirdhruvā  

sutabheśanavāṃśaiśca tulyā vā santatirbhavet 
sutabhāvaphalenaivaṃ piṇḍaṃ saṃguṇya pūrvavat  

putrakaṣṭaṃ vijānīyāt śeṣamṛkṣaṃ gate śanau 
evaṃ dharmaṃ ca vidyāṃ ca kalpayet kālacittamaḥ  

śatrusyākaṣṭavargaṃ ca nikṣipyākāśacāriṣu 
yatra yatra phalāni syurbhūyāṃsi kali tatra tu  

vittaṃ kalatraṃ bhūmiṃ ca tattaddeśād vinirdiśet 
śukrājjāmitrato dāralabdhiścintyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ  

jāmitratattrikoṇastharāśidigdeśasambhavā 
sukheduḥkhe striyāścintye piṇḍaṃ samvardhya pūrvavat  

sanaiścarāśritasthānādaṣṭamaṃ mṛtyubhaṃ smṛtam 
tadeva cāyuṣaḥ sthānaṃ tasmādāyurvicintayet  

lagnātprabhṛti mandāntaṃ phalānyekatra kārayet 
tadyogaphalatulyābde vyādhiṃ vairaṃ samādiśet  

evaṃ mandādilagnāntaṃ phalānyekatra yojayet 
tattulyavarṣe jātasya tasya vyādhibhayaṃ vadet  

dvayoryogasame varṣe kaṣṭaṃ mṛtyusamaṃ diśet 
daśāriṣṭasamāyogo mṛtyureva na saṃśayaḥ  

piṇḍaṃ saṃsthāpya guṇayet śaneraṣṭamagaiḥ phalaiḥ 
saptaviṃśatihṛccheṣatulyamṛkṣaṃ gate śanau  

tattrikoṇarkṣage vāpi jātakasya mṛtiṃ vadet 
arkahṛccheṣarāśau vā tattrikoṇe'pi tad vadet  

śanaiścarāṣṭavargeṣu yatra nāsti phalaṃ gṛhe 
tatra naiva śubhaṃ tasya yadā yāti śanaiścaraḥ  

yatra rāśau śubhādhikyaṃ tatra yāte śanaiścare 
jātakasya dhruvaṃ jñeyaṃ tasmin kāle śubhaṃ phalam

medskiphrulemedskip

        athā'ṣṭavargāyurdāyādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

athātrāyuḥ pravakṣye'hamaṣṭavargasamudbhavam 
dinadvayaṃ virekhāyāṃ rekhāyāṃ sārdhavāsaram  

dinamekaṃ dvirekhāyāṃ trirakhāyāṃ dinārdhakam 
vedatulyāsu rekhāsu sārdhasaptadinaṃ smṛtam  

dvivarṣaṃ pañcarekhāsu ṣaḍrekhāsu catuḥsamā 
ṣaḍvarṣaṃ saptarekhāsu vasavo'ṣṭāsu vatsarāḥ  

evaṃ yadāgatāyuḥ syāt sarvakheṭasamudbhavam 
tadardhaṃ sphuṭamāyuḥ syādaṣṭavargabhavaṃ nṛṇām  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha samudāyāṣṭakavargādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

dvādaśāraṃ likheccakaṃ janmalagnādibhairyutam 
sarvāṣṭakaphalānyatra saṃyojya pratibhaṃ nyaset  

samudāyābhidhāno'yamaṣṭavargaḥ prakathyate 
ataḥ phalāni jātānāṃ vijñeyāni dvijottama  

triṃśādhikaphalā ye syū rāśayaste śubhapradāḥ 
pañcaviṃśāditriṃśāntaphalā madhyaphalā smṛtāḥ  

ataḥ kṣīṇaphalā ye te rāśayaḥ kaṣṭaduḥkhadā 
śubhe śreṣṭhaphalān rāśīn yojayenmatimānnaraḥ  

kaṣṭarāśīn sukāryeṣu varjayed dvijasattama 
śreṣṭharāśigataḥ kheṭaḥ śubho'nyatrā'śubhapradaḥ  

tanvādivyayaparyantaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhāvphalāni vai 
adhike śobhanaṃ jñeyaṃ hīne hāniṃ vinirdiśet  

madhye madhyaphalaṃ brūyād tattadbhāvasamudbhavam 
madhyāt phalādhike lābho lābhāt kṣīṇagatovyayaḥ  

lagnaṃ phalādhikaṃ yasya bhogavānarthavān hi saḥ 
viparītena dāridryaṃ bhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ  

daśāvadiha bhāvānāṃ kṛtvā khaṃḍatrayaṃ budhaḥ 
paśyet pāpasamārūḍhaṃ khaṃḍe kaṣṭakaraṃ vadet  

saumyairyuktaṃ śubhaṃ brūyānmiśrairmiśraphalaṃ yathā 
kramād bālyādyavasthāsu khaṃḍatrayaphalaṃ vadet  

rekhābhiḥ saptabhiryukte māsemṛtyubhayaṃ nṛṇām 
suvarṇaṃ viṃśatipalaṃ dadyāt dvau tilaparvatau  

rekhābhiraṣṭabhiryukte māse mṛtyubaśo naraḥ 
asatphalavināśāya dadyāt karpūrajāṃ tulām  

rekhābhirmavabhiyukte māse sarpabhayaṃ vadet 
aśvaiścaturbhiḥ saṃyuktaṃ rathaṃ dadyācchubhāptaye  

rekhābhirdaśabhiryukte māse śastrabhayaṃ tathā 
dadyācchubhaphalāvāptyai kavacaṃ vajrasaṃyutam  

abhiśāpabhayaṃ yatra rekhā rudrasamā dvija 
dikpalasvarṇaghaṭitāṃ pradadyāt pratimāṃ vidhoḥ  

yukte dvādaśarekhābhirjale mṛtyubhayaṃ vadet 
saśasyabhūmiḥ viprāya datvā śubhaphalaṃ bhavet  

viśvapramitarekhābhirvyāghrānmṛtyubhayaṃ tathā 
viṣṇorhiraṇyagarbhasya dānaṃ kuryāccubhāptaye  

śatrapramitarekhābhiryukte māse mṛterbhayam 
varāhapratimāṃ dadyāt kanakena vinirmitām  

tithitiśca nṛpād bhītirdadyāt tatra gajaṃ dvija 
riṣṭaṃ ṣoḍaśabhirdadyāt mūrtiṃ kalpatarostathā  

saptendubhirvyādhibhayaṃ dadyāt dhenuṃ guḍaṃ tathā 
kalaho'ṣṭendubhirdadyād ratnagobhūriraṇyakam  

aṅkendubhiḥ pravāsaḥ syācchāntiṃ kuryād vidhānataḥ 
viṃśatyā buddhināśaḥ syād gaṇeśaṃ tatra pūjayet  

rogapīḍaikaviṃśatyā dadyād dhānyasya parvatam 
yamāśvibhirbandhupīḍā dadyādādarśakaṃ dvija  

trayoviṃśatrisaṃyukte māse kleśamavāpnuyāt 
sauvarṇīṃ pratimāṃ dadyādraveḥ saptapalairbudhaḥ  

vedāśvibhirbandhuhīno dadyād gidaśakaṃ nṛpaḥ 
sarvarogavināśārthaṃ japahomādikaṃ caret  

dhīhāniḥ pañcaviṃśatyā pūjyā vāgīśvarī tadā 
ṣaḍviṃśatyā'rthahāniḥ syāt svarṇaṃ dadyādvicakṣaṇaḥ  

tathā ca saptaviṃśatyā śrīsuktaṃ tatra saṃjapet 
aṣṭaviṃśatisaṃyukte māse māse hāniśca sarvathā  

sūryahomaśca vidhinā karttavyaḥ śubhakāṃkṣibhiḥ 
ekonatriṃśatā cāpi cintavyākulito bhavet  

ghṛtavastrasuvarṇāni tatra dadyāt vicakṣaṇaḥ 
triṃśatā pūrṇadhānyāptiriti jātakanirṇayaḥ  

triṃśādhikāmī rekhābhirdhanaputrasukhāptayaḥ 
catvāriṃśādhikābhiśca puṇyaśrīrupacīyate  

aṣṭavargeṇa ye śuddhāste śuddhāḥ sarvakarmasu 
ato'ṣṭavargasaṃśuddhiraneṣyā sarvakarmasu  

tāvadgocaramanveṣyaṃ yāvanna prāpyate'ṣṭakam 
aṣṭavarge tu samprāpte gocaraṃ viphalaṃ bhavet  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha raśmiphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atha raśmīn pravakṣyāmi grahāṇāṃ dvijasattama 
din naveṣviṣusaptāṣṭaśarāḥ svocce karo raveḥ  

nīca khaṃ cāntare proktā raśmayaścānupāttaḥ 
nīconaṃ tu grahaṃ bhārdhādhikaṃ cakrādviśodhayet  

svīyaraśmihataṃ ṣaḍbhirbhajet syū raśmayaḥ svakāḥ 
aparairatra saṃskāraviśeṣaḥ kathito yathā  

svoccabhe te triguṇitāḥ svatrikoṇe dvisaṃguṇāḥ 
svame trighnā dvisaṃbhaktā adhimitragṛhe tathā  

vedaghnā rāmasaṃbhaktā mitrame ṣaḍguṇāstataḥ 
pañcabhaktāstathā śatrugṛhe ced dalitāḥ karāḥ  

adhiśatrugṛhe dvighnāḥ pañcabhaktāḥ same samāḥ 
śaniśukrau vinā tārāgrahā aste gatā yadi  

viraśmayo bhavantyevaṃ jñeyāḥ spaṣṭakarā dvija 
raśmiyogavaśādevaṃ phalaṃ vācyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ  

ekādi pañcaparyantaṃ raśmisaṃkhyā bhavedyadi 
daridrā duḥkhasaṃtaptā api jātāḥ kulottame  

parato daśakaṃ yāvat nirdhanā bhāravāsakāḥ 
strīputragṛhahīnāśca jāyante manujā bhuvi  

akādaśasvalpaputrāḥ svalpavittāśca mānavāḥ 
dvādaśasvalpavittāśca dhūrtā mūrkhāśca nirbalāḥ  

cauryakarmaratā nityaṃ cet trayodaśa raśmayaḥ 
caturdaśasu dharmātmā kuṭumbānāṃ ca poṣakāḥ  

kulocitakriyāsakto dhanavidyāsamanvitaḥ 
raśmibhiḥ pañcadaśabhiḥ sarvavidyāguṇānvitaḥ  

svavaṃśamukhyo dhanavānityāha bhagavān vidhiḥ 
parataśca kuleśānā bahubhṛtyā kuṭumbinaḥ  

kīrtimanto janaiḥ pūrṇāḥ sarve ca sukhinaḥ kramāt 
pañcāśajjanapālaścedekaviṃśatiraśmayaḥ  

dānaśīlaḥ kṛpāyukto dvāviṃśatisuraśmiṣu 
sukhayuk saumyaśīlaścet trayoviṃśatiraśmayaḥ  

ātriṃśat parataḥ śrīmān sarvasattvasamanvitaḥ 
rājapriyaśca tejasvī janaiśca bahubhirvṛtaḥ  

ata ūrdhvaṃ tu sāmantaścatvāriṃśat karāvadhi 
janānāṃ śatamārabya sahasrāvadhipoṣakaḥ  

ata ūrdhvantu bhūpālaḥ paṃcāśat kariṇāvadhi 
tata ūrdhvakarairvipra cakravartī nṛpo bhavet  

evaṃ prasūtikālotthanabhogakarasambhavam 
kulakramanusāreṇa jātakasya phalaṃ vadet  

kṣatriyaścakravartī vaiśyo rājā prajāyate 
śūdraśca sadhano vipro yajñakarmakriyārataḥ  

uccābhimukhakheṭasya karāḥ puṣṭaphalapradāḥ 
nīcābhimukhakheṭasya tato nyūnaphalaprdāḥ  

sarveṣāmeva kheṭānāmevaṃ raśmivaśāddvija 
śubhaṃ vā'pyaśubhaṃ cāpi phalaṃ bhavati dehinām  

raśmijñānaṃ vinā samyak na phalaṃ jñātumarhati 
tasmādraśmīn prasādhyaiva phalaṃ vācyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha sudarśanacakraphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

athocyate mayā vipra rahasyaṃ jñānamuttamam 
jagatāmupakārāya yat proktaṃ brahmaṇa svayam  

cakraṃ sudarśanaṃ nāma yadvaśāt prasphuṭaṃ phalam 
nṛṇāṃ tanvādibhāvānāṃ jñātuṃ śaknoti daivavit  

janmato mṛtyuparyantaṃ varṣamāsadinodbhavam 
śubhaṃ vā'pyaśubhaṃ sarvaṃ tacchṛṇuṣvaikamānasaḥ  

ekakendrodbhavaṃ ramyaṃ likhed vṛttatrayaṃ dvija 
dvādaśāraṃ ca tat kuryād bhavedevaṃ sudarśanam  

tatrādyavṛtte lagnādyā bhāvā lekhyāḥ sakhecarāḥ 
tadūrdhvavṛtte candrācca bhavāḥ kheṭasamanvitāḥ  

tadūrdhvavṛtte sūryācca kramāt bhavā grahānvitāḥ 
evamekaikabhāve'tra bhavedbhānāṃ trayaṃ trayam  

atra tu prathamo bhāvo lagnenduravibhiryutaḥ 
taṃ prakalpya tanuṃ tvagre jñeyā bhāvā dhanādayaḥ  

tatra tatra grahasthityā jñeyaṃ tattatphalaṃ budhaiḥ 
tanubhāve śubhaḥ sūryo jñeyo'nyatrāśubhapradaḥ  

pāpo'pi svoccarāśistho na bhavatyaśubhapradaḥ 
evaṃ śubhā'śubhaṃ dṛṣṭvā tattadbhāvaphalaṃ vadet  

yo bhāvaḥ svāmisaumyābhyāṃ yukto dṛṣṭo'yamedhate 
pāpairdṛṣṭo yuto yo vā tasya hāniḥ prajāyate  

jñeyaṃ sagrahabhāvasya grahayogasamaṃ phalam 
agrahasya tu bhāvasya grahadṛṣṭisamaṃ phalam  

śubhaireva śubhaṃ pāpairśubhaṃ miśrakhecaraiḥ 
śubhādhike śubhaṃ jñeyamaśubhaṃ tvaśubhādhike  

evaṃ bhāveṣu kheṭānāṃ yogaṃ dṛṣṭiṃ vilokya ca 
tāratamyena vācyāni phalāni dvijasattama  

yatra naiva grahaḥ kaścinna dṛṣṭi kasyacid bhavet 
tadā tadbhāvajaṃ jñeyaṃ tatsvāmivaśataḥ phalam  

śubho'pi śubhavargeṣu hyadhikeṣvaśubhapradaḥ 
pāpo'pi śubhavargeṣu hyadhikeṣu śubhapradaḥ  

svabhoccasya śubhasyātra vargā jñeyāḥ śubhavāhāḥ 
śatroḥ krūrasya nīcasya ṣaḍvargā aśubhapradāḥ  

evaṃ sarveṣu kheṭeṣu bhaveṣvapi dvijottama 
śubhāśubhatvaṃ sañcinyta tatastatphalamādiśet  

yadā sudarśanādeva phalaṃ siddhyati dehanām 
tadā kiṃ munibhiḥ sarvairlagnādeva phalaṃ smṛtam  

iti ma saṃśayo jātastaṃ chettumarhati 
pṛthagbhagau yadā'rkendū lagnādanyatra saṃsthitau  

tadā sudarśanāccakrāt phalaṃ vācyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ 
ekabhe dvau trayo vā cet tadā lagnāt phalaṃ vadet  

atha vipra pravakṣye'haṃ prativarṣādijaṃ phalam 
asmāt sudarśanādeva daśāntaradaśāvaśāt  

tanvādyairvarṣamāśārdhadvikadhasrān pravartayet 
bhaveśādidvādaśānāṃ daśā varṣeṣu kalpayet  

tadādyantardaśāstadvanmāsādau tadbalaiḥ phalam 
taṃ taṃ bhāvaṃ prakalpyāṅkaṃ tattattanvādijaṃ dvija  

tat tallagnāt kendrakoṇāṣṭame saumyāḥ śubhapradāḥ 
yatra bhāve saiṃhikeyo bhavet tadbhāvahānikṛt  

pāpā vā yatra bahavastattadbhāvavināśanam 
viriṣphāriśubhaiḥ pāpaistriṣaḍāyasthitaiḥ śubham  

evaṃ pratyabdamāsādau bhāvānāṃ phalacintanam 
dvādaśānāṃ daśā'vṛttyā daśāścāyuṣi cintayet  

evaṃ sudarśanāccakrād varṣamāsādijaṃ phalam 
jñātvā tathāṣṭavargotthamubhābhyāṃ phalanirṇayaḥ  

ubhayatra samatve hi sampūrṇaṃ tat phalaṃ vadet 
viṣamatve yadādhikyaṃ tatphalaṃ ca balakramāt  

medskiphrulemedskip

      atha paṃcamahāpuruṣalakṣaṇādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atha vakṣyāmyahaṃ pañcamahāpuruṣalakṣaṇam 
svabhoccagatakendrasthairbalibhiśca kujādibhiḥ  

kramaśo rucako bhadro haṃso mālavya eva ca 
śaśaścaite budhaiḥ sarvairmahāntaḥ puruṣāḥ smṛtāḥ  

dīrghānano mahotsāho svacchakāntirmahābalaḥ 
cārubhrūrnīlakeśaśca suruciśca raṇapriyaḥ  

raktaśyāmo'rihantā ca mantraviccoranāyakaḥ 
krūrobhartā manuṣyāṇāṃ kṣāmā'ṅghrirdvijapūjakaḥ  

vīṇāvajradhanuḥpāśavṛṣacakrāṅkitaḥ kare 
mantrābhicārakuśalī dairdhye caiva śatāṃgulaḥ  

mukhadairghyasamaṃ madhyaṃ tasya vijñaiḥ prakīrtitam 
tulyastulāsahasreṇa rucako dvijapuṅgava  

bhunakti vindhyasahyādripradeśaṃ saptatiṃ samāḥ 
śatreṇa vahninā vāpi sa prayāti surālayam  

śārdūlapratibhah pīnavakṣā gajagatiḥ pumān 
pīnājānubhujaḥ prājñaścaturasraśca yogavit  

sāttvikaḥ śobhanāṃghraśca śobhanaśmaśrusaṃyutaḥ 
kāmī śaṅkhagadācakraśarakuñjaracihnakaiḥ  

dhvajalāṅgalacihnaiśca cihnitāṃghrikarāmbujaḥ 
sunāsaśśāstravid dhīraḥ kṛṣṇākuñcitakeśabhṛt  

svatantraḥ sarvakāryeṣu svajanaprīṇanakṣamaḥ 
aiśvaryaṃ bhujyate cāsya nityaṃ mitrajanaiḥ paraiḥ  

tulayā tulito bhārapramitaḥ strīsutānvitaḥ 
sakṣemo bhūpatiḥ pāti madhyadeśaṃ śataṃ samāḥ  

haṃso haṃsasvaro gauraḥ sumukhonnatanāsikaḥ 
śleṣmalo madhupiṅgākṣo raktavarṇanakhaḥ sudhīḥ  

pīnagaṇḍasthalo vṛttaśirāḥ sucaraṇo nṛpaḥ 
matsyā'ṅkuśadhanuḥśaṃkhakañjakhaṭvāṅgacihnakaiḥ  

cihnatāṃghrikaraḥ strīṣu kāmārto naiti tuṣṭatām 
ṣaṇṇvatyaṃgulo dairghye jalakrīḍārataḥ sukhī  

gaṅgāyamunayormadhyadeśaṃ pāti śataṃ samāḥ 
vanānte nidhanaṃ yāti bhuktvā sarvasukhaṃ bhuvi  

samauṣṭhaḥ kṛśamadhyaśca candrakāntiruciḥ pumān 
sugandho nātiraktāṅgo na hrasvo nātidīrghakaḥ  

samasvaccharado hastināda ājānubāhudhṛk 
mukhaṃ viśvāṃgulaṃ dairghye vistāre ca daśāṅgulam  

mālavyo mālavākhyaṃ ca deśaṃ pāti sasindhukam 
sukhaṃ saptativarṣāntaṃ bhuktvā yāti sulālayam  

tanudvijamukhaḥ śūro nātihrasvaḥ kṛśodaraḥ 
madhye kṣāmaḥ sujaṃghaśca matimān pararandhravit  

śakto vanādridurgeṣu senānīrdanturaḥ śaśaḥ 
caṃcalo dhātuvādī ca strīśakto'nyadhānānvitaḥ  

mālāvīṇāmṛdaṅgā'strarekhāṅkitakarāṃghrikaḥ 
bhūpo'yaṃ vasudhā pāti jīvan khādrisamāḥ sukhī  

medskiphrulemedskip

       atha paṃcamahābhūtaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atha pañcamahābhūtacchāyājñānaṃ vadāmi te 
jñāyate yena kheṭānāṃ vartamānadaśā budhaiḥ  

śikhibhūkhāmbuvātānāmadhipā maṅgalādayaḥ 
tattadbalāvaśājjñeyaṃ tattadbhūtabhavaṃ phalam  

sabale maṅgale vahnisvabhāvo jāyate naraḥ 
budhe mahīsvabhāvaḥ syādākāśaprakṛtirgurau  

śukre jalasvabhāvaśca mārutaprakṛtiḥ śanau 
miśrairmiśrasvabhāvaśca vijñeyo dvijasattama  

sūrye vahnisvabhāvaśca jalaprakṛtiko vidhau 
svadaśāyāṃ grahāśchāyāṃ vyaṃjayanti svabhūtajām  

kṣudhārtaścapalaḥ śūraḥ kṛśaḥ prājño'tibhakṣaṇaḥ 
tīkṣno gauratanurmānī vahniprakṛtiko naraḥ  

karpūrotpalafandhāḍhyo bhogī sthirasukhī balī 
kṣamāvān siṃhanādaśca mahīprakṛtiko naraḥ  

śabdārthavit sunītijño pragalbho jñānasaṃyutaḥ 
vivṛtāsyo'tidīrghaśca vyomaprakṛtisambhavaḥ  

kāntimān bhāravāhī ca priyavāk pṛthivīpatiḥ 
bahumitrā mṛdurvidvān jalaprakṛtisambhavaḥ  

vāyutattvādhiko dātā krodhī gauro'ṭanapriyaḥ 
bhūpatiśca durādharṣaḥ kṛśāṅgo jāyate janaḥ  

svarṇadīptiḥ śubhā dṛṣṭiḥ sarvakāryārthasiddhitā 
vijayo dhanalābhaśca vahnibhāyāṃ prajāyate  

iṣṭagandhaḥ śarīre syāt susnigdhanakhadantatā 
dharmārthasukhalābhaśca bhūmicchāyā yadā bhavet  

svaccā gaganajā chāyā vākpaṭutvapradā bhavet 
suśabdaśravaṇodbhūtaṃ sukhaṃ tatra prajāyate  

mṛdutā svasthatā dehe jalacchāyā yadā bhavet 
tadā'bhiṣṭarasasvādasukhaṃ bhavati dehinaḥ  

mālinyaṃ mūḍhatā daityaṃ rogaśca pavanodbhavāḥ 
tadā ca śokasantāpau vāyucchāyā yadā bhavet  

evaṃ phalaṃ budhairjñeyaṃ sabaleṣu kujādiṣu 
nirbaleṣu tathā teṣu vaktavyaṃ vyatyayād dvija  

nīcaśatrubhagaiścāpi viparītaṃ phalaṃ vadet 
phalāptirabalaiḥ kheṭaiḥ svapnacintāsu jāyate  

tadduṣṭaphalaśāntyarthamapi cājñātajanmanām 
phalapaktyā daśā jñeyā vartamānā nabhaḥsadām  

medskiphrulemedskip

       atha sattvādiguṇaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atho guṇavaśenāhaṃ kathayāmi phalaṃ dvija 
sattvagrahodaye jāto bhavetsattvādhikaḥ sudhīḥ  

rajaḥkheṭodaye vijño rajoguṇasamanvitaḥ 
tamaḥkheṭodaye mūrkho bhavejjātastamo'dhikaḥ  

guṇasāmyayuto jāto guṇasāmyakhagodaye 
evaṃ caturvidhā vipra jāyanto jantavo bhuvi  

uttamo madhyamo nīca udāsīna iti kramāt 
teṣāṃ guṇānahaṃ vakṣye nāradāriprabhāṣitān  

śamo damastapaḥ śaucaṃ kṣāntirārjavameva ca 
alobhaḥ satyavāditvaṃ jane sattvādhike guṇāḥ  

śauryaṃ tejo dhṛtirdākṣyaṃ yuddhe cā'pyapalāyanam 
sādhūnāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ ceti guṇā jñeyā rajo'dhike  

lobhaścāsatyavāditvaṃ jāḍyamālasyameva ca 
sevākarmapaṭutvaṃca guṇā ete tamo'dhike  

kṛṣikarmaṇi vāṇijye paṭutvaṃ paśupālane 
satyāsatyaprabhāṣitvaṃ guṇasāmye guṇā ime  

gataiśca lakṣaṇairlakṣya uttamo madhyamo'dhamaḥ 
udāsīnaśca viprenda taṃ tatkarmaṇi yojayet  

dvābhyāmeko'dhiko yaśca tasyādhikyaṃ nigadyate 
anyathā guṇasāmyaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ dvijasattama  

sevyasevakayorevaṃ kanyakāvarayorapi 
guṇaiḥ sadṛśayoreva prītirbhavati niścalā  

udāsīno'dhamasyaivamudāsīnasya madhyamaḥ 
madhyamasyottamo vipra prabhavatyāśrayo mude  

ato'varā varāt kanya sevyataḥ sevako'varaḥ 
guṇaistataḥ sukhotpattiranyathā hānireva hi  

vīryaṃ kṣetraṃ prasūteśca samayaḥ saṅgatistathā 
uttamādiguṇe heturbalavānuttarottaram  

ataḥ prasūtikālasya sadṛśo jātake guṇaḥ 
jāyate taṃ parīkṣyaiva phalaṃ vācyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ  

kālaḥ sṛjati bhūtani pātyatho saṃharatyapi 
iśvaraḥ sarvalokānāmavyayo bhagavān vibhu  

tacchaktiḥ prakṛtiḥ proktā munibhistriguṇātmikā 
tathā vibhakto'vyakto'pi vyakto bhavati dehinām  

caturdhā'vayavāstasya svaguṇaiśca caturvidhaḥ 
jāyante hyuttamo madhye udāsīno'dhamaḥ kramāt  

uttame tūttamo janturmadhye'ṅge ca madhyamaḥ 
udāsīne hyadāsīno jāyate cā'dhame'dhamaḥ  

uttamāṅgaṃ śaristasya madhyamāṅgamuraḥsthalam 
jaṃghādvayaudāsīnamadhamaṃ padamucyate  

evaṃ guṇavaśādeva kālabhedaḥ prajāyate 
jātibhedastu tadbhedājjāyate'tra carācare  

evaṃ bhagavatā sṛṣṭaṃ vibhunā svaguṇaiḥ samam 
caturvidhena kālena jagadetaccaturvidham  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha naṣṭajātakādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

janmakālavaśādevaṃ phalaṃ proktaṃ tvayā mune 
yajjanmasamayo'jñāto jñeyaṃ tasya phalaṃ katham  

śubhaṃ vā'pyaśubhaṃ vāpi manujasya purākṛtam 
asti kaścidupāyaścet taṃ bhavān vaktumarhati  

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā vipra lokānugrahamānasā 
kathayāmi tava snehāt phalamajñātajanmanām  

varṣāyanartumāsārdhatithinakṣatrabhādiṣu 
yadajñātaṃ ca tanmānaṃ jñāyate praśnalagnataḥ  

praśnāṅgadvādaśāṃśarkṣasthite janma vadet gurau 
ayanaṃ lagnapūrvārdhe saumyaṃ yāmyaṃ parārdhake  

ṛturlagnadṛkāṇarkṣasvāmibhiḥ śaśirādayaḥ 
śaniśukrakujendujñajīvairgrīṣmastu bhānunā  

ayanartuvirodhe tu parivartyāḥ parasparam 
budhacandra surācāryāḥ kujaśukraśanaiścaraiḥ  

māso dṛkāṇapūrvārdherpūrvo'nyastu parārdhake 
anupātāt tithirjñeyā bhāskarāṃśasamā dvija  

tadvaśādiṣṭakālo yo janmakālasamo hi saḥ 
tatra grahāṃśca bhāvāṃśca jñātvā tasya phalaṃ vadet  

gururdvādaśabhrvarṣaiḥ punastadrāśigo bhavet 
tat kasmin paryayo tasya jñeyaḥ saṃvatsaro mune  

saṃvastarasya sandehe praśnakarturdvijottama 
vayo'numānatastatra dvādaśa dvādaśa kṣipet  

tatrāpi saṃśaye jāte gururlagnatrikoṇagaḥ 
kalpyo vayo'numānena vatsaraḥ pūrvavat tataḥ  

jñātvā māsaṃ sasūryāṃśaṃ kālajñānaṃ kathaṃ bhavet 
bhagavanniti me brūhi lokānugrahacetasā  

sakrānteriṣṭasūryāṃśatulye'hni dvijasattama 
raviraudayikaḥ sādhyastasyeṣṭārkasya cāntaram  

kalīkṛtya svaṣaṇnighnaṃ sphuṭārkagatibhājitam 
labdhaṃghaṭyādimānaṃ yat tāvān sūryodayāt param  

pūrvaṃ janmeṣṭakālo hi kramāj jñeyo vipaścitā 
sādhitaudayikādarkādiṣṭe'rke'nikahīnake  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha pravrajyāyogādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atha vipra pravakṣyāmi yogaṃ pravrajyakābhidham 
pravrajanti janā yena sampradāyāntaraṃ gṛhāt  

caturādibhirekasthaiḥ pravrajyā balibhiḥ samāḥ 
ravyādibhistapasvī ca kapālī raktavastrabhṛt  

ekadaṇḍī yatiścakradharo nirgranthikaḥ kramāt 
jñeyā vīryādhikasyaiva sabaleṣu bahuṣvapi  

sūryeṇā'staṃ gatāste cedapi vīryasamanvitāḥ 
adīkṣitāstadā jñeyā janāstadgatabhaktayaḥ  

astaṃgatā nirbalāścet sabalaśca raviryadā 
tadā ravibhavā jñeyā pravrajyā dvijasattama  

janmabheśo'nyakheṭaiścedadṛṣṭaḥ śanimīkṣate 
tayorbalavaśāttatra pravrajyāmāpnuyānnaraḥ  

nirbalo janmabheśaścet kevalenārkiṇekṣitaḥ 
tadā śanibhavameva pravrajyāṃ āpnuyājjanaḥ  

śanidṛkkāṇasaṃsthe ca śanibhaumanavāṃśake 
śanidṛṣṭe vidhau jñeyā pravrajyā śanisambhavā  

kujādiṣu jayī śukraḥ saumyago yāmyago'pi vā 
jayī saumyagataścānyaḥ parasparayutau bhavet  

pravrajyākārakaḥ kheṭo yadyanyena parājitaḥ 
tadā labdhāṃ parivrajyāṃ parityajati tāṃ punaḥ  

bahavo janmakāle cet pravrajyākārakā grahāḥ 
balatulyāstadā tatra pravrajyā katamā bhavet  

bahavo balinaścet syuḥ pravrajyākārakā grahāḥ 
tadā prāpnoti sarveṣāṃ teṣāṃ pravrajyakāṃ dhruvam  

tattadgrahadaśākāle pravrajyāṃ yāti tadbhavām 
tyaktvā gṛhītapūrvāṃ tāmanyāṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ  

dṛṣṭeṣvindvijyalagneṣu śaninā navame guruḥ 
rājayoge'tra jāto'sau tīrthikṛnna'tra saṃśayaḥ  

dharmasthānagate mande grahadṛṣṭivivarjite 
rājayoge'tra yo jātaḥ sa rājā dīkṣito bhavet  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha strījātakādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

bahudhā bhavatā proktaṃ yajjātakaphalaṃ mune 
tannārīṇāṃ kathaṃ jñeyamiti me kathayā'dhunā  

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā vipra tadapi pravadāmyaham 
strīṇāṃ puṃbhiḥ samaṃ jñeyaṃ phalamuktaṃ vipaścitā  

viśeṣastatra yo dṛṣṭaḥ saṃkṣepāt kathayāmi tat 
lagne dehaphalaṃ tasyāḥ pañcame prasavastathā  

saptame patisaubhāgyaṃ vaidhavyaṃ nidhane dvija 
strīṇāmasambhavaṃ yadyat tatphalaṃ tatpatau vadet  

lagnendū samabhe yasyāḥ sā nārī prakṛtisthitā 
kanyocitaguṇopetā suśīlā śubhalakṣaṇā  

śubhekṣitau surūpā ca sadā dehasukhānvitā 
viṣame puruṣākārā duḥśīlā pāpavīkṣitau  

pāpāḍhyau ca guṇairhīnā miśre miśraphalaṃ vadet 
lagnendvoryo balī tasya phalaṃ tasya viśeṣataḥ  

lagnendvoryo balī vipra triṃśāṃśaistadadhiṣṭhitaiḥ 
graharāśivaśād vācyaṃ phalaṃ strīṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ  

kanyaivāragṛhe duṣṭā bhaumatriṃśāṃśake bhavet 
kucaritrā tathā śaukre samāyā bodhane smṛtā  

jaive sādhvī śanau dāsī jñarkṣe kauje chalānvitā 
śaukre prakīrṇakāmā sā baudheṃ'śe ca guṇānvitā  

klībā'rkyaṃśe satī jaive kaujai duṣṭā sitarkṣake 
śaukre khyātaguṇā baudhe kalāsu nipuṇā bhavet  

jaive guṇavatī mānde punarbhūścandrabhe tataḥ 
svatantrā kujātriṃśāṃśe śaukre ca kulapāṃsanā  

baudhe śilpakalā'bhijñā jaive bahuguṇā śanau 
patighnī cārkabhe kauje vācālā bhārgave satī  

baudhe puṃśceṣṭitā jaive rājñī mānde kulacyutā 
kauje bahuguṇā'ryarkṣe śaukre cāpyasatī matā  

baudhe vijñānasaṃyutā jaive'nekaguṇānvitā 
mānde cālparatiḥ proktā dāsī kauje tathā'rkibhe  

suprajñā ca bhavecchaukre baudhe duḥsthā tathā khalā 
jaive pativratā proktā mānde nīcajanānugā  

mande śūnye śubhādṛṣṭe patiḥ kāpuruṣo bhavet 
carabhe ca pravāsī syāt klīvastatra jñamandayoḥ  

sūrye'stabhe patityaktā bālye ca vidhavā kuje 
śanāvaśubhasandṛṣṭe yāti kanyaiva vṛddhatām  

vidhavāstagataiḥ pāpaiḥ saumyaistu sadhavā satī 
miśrakheṭaiḥ pūnarbhūḥ sā jñeyā miśraphalānvitā  

mithoṃ'śasthau sitārau cedanyāsaktā tadā'ṅganā 
saptame ca sthite candre tadā bharturanujñyā  

śukrabhe śanibhe vāpi senduśukre ca lagnage 
mātrā saha tadā nārī vandhakī bhavati dhruvam  

kujarkṣe vā tadaṃśe'ste strīlolaḥ krodhanaḥ patiḥ 
baudharkṣāṃśe tathā vidvān kalāsu nipuṇaḥ sudhīḥ  

jaive sarvaguṇopetaḥ patiraste jitendriyaḥ 
śaukre saubhāgyasaṃyuktaḥ kāntaḥ strījanavallabhaḥ  

saurerkṣa vātha saurāṃśe vṛddho mūrkhaśca saptame 
atīvāmṛdurarkāṃśe tadṛkṣevā'tikarmakṛt  

aste karke tadaṃśe vā kāntaḥ kāmī mṛduḥ patiḥ 
miśre miśraphalaṃ vācyaṃ bhāṃśayośca balakramāt  

sūrye'ṣṭamagate jātā duḥkhadāridryasaṃyutā 
kṣatāṅgī khedayuktā ca bhaveddharmaparāṅmukhī  

candre'ṣṭamagate nārī kubhagā kustano kudṛg 
vastrābharaṇahīnā ca rogiṇī cātigarhitā  

kuje'ṣṭamagate bālā kṛśāṅgī rogasaṃyutā 
vidhavā kāntihīnā ca śokasantāpaduḥkhitā  

budheṣṭamagate jātā dharmahīnā bhayāturā 
abhimānadhanairhīnā nirguṇā kalahapriyā  

gurāvaṣṭamage bālā viśīlā svalpasantatiḥ 
pṛthuvādakarā patyā tyaktā bahvaśanā bhavet  

śukre'ṣṭamagate jātā pramattā dhanavarjitā 
nirdayā dharmahīnā ca malinā kapaṭānvitā  

śanāvaṣṭamage jātā duḥsvabhāvā malimlucā 
pravaṃcanaparā nārī bhavet patisukhojjñitā  

rāhāvaṣṭamabhāvasthe kurūpā pativarjitā 
kaṭhorahṛdayā rogairyuktā ca vyabhicāriṇī  

śaśiśukrau yadā lagne mandarābhyāṃ yutau tadā 
bandhyā bhavati sā nārī sutabhe pāpadṛgyute  

kujāṃśestagate sauridṛṣṭe nārī sarugbhagā 
śubhāṃśe saptame jñeyā subhagā pativallabhā  

budhabhe lagnage sūtau candraśukrayute dvija 
jñeyā pitṛgṛhe nārī sā sarvasukhasaṃyutā  

lagne candrajñaśukreṣu bahusaukhyaguṇānvitā 
jīva tatrātisampannā putravittasukhānvitā  

lagnādaṣṭamagau syātāṃ candrārkau svarkṣagau tadā 
bandhyā'tha kākabandhyā cedevaṃ candrabudhau yadā  

śanimaṅgalabhe lagne candrabhārgavasaṃyute 
pāpadṛṣṭe ca sā nārī bandhyā bhavati niścayāt  

sarāhau saptame sūrye pañcame pāpasaṃyute 
śukrejyarāhavo mṛtyau mṛtāpatyā ca sā bhavet  

śukrejyāvaṣṭame sārau saptame vā kujo bhavet 
śaninā dṛgyuto nārī galadgarbhā prakīrtitā  

pāpakartarike lagne candre jātā ca kanyakā 
samastaṃ pitṛvaṃśaṃ ca pativaṃśaṃ hihanti sā  

sasarpāgnijaleśarkṣe bhānumandāravāsare 
bhadrātithau januryasyāḥ sā viṣākhyā kumārikā  

sapāpaśca śubhau lagne dvau pāpau śatrubhasthitau 
yasyā januṣi sā kanyā viṣākhyā parikīrtitā  

viṣayoge samutpannā mṛtavatsā ca durbhagā 
vastrābharaṇahīnā ca śokasantaptamānasā  

saptameśaḥ śubho vāpi saptame lagnato'thavā 
candrato vā viṣaṃ yogaṃ vinihanti na saṃśayaḥ  

lagne vyaye sukhe vāpi saptame cā'ṣṭame kuje 
śubhadṛgyogahīne ca patiṃ hanti na saṃśayaḥ  

yasmin yoge samutpannā patiṃ hanti kumārikā 
tasmin yoge samutpanno patnīṃ hanti naro'pi ca  

strīhantrā pariṇītā cet patihantrī kumārikā 
tadā vaidhavyayogasya bhaṅgo bhavati niścayāt  

mithoṃ'śasthau mithodṛṣṭau sitārkī vā sitarkṣake 
ghaṭāṃśe lagnage nārī pradīptaṃ madanānalam  

saṃśāntiṃ nayati strībhiḥ sukhībhirmadanāturā 
parābhiḥ puruṣākārasthitabhirdvijasattama  

kujajñaguruśukraiśca balibhiḥ samabhe tanau 
kuśalā'nekaśāstreṣu sā nārī brahmavādinī  

krūre saptamage kaścit khecaro navame yadi 
sā pravrajyāṃ tadāpnoti pāpakhecarasaṃbhavām  

vilagnādaṣṭame saumye pāpadṛgyogavarjite 
mṛtyuḥ prāgeva vijñeyastasya mṛtyurna saṃśayaḥ  

aṣṭame śubhapāpau cet syātāṃ tulyabalau yadā 
saha bhartrā tadā mṛtyuṃ prāptvā svaryāti niścayāt
