medskiphrulemedskip

          atha aṃgalakṣaṇaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

bahudhā bhavtā proktaṃ janmakālāt śubhāśubham 
śrotumicchāmi nāroṇāmaṅgacihnaiḥ phala mune  

śṛṇu vipra pravakṣyāmi nārīṇāmaṅgalakṣaṇam 
phalaṃ yathā'ha pārvatyai bhagavān śaṅkarastathā  

snigdhaṃ pādatalaṃ strīṇāṃ mṛdulaṃ māṃsalaṃ samam 
raktamasvedamuṣṇaṃ ca bahubhogapradāyakam  

vivarṇaṃ puruṣaṃ rūkṣaṃ khaṇḍitaṃ viṣamaṃ tathā 
sūrpākārañca śuṣkaṃ ca duḥkhadaurbhāgyadāyakam  

śaṅkhasvastikacakrā'bjadhvajamīnā'tapatravat 
yasyāḥ pādatale cihnaṃ sā jñeyā kṣitipāṅganā  

bhavet samastabhogāya tathā dīrghordhvarekhikā 
rekhāḥ sarpā'khukākābhā duḥkhadāridryasūcikāḥ  

raktāḥ samunnatāḥ snigdhā vṛttāḥ pādanakhāḥ śubhāḥ 
sphuṭitāaḥ kṛṣṇavarṇāśca jñeyā aśubhasūcakāḥ  

unnato māṃsalo'ṅguṣṭho vartulo'tulabhogadaḥ 
vakro hrasvaśca cipiṭo duḥkhadāridryasūcakaḥ  

mṛdavo'ṅgulayaḥ śastā ghanā vṛttāśca māṃsalāḥ 
dīrghāṅgulībhiḥ kulaṭā kṛśābhirdhanavarjitā  

bhaveddhrasvābhiralpāyurviṣamābhiśca kuṭṭanī 
cipaṭābhirbhaveddāsī viralābhaśca nirdhanā  

yasya mithaḥ samārūḍhāḥ pādāṅgulyo bhavanti hi 
bahunapi patīn hitvā parapreṣyā ca sā bhavet  

yasyā pathi calantyāśca rajo bhūmeḥ samucchalet 
sā pāṃsulī bahvennārī kulatrayavighātinī  

yasyāḥ kaniṣṭhikā bhūmiṃ gacchantyā na parispṛśet 
sā hi pūrvapatiṃ hatvā dvitīyaṃ kurute patim  

madhyamā'nāmikā cāpi yasyā bhūmiṃ na saṃspṛśet 
patihīnā ca sā nārī vijñeyā dvijasattama  

pradeśinī bhavedyasyā aṃguṣṭhādvyatirekiṇī 
kanyaiva dūṣitā sā syāt kulaṭā ca tadagrataḥ  

unnataṃ pādapṛṣṭhaṃ cet tadā rājñī bhaveddhruvam 
asvedamaśirāḍhyañca māṃsalaṃ masṛṇaṃ mṛdu  

anyathā dhanahīnā ca śirālaṃ cettadā'dhvagā 
romāḍhyaṃ ced bhaveddāsī nirmāsaṃ yadi durbhagā  

subhagā samapārṣṇiḥ strī pṛthupārṣṇiśca durbhagā 
kulaṭonnatapārṣṇiśca dīrghapārṣṇiśca duḥkhitā  

arome ca same snigdhe yasyā jaṃgha suvartule 
visire ca suramye sā rājapatnī bhaveddhruvam  

vartulaṃ māṃsalaṃ snigdhaṃ jānuyugmaṃ śubhapradam 
nirmāsaṃ svairacāriṇyā nirdhanāyāśca viślatham  

ghanau karikarākārau vartulau mṛdulau śubhau 
yasyā ūrū śirāhīnau sā rājñī bhavati dhruvam  

cipiṭau romaśau yasyā vidhavā durbhagā ca sā 
caturbhirviśatiyutairaṃgulaiśca samā kaṭiḥ 
samunnatanitambāḍhyā praśastā syāt mṛgīdṛśām  

vinatā cipaṭā dīrghā nirmāṃsā saṃkaṭā kaṭiḥ 
hrasvā romaiḥ samāyuktā duḥkhavaidhavyasūcikā  

natimbaḥ śubhadaḥ strīṇāmunnato māṃsalaḥ pṛthuḥ 
sukhasaubhāgyadaḥ prokto jñeyo duḥkhaprado'nyathā  

strīṇāṃ gūḍhamaṇistuṅgo raktābho mṛduromakaḥ 
bhagaḥ kamaṭhapṛṣṭhābhaḥ śubho'śvatthagalākṛtiḥ  

kuraṅgakhurarūpo yaścullikodarasaṃnibhiḥ 
romaśo dṛśyanāsaśca vivṛttāsyo'śubhapradaḥ  

vāmonnatastu kanyājaḥ putrojo dakṣiṇonnataḥ 
śaṅkhāvarto bhago yasyāḥ sā vigarbhā'ṅganā matā  

mṛdvī vastiḥ praśastā syād vipulālpasamunnatā 
romāḍhyā ca śirālā ca rekhāṅkā na śubhapradā  

gambhīrā dakṣiṇāvartā nābhiḥ sarvasukhapradā 
vyaktagranthiḥ samuttānā vāmāvartā na śobhanā  

pṛthukukṣiḥ śubhā nārī sūte sā ca bahūn sutān 
bhūpatiṃ janayet putraṃ maṇḍūkābhena kukṣiṇā  

unnatena valībhājā sāvartena ca kukṣiṇā 
vandhyā saṃnyāsinī dāsī jāyate kramado'balā  

same samāṃśe mṛdule pārśve strīṇāṃ śubhaprade 
unnate romasaṃyukte śirāle cā'śubhaprade  

nirlobhaṃ hṛdayaṃ strīṇāṃ same sarvasukhapradam 
vistīrṇaṃ ca salomaṃ ca vijñeyamaśubhapradam  

samau pīnau ghanau vṛttau dṛḍhau śastau payodhrau 
sthūlāgrau viralau śuṣkau strīṇāṃ naiva śubhapradau  

dakṣiṇonnatavakṣojā nārī putravatī matā 
vāmonnatastanī kanyāprajā proktā purātanaiḥ  

nārīṇāṃ cūcuke śaste śyāmavarṇe suvartule 
antarbhagne ca dīrghe ca kṛśe cāpi na śobhane  

strīṇāṃ skandhau samau puṣṭau gūḍhasandhī śubhapradau 
romāḍhyāvunnatau vakrau nirmāsāvaśubhau smṛtau  

susūkṣmarome nārīṇāṃ puṣṭe snigdhe śubhaprade 
kakṣe śirāle gambhīre na śubhe svedamedure  

gūḍhāsthī komalagranthī viśirau ca biromakau 
saralau suvartulau caiva bhujau śastau mṛgīdṛśām  

nirmāṃsau sthūlaromāṇau hrasvau caiva śirātatau 
vakrau bhujau ca nārīṇāṃ kleśāya parikīrtitau  

sarojamukulākāro karāṃguṣṭhau mṛgīdṛśām 
sarvasaukhyapradau proktau kṛśau vakrau ca duḥkhadau  

strīṇāṃ karatalaṃ raktaṃ madhyonnatamarandhrakam 
mṛdulaṃ cālparekhāḍhyaṃ jñeyaṃ sarvasukhapradam  

vidhavā bahurekheṇa rekhāhīnena nirdhane 
bhikṣukā ca śiroḍhyena nārī karatalena hi  

pāṇipṛṣṭhaṃ śubhaṃ strīṇāṃ puṣṭaṃ mṛduviromakam 
śirālaṃ romaśaṃ nimnāṃ dukhadāridryasūcakam  

yasyāḥ karatale rekhā vyaktā raktā ca vartulā 
snigdhā pūrṇā ca gambhīrā sā sarvasukhabhāginī  

matsyena subhagā jñeyā svastikena dhanānvitā 
rājapatnī sarojena jananī pṛthivīpateḥ  

sārvabhaumapriyā pāṇau nadyāvarte pradakṣiṇe 
śaṅkhātapatrakamaṭhairbhūpasya jananī bhavet  

rekhā tulākṛtiḥ pāṇau yasyāḥ sā hi baṇigvadhūḥ 
gajavājivṛṣābhā vā kare vāme mṛgīdṛśaḥ  

rekhā prasādavajrābhā sūte tīrthakaraṃ sutam 
kṛṣīvalasya patnī syācchakaṭena yugena vā  

cāmarāṅkuśacāpaiśca rājapatnī pativratā 
triśūlā'sigadāśaktidundubhyākṛtirekhayā  

aṅguṣṭhamūlānnirgatyā rekhā yāti kaniṣṭhikām 
sā nāri patihantrī syād dūratastāṃ parityajet  

kākamaṇḍūkajambūkavṛkavṛścikabhoginaḥ 
rāsabhoṣṭraviḍālābhā rekhā duḥkhapradāḥ striyāḥ  

mṛdulāśca suparvāṇo dīrghā vṛttāḥ kramāt kṛśāḥ 
aromakāḥ śubhāḥ strīṇāmaṅgulyaḥ parikīrtitāḥ  

atihrasvāḥ kṛśā vakrā viralā romasaṃyutāḥ 
bahuparvayutā vā'pi parvahīnāśca duḥkhadāḥ  

raktavarṇā nakhāstuṅgā saśikhāśca śubhapradāḥ 
nimnā vivarṇā pītā vā puṣpitā duḥkhadāyakāḥ  

antarnimagnavaṃśāsthi pṛṣṭhaṃ syānmāṃsalaṃ śubham 
saśiraṃ romayuktaṃ vā vakraṃ cā'śubhadāyakam  

strīṇāṃ kaṇthastrirekhāṅkastvavyaktāsthiśca vartulaḥ 
māṃsalo mṛdulaiścaiva praśastaphaladāyakāḥ  

sthūlagrīvaḥ ca vidhavā vakragrīva ca kiṅkarī 
bandhyā ca cipiṭagrīvā laghugrīvā ca niḥsutā  

śreṣṭhā kṛkāṭikā ṛjvī samāṃsā ca samunnatā 
śuṣkā śirālā romāḍhyā viśālā kuṭilā'subhā  

aruṇaṃ mṛdulaṃ puṣṭaṃ praśastaṃ cibukaṃ striyāḥ 
āyataṃ romaśaṃ sthūlaṃ dvidhābhaktamaśobhanam  

kapolāvunnatau strīṇāṃ pīnau vṛttau śubhapradau 
romaśau puruṣau nimnau nirmāṃsau cā'śubhapradau  

strīṇāṃ mukhaṃ samaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ vartulaṃ ca sugandhimat 
susnigdhaṃ ca manohāri sukhasaubhāgyasūcakam  

vartulaḥ pāṭalaḥ snigdhārekhābhūṣitamadhyabhūḥ 
manoharo'dharo yasyāḥ sā bhaved rājavallabhā  

nirmāṃsaḥ sphuṭito lambo rūkṣo vā śyāmavarṇakaḥ 
sthūlo'dharaśca nārīṇāṃ vaidhavyakleśasūcakaḥ  

raktotpalanibhaḥ snigdha uttaroṣṭho mṛgīdṛśām 
kiñcinmadhyaunnato'romā sukhasaubhāgyago bhavet  

snigdhāgugdhanibhāḥ strīṇāṃ dvātriṃśaddaśanāḥ śubhāḥ 
adhastādupariṣṭhācca samāḥ stokasamunnatāḥ  

adhastādadhikāḥ pītāḥ śyāmā dīrghā dvipaṅktayaḥ 
vikaṭā viralāścāpi daśanā na śubhāḥ smṛtāḥ  

śoṇā mṛdvī śubhā jihvā strīṇāmatulabhogadā 
duḥkhadā madhyasaṅkīrṇā purobhāge'tivistarā  

sitayā maraṇaṃ toye śyāmayā kalahapriyā 
māṃsalayā dhanairhīnā lambayā'bhakṣyabhakṣiṇī  

pramādasahitā nārī jihvayā ca viśālayā 
susnigdhaṃ pāṭalaṃ strīṇāṃ komalaṃ tāluśobhanam  

śvete tāluni vaidhavyaṃ pīte pravrajitā bhavet 
kṛṣṇe santatihīnā syādrūkṣe bhūrikuṭumbinī  

alakṣitaradaṃ strīṇāṃ kiñcitphullakapolakam 
smitaṃ śubhapradaṃ jñeyamanyathā tvaśubhapradam  

samavṛttapuṭā nāsā laghucchidrā śubhapradā 
sthūlāgrā madhyanimnā vā na praśastā mṛgīdṛśām  

raktāgrā'kuñcitāgrā vā nāsā vaidhavyakāriṇī 
dāsī sā cipiṭā yasyā hrasvā dīrghā kalipriyā  

śubhe vilocane strīṇāṃ raktānte kṛṣṇatārake 
gokṣīravarṇe viśade susnigdhe kṛṣṇapakṣmiṇī  

unnatākṣī na dīrghāyurvṛttākṣī kulaṭā bhavet 
ramaṇī madhupiṅgākṣī sukhasaubhāgyabhāginī  

puṃścalī vāmakāṇākṣī vandhyā dakṣiṇakāṇikā 
pārāvatākṣī duḥśīlā gajākṣī naiva śobhanā  

mṛdubhiḥ pakṣmabhiḥ kṛṣṇairghanaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ subhāgyayuk 
viralaiḥ kapilaiḥ sthūlairbhāminī dukhabhāginī  

vartulau kārmukākārau snigdhe kṛṣṇe asaṃhate 
subhruvau mṛduromāṇau subhruvāṃ sukhakīrtidau  

karṇau dīrghau śubhāvartau sutasaubhāgyadāyakau 
śaṣkulīrahitau nindyau śirālau kuṭilau kṛśau  

śirāvirahito bhālaḥ nirlomā'rdhaśaśiprabhaḥ 
animnastryaṅgulastroṇāṃ sutasaubhāgyasaukhyadaḥ  

spaṣṭasvastikacihnaśca bhālo rājyapradaḥ striyāḥ 
pralambo romaśaścaiva prāṃśuśca duḥkhadaḥ smṛtaḥ  

unnato gajakumbhābho vṛtto mūrdhā śubhaḥ striyāḥ 
sthūlo gīrgho'thavā vakro duḥkhadaurbhāgyasūcakaḥ  

kuntalāḥ komalāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ sūkṣmā dīrghaśca śobhanā 
piṅgalāḥ puruṣā rūkṣā viralā laghavo'śubhāḥ  

piṅgalā gauravarṇāyā śyāmāyāḥ śyāmalāḥ śubhāḥ 
nārīlakṣaṇataścaivaṃ narāṇāmapi cintayet  

medskiphrulemedskip

       atha tilādilāṃchanaphalādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

athā'haṃ dehajātānāṃ lāṃchanānāṃ phalaṃ bruve 
āvartānāṃ tilānāṃ ca maśakānāṃ viśeṣataḥ  

aṅganānāṃ ca vāmāṃge dakṣiṇāṅge nṛṇāṃ śubham 
raktābhaṃ tilakābhaṃ vā lomnāṃ cakramathāpi vā  

tilādilāṃchanaṃ strīṇāṃ hṛdi saubhāgyasūcakam 
yasyā dakṣiṇavakṣoje rakte tilakalāṃchane  

sā santatitatiṃ sūte sukhasaubhāgyasaṃyutām 
raktābhaṃ tilakaṃ yasyāḥ striyā vāme stane bhavet  

eka eva sutastasyā bhavatīta vido viduḥ 
putrīputrayutā jñeyā tilake dakṣiṇe stane  

bhruvormadhye lalāṭe vā lāṃchanaṃ rājasūcakam 
kapole maśako rakto nityaṃ miṣṭhānnadāyakaṃ  

bhagasya dakṣiṇe bhāge lāṃchanaṃ yadi yoṣitaḥ 
sā hi pṛthvīpateḥ patnī sūte vā bhūpatiṃ sutam  

nāsāgre lāñchane raktaṃ rājapatnyāḥ prajāyate 
kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ tu yasyāḥ sā puṃścali vidhavā'tha vā  

nābheradho nṛṇāṃ strīṇāṃ lāñchanaṃ ca śubhapradam 
karṇe gaṇḍe kare vā'pi kaṇṭhe vā'pyatha lāñchanaṃ  

prāggarbhe putradaṃ jñeyaṃ sukhasaubhāgyadaṃ tathā 
tilādi lāñchanaṃ vipra gulphageśe ca duḥkhadam  

triśūlākṛti cihna ca lalāṭe yadi jāyate 
nārī rājapriyā jñeyā bhūpatiśca naro bhavet  

lomnāṃ pradakṣiṇāvarto hṛdi nābhau kare śrutau 
dakṣapṛṣṭhe śubho vastau vāmāvarto'śubhapradaḥ  

kaṭyāṃ guhye'thavā'varto strīṇāṃ daurbhāgyasūcakaḥ 
udare hanti bhartāraṃ madhyapṛṣṭhe ca puṃścalī  

kaṇṭhe lalāṭe sīmante madhyabhāge ca mūrdhani 
āvarto na śubhaḥ strīṇāṃ pusāṃ vā'pi dvijottama  

sulakṣaṇā sucaritā api mandāyuṣaṃ patim 
dīrghāyuṣaṃ prakurvanti pramadāśca mudāspadam  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha pūrvajanmaśāpadyotanādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

maharṣe bhavatā proktaṃ phalaṃ strīṇāṃ nṛṇāṃ pṛthak 
adhunā śrotumicchāmi tvatto vedavidāṃvara  

aputrasya gatirnāsti śāstreṣu śrūyate mune 
aputraḥ kena pāpena bhavatīti vada prabho  

janmalagnācca tajjñānaṃ kathaṃ daivavidāṃ bhavet 
aputrasya sutaprāpterupāyaṃ kṛpayocyatām  

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā vipra kathyate hi tathā mayā 
yathomayā hi pṛṣṭena śivena kathitaṃ purā  

kena yogena pāpena jñāyate'patyanāśanam 
teṣāṃ ca rakṣaṇopāyaṃ kṛpayā nātha me vada  

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā devi kathayāmi tavā'dhunā 
santānahāniyogāṃśca tadrakṣopāyasaṃyutān  

gurulagneśa dāreśaputrasthānādhipeṣu ca 
sarveṣu balahīneṣu vaktavyā tvanapatyatā  

ravyārarāhuśanayaḥ sabalāḥ putrabhāvagāḥ 
tadā'napatyatā cet syurabalāḥ putrakārakāḥ  

putrasthānagate rāhau kujena ca nirīkṣite 
kujakṣetragate vā'pi sarpaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

putraśe rāhusaṃyukte putrasthe bhānunandane 
candreṇa saṃyute dṛṣṭe sarpaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

kārake rāhusaṃyukte putreśe balavarjite 
lagneśe kujasaṃyukte sarpaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

kārake bhaumasaṃyukte lagne ca rāhusaṃyute 
putrasthānādhipe duḥsthe sarpaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

bhaumāṃśe bhaumasaṃyukte putreśe somanandane 
rāhumāndiyute lagne sarpaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

putrabhāve kujakṣetre putreśe rāhusaṃyute 
saumyadṛṣṭe yute vā'pi sarpaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

putrasthā bhānumandārāḥ svabhānuḥ śaśijo'ṅgirāḥ 
nirbalau putralagneśau sarpaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagneśe rāhusaṃyukte putreśe bhomasaṃyute 
kārake rāhuyukte vā sarpaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

grahayogavaśenaivaṃ nṛṇāṃ jñātvā'napatyatā 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ nāgapūjāṃ samārabhet  

svagṛhyoktavidhānena pratiṣṭhāṃ kārayet sudhīḥ 
nāgamūrti suvarṇena kṛtvā pūjāṃ samācaret  

gobhūtilahiraṇyādi dadyād vittānusārataḥ 
evaṃ kṛte tu nāgendraprasādāt vardhate kulam  

putrasthānaṃ gate bhānau nīce mandāṃśakasthite 
pārśvayoḥ krūrasambandhe pitṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

putrasthānādhipe bhānau trikoṇe pāpasaṃyute 
krūrāntare pāpadṛṣṭe pitṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

bhānurāśisthite jīve putreśe bhānusaṃyute 
putre lagne ca pāpāḍhye pitṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagneśe durbale putre putreśe bhānusaṃyute 
putre lagne pāpayute pitṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

pitṛsthānādhipe putre putreśe vāpi karmage 
putre lagne ca pāpāḍhye pitṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

pitṛsthānādhipe bhaumaḥ putreśena samanvitaḥ 
lagne putre pitṛsthāne pāpe santatināśanam  

pitṛsthānādhipe duḥsthe kārake pāparāśige 
sapāpau putralagneśau pitṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagnapañcamabhāvasthā bhānubhaumaśanaiścarāḥ 
randhre riṣphe rāhujīvau pitṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagnādaṣṭamage bhānau putrasthe bhānunandane 
putreśe rāhusaṃyukte lagne pāpe sutakṣayaḥ  

vyayeśe lagnabhāvasthe randhreśe putrarāśige 
pitṛsthānādhipe randhre pitṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

rogeśe putrabhāvasthe pitṛsthānādhipe ripau 
kārake rāhusaṃyukte pitṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ gayāśrāddhaṃ ca kārayet 
brāhmaṇān bhojayedatra ayutaṃ vā sahasrakam  

athavā kanyakādānaṃ godānaṃ ca samācaret 
evaṃ kṛte pituḥ śāpānmucyate nā'tra saṃśayaḥ  

vardhate ca kulaṃ tasya putrapautradibhiḥ sadā 
grahayogavaśādevaṃ phalaṃ brūyāt vicakṣaṇaḥ  

putrasthānādhipe candre nīce vā pāpamadhyage 
hibuke pañcame pāpe mātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lābhe mandasamāyukte mātṛsthāne śubhetare 
nīce pañcamage candre mātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

putrasthānādhipe duḥsthe lagneśe nīcarāśige 
candre ca pāpasaṃyukte mātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

putreśe'ṣṭāririṣphesthe candre pāpāṃśasaṃgate 
lagne putre ca pāpāḍhye mātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

putrasthānādhipe candre mandarāhvārasaṃyute 
bhāgye vā putrabhāve vā mātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

mātṛsthānādhipe bhaume śanirāhusamanvite 
candrabhānuyute putre lagne vā santatikṣayaḥ  

lagnātmajeśau śatrusthau randhre mātradhipaḥ sthitaḥ 
pitṛnāśādhipau lagne mātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

ṣaṣṭhāṣṭameśau lagnasthau vyaye mātradhipaḥ sute 
candrajīvau pāpayuktau mātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

pāpamadhyagate lagne kṣīṇe candre ca saptama 
mātṛputre rāhumandau mātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

nāśasthānādhipe putre putreśe nāśarāśige 
candramātṛpatau duḥsthe mātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

candrakṣetre yadā lagne kujarāhusamanvite 
candramandau putrasaṃsthau mātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagne putre mṛtau riṣphe kujo rāhū raviḥ śaniḥ 
mātṛlagnādhipau duḥsthau mātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

nāśasthānaṃ gate jīve kujarāhusamanvite 
putrasthānau mandacandrau mātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

evaṃ yogaṃ budhaidṛṣṭvā vijñeyā tvanapatyatā 
tataḥ santānarakṣārthaṃ karttavyā śāntiruttamā  

setusnānaṃ prakartavyaṃ gāyatrīlakṣasaṃkhyakā 
raupyamātraṃ payaḥ pītvā grahadānaṃ prayatnataḥ  

brāhmaṇān bhojayettadvadaśvatthasya pradakṣiṇam 
kartavyaṃ bhaktiyuktena cāṣṭottarasahasrakam  

evaṃ kṛte mahādevi śāpānmokṣo bhaviṣyati 
suputraṃ labhate paścāt kulavṛddhiśca jāyate  

atho yogān pravakṣyāmi bhrātṛśāpasamudbhavān 
yajjñātvā'patyarakṣārthaṃ yatnaṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ  

bhrātṛsthānādhipe putre kujarāhusamanvite 
putralagneśvarau randhre bhrātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagne sute kuje mande bhrātṛpe bhāgyarāśige 
kārake nāśabhāvasthe bhrātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

bhrātṛsthāne gururnīce mandaḥ pañcamagate yadi 
nāśasthāne tu candrārau bhrātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

tanusthānādhipe riṣphe bhaumaḥ pañcamago yadi 
randhre sapāpaputreśe bhrātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

pāpamadhyagate lagne pāpamadhye sute'pi ca 
lagneśaputrapau duḥsthau bhrātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

karmeśe bhrātṛbhāvasthe pāpayukte tathā śubhe 
putrage kujasaṃyukte bhrātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

putrasthāne budhakṣetre śamirāhusamanvite 
riṣphe vidārau vijñeyo bhrātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagneśe bhrātṛbhāvasthe bhrātṛsthānādhipe sute 
lagnabhrātṛsute pāpe bhrātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

bhrātrīśe mṛtyubhāvasthe putrasthe kārake tathā 
rāhumandeyute dṛṣṭe bhrātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

nāśasthānādhipe putre bhrātṛnāthena saṃyute 
randhre ārārkisaṃyukte bhrātṛśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

bhrātṛśāpavimokṣārthaṃ vaṃśasya śravaṇaṃ hareḥ 
cāndrāyaṇś caret paścāt kāveryyā viṣṇusannidhau  

aśvatthasthāpanaṃ kuryād daśadhenūśca dāpayet 
patnīhastena putrecchurbhūmiṃ dadyāt phalānvitām  

evaṃ yaḥ kurute bhaktyā dharmapatnyā samanvitaḥ 
dhruvaṃ tasya bhavet putraḥ kulavṛddhiśca jāyate  

putrasthāne budhe jīve kujarāhusamanvite 
lagne mande sutabhāvo jñeyo mātulaśāpataḥ  

lagneputreśvarau putre budhabhaumārkisaṃyutau 
jñeyaṃ mātulaśāpatvājjanasya santatikṣayaḥ  

lupte putrādhipe lagne saptame bhānunandane 
lagneśe budhasaṃyukte tasyāpi santatikṣayaḥ  

jñātisthānādhipe lagne vyayeśena samanvite 
śaśisaumyakuje putre vijñeyaḥ santatikṣayaḥ  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ viṣṇusthāparamācaret 
vāpīkūpataḍāgādikhananaṃ sutabandhunam  

putravṛddhirbhavettasya saṃpadvṛddhiḥ prajāyate 
iti yogavaśādevaṃ śāntiṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ  

balagarvva yo martyo brāhmaṇānavamanyate 
taddoṣād brahmaśāpācca tasya syāt santatikṣayaḥ  

gurukṣetre yadā rāhuḥ putre jīvārabhānujāḥ 
dharmasthānādhipe nāśe brahmaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

dharmeśe putrabhāvasthe putreśe nāśarāśige 
jīvārarāhubhiryukte brahmaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

dharmabhāvādhipe nīce vyayeśe putrabhāvage 
rāhuyutekṣite vāpi brahmaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

jīve nīcagate rāhau lagne vā putrarāśige 
putrasthānādhipe duḥsthe brahmaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

putrabhāvādhipe jīve randhre pāpasamanvite 
putreśe sārkacandre vā brahmaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

mandāṃśe mandasaṃyukte jīve bhaumasamanvite 
putreśe vyayarāśisthe brahmaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagne guruyute mande bhāgye rāhusamanvite 
vyaya vā gurusaṃyukte brahmaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

tasya doṣasya śāntyarthaṃ kuryāccāndrāyaṇaṃ naraḥ 
brahmakṛcchratryaṃ kṛtvā dhanuṃ dadyāt sadakṣiṇām  

pañcaratnāni deyāni suvarṇasahitāni ca 
brāhmaṇān bhojayet paścādyathāśakti dvijottama  

evaṃ kṛte tu satputraṃ labhate nā'tra saṃśayaḥ 
muktaśāpo viśuddhātmā sa naraḥ sukhamedhate  

dāreśe putrabhāvasthe dāreśasyāṃśape śanau 
putreśe nāśarāśisthe patnīśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

nāśasaṃsthe kalatreśe putreśe nāśarāśige 
kārake pāpasaṃyukte patnīśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

putrasthānagate śukre kāmape randhramāśrite 
kārake pāpasaṃyukte patnīśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

kuṭumbe pāpasaṃyukte kāmape nāśarāśige 
putre pāpagrahairyukte patnīśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

bhāgyasthānagate śukre dāreśe nāśarāśige 
lagne sute ca pāpaḍhye patnīśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

bhāgyasthānādhipe śukre putreśe śatrurāśige 
gurulagneśadāreśā duḥsthāścet santatikṣayaḥ  

putrasthāne bhṛgukṣetre rāhucandrasamanvite 
vyaye lagne dhane pāpe patnīśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

saptame mandaśukrau ca randhreśe putrabhe ravau 
lagne rāhusamāyukte patnīśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

dhane kuje vyaye jīve putrasthe bhṛgunandane 
śanirāhuyute dṛṣṭe patnīśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

nāśasthau vittadāreśau putre lagne kuje śanau 
kārake pāpasaṃyukte patnīśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagnapañcamabhāgyasthā rāhumandakujāḥ kramāt 
randhrasthau putradāreśau patnīśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

śāpamuktyai ca kanyāyāṃ satyāṃ taddānamācaret 
kanyābhāve ca śrīviṣṇormūrti lakṣmīsamanvitām  

dadyāt svarṇamayīṃ vipra daśadenusamanvitām 
śayyāṃ ca bhūṣaṇaṃ vastraṃ dampatibhyāṃ dvijanmanām  

dhruvaṃ tasya bhavet putro bhāgyavṛddhiśca jāyate 
karmalope pitṛṇāṃ ca pretatvaṃ tasya jāyate  

tasya pretasya śāpācca putrābhāvaḥ prajāyate 
ato'tra tādṛśān yogāt janmalagnāt pravacmyaham  

putrasthānau mandasūryau kṣīṇacandraśca saptame 
lagne vyaye rāhujīvau pretaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

putrasthānādhipe mande nāśasthe lagnage kuje 
kārake nāśabhāve ca pretaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagne pāpe vyaye bhānau sute cārārkisomajāḥ 
putreśe randhrabhāvasthe pretaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagne svarbhānunā yukte putrasthe bhānunandane 
gurau ca nāśarāśisthe pretaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagne rāhau saśukrejye candre mandayute tathā 
lagneśe mṛtyurāśisthe pretaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

putrasthānādhipe nīce kārake nīcarāśige 
nīcasthagrahadṛṣṭe ca pretaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

lagne mande sute rāhau randhre bhānusamanvite 
vyaye bhaumena saṃyukte pretaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

kāmasthānādhipe duḥsthe putre candrasamanvite 
mandamāndiyute lagne pretaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

vadhasthānādhipe putre śaniśukrasamanvite 
kārake nāśarāśisthe pretaśāpāt sutakṣayaḥ  

asya doṣasya śāntyarthaṃ gayāśrāddhaṃ samācaret 
kuryāṃdrudrābhiṣekañca brahmamūrti pradāpayet  

dhenuṃ rajatapātraṃ ca tathā nīlamaṇiṃ dvija 
brāhmaṇān bhojayet paścāt tebhyaśca dakṣiṇāṃ diśet  

evaṃ kṛte manuṣyasya śāpamokṣā prajāyate 
putrotpattirbhavettasya kulavṛddhiśca jāyate  

tathā jñaśukraje doṣe putrāptiḥ śambhupūjanāt 
jīvacandrakṛte vipra mantrayantrauṣadhāditaḥ  

rāhuje kanyakādānāt sūryaje harikīrtanāt 
godānāt ketuje doṣe rudrajāpāt kujā'rkije  

sarvadoṣavināśāya śubhasantānalabdhaye 
harivaṃśakathā bhaktyā śrotavyā vidhinā dvija  

medskiphrulemedskip

          atha grahaśāntyadhyāyaḥ  

medskip

grahāṇāṃ doṣaśāntyarthaṃ teṣāṃ pūjāvidhiṃ vada 
mānavānāṃ hitārthāya saṃkṣepāt kṛpayā mune  

grahā sūryādayaḥ pūrvaṃ mayā proktā dvijottama 
jagatyāṃ sarvajantūnāṃ tadadhīnaṃ sukhā'sukham  

tasmāt suśāntikāmo vā śrīkāmo vā sucetasā 
vṛṣṭāyāyuḥ puṣṭikāmo vā teṣāṃ yajñaṃ samācaret  

tābhrācca sphaṭikādraktacandanāt svarṇakādubhau 
rajatādayasaḥ sīsāt kāṃsyāt kāryāḥ krāmad grahāḥ  

pūrvoktaiḥ svasvavarṇairvā paṭe lekhyā dvijottamaiḥ 
svasvoktadigvibhāgeṣu gandyādyairmaṇḍaneṣu vā  

padmāsanaḥ padmahastaḥ padmapatrasamadyutiḥ 
saptāśvarathasaṃsthaśca dvibhujaśca divākaraḥ  

śvetaḥ śvetāmbaro devo daśāśvaḥ śvetabhūṣaṇaḥ 
gadāhasto dvibāhuśca vidhātavyo vidhurdvija  

raktamālyāmbaradharo śaktiśūlagadādharaḥ 
varadastu caturbāhurmaṅgalo meṣavāhanaḥ  

pītamālyāmbaradharaḥ karṇikārasamadyutiḥ 
khaḍgacarmagadāpāṇiḥ siṃhastho varado budhaḥ  

guruśukrau kramāt pītaśvetavarṇau caturbhujau 
daṇḍinau varadau kāryau sākṣasūtrakamaṇḍalū  

indranīladyutiḥ śūlī varado gṛdhravāhanaḥ 
vāṇavāṇāsanadharo vijñeyo'rkasuto dvija  

karālavadanaḥ khaḍgacarmaśūlī varapradaḥ 
siṃhastho nīlavarṇaśca rāhurevaṃ prakalpyate  

dhūmrā dvibāhavaḥ sarve gadino vikṛtānanāḥ 
gṛdhrāsanā nityaṃ ketavaḥ syurvarapradā  

sarve kirīṭinaḥ kāryā grahā lokahitapradāḥ 
svāṃgulenocchritā vijñaiḥ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ sadā  

yathāvarṇaṃ pradeyāni sudṣpāṇi vasanāni ca 
gandho dīpo baliścaiva dhūpo deyaśca gugguluḥ  

yasya grahasya yaddravyamannaṃ yasya ca yat priyam 
tacca tasyai pradātavyaṃ bhaktiyuktena cetasā  

ākṛṣṇena imaṃ devā agnirmūrdhā divaḥ kakut 
udbudhyasveti mantrāṃśca japedatha bṛhaspate  

annāt pariśrutaśceti śanno devīrabhīṣṭaye 
kayā naścitra ityevaṃ ketu kṛṇvannimāṃstathā  

sapta rudrā diśo nandā navacandrā nṛpāstathā 
tripakṣā aṣṭacandrāśca saptacandrāstathaiva ca  

imāḥ saṃkhyāḥ sahasraghnā japasaṃkhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
kramādarkādikheṭānāṃ prītyarthaṃ dvijapuṅgava  

arkaḥ palāśaḥ khadirastvapāmārgastu pippalaḥ 
udumbaraḥ śamī durvā kuśāśca samidhaḥ kramāt  

hotavyā madhusarpibhyāṃ dadhnā kṣīreṇa vā yutāḥ 
ekaikasya tvaṣṭa śatamaṣṭāviṃśatireva vā  

guḍaidanaṃ pāyasaṃ ca haviṣyaṃ kṣīraṣāṣṭikam 
dadhyodanaṃ haviścūrṇaṃ māṃsaṃ citrānnameva ca  

dadyād grahakramādevaṃ viprebhyo bhojanaṃ dvija 
śaktito vā yathālābhaṃ deyaṃ satkārapūrvakam  

dhenuḥ śaṅkhastathā'naḍvān hema vāso hayaḥ kramāt 
kṛṣṇā gaurāyasaṃ chāga etā ravyādidakṣiṇāḥ  

yasya yaśca yadā duḥsthaḥ sa taṃ yatnena pūjayet 
eṣāṃ dhātrā varo dattaḥ pūjitāḥ pūjayiṣyatha  

mānavānāṃ grahādhīnā uñchrāyāḥ patanāni ca 
bhāvā'bhāvau ca jagatāṃ tasmāt pūjyatamā grahāḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha'śubhajanmakathanādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

athā'nyat saṃpravakṣyāmi sulagne sugraheṣvapi 
yadanyakāraṇenāpi bhavejjanmā'śubhapradam  

darśe kṛṣṇācaturdaśyāṃ viṣṭyāṃ sodarabhe tathā 
pitṛbhe sūryasaṃkrāntau pāte'rkendugrahe tathā  

vyatīpātādiduryoge gaṇḍānte trividhe'pi vā 
yamaghaṇṭe'vabhe dagdhayoge trītarajanma ca  

prasavasya trikāre'pi jñeyaṃ janmā'śubhapradam 
śāntyā bhavati kalyāṇaṃ tadupāyaṃ ca vacmyaham  

medskiphrulemedskip

       atha darśajanmaśāntyadhyāyaḥ  

medskip

maitreya darśajātānāṃ mātāpitrordaridratā 
taddoṣaparihārāya śāntiṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ  

kalaśasthāpanaṃ kṛtvā prathamaṃ vidhipūrvakam 
udumbaraṭāśvatthacūtānāṃ pallavāṃstathā  

sanimbānāṃ ca mūlani tvacastatra vinikṣipet 
paṃcaratnāni nikṣipya vastrayugmena ceṣṭayet  

sarve samudra iti cā'pohiṣṭhāditryṛcena ca 
āmantrya kalaśe tacca sthāpayed vahnikoṇake  

darśasya devayoścā'tha candrabhāskarayoḥ kramāt 
pratimāṃ svarṇajāṃ nityaṃ rājatīṃ tāmrajāṃ tathā  

āpyāyasveti mantrena' savitā paścāttameva ca 
upacāraiḥ samārādhya tato homaṃ samācaret  

samidhaśca caruṃ vidvān krameṇa juhuyāt vratī 
bhaktyā savitṛmantreṇa somo dhenuśca mantrataḥ  

aṣṭottaraśataṃ vāpi aṣṭaviṃśatireva vā 
abhiṣekaṃ tathā kuryāt dampatyośca suputrayoḥ  

hiraṇyaṃ rajataṃ caiva kṛṣṇadhenuśca dakṣiṇā 
brāhmaṇān bhojayet śaktyā tataḥ kṣemamavāpnuyāt  

medskiphrulemedskip

       atha kṛṣṇacaturdaśījanma śāntyadhyāyaḥ  

medskip

kṛṣṇapakṣacaturdaśyāḥ ṣaḍbhāgeṣu phalaṃ kramāt 
janma cet prathame bhāge tadā jñeyaṃ śubhaṃ dvija  

dvitīye pitaraṃ hanti mātaraṃ ca tṛtīyake 
caturthe mātulaṃ caiva pañcame vaṃśanāśanam  

ṣaṣṭhe tu dhananāśaḥ syādātmano nāśa eva vā 
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ śāntiṃ kuryād prayatnataḥ  

śivasya pratimāṃ kuryāt sauvarṇīṃ karṣasammitām 
tadardhārdhamitāṃ vā'pi yathāvittaṃ manoharām  

bālacandrakirīṭāñca śvetamālyāmbarānvitām 
trinetrāṃ ca vṛṣāsīnāṃ varābhayakarāmatha  

trayambakaṃ ceti mantreṇa pūjāṃ kuryādatandritaḥ 
āvāhya vāruṇairmantrairācāryo mantratattvavit  

imaṃ me varuṇe tyevaṃ tattvā yāmī tyṛcā punaḥ 
ttvanna agne ityanayā satvaṃ no ityṛcāpi ca  

āgneyaṃ kumbhamārabhya pūjayed bhaktitaḥ kramāt 
ā nobhadreti sūktaṃ ca bhadrā agneśca sūktakam  

japtvā puruṣasūktaṃ ca kandrudreti tathā japet 
śaṅkarasyā'bhiṣekaṃ ca grahapūjāṃ ca kārayet  

samidājyacarūṃścaiva tilamāṣāṃśca sarpapān 
aśvasthalpakṣapālāsakhādirāḥ samidhaḥ śubhāḥ  

aṣṭottaraśataṃ vahnau juhuyād vidhipūrvakam 
aṣṭaviṃśatisaṃkhyā vā homaṃ kuryāt pṛthak pṛthak  

mantreṇa tryambakenātha tilān vyāhṛtibhistathā 
grahahomaṃ ca vidhivat kuryād kṣemaṃ tato bhavet  

abhiṣekaṃ ca jātasya tatpitroścāpi mantravit 
kuryāt tato yathāśakti brāhmaṇān bhojayet sudhīḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha bhardāvamaduryogaśāntyadhyāyaḥ  

medskip

athā'haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi bhadrāyāmavame tathā 
vyātoopātādiduryoge yamaghaṇṭādike ca yat  

janmāśubhaphalaṃ proktaṃ tasya śāntividhiṃ dvija 
prāpte prasūtiduryoge śāntiṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ  

daivajñairdarśite vā'pi sulagne sudine gṛhī 
pūjanaṃ devatānāṃ ca grahāṇāṃ yajanaṃ tathā  

śaṅkarasyā'bhiṣekaṃ ca ghṛtadīpaṃ śivālaye 
āyurvṛddhikaraṃ kuryādaśvatthasya pradakṣiṇam  

havanaṃ viṣṇumantreṇa satamaṣṭottaraṃ sudhīḥ 
brāhmaṇān bhojayet śaktyā tataḥ kalyāṇamāpnuyāt  

medskiphrulemedskip

       athaika nakṣatra jātaśāntyadhyāyaḥ  

medskip

atha yadyekanakṣatre bhrātrorvā pitṛputrayoḥ 
prasūtiśca tayormṛturathaivakasya niścayaḥ  

tatra śāntiṃ pravakṣyāmi gargādimunibhāṣitam 
sudine śubhanakṣatre candratārābalānvite  

riktāvaviṣṭivivarjye ca samaya śāntimācaret 
śanerīśānadigbhāge nakṣatrapratimāṃ śubhām  

tannakṣatroktamantreṇa pūjayet kalaśopari 
raktavastreṇa saṃchādya vastrayugmena veṣṭayet  

svasvaśākhoktamārgeṇa kuryādagnimukhaṃ tathā 
punastenaiva mantreṇa hunadaṣṭottaraṃ śatam  

pratyekaṃ samidannājyaiḥ prāyaścittāntameva hi 
abhiṣekaṃ tataḥ kuryādācāryaśca dvayorapi  

ṛtvigbhyo dakṣiṇāṃ dadyādācāryāya viśeṣataḥ 
brāhmaṇān bhojayed bhaktyā vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha saṃkrāntijanmaśāntyadhyāyaḥ  

medskip

ghorādhvāṃkṣīmahodaryo mandā mandākinī tathā 
miśrā ca rākṣasī sūryasaṃkrāntiḥ sūryavāsarāt  

saṃkrāntau ca naro jāto bhaved dāridrya duḥkhabhāk 
śāntyā sukhamavāpnoti tataḥ śāntividhi bruve  

navagrahamakhaṃ kuryāt tasya doṣopaśāntaye 
gṛhasya pūrvadigbhāge gomayenopalipya ca  

svalaṃkṛtapradeśe tu brīhirāśiṃ prakalpayet 
pañcadroṇamitaṃ dhānyaistadardhaṃ taṇḍulaistathā  

tadardhaṃ ca tilaiḥ kuryādrāśiṃ ca dvijasattama 
pṛthak tritayarāśau tu likhedaṣṭadalaṃ budhaiḥ  

puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā tu ācāryaṃ vṛṇuyāt purā 
dharmajñaṃ mantratattvajñaṃ śāntikarmaṇi kovidam  

rāśiṣu sthāpayet kumbhānavraṇān sumanoharān 
tīrthodakena sampūrya samṛdauṣadhapallavam  

paṃcagavyaṃ kṣipettatra vastrayugmena veṣṭayet 
kumbhopari nyaset pātraṃ sūkṣmavastreṇa veṣṭitam  

pratimāṃ sthāpayet tatra sādhipratyadhidaivatām 
adhidaivaṃ bhavet sūryaścandraḥ pratyadhidaivatam  

candrādityākṛtī pārśve madhye saṃkrāntimarcayet 
pratimāṃ pūjane pūrvaṃ vastrayugmaṃ nivedayet  

tato vyāhṛtipūrrveṇa tattanmantreṇa pūjayet 
traiyambakeṇa mantreṇa pradhānapratibhāṃ pūjayet  

utsūrya iti mantreṇa sūryapūjāṃ samācaret 
āpyāyasveti mantreṇa candrapūjāṃ samācaret  

upacāraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiryadvā pañcopacārakaiḥ 
mṛtyuṃjayana mantreṇa pradhānapratimāṃ spṛśan  

aṣṭottarasahasraṃ cā'pyaṣṭottaraśataṃ japet 
athā'ṣṭāviṃśatiṃ vāpi japenmantraṃ svaśaktitaḥ  

kumbhebhyaḥ paścime deśe sthaṇḍile'gniṃ prakalpayet 
svagṛhyoktavidhānena kārayet saṃskṛtānalam  

trayambakena mantreṇa samidājyacarūn hunet 
aṣṭottarasahasraṃ vā aṣṭottaraśataṃ yathā  

aṣṭaviṃśatimevāpi kuryād homaṃ svaśaktitaḥ 
mṛtyuṃjayena mantreṇa tilahomaśca kārayet  

tataḥ sviṣṭakṛtaṃ hutvāabhiṣekaṃ ca kārayet 
brahmaṇān bhojayet paścādevaṃ śāntimavāpnuyāt

medskiphrulemedskip

             atha grahaṇajātaśāntyadhyāyaḥ  

medskip

sūryendugrahaṇe kāle yeṣāṃ janma bhaved dvija 
vyādhiḥ kaṣṭaṃ ca dāridryaṃ teṣāṃ mṛtyubhayaṃ bhavet  

ataḥ śāntiṃ pravakṣyāmi janānāṃ hitakāṅkṣayā 
sūryasyendośca graheṇaṃ yasminṛkṣe prajāyate  

tannakṣatrapate rūpaṃ suvarṇena prakalpayet 
sūryagrahe sūryarūpaṃ suvarṇena svaśaktitaḥ  

candragrahe candrarūpaṃ rajatena tathaiva ca 
rāhurūpaṃ prakurvīta sīsakena vicakṣaṇaḥ  

śucau deśe samaṃ sthānaṃ gomayena pralepayet 
tatra ca sthāpayed vastraṃ nūtanaṃ sumanoharam  

trayāṇāmeva rūpāṇāṃ sthāpanaṃ tatra kārayet 
sūryagrahe pradātavyaṃ sūryaprītikaraṃ ca yat  

raktākṣataṃ raktagandhaṃ raktamālyāmbarādikam 
candragrahe pradātavyaṃ candraprītikaraṃ ca yat  

śvetagandhaṃ śvetapuṣpaṃ śvetamālyāmbarādikam 
rāhave ca pradātavyaṃ kṛṣṇapuṣpāmbarādikam  

dadyānnakṣatranāthāya śvetagandhādikaṃ tathā 
sūryaṃ sampūjayeddhīmānākṛṣṇeti ca mantrataḥ  

athā candraṃ ime devā iti mantreṇa bhaktitaḥ 
dūrvābhi pūjayedrāhuṃ kayā na iti mantrataḥ  

sūryendvorarkapālāśamidbhirjuhuyāt kramāt 
tathā ca rāhoḥ prītyarthaṃ dūrvābhirdvijasattama  

brahmavṛkṣasamidbhiśca bheśāya juhuyāt punaḥ 
abhiṣekaṃ tataḥ kuryāt jātasya kalahodakaiḥ  

ācāryaṃ pūjayedbhaktyā suśānto vijitendriyaḥ 
brāhmaṇān bhojayetvā tu yathāśakti visarjayet  

evaṃ grahaṇajātasya śāntiṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ 
sarvavighnaṃ vinirjitvā saubhāgyaṃ labhate naraḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

         atha gaṇḍāntajātaśāntyadhyāyaḥ  

medskip

tithinakṣatralagnānāṃ gaṇḍāntaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam 
janmayātrāvivāhādau bhavettannidhanapradam  

pūrṇānandākhyayostithyoḥ sandhau nāḍīcatuṣṭayam 
adha ūrdhvaṃ ca maitreya tithigaṇḍāntamucyate  

revatīdāsrayoḥ sāpramaghayoḥ śākramūlayoḥ 
sandhau nakṣatragaṇḍāntamevaṃ nāḍīcatuṣṭayam  

mīnājayoḥ karkiharyorlagnayoralicāpayoḥ 
sandhau ca lagnagaṇḍāntamadhaūrdhva ghaṭīmitam  

eṣu cābhuktamūlākhyaṃ mahāvighnapadaṃ smṛtam 
indrarākṣasayoḥ sandhau pañcāṣṭaghaṭikāḥ kramāt  

atha gaṇḍāntajātasya śiśoḥ śāntividhiṃ bruve 
gaṇḍāntakālajātasya sūtakāntyadine pitā  

śāntiṃśubhe'hni vā kuryāt paśyet tāvanna taṃ śiśum 
vṛṣabhaṃ tithigaṇḍānte nakṣatre dhanumeva ca  

kāñcanaṃ lagnagaṇḍānte dadyāttaddoṣapraśāntaye 
ādyabhāge prajātasya pituścāpyabhiṣecanam  

dvitīye tu śiśormāturabhiṣekaṃ ca kārayet 
suvarṇena tadardheṇa yathāvittaṃ dvijottama 
tithibheṣādirūpaṃ ca kṛtvā vastrasamanvitam  

upacārairyathāśakti kalahopari pūjayet 
pūjānte samidannajyairhoma kuryādyathāvidhi  

brāhmaṇān bhojayet paścādevaṃ doṣātpramucyate 
āyurārogyamaiśvaryaṃ samprāpnoti dine dine  

medskiphrulemedskip

       atha abhuktamūlaśāntyadhyāyaḥ  

medskip

jyeṣṭhāmūlamayoryasmādadhipāvindrarākṣasau 
mahāvairāt tayoḥ sandhirmahādoṣapradaḥ smṛtaḥ  

abhuktamūlajaṃ putraṃ putrīṃ vā'pi parityajet 
athavā'bdāṣṭakaṃ tātastanmukhaṃ na vilokayet  

taddoṣaparihārārthamatha śāntividhiṃ bruve 
tatrā'dau doṣabahulyān mūlaśāntirnigadyate  

janmato dvādaśāhe vā tadṛkṣe vā śubhe dine 
jātasya vā'ṣṭame varṣe śāntiṃ kuryād vidhānataḥ  

susame ca śubhe sthāne gomayenopalepite 
maṇḍapaṃ svagṛhāt prācyāmudīcyāṃ vā prakalpayet  

caturdvārasamāyuktaṃ toraṇādyairalaṅkṛtam 
kuṇḍaṃ grahādiyajñārthaṃ tadbahiśca prakalpayet  

suvarṇena tadardhena tadardhārdhena vā punaḥ 
nakṣatradevatārūpaṃ kuryād vittānusārataḥ  

śyāmavarṇaṃ mahograṃ ca dviśiraskaṃ vṛkānanam 
khaḍgacarmadharaṃ tadvad dhyeyaṃ kuṇapavāhanam  

suvarṇasya ca mūlyaṃ vā sthāpayitvā prapūjayet 
suvarṇaṃ sarvadaivatyaṃ yataḥ śāstreṣu niścitam  

ācāryaṃ varayet paścāt svastivācanupūrvakam 
kalaśasthāpanaṃ kuryāt svagṛhyoktavidhānataḥ  

pañcagavyādikaṃ kṣepyaṃ kalaśe tīrthavāri ca 
śatauṣadhyādikaṃ tatra śatacchidraghaṭe kṣipet  

vaṃśapātraṃ ca saṃsthāpya tatra vai paścimāmukham 
arceyennirṛtiṃ devaṃ śuklavastrākṣatādibhiḥ  

indraṃ tadadhidevaṃ ca jalaṃ pratyadhidaivatam 
svasvaśākhoktamantreṇa pradhānādīnprapūjayet  

devādhidevaprītyarthaṃ homaṃ kuryādyathāvidhi 
aṣṭottaraṃ sahasraṃ vā śataṃ vā niyatendriyaḥ  

mṛtyupraśamanārthaṃ ca mantraṃ trayambakaṃ japet 
prārthayecca tato devamabhiṣekārthamādarāt  

bhadrāsanopaviṣṭasya sastrīputrasya mantravit 
ācāryo yajamānasya kuryāt prītyābhiṣecanam  

vastrāntaritakumbhābhyāṃ snāpayettadanantaram 
śuklāmbaradharastadvat śvetagandhānulepanaḥ  

dhenuṃ payasvinīṃ dadyādācāryāya ca śaktitaḥ 
ṛtvigbhyo dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād brāhmaṇāṃścāpi bhojayet  

yatpāpaṃ yacca me dauḥsthyaṃ sarvagātreṣvavasthitam 
tatsarvaṃ bhakṣayājya tvaṃ lakṣmīṃ puṣṭiṃ ca vardhaya  

anenaiva tu mantreṇa samyagājyaṃ vilokayet 
mūlagaṇḍodbhavastaivaṃ sarpapāpaṃ praṇaśyati  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha jyeṣṭhādi gaṇḍaśāntyadhyāyaḥ  

medskip

jyeṣṭhāgaṇḍāntajātastu pituḥ svasya ca nāśakaḥ 
tasya śāntividhiṃ vakṣye sarvavighnopaśāntaye  

mūlaśāntisamaṃ sarvamātrāpi maṇḍapādikam 
indro'tra devatā tadvadadhidevo'nalastathā  

vijñeyaṃ ca tathā vipra rakṣaḥ pratyadhidaivatam 
yathāśakti suvarṇena kuryādindrasvarūpakam  

vajrāṅkuśadharaṃ divyaṃ gajarājoparisthitam 
śālitaṇḍulasaṃyuktakumbhasyopari pūjayet  

svasvagṛhyoktamantreṇa gandhapuṣpākṣatādibhiḥ 
abhiṣekaṃ ca homaṃ ca kuryād brāhmaṇabhojanam  

indrasūktaṃ japed bhaktyā mantraṃ mṛtyuñjayaṃ tathā 
prārthayedindradevaṃ ca tataḥ śāntimavāpnuyāt  

atha vā śaktyabhāve tu kuryād godānameva hi 
yataḥ samastabhūdānād godānamatiricyate  

mūlendrāhimaghāgaṇḍajāte dadyād gavāṃ trayam 
goyugmaṃ pauṣṇadāsrotthe gaṇḍānte ca dvijanmane  

anyagaṇḍe ca duryoge gāmekāṃ hi pradāpayet 
gorabhāve ca viprāya dadyāt tanmūlyameva hi  

jyeṣṭhanakṣatrajā kanyā vinihanti dhavāgrajam 
viśākhāntyapadotpannā kanyā devaraghātinī  

tasyāḥ pradānakāle'to godānamapi kārayet 
āśleṣāntyatripādotthau mūlādyatripadodbhavau  

kanyāsutau hataḥ śvaśrūṃ śvaśurañca yathākramam 
tayorvivāhakāle'taḥ śāntiṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ  

tattadoṣavināśāya yathāvittānusārataḥ 
dhavāgrajadyabhāve tu na doṣāya prajāyate  

medskiphrulemedskip

        atha trītarajanmaśāntyadhyāyaḥ  

medskip

athā'nyat saṃpravakṣyāmi janmadoṣapradaṃ dvija 
sutatrye sutājanma tattraye sutajanma cet  

tadā'riṣṭabhayaṃ jñeyaṃ pitṛmātṛkuladvaye 
tatra śāntividhiṃ kuryād vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ  

sūtakānte'tha vā śuddhe samaye ca śubhe dine 
ācāryamṛtvijo vṛtvā grahayajñapuraśaram  

brahmaviṣṇu maheśendrapratimāḥ svarṇajāḥ śubhāḥ 
pūjayed dhānyarāśisthakalaśopari bhaktitaḥ  

catvāri rudrasūktāni śāntisūktāni sarvaśaḥ 
vipra eko japed homakāle ca sucisaṃyataḥ  

ācāryo juhuyāttatra samidājyatilāṃścarum 
aṣṭottaraṃ sahasraṃ vā śataṃ vā'ṣṭau ca viṃśatim  

brahmādisarvadevebhyaḥ svasvagṛhyoktamantrataḥ 
tataḥ sviṣṭakṛtaṃ hutvā baliṃ pūrṇāhutiṃ punaḥ  

abhiṣekaṃ ca jātasya sakuṭumbasya kārayet 
ṛtvigbhyo dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād brāhmaṇāṃścāpi bhojayet  

kāṃsyājyavīkṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā dīnānāthāṃśca tarpayet 
evaṃ śāntyā ca maitreya sarvāriṣṭaṃ vilīyate  

medskiphrulemedskip

       atha prasavavikāraśāntyadhyāyaḥ  

medskip

athā'haṃ sampravakṣyāmi vikāraṃ prasavodbhavam 
yenā'riṣṭaṃ samastasya grāmasya ca kulasya ca  

atyalpe vā'dhike kāle prasavo yadi jāyate 
hīnāṅgovā'dhikāṅgo vā viśirā dviśirāstathā  

nāryā paśvākṛtirvāpi paśuṣvapi narākṛtiḥ 
prasavasya vikāro'yaṃ vināśāyopajāyate  

yasya striyāḥ paśunāṃ vā vikārāḥ prasavodbhavaḥ 
aniṣṭaṃ bhavane tasya kule'pi ca mahad bhavet  

taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ śāntiḥ kāryā prayatnataḥ 
strī vā gauvaṃḍavā vāpi parityājyā hitārthinā  

nāryāḥ pañcadaśe varṣe janmataḥ ṣoḍaśo'pi vā 
garbho vā prasavo vā'pi na śubhāya prajāyate  

siṃharāśisthite'rka gaunakrasthe mahiṣī tathā 
prasūtā svāminaṃ hanti svayaṃ cāpi vinaśyati  

brāhmaṇāya pradadyāt tāṃ śāntiṃ vāpi samācaret 
brahmaviṣṇumaheśānāṃ grahāṇāṃ caiva pūjanam  

sarvaṃ homādikaṃ karma kuryāt tritaraśāntivat 
tato gṛho sukhī bhūtvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  

evaṃ tvariṣṭe samprāpte naraḥ śāntiṃ karoti yaḥ 
sarvān kāmānavāpnoti cirajīvī sukhī ca saḥ  

medskiphrulemedskip

           athopasaṃhārādhyāyaḥ  

medskip

yacchāstraṃ brahmaṇā proktaṃ nāradāya mahātmane 
tadeva śaunakādibhyo nāradaḥ prāha sādaram  

tato mayā yathā jñātaṃ tubhyamuktaṃ tathā dvija 
nāsūyakāya dātavyaṃ paranindāratāya vā  

jaḍāya durvinītāya nājñātāya kadācana 
deyametatsurilāya bhaktāya satyavādine  

medhāvine vinītāya samyag jñātakulāya ca 
puṇyadaṃ jyautiṣaṃ śāstramagryaṃ vedāṅgamuttamam  

jānāti kālamānaṃ yo graharkṣāṇāṃ ca saṃsthitim 
horāśāstramidaṃ samyak sa vijānāti nā'paraḥ  

horāśāstrārthatattvajñaḥ satyavāg vijitendriyaḥ 
śubhā'śubhaṃ phalaṃ vakti satyaṃ tadvacanaṃ bhavet  

ye suśāstraṃ paṭhantīdaṃ ye vā śṛṇvanti bhaktitaḥ 
teṣāṃmāyurbalaṃ vittaṃ vṛddhimeti yaśaḥ sadā  

itthaṃ parāśareṇoktaṃ horāśāstraṃ camatkṛtam 
navaṃ navajanaprītyai vividhādhyāyasaṃyutam  

śreṣṭhaṃ jagaddhitāyedaṃ maitreyāya dvijanmane 
tataḥ pracaritaṃ pṛthvyāmādṛtaṃ sādaraṃ janaiḥ  

granthe'smin pṛthagadhyāyairviṣayā viniveśitāḥ 
sṛṣṭikramo'vatārāśca guṇāḥ kheṭasya bhasya ca  

viśeṣalagnaṃ vargāśca tadvivekaśca rāśidṛk 
ariṣṭaṃ tadvibhaṅgaśca viveko bhāvajastathā  

bhāvānāṃ ca phalādhyāyo bhāveśotthaphalaṃ tathā 
aprakāśaphalaṃ spaṣṭakheṭadṛṣṭiprasādhanam  

tataḥ spaṣṭabalādhyāyaḥ iṣṭakaṣṭaprasādhanam 
padaṃ copapadaṃ tadvadargalā tvatha kārakāḥ  

kārakāṃśaphalaṃ yogakārakādhyāya eva ca 
nābhasā vividhā yogāścandrayogo'rkayogakaḥ  

rājayogastataḥ prokto rājasambandhayogakaḥ 
viśeṣadhanayogāśca yogā dāridryakārakāḥ  

āyurmārakabhedāśca grahāvasthāḥ phalānvitāḥ 
nānāvidhadaśādhyāyāstatphalādhyāyaḥ saṃyutāḥ  

antaḥpratyantaraprāṇasūkṣmasaṃjñāśca tadbhidāḥ 
sūryādyaṣṭakavargaśca trikoṇapariśodhanam  

ekādhipatyasaṃśuddhistataḥ piṇḍaprasādhanam 
tataścā'ṣṭakavargāṇāṃ prasphuṭāni phalāni ca  

tato'pyaṣṭakavargāyuḥsādhanaṃ ca tataḥ param 
samudāyāṣṭavargotthaphalādhyāyaḥ parisphuṭaḥ  

graharaśmiphalādhyāyaḥ sudarśanaphalaṃ tathā 
mahāpuruṣacihnāni mahābhūtaphalāni ca  

guṇatrayaphalādhyāyastato'pyajñātajanmanām 
janmalagnādivijñānaṃ pravrajyālakṣaṇāni ca  

strīṇāṃ ca phalavaiṣṭyamaṅgalakṣmaphalāni ca 
pūrvapāpotthaśāpotthayogā vaiputryakārakāḥ  

satputraprāptyupāyāśca sahaiva pratipāditāḥ 
janmanyaniṣṭalagnarkṣatithyādipratipādanam  

tattacchāntividhiścaiva saṃkṣepeṇa pradarśitaḥ 
prasavasya vikārāśca kathitāḥ śāntisaṃyutāḥ  

evaṃ jātakavarye'tra niviṣṭā viṣayāḥ śatam 
vijñāya vibudhāstvetān prāpnuvantu yaśaḥ śriyam
